PVV_i.0,0–1.1,2	vimukta āvaraṇa kleśam dīpta akhila guṇa śriyam svayam api kṛtinām mahadbhiḥ anyaiḥ api gamitaḥ bahu vistaraiḥ nna yoyam aham api na nija eka lābha lubdhaḥ na ca para kṛtya rasa abhilāṣa muktaḥ śāstra ādau= avidhnena tad samāpti artham bhagavati prasāda janane śrotṛ jana anugraha arthañca stuti pūrvakam ācāryaḥ namaskāra ślokam āha vidhūta kalpanā jāla gambhīra udāra mūrtaye namaḥ samantabhadrāya samanta spharaṇa tviṣe vidhūtam vidhvastam anutpattika dharma tām āpāditam kalpanā grāhya grāhaka adhya āropaḥ sā eva jālam bandhana hetu tvāt yāsām tāḥ vidhūta kalpanā jālāḥ etena dharma kāyaḥ uktaḥ dvaya śūnyatāyāḥ dharmadhātu tvāt tad adhigamasya dharma kāya tvāt gambhīrāḥ ca khaḍga śrāvaka ādya viṣaya tvāt udārāḥ ca sakala jñeya satva artha vyāpanāt iti gambhīraḥ ābhyām sa ambhogika nairmmāṇika kāyau= uktau tayoḥ eva sva rūpa tvāt vidhūta kalpanā jālāḥ gambhīra udārāḥ mūrttayaḥ yasya sa vidhūta kalpanā jāla gambhora udāra etena sva artha sampad uktā trikāya lakṣaṇa tvāt tasyāḥ 
PVV_1.1,3	 samantam niravaśeṣam bhadram kalyāṇam para artha sampad sambhāra lakṣaṇam yasmāt asau samantabhadraḥ anayā bhagavat nāma vyutpattyā para artha sampad abhihitāḥ samantataḥ spharanti iti samanta spharaṇyaḥ tviṣaḥ tāvat tviṣaḥ deśanā yasya sa samanta spharaṇa tviś vastu tattva avabhāsana upāya tā ca tu iṣ deśanayoḥ sādharmyam anena para artha sampad upāyaḥ darśitaḥ deśanā dvāreṇa bhagavatā jagat artha karaṇāt etena stutiḥ uktāḥ asādhāraṇānām sva para artha sampatti tad upāyānām upadarśanāt sarvu atra namaḥ śabda yogāt caturthī anena namaskāra ubhihitaḥ yadā tu samantabhadra śabdaḥ rūḍhyā bodhisattva viśeṣe vartate tadā api pada vyākhyānam pūrvavat eva ayantu viśeṣaḥ vidhūta kalpanā jāla tvam bodhisattva bhūmi āvaraṇa prahāṇataḥ veditavyam gāmbhīryantu khaḍga śrāvakā viṣaya tvāt audāryantu darśa bhūm īśvara bodhisattva māhātmya atiśayataḥ kāyatrayantu bodhisattvānām api asti prakarṣa niṣṭha āgamanāt tu bhagavatām vyavasthāpyate deśanā ca prasiddhā eva teṣām 
PVV_1.2,0–1.2,1	 śrotṛ doṣa bāhulyāt śāstreṇa para upakāram apaśyan sūkta abhyāsa bhāvita citta tām eva ātmanaḥ śāstra ārambha kāraṇandarśayan vakra uktyā doṣa tāpa nayanena śāstre śrotṛt pravartayitumā ha prāyas prākṛta saktiḥ apratibala prajñaḥ janaḥ kevalam na anarthyeva su bhāṣitaiḥ parigatāḥ vidveṣṭi apīrṣya amalaiḥ tena ayam na para upakāraḥ iti naḥ cintā api cetaḥ tatas sūkta abhyāsa vibarddhita vyasanam iti atra anubaddha spṛham 
PVV_1.2,2	 prāyas bhūyān bāhulyena vā janaḥ prākṛteṣu bahis śāstreṣu saktiḥ abhiṣvaṅgaḥ yasya sa prākṛta saktiḥ anena kuprajña tvam śrotṛ doṣaḥ uktaḥ apratibalā śāstra artha grahaṇam pratyaśaktā prajñā yasya asau= apratibala prajñaḥ anena ajña tvam uktam kevalam na anarthyeva sūbhāṣitaiḥ kintu su bhāṣita abhidhāyinam īrṣyā para saṃpattau cetasaḥ vyāroṣaḥ sā eva malaḥ citta malinīkaraṇāt taiḥ parigataḥ yuktaḥ san vidveṣṭi api īrṣyā malaiḥ iti vyakti apekṣayā bahuvacanam anena yathākramam anarthi tvam amādhyasthi añca uktam tena śrotṛ doṣa kalā arpena ripsitaḥ vārttika ākhyaḥ granthaḥ param upakaroti iti para upakāraḥ iti naḥ asmāka na asti kathantarhi śāstra karaṇe pravṛttiḥ iti āha cetaḥ ciram dīrgha kālam sya abhyāsena vivarddhita vyasanam vistārita abhiṣvaṅgam iti hetoḥ atra vārtika karaṇe jāta abhilāṣam etena kuprajña tā ādi doṣa jātam ātmanaḥ bodhitāḥ śrotāraḥ tad parihāreṇa śāstre pravartitāḥ eva bhavanti 
PVV_i.0–2,1–1.3,3^1	 ayam ācā ryaḥ bṛhat ācāryīya pra mā ṇa sa mu cca yaḥ śā stre vārttikam cikīrṣuḥ svatas kṛta bhagavat namaskāraḥ tad śāstra ārambha samaye tad ācārya kṛta bhagavat namaskāra ślokam vyākhyātu kāmaḥ prathamam pramāṇa sāmānya lakṣaṇam āha pramāṇam avisaṃvādi jñānam jñānam pramāṇaṃna ajñānam indriya artha sannikarṣa ādi kīdṛśam avisaṃvādi visaṃvādanam visaṃvādaḥ vañjanam tad yogāt visaṃvādi na tathā asau= avisaṃvādi avisamvādanam uktam iti arthaḥ kim punar iti āha artha kriyā sthitiḥ avisaṃvādanam yathā upadarśita arthasya kriyāyāḥ sthitiḥ pramāṇa yogya tā avisaṃvādanam atas ca yatas jñānāt artham paricchidya api na pravartate pravṛttaḥ vā kutaścid pratibandha ādeḥ artha kriyāt na adhigacchati tat api pramāṇam eva pramāṇa yogya tā lakṣaṇasya avisaṃvādasya sattvāt sā eva pramāṇa yogya tā katham asatyām artha kriyā prāptau niścīyate iti ced yat tāvat asakṛt vyavahāra abhyāsāt darśana mātreṇa upalakṣita bhrama vivikta svarūpa viśeṣam sādhana adhyakṣam tasya svatas eva pramāṇa yogya tā niścayaḥ kṛtrima akṛtrima m aṇiḥ upyādi tatva niścaya vat aṃnumānasya ca sādhya pratibaddha janmanaḥ vyabhicāra āśaṅkā virahāt 
PVV_1.3,3^2	 artha kriyā nirbhāsantu pratyakṣam svatas eva artha kriyā anubhava ātmakam na tatra para artha kriyā apekṣyate iti tat api svatas niścita prāmāṇyam atas eva artha kriyā paraṃpara anusaraṇāt anavasthā doṣa upi dusthaḥ eva yat tu a nabhyastad aśāyām saṃdigdha prāmāṇyam utpattau tasya artha kriyā jñānāt anumānāt vā prāmāṇyam niścīyate etat ca avisaṃvādanam bāhya artha itara vādayoḥ samānam pramāṇa lakṣaṇam vi jñāḥ na nayepi sādhana nirbhāsa jñāna anantaram arthaṃkriyā nirbhāsa jñānam eva saṃvādaḥ atas vijñaptimātra tve pramāṇa itara vibhāga vyavahāraḥ asaṃkīrṇṇaḥ 
PVV_1.3,4–1.3,6	 nanu śabda gandha rasa sparśān citra rūpañca paśyataḥ jñānasya param artha kriyā jñānam na asti iti tad pramāṇan na syāt iti āha śābdepi abhiprāya nivedanāt śābde śabda janite jñāne api śabdāt gandha ādi viṣaye api abhiprāyasya abhipreta artha kriyāyāḥ nivedanāt pratipādanāt prāmāṇyam artha kriyā hi kvacid svarūpa pratipattiḥ eva kvacid tatas anyāḥ yathāsambhavam vyavahāra viṣayaḥ tad prāpaṇañca prāmāṇyam iti na avyāpakam pramāṇa lakṣaṇam 
PVV_1.4,0–1.4,2	 nanu śabdasya artha pratibandha abhāvāt na prāmāṇyam syāt iṣyate ca anumāna tvāt iti āha vaktṛ vyāpāra viṣayaḥ yorthaḥ buddhau prakāśate prāmāṇyam tatra śabdasya na artha tattva nibandhanam vaktṛḥ vyāpāraḥ vivakṣā tasya viṣayaḥ yaḥ arthaḥ samāropita bahī rūpaḥ jñāna ākāraḥ prakāśate buddhau vivakṣā ātmikāyām tatra śabdasya prāmāṇyam liṅga tvam śabdāt uccaritāt vivakṣita artha pratibhāsī vikalponumīyate iti arthaḥ tad kārya tvāt tad śabdasya na tad pratibandha abhāvāt 
PVV_1.5,0–1.5,2	 nanu ghaṭoyam iti ādi jñānāt pravartamānasya sambandha usti eva iti tat pramāṇam syāt iti āha gṛhīta grahaṇāt na iṣṭam sāṃvṛtam dhī pramāṇa tā pravṛtteḥ tad pradhāna tvāt heya upādeya vastuni gṛhīta gra darśana uttara kālam sāṃvṛtam vikalpa jñānam pramāṇam na iṣṭam darśana gṛhītasya eva grahaṇāt tena eva ca prāpayitum śakya tvāt sāṃvṛtam akiñcitkaram eva kasmāt punar ddhiyaḥ pramāṇatā iṣyate na indriya ādeḥ heya upādeya vastu viṣayāyāḥ pravṛtteḥ tat jñāna pradhāna tvāt dhiyaḥ eva prāmāṇyam na hi indriyam asti iti eva pravṛttiḥ kintarhi jñāna sadbhavāt sādhakatamañca pramāṇam tasya avyavahita vyāpāra tvāt 
PVV_1.6,0–1.6,2	 evam phala arthinām pravṛtti vyavahāra kāri tvena dhiyaḥ prāmāṇyam pratipāditam sāmpratam adhigama phala vibhāga kāri tvam āha viṣaya ākāra bhedāt ca dhiyodhi gama bhedataḥ dhiyaḥ viṣayasya iva ākāraḥ viṣaya ākāraḥ nīla ādiḥ tasya bhedāt viśeṣāt adhisya artha pratīteḥ bhedāt viśeṣāt hiya eva prāmāṇyam nīla svarūpam hi jñānam nīlapratītiḥ anyādṛśam anyathā iti dhīḥ eva pramāṇam 
PVV_1.6,3–1.6,6	 nanu yathā adhigama sādhanam ākāraḥ tathā indriyam api tat utpatteḥ atas āha bhāvāt eva asya tad bhāve tasya ākārasya bhāve asya adhigamasya bhāvāt eva sādhanam avyavahita tvāt na tu indriya ādi tad bhāvepi jñāna anutpattau= adhi gama abhāvāt kaścid āha sarva jñānānām abādhita tva lakṣaṇam prāmāṇyam svatas eva sidhyate bādha kāraṇa doṣa jñānābhyām kvacid tat apohyate yathā śuktikāyām rajata jñāne candra dvaya darśane vā tat ca idam ayuktam yatas svarūpasya svatas gatiḥ 
PVV_1.6,7	 svarūpasya svatas gati rna prāmāṇyasya svatas hi prāmāṇyasya abhivyaktiḥ vvaktavyā na tu utpattiḥ jñāna ātma bhūtasya svasmāt utpatti virodhāt yadi ca svatas abādhita tvam prāmāṇyam abhivyaktyā vyavasthāpitam na tasya bādhakānām sahasreṇa api bādhaḥ yuktaḥ atha sambhavati bādhake bādhaka adarśanam yatra tatra ābādhita tvam apodyate bādhaka darśanena evantarhi bādhakā darśanāt na ābādhita tvam kintarhi bādhaka abhāvāt tasya ca adarśanāt anyat na sādhanam tad ced asādhanam na ābādhita tvam nāma prāmāṇyam na api asya svatas siddhiḥ atas prathamam bādhaka adarśanāt prasaktam abādhita tvam bādha darśanāt apodyate iti kim atra ayuktam īdṛśaḥ eva bādhya bādhaka bhāvaḥ sarvvataḥ 
PVV_1.6,8	 kīdaśaḥ atra prasaṅga arthaḥ kim sattvam uta sattva niścayau sambhāvanā mātram vā tatra na tāvat anayoḥ pakṣayoḥ apavādaḥ yuktaḥ sataḥ kenacid api bādhitum aśakyatvāt antyepi na svatas abādhita tva niścayaḥ tad viruddha tvāt sambhāvanāyāḥ aniścitam eva tatra ābādhita tvam katham anyathā utpadyate iti ced na tarhi svatas prāmāṇya niścayaḥ iti yatra api bādha darśanam na asti tatra api anāśvāsaḥ eva evañca bādhya bādhaka bhāvaḥ sat asat tā pa kṣaya uḥ asaṅgataḥ veditavyaḥ 
PVV_1.7,0–1.7,1^1	 prāmāṇyam vyavahāreṇa yadi svarūpa mātram svatas gamyate na prāmāṇyam kathantarhi tat avagamyam iti āha prāmāṇyam vyavahāreṇa artha kriyā jñānena yasya sādhana jñānasya tādātmyāt anubhūtepi prāmāṇye sa āśaṅkā vyavaharttāraḥ a nabhyāsa vaśāt anutpanna anurūpa niścayāḥ tatra artha kriyā jñānena prāmāṇya niścayaḥ anyatra tu vibhrama śaṅkā saṅkocāt utpattau= eva svarūpasya prāmāṇyasya svatas gatiḥ iti uktam athavā cakṣuḥ vijñānena rūpakṣaṇaḥ ekaḥ dṛśyate na bhāvī prāpyaḥ na api sparśaḥ tad kayam anya darśanam anya prāptyā pramāṇam evam hi ati prasaṅgaḥ syāt anumānañca vyāpti grahaṇa sāpekṣam vyāptiḥ ca pratyakṣeṇa puras vartti rūpa mātra grāhiṇā kathaṃśakya grahāḥ 
PVV_1.7,1^2	 deśa kāla vyakti vyāptyā ca vyāptiḥ ucyate yatra yatra dhūmaḥ tatra tatra agniḥ iti pratyakṣa pṛṣṭha jaḥ ca vikalpaḥ na pramāṇam pramāṇa vyāpāra anukārī tvasā āviṣyate yatra ayam adhyakṣavya apāram atikramya adhikam āropayati tatra na pramāṇam amūlaka tvāt tasya pramāṇa prameyasya vijātīya vyāvṛtteḥ adhyakṣeṇa dṛṣṭa tvāt asti eva mūlam iti ced na sajātīya vyāvṛttyā viśeṣita tvāt tasyāḥ anyathā śābaleyanā śam pratiyatā pratyakṣeṇa go mātra nāśaḥ vyavasthāpyeta anumānāt ca vyāpti grahaṇe anavasthā pattiḥ atas āha svarūpasya svatas gatiḥ 
PVV_1.7,2–1.7,3	 sva rūpa mātram svatas gamyate na prāpya rūpa sāpekṣam prāmāṇyat nāma kiñcid asti kathantarhi tad vyavasthā iti āha prāmāṇyam vyavahāreṇa sāṃvyavahārikasya idam pramāṇasya lakṣaṇam saṃvyavahāraḥ ca bhāvi bhūta rūpa ādi kṣaṇānām ekatvena saṃvāda viṣayonavagītaḥ saru u asya sādhya sādhanayoḥ eka vyakti darśanesamasta tad jātīya tathā tva vyavasthānam samvā dam avadhārayanti vyavaharttāraḥ tad anurodhāt prāmāṇyam vyavasthāpyate tattvataḥ tu sva samvedana mātram apravṛtti nivṛttikam 
PVV_1.7,4–1.7,6	 nanu yatra tāvat abhyasta sādhana jñāna ādiṣu nirasta bhramāḥ vyavahāriṇaḥ teṣām svatas eva prāmāṇya niścayaḥ yat tu a nabhyasta sādhanam jñānam tasya api vyavahāreṇa iti niṣphalam śāstra praṇayanam iti āha śāstram moha nirtanam yadi vyavahārataḥ pramāṇa svarūpa siddhiḥ paraspara virodhīni lakṣaṇa śāstrāṇi na syuḥ tasmāt śāstreṇa lakṣaṇa upadarśanāt tad viṣayaḥ saṃmohaḥ nivartanīyaḥ yena para loka niḥśreyasa ādeḥ vyavahāra aprasiddhasya siddhiḥ bhavati 
PVV_1.7,7–1.7,9	 tat evam avisamvādanam pramāṇa lakṣaṇa mukta bhidānīm anyat āha ajñāta artha prakāśaḥ vā prakāśanam prakāśaḥ ajñā tasya arthasya prakāśaḥ jñānam tad pramāṇam artha grahaṇena dvi candra ādi jñānasya nirāsaḥ ajñāta grahaṇena sāmvṛtasya avayavi ādi viṣayasya pṛthak gṛhītānām eva rūpa ādīnām ekatvena vikalpanāt smaraṇañca pūrva gṛhīta artha vikalpa rūpa tvāt na adhika grāhi gṛhīte ca prāktanam eva pramāṇam idānīntu smaraṇam apra vartakam tasya eva sandehāt 
PVV_1.7,10–1.7,11	 nanu avisamvādāt eva ajñāta artha prakāśaḥ jñātavyaḥ anyathā pīta śaṃkha jñānam api pramāṇam syāt tathā ca avisamvādi tvam eva pramāṇam astu kim anena abhi hitena syāt etat yadi sambhavitva mātre lakṣaṇam syāt kim nu uddiṣṭa tvena anyathā jñāna tva sattva ādikam api lakṣaṇam syāt nanu avisamva ādibhyaḥ ajñāta artha prakāśakam jñāyate na tu jñāna tva ādibhyaḥ iti pūrvvasya apekṣaṇīya tā lakṣaṇena na tu pareṣām iti viśeṣaḥ yadi evam tadā avisamvādi tvepya jñāta artha prakāśanam apekṣate eva na anyathā sāṃvṛtasya nirāsaḥ śakyaḥ karttum tasmāt ubhayam api paraspara sāpekṣam eva lakṣaṇamba uddhavyam 
PVV_1.8,0–1.8,9	 nanu sva lakṣaṇa pratīteḥ ūrddhvam sāmā nyaviṣayam jñānam ajñāta artha prakāśaka tvāt pramāṇam prāptam tat eva āha svarūpa adhigateḥ param prāptam sāmānya vijñānam pramāṇam iti śeṣaḥ atra āha avijñāte sva lakṣaṇe yat jñānam iti abhiprāyāt ajñāta sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam yat jñānam tad pramāṇam na jñāta viṣayam iti abhiprāyāt na atiprasa ṅgaḥ evantarhi anumānam api sāmānya viṣaya tvāt pramāṇam na syāt na etat asti tat api ca lakṣa ṇam eva anityādi rūpa tayā viṣayīkaroti kim punar adhigata sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam eva pramāṇam iṣṭam sva lakṣaṇa vicārataḥ sva lakṣaṇa vicārataḥ artha kriyā arthibhiḥ sva lakṣaṇa meva pramāṇena anviṣyate tasya eva artha kriyā sādhana tvāt yat eva ca taiḥ anviṣyate tat eva śāstre vicāryate sāṃvyavahārika pramāṇa adhikārāt 
PVV_1.9,0–1.9,7	 yathā ukta dvividha lakṣaṇam uktam yat pramāṇam tadvat pramāṇam bhagavān tadvat bhagavān pramāṇam yathā abhihitasya satya catuṣṭayasya avisamvādanāt tasya eva paraiḥ ajñātasya prakāśanāt ca yadi evam namaskāra śloke pramāṇāya iti eva astu pragāṇa bhūtāya iti kimartham iti āha abhūta vinivṛttaye bhūta unktiḥ bhūta śabda nirdeśaḥ abhūtasya nityasya nivṛtti artha nityam pramāṇam na asti iti arthaḥ sādhana apekṣā tatas yuktām pramāṇatā tatas sādhana apekṣā pramāṇatā yuktāḥ bhagavataḥ ca prāmāṇya sādhanam vakṣyamāṇam 
PVV_1.10–1.11,0–1.10–1.11,3	 nityam pramāṇam na eva asti prāmāṇyāt kasmāt punar nityam pramāṇam na eva asti āha vastunā urtha kriyā kāriṇaḥ sataḥ gateḥ jñānasya prāmāṇyāt na asti nityam pramāṇam atra eva kāraṇam āha vastu saṃgateḥ jñeya anityatayā tasyāḥ adhrauvyāt jñeyasya vastunaḥ artha kriyā kāri tvena anitya tvāt tasyāḥ vastu saṅgateḥ api tat janyāya dhrauvyāda nitya tvāt 
PVV_1.10–1.11,4–1.10–1.11,7	 syāt etat anitya viṣayam anityam eva jñānam kevalam yasya tat jñānam sa jñātā nityaḥ bhaviṣyati iti āha krama janmanām nityāt utpatti viśleṣāt apekṣāyāḥ ayogataḥ jñānasya nityāt jñātuḥ utpatteḥ vvi śleṣāt nityam hi sadā eka rūpam yadi krama janmanām jñānānām arjana samartham sakṛt eva tāni kuryyāt atha samartham api nityam krami sahakāryi apekṣayā krameṇa karoti tat ayuktam apekṣāyāḥ ayogāt 
PVV_1.10–1.11,8–1.10–1.11,13	 kasmāt sahakāri apekṣā na yuktā iti āha kathañcid na upakārya tvāt nityasya sarvvadā aviśiṣṭa svabhāvasya paraiḥ saha kāribhiḥ kathañcid na upakārya tvāt kva tad apekṣā tatas sarvu ajñānāni sakṛt eva kuryyāditya vāryyaḥ prasaṅgaḥ syāḥ detat santāna viśeṣāt nisarga siddhāṃpara aparakṣaṇa ātmakam sādhana apekṣā śūnyam anityam eva pramāṇam bhaviṣyati iti āha anityepya pramāṇa tā anityepi api śabdāt nityepya pramāṇa tā sādhana abhāvaḥ iti arthaḥ 
PVV_i.i–2,0	 nanu santi eva sādhanāni yathā sthitvā pravṛtteḥ saṃsthāna viśeṣāt artha kriyā sādhana tvāt kārya tva ādeḥ ca vimati adhikaraṇāni tanu bhuvana karaṇa ādīni upādāna ādi abhijña buddhimat pūrvvakāṇi turyya ādi vat prāsāda ādi vat vā asya ādi vat ghaṭa ādi vat ce ti evamādīni sthitvā pravṛtti ādayaḥ turī tantu ādiṣu upādāna ādi abhijña buddhimat pūrvvaka tva mātreṇa upalabdha vyāpta yodhi karaṇa siddhānta nyāyena nitya vyāpi saru vajña nitya buddhi āśraya ātma viśeṣa viśiṣṭam eva pakṣe sādhyam upanayanti dhūmaḥ iva parvata varttinam dahanam na hi anityena avyāpinā vā nānā deśa kāla kārya jātam śakya kriyam na api sarvu asya kāryasya upādāna kāraṇa ani asarvva vid veditum samarthaḥ na api anityayā buddhyā atīta anāgata kāla vartti vastu jātam jñātum śakyam tad vedanāt ca sarvvavid na ca ete hetavaḥ asiddhāḥ dharmiṇi sattva niścayāt na ca viruddhāḥ sa pakṣe sattvāt na anaikāntikāḥ sādhya sādhanayoḥ vyāpti niścayāt na ca kāla atyaya apadiṣṭāḥ sādhya sādhana bādhana abhāvāt na api prakaraṇa samāḥ viparyaya sādhaka hetu abhāvāt iti atra āha 
PVV_1.12,0–1.12,1	 sthitvā pravṛttiḥ saṃsthāna viśeṣa artha kriyā ādiṣu iṣṭa siddhiḥ sthitvā pravṛttiḥ saṃsthāna viśeṣa artha kriyā artha kriyā ādiṣu sādhaneṣu upādāna ādi abhijña buddhimat pūrvvaka tve sādhye iṣṭa siddhiḥ asmākam vayam api sādhāraṇā sādhāraṇa cetanā lakṣaṇa karma nirmitam jagat vicitram icchāmaḥ tad sādhayatā ca pareṇa sāhāyyakam anuṣṭhitam yena sādhya gatena viśeṣeṇa vinā dharmiṇi liṅgam anupapannam tasya eva adhikaraṇa siddhāntena pratītiḥ yathā parvvata varttinaḥ dhūmāt vahneḥ parvvata vartti tvasya na hi anya deśa sthena agninā janyamānasya dhūmasya parvata vartti tvam upapadyate na tu evam nitya tva sarvu ajña tva vyāpi tvā ādi vinā cetanasya tanu bhuvana ādi gatam sthitvā pravṛtti ādikam anupapannam nitya tva ādi viparyaya yoginā api cetanena kriyamāṇam tat ghaṭataḥ eva 
PVV_1.12,2	 nanu uktam eva anitya avyāpinaḥ sarvu adeśa kāla vartti kāryam akāryam asarvvavidaḥ ca sarvvā upādāna ādi abhijña tā na asti ityādinā satyam uktam ayuj tantu uktam karttuḥ ekatva asiddheḥ ekasya karttuḥ aneka deśa kālam kāryam kurvvāṇasya tad upādāna ādikam jānān asya nitya tva ādikam antareṇa sthitvā pravṛtti ādi na upapadyate iti syāt api tādṛśasya adhikaraṇa siddhāntena pratipattiḥ anekena api tu nānā deśa kāla varttinā sva sva kāryasya upādāna ādi jānatā kriyamāṇam sthitvā pravṛtti ādi saṅgatam eva atas eva eka tvasya api tatas eva siddhiḥ ayuktā anekasya api hetu tva yogāt pakṣā yoga vyavacchedaḥ eva tu sādhyasya adhikaraṇa siddhāntena sidhyatu na tu tad adhikaḥ vahneḥ iva ca andana tva ādiḥ 
PVV_1.12,3	 nanu anekaḥ eva te cetanā vantobhimatāḥ na ca upādāna ādikam tanu ādīnām te jānate na api tad kartṛ tvam ātmanaḥ manyante tat katham amī karttāraḥ atha ādhipatya mātreṇa eṣām karttṛ tvam na tu upakaraṇa ādya ayojanena vyāpāreṇa yathā candrasya candra kānta drutau tena upādāna ādi abhijña tā kartṛ tva abhimānaḥ ca na eṣām evantarhi upādāna ādi abhijña cetana pūrvvaka tve sādhye na iṣṭa siddhiḥ vvaktavyā yadi evam bhavataḥ eva sūkṣma īkṣikā tadā cetanā pūrvvaka tva mātram sādhaya dṛṣṭānte ca kumbhakāra tva vat sat api upādāna ādi abhijña tvam aprayojakam manyasva 
PVV_1.12,4–1.12,6	 sat katham pariharttavyam iti ced tat kim kumbhakāra tvam aparihārya aprayojaka tvāt tyajyate iti ced upādāna ādi abhijña tvepi samānam etat upādāna ādikam ajānatā upi buddhimataḥ anekasya adhiṣṭhāna mātreṇa api kāryyāṇām utpatti yogāt asiddhiḥ vā dṛṣṭānte saṃśayaḥ athavā atha nitya tva ādi viśiṣṭa puruṣa pūrvvaka tvam eva sādhyam tadā asiddhiḥ dṛṣṭānte sādhya śūnyaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti arthaḥ na hi kvacid dṛṣṭānte tādṛśam sādhyam upalabdham yena vyāptiḥ pratīyeta asiddha vyāptikaḥ ca hetuḥ anaikāntikaḥ eva sthitvā pravṛtteḥ artha kriyā samartha tvāt iti hetvoḥ saṃśayaḥ athavā anaikāntika tvam tena eva tu abhimata puruṣeṇa na hi asau sthitvā pravartamānaḥ kāryyeṣu artha kriyākārī vā tathā puruṣa adhiṣṭhitaḥ anavasthā prasaṅgāt 
PVV_1.13,0–1.13,2	 siddham yādṛś adhiṣṭhātṛ bhāva abhāva anuvṛttimat sanniveśa ādi athavā yādṛśa buddhimat pūrvvakam sanniveśa ādi dṛṣṭānte dṛṣṭam tasya dharmiṇī a siddhiḥ iti āha ghaṭe dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇi sanniveśa ādi yādṛśam pṛthu budhna udara ādi dṛṣṭa eka vyākti jātyā viśeṣitam adhiṣṭhātuḥ puṃsaḥ anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāna vat vyavahāra pragalbha puruṣāṇām tad siddhānta anurodha rahitānām pratyakṣa balena anurūpa niścaya utpādāt siddham niścitam tat yuktam tasmāt yat anumīyate

PVV_1.26,0–1.26,2	 api ca yeṣu satsu bhavati eva yat tebhyaḥ anyasya kalpane tad hetu tvena sarvatra hetūnām anavasthitiḥ yeṣu kāraṇeṣu satsu yad kāryam bhavati eva tebhyaḥ kāraṇebhyonyasya padārthasya tad kārya hetu tvena kalpane sarvu atra kārya hetūnām anavasthitiḥ prāpnoti aparāpara kalpanayā tasmāt dṛṣṭa sāmarthyāḥ eva kṣiti bīja ādayaḥ kāraṇam aṅkurasya na īśvara ādiḥ adṛṣṭa sāmarthyaḥ 
PVV_1.27,0–1.27,2	 nanu kṣiti ādiḥ api akāraka avasthātaḥ na viśiṣṭasva bhāvaḥ kāraṇa avasthāyām aṅkurasya iti āha svabhāva pariṇāmena hetuḥ aṅ kurajanmani bhūmi ādiḥ tasya saṃskāre tad viśeṣasya darśanāt upasarpaṇa pratyayāt adṛṣṭa saha kāriṇaḥ prāpta kārya utpāda anuguṇa atiśayā bhūmi ādiḥ kārya anuguṇa atiśaya tāratamya m uktā apara aparakṣaṇa lakṣaṇena antya avasthā prāptā aṅkura janmani hetuḥ bhavati sa tu pūrvva para eka rūpaḥ krama ākramayoḥ artha kriyā virodhāt kutas etat iti ced tasya bhūmi ādeḥ karṣaṇa pāṃsu prakṣepa ādinā saṃskāre tasya aṅakurasya puṣṭatara ādi viśeṣasya darśanāt

PVV_1.36,0–1.36,3^1	 nanu īdṛśasya pramāṇasya kim sādhanam iti āha sādhanam karuṇā abhyāsāt sā buddheḥ deha saṃśrayāt asiddhā abhyāsaḥ iti ca id na āśraya pratiṣedhataḥ sādhanam karuṇā duḥkha aduḥkha hetoḥ ca samuddharaṇa kāma tā karuṇā sā bhagavataḥ prāmāṇyasya sādhanam sā eva karuṇā iti atas āha abhyāsāt sā gautra viśeṣāt kalyāṇa mitra saṃsarggāt anuśaya darśanāt ca kaścid mahāsattvaḥ kṛpāyām upajāta spṛhaḥ sā dara nirantara aneka janma paramparā prabhava abhyāsena sa ātmībhūta kṛpayā preryamāṇaḥ sarvu asattvānām samudaya hā anyā duḥkha hānāya mārga bhāvanayā nirodha prāpaṇāya ca deśanām kartu kāmaḥ svayam asākṣātkṛtasya deśanāyām vipralambha sambhāvanāt catur ārya satyāni sākṣāt karoti iti bhagavati sādhanam kṛpā prāmāṇyasya

PVV_1.37,0–1.37,2	 prāṇa apāna indriya dhiyām dehāt eva na kevalāt sajāti nirapekṣāṇām janma janma parigrahe atiprasaṅgāt prāṇaḥ vāyuḥ ūdrdhva ga tad viparītaḥ apānaḥ indriyāṇi cakṣuḥ ādīni dhīḥ buddhiḥ tāsām sa jāti nirapekṣāṇām kāraṇa bhūta pūrvvasa jāti prāṇa ādi puñja nirapekṣāṇām dehāt eva bhavati kutas iti āha janma parigrahe ati prasaṅgāt yadi mahābhūtebhyaḥ eva kevalebhyaḥ prāṇa ādīnām janma grahaḥ tadā sarvu asmāt bhaveyuḥ iti sarvam prāṇi mayam jagat syāt na ca asti etat tasmāt pūrvvasa jāti sāpekṣāṇām eva akṣa ādīnām dehāt janma iti pūrvva janma pratibandha siddhiḥ

PVV_1.80,0–1.81,2	 tasmāt svasya eva saṃskāram niyamena anuvartate tat na antarīyakam cittam atas citta samāśritam tasmāt svasya eva saṃskāram niyamena anuvartate tat na antarīyakam cittam eṣitavyam atas cittam āśritam cittam citta saṃskārasya eva anuvartanāt deha saṃskārantu vyabhicarati pratisaṃkhyāna balinām iti uktam cetaḥ śarīrayoḥ bheda pakṣeṇa āśraya āśrayi bhāvaḥ ayuktaḥ iti pratipādya śaktipakṣepya bheda ātmake doṣam āha yathā śruta ādi saṃskāraḥ kṛtaḥ cetasi cetasi kālena vyajyate abhedāt syāt dehepi tatas guṇaḥ yathā śruta ādisam punar yathā prabodha pratyayam cetasi kālena krama bhāvinā vyajyate tathā abhedāt citta śarīrayoḥ syāt dehepi tatas saṃskāra prabodhakāt pratyayāt guṇaḥ abhivyaktaḥ tatas ca deham paśyatā śruta ādi saṃskāra upi tad ātma bhūtaḥ dṛśyaḥ dṛśyeta tasmāt dehasya āśraya tva pratiṣedhāt tad vināśe citta vināśaḥ na iti janma paramparāsu yuktaḥ kṛpā abhyāsaḥ

PVV_1.153–1.155,9–1.153–1.155,15	 rāga ādeḥ vikāraḥ api sukha ādi jaḥ rāga ādeḥ doṣa sāmya avasthāyām vikāra upi vṛddhi lakṣaṇaḥ yaḥ sa sukha ādi jaḥ āntara dhātu sāmya sparśa prabhavena sukha ādinā varddhante rāga ādayaḥ vaiṣamya jena duḥkhena rāga āsya anudbhavaḥ yadi vācyam kena udbhavaḥ sāmyāt mada vṛddhiḥ smaraḥ tatas vaiṣamya jena duḥkhena dveṣasya utpādanāt tad viruddhasya rāga āsya anudbhavaḥ yadi mataḥ tadā vācyam kena hetūnā rāgasya udbhavaḥ sāmyāt doṣāṇām madasya śukrasya vṛddhiḥ smaraḥ rāgaḥ śukra vṛddheḥ yat i iṣṭam etat api ayuktam yatas rāgī viṣama doṣaḥ api dṛṣṭaḥ sāmye api na aparaḥ rāgī viṣama doṣaḥ api rāga caritaḥ kaścid dṛṣṭaḥ sāmya īpi na aparaḥ pratisaṃkhyāna balī manda rāga prakṛtiḥ vvā dṛṣṭaḥ

PVV_1.180–1.184,14–1.180–1.184,18	 tat tasya kāraṇam prāhuḥ tat teṣām api vidyate sati eva yasmin vastuni yasya janma yasya vikāre sati eva vā yasya vikriyā tat tasya janminaḥ vikāriṇaḥ ca kāraṇam prāhuḥ vvidvāṃsaḥ tad janma sati eva bīja udaka pṛthivī ādiṣu tad utkarṣa apakarṣa ādi vikāre ca vikṛta tvam teṣām kaṇṭaka ādīnām api asti iti tepi sa hetukāḥ eva evam skandhāḥ api nanu sparśe sati bhavati cakṣuḥ vvijñānam asati ca na bhavati na ca tat kāraṇam atas ativyāptiḥ iti āha sparśasya rūpa hetu tvāt darśane asti nimitta tā sparśasya rūpa ādi avinirbhāginaḥ saha kāri bhāvena rūpa hetu tvāt darśane cakṣuḥ vvijñāne asti nimitta tā pāramparyeṇa iti na ati vyāptiḥ 
PVV_1.185–1.186,0–1.185–1.186,5	 etat ca vyatirekam abhyupagamya uktam na tu rūpam upadarśya sparśa abhāve netra buddheḥ abhāvaḥ śakya darśanaḥ rūpa sparśayoḥ avinirbhāga vartti tvāt tasya ca duḥkhasya nityānām pratiṣedhena na īśvara ādeḥ ca sambhavaḥ asāmarthyāt atas hetuḥ bhava vāñchā nityānām krama ākramābhyām artha kriyā āyām asāmarthyāt pratiṣedhena ca na īśvara ādeḥ ādi grahaṇāt pradhāna puruṣa ādeḥ kāraṇāt sambhavaḥ utpādaḥ atas nityāt anutpatteḥ duḥkhasya hetuḥ bhava vāñchā janma tṛṣṇā janma sthāna avasthā sattva ādi abhilāṣa ātmikā parigrahaḥ yasmāt deśa viśeṣasya tad prāpti āśā kṛtaḥ tṛṇām yasmāt deśa viśeṣasya parigrahaḥ tad prāpti tṛṣṇā kṛtaḥ nṛṇām nṛ śabdaḥ prāṇi upalakṣaṇaḥ tatas garbha sthāna ādānam api tat tṛṣṇā kṛtam eva 
PVV_1.187–1.189,0–1.187–1.189,3	 nanu uktam bha ga vaḥ tā tatra katamassamudayaḥ ārya satyam paunarbhāvikī nandī ti tat katham ekā bhava tṛṣṇā ucyate samudaya satyam iti atra āha sā bhava it śā apti anāpti icchoḥ pravṛttiḥ sukha duḥkhayoḥ yatas api prāṇinaḥ kāma vibhava icche ca te mate yatas kāraṇāt prāṇinaḥ sukha duḥkhayoḥ krameṇa āpti anāpti icchoḥ pravṛttiḥ garbha sthāna parigraha āyātaḥ sā bhavet chā api kāma vibhava icche ca te mate sukha prāpti icchā kāma tṛṣṇā duḥkha viyoga icchā vibhava tṛṣṇā bhava tṛṣṇāyām sukha duḥkha prāpti parihāra icchā pūrvvikāyām garbha sthāna upādāna icchā ātmikāyām dvayoḥ api saṃgrahāt avirodhaḥ 
PVV_1.187–1.189,4–1.187–1.189,6	 sarvatra ca ātma snehasya hetu tvāt saṃpravartate asukhe sukha saṃjñasya samudayasya ca samudaya ātmaka tvāt sarvu atra viṣaye asukhe sukha rahite sukha saṃjñasya duḥkha viparyayaḥ tasya anena aśucau śuci viparyāsa upi kathitaḥ na hi aśucau tathā manyamāna kasyacid sukha saṃjñā aatma snehena iti ātma snehasya hetu tvāt iti ahaṅkāram amakāra utthāpitasya anena ātmani ātma sneha viparyāse uktaḥ saṃpravartate iti anena anitya viparyāsaḥ sūcitaḥ na hi nitya viparyāsamvinā phala arthī pravartate 
PVV_1.187–1.189,7–1.187–1.189,10	 tasmāt tṛṣṇā bhava āśrayaḥ tat evam catur vviparyāsa vāsita mānasaḥ eva ātma snehāt sukha duḥkha prāpti parijihīrṣayā pravartate tathā garbha sthānepi sukha duḥkha prāpti parihāra icchā eva tṛṣṇā tasmāt tṛṣṇā hetuḥ anena hetutaḥ ākhyātam virakta janma adṛṣṭeḥ iti ācāryāḥ saṃpracakṣate adeha rāga at ṛṣṭeḥ ca dehāt rāga samudbhavaḥ 
PVV_1.187–1.189,11–1.187–1.189,14	 nanu viraktasya janma adṛṣṭeḥ iti ācāryāḥ gau te mā dayopi saṃpracakṣate adehasya rāga adṛṣṭeḥ ca dehāt rāga samudbhavaḥ sthitaḥ taṃtaḥ na dehī vīta rāgaḥ atra āha nimitta upagamāt iṣṭam upādānam tu vāryate nimittasya sahakāri kāraṇasya upagamāt dehosya rāgasya saha ākāri kāraṇam iṣṭam tatas na aniṣṭam āpadyate upādānantu dehaḥ rāgasya vāryate rāgaḥ eva tu upādāna kāraṇam na ca rāgaḥ janma hetuḥ viraktasya karuṇayā janma sambhavāt raktasya api tṛṣṇayā eva janma grahaḥ anena pratyayate iti vyākhyātam 
PVV_1.190,0–1.190,1	 imām tu yuktim anvicchan bādhate sva matam svayam janmanā sahabhāvaḥ ced jātānām rāga darśanāt virakta janma adṛṣṭeḥ iti imām yuktim anvicchan cā rvvā kaḥ sva matam svayam rāga hetukaḥ dehaḥ tad hetukaḥ ca rāgaḥ iti anyonya hetu tvāt janma prabandha siddheḥ vīta rāga abhyupagamāt ca sva mata bādhā asya janmanā sahabhāvaḥ rāga ādīnām na pūrvvam rāgosti jātānām rāga darśanāt atas na rāgaḥ deha hetuḥ iti ced 
PVV_1.191–1.194,0–1.191–1.194,4	 sa bhāga jāteḥ prāk siddhiḥ nanu evam deha upi na syāt rāga hetuḥ sahabhāvāt na ca ahetuka tā tatas sabhāgāt sajātīyāt rāgajjāteḥ utpādāt prāc rāgasya siddhiḥ iti āyātam nanu avidyā tṛṣṇā karma ca janma kāraṇam tat katham tṛṣṇā eva kevalā samudayaḥ uktaḥ iti āha kāraṇa tve api na uditam ajñānam uktā tṛṣṇā eva santāna preraṇāt bhave ānantaryāt ca karma api sati tasmin= asaṃbhavāt 
PVV_1.191–1.194,5	 kāraṇa tvepi na uditam ajñānam avidyā moha apara saṃjñakam uktā tṛṣṇā eva tayā eva santā asya pañca skandha santateḥ preraṇāt kim artham bhave janma nimittam karma api hetu tve api na uktam samudaya tvena sati tasmin= ajñāne karmaṇi ca tṛṣṇā asaṃmukhībhāve abhāvāt janmanaḥ ānantaryāt ca tṛṣṇāyāḥ satoḥ api moha karmaṇoḥ tṛṣṇāyāḥ asaṃmukhībhāve janmanaḥ ākṣepakatva asaṃbhavāt yathā vimuktiḥ cittasya iti uktaḥ samudayaḥ 
PVV_1.191–1.194,6–1.191–1.194,9	 tad anānyantikam hetoḥ pratibandha ādi sambhavāt tat etat yathā ukta kāraṇa samudaya svabhāvam duḥkham anātyantikam saṃbhavat ucchedam duḥkha hetoḥ tṛṣṇāyāḥ pratibandhasya saṃbhāvyamāna tvāt ādi śabdāt avidyā ādeḥ sahakāriṇaḥ vaikalya sambhavāt anena nirodhaḥ eva na asti iti vādinaḥ pratinirodhate iti kathitam saṃsāri tvāt aniḥ mokṣaḥ na iṣṭa tvāt aprasiddhitaḥ 
PVV_1.191–1.194,10–1.191–1.194,11	 nanu saṃsāri tvāt aniḥ mmokṣaḥ muktiḥ na asti kasyacid tat katham nirodha sambhāvanā na eṣa doṣaḥ iṣṭa tvāt kaḥ nāma muktim saṃsāriṇaḥ icchati aprasiddhitaḥ tasya na hi saṃsārīm kaścid asti kintu duḥkham kevalam hetu balāt pravartate tad abhāvāt ca na bhavati iti brūmaḥ yadi saṃsārī kaścid na asti kaḥ mukti arthī kim artham pravartate iti āha 
PVV_1.191–1.194,12–1.191–1.194,14	 yāvat ca ātmani na premṇaḥ hāniḥ sa paritasyati tāvat duḥkhitam āropya na ca svasthaḥ avatiṣṭhate yāvat ca ātmani ekatva ahaṃkāra viṣayeṣu skandheṣu premṇaḥ snehasya na hāniḥ tāvat duḥkhitam ātmānam āropya sa prāṇi abhimataḥ duḥkha santānaḥ paritasyati duḥkham āste na ca duḥkha hetu apagama upāyābhyām sa kleśamvinā svasthaḥ avatiṣṭhate

PVV_1.198–1.200,5–1.198–1.200,10	 vinā tena udya hetau na dveṣaḥ na doṣaḥ atas kṛpā matā tena sattva graheṇa vinā adya hetau= apakāriṇi na dveṣa usti ātmanaḥ adarśanāt tad apakāra bhrānti abhāvāt atas doṣa mūlasya ātma grahasya abhāvāt utpadyamānā kṛpā yadi pūrvva karmmā vedhataḥ tadā eva na nirvvāṇam tadā sāṃsārika tā eva syāt iti āha na amuktiḥ pūrva saṃskāra kṣaye anya apratisandhitaḥ akṣīṇa śaktiḥ saṃskāraḥ yeṣām tiṣṭhanti te anadhāḥ manda tvāt karuṇāyāḥ ca na yatnaḥ sthāpane mahān 
PVV_1.198–1.200,11	 na amuktiḥ kintu muktiḥ eva pūrvva saṃskāra kṣaye pūrvva karma āvedha kṣaye sati anyasya duḥkhasya hetu vaikalyāt apratisandhitaḥ yeṣām punar mahā kṛpāṇām prāṇi dhāna paripuṣṭasya janma ākṣepaka karmaṇaḥ saṃskāraḥ akṣīṇa śaktiḥ te anadhāḥ samyaksambuddhāḥ yāvat ākāśan tiṣṭhanti eva śrāvakāṇa an tu karmaṇaḥ niyata kāla sthitika deha ākṣepaka tvāt manda tvāt karuṇāyāḥ yatnaḥ ca mahān sthāpane na asti iti na sadā sthitiḥ 
PVV_1.201–1.205,0–1.201–1.205,4	 tiṣṭhanti eva para adhīnā yeṣām tu mahatī kṛpā tiṣṭhanti eva sarvvadā te para adhīnāḥ pareṣām upakaraṇīkṛta ātmānaḥ mahā munayaḥ yeṣām akāraṇa vatsalānām mahatī kṛpā satkāya dṛṣṭeḥ vigamāt ādyaḥ eva abhavaḥ bhavet mārge ced sahajā hāneḥ na hānau vā bhavaḥ kutas nanu ādyaḥ eva mārgge darśana mārgge satkāgamāt srotaḥ āpannasya bhavaḥ janma antara bandhaḥ na bhavet iti ced sahajā hāneḥ na dvidhā hi sat kāya dṛṣṭiḥ ābhisāṃskārikī yā skandha vyatirikta ātmā adhyavasāyinī sahajā ca tatra prathamā darśana mārgge hīyate na dvitīyā bhāvanā mārga heyāḥ sā ca mohaḥ tṛṣṇāyāḥ ca hetuḥ iti bhavati janma prabandhaḥ yadi tu paṭutara prajñasya ādya eva mārggaḥ mārgga antara svabhāvaḥ tadā hānau vā sahajāyāḥ ātma dṛṣṭeḥ punarbhavaḥ kutas

PVV_1.201–1.205,15–1.201–1.205,17	 duḥkhasya utpāda hetu tvam bandhaḥ nityasya tat kutas aduḥkha utpāda hetu tvam mokṣaḥ nityasya tat kutas duḥkhasya upādāna skandhānām utpāda hetu tvam bandhaḥ tad kutas nityasya krama yaugapadyābhyām artha kriyā virahān aduḥkha utpāda hetu tvam duḥkham pratyaya hetu tā mokṣaḥ na hi pūrvvāpara ekasya bhāvasya duḥkha hetoḥ paścāt ahetu tvam yuktam 
PVV_1.201–1.205,18–1.201–1.205,20	 syāt etat na nityasya hetu tvam bandha mokṣau ca yuktau= iti nitya tva anitya tvābhyām avācyasya pudgalasya tau bhaviṣyate iti manvānam vai bhā ṣi kaḥ mpratyāha anitya tvena yaḥ avācyaḥ sa hetuḥ na hi kasyacid anitya tvena yaḥ avācyaḥ anitya tvam upalakṣaṇam nitya tvena api avācyaḥ sa hetuḥ na hi tasma eva abhāvāt tathā hi yadi asau= anityaḥ na bhavati syāt nityaḥ 
PVV_1.206,0–1.206,3	 atha nityaḥ na bhavati syāt anityaḥ anyonya abhāva lakṣaṇa tvāt anayoḥ eka vidhi pratiṣedhasya apara pratiṣadha vidhinā antarīyaka tvāt na kvacid vastuni dvaya pratiṣedha sambhavaḥ iti pudgalasya abhāvāt ahetu tvam atas bandha mokṣau= api avācye pudgale na yujyete atha nitya tvena avācya tvāt na doṣaḥ iti ced nanu evam anityaḥ eva uktaḥ syāt tathā hi nityam tam āhuḥ vidvāṃsaḥ yaḥ svabhāvaḥ na naśyati nityam tam āhuḥ vvidvāṃsaḥ yaḥ svabhāvaḥ sarvadā na naśyati sa ced īdṛśaḥ na bhavati anityaḥ eva syāt 
PVV_1.207,0–1.207,5	 tyaktvā imām hrepaṇīm dṛṣṭim ataḥ anityaḥ saḥ ucyatām akṣa imām pudgala dṛṣṭim pudgala nairātmya vādinaḥ saṃskāra aniti a tāvādinaḥ ca śāstuḥ śiṣyāṇām hrepaṇīm lajjā varddhanīm tyaktvā anityaḥ sa pudgalaḥ ucyatām yena bandha yujyete eka ākāraḥ nirodhaḥ vyākhyātaḥ   trayaḥ ākārāḥ vakṣyante uktaḥ mārgaḥ tad abhyāsāt āśrayaḥ parivartate mārga satyam catur ākāram vaktum āha uktaḥ mārgaḥ śāstṛ pada vyākhyā avasare nairātmya darśana lakṣaṇaḥ tasya abhyāsa ādā kleśa vāsanā bhūtayā la yaḥ vi jñāḥ nam parivartate kliṣṭa daśā nirodhāt kleśa visaṃyukta citta prabandha ātmanā pariṇamati 
PVV_1.208–1.210,0–1.208–1.210,5	 anena mārgataḥ iti mārga ākāraḥ darśitaḥ kleśa visaṃyoga hetu tvāt sātmye api doṣa bhāvaḥ ced mārga vat mārgasya abhyāsa prakarṣāt sātmya īpi prakṛti tve ca prāpte punar doṣāṇām moha ādīnām bhāvaḥ prāpnoti ced mārga vat yathā bandha avasthāyām doṣa sātmya īpi mārgaḥ abhyāsa vaśāt āvirbhavati atra āha na avibhu tvataḥ na avibhu tvataḥ asāmarthyāt mārga sātmye api sthitasya cetasi na doṣāṇām utpattum sāmarthyam asti tad nidāna bhūtasya satva darśanasya unmūlita tvāt 
PVV_1.208–1.210,6–1.208–1.210,12	 anena śāntate iti nirodha ākāraḥ uktaḥ doṣāṇām sarvu athā śānta tvāt satva darśanam eva punar kasmāt na bhavati iti āha viṣaya grahaṇam dharmom vijñānasya yathā asti saḥ gṛhyate saḥ asya janakaḥ vidyamāna ātmanā iti ca viṣaya grahaṇam vijñānasya tāvat sati grāhya grāhaka bhāvaḥ dharmaḥ yathā ca asti sa sa viṣayaḥ tathā gṛhyate vijñānena viṣayiṇā sa ca viṣayosya vijñānasya janakaḥ vidyamānena ātmanā yathā avasthitena rūpeṇa eṣā prakṛtiḥ asyāḥ tad nimitta antarataḥ skhalat vyāvṛttau pratyaya apekṣam adṛḍham sarpa buddhi vat 
PVV_1.208–1.210,13–1.208–1.210,16	 yathā avasthita vastu grahaṇañca na ātmā eṣā prakṛtiḥ svabhāvaḥ jñānasya viṣayiṇaḥ yathā svabhāvam sva grāhi jñān a jananañca viṣayasya prakṛtiḥ asyāḥ prakṛteḥ tat jñānam nimitta antarataḥ āntarāt avidyā rūpāt āgantukāt ca viṣaya doṣa ādeḥ skhalat viṣaya grahaṇa viparīta ākāram bhavati tat ca vyāvṛttau viṣaya viparīta grahaṇa ākāra tāyāḥ nivṛtti artha pratyaya apekṣam bhrānti nivartaka kāraṇam apekṣyamāṇam adṛḍham asthāṣṇu sarpa buddhi vat yathā sarpabuddhiḥ rajvā bhrānti nimittā jātāḥ rajju svarūpa grāhiṇaḥ pratyayāt nivṛttā na punar udbhavati iti tathā bhrānti nimitta nirāsāt dṛṣṭe nairātmye vastuni sati na asti sattve dṛṣṭi sambhavaḥ jñānasya viṣaya svarūpa grahaṇa pravaṇa tvāt viṣayasya ca su a ākāra arpaṇa pravṛtta tvāt kiñca prabhāsvaram idañcittam prakṛti āgantavaḥ malāḥ prabhāsvaram anātma bhūta doṣa sañcayam idam cittam prakṛtyā svabhāvena ye tu manaḥ doṣāḥ dṛśyante te bhrānti nimitta upanīta tvāt āgantavaḥ asvabhāva bhūtāḥ cetasaḥ tamaḥ tuhina ādayaḥ iva nabhasaḥ 
PVV_1.211–1.222,0–1.211–1.222,4	 tad prāk api asamarthānām paścāt śaktiḥ kaḥ tad maye tad prāk api tasmāt nairātmya darśanāt pūrvvam api tatas śruta cintā adhyavasā nepya āpāta viṣkambhanāt utpattum asamarthānām malānām paścāt mārga niṣpattau śaktiḥ utpattum kva tad maye mārga sātmye svarūpe etat eva āha na alam praroḍhum atyantam syandinyām agni vat bhuvi bādhaka utpatti sāmarthya garbhe śaktaḥ api vastuni 
PVV_1.211–1.222,5	 śaktaḥ api addhatopi manaḥ malaḥ na alam atyantam praroḍhum vastuni citta santāne kīdṛśe bādhaka utpatti sāmarthya garbhe sarva dṛṣṭi bādhakasya nairātmya darśanasya mārga satya utpattiḥ tasyām prabhaviṣṇu tvam tad garbhe ānantaryasya garbhe tasmin syandinyām bhuvi agni vat yathā hi vahneḥ hetu balāt utpannopi syandinyām bhuvi bādhakavatyām na atyantam prarohati tathā mārga utpatti sāmarthya garbhe cetasi utpannāḥ api malāḥ na atyantam virohanti sa ātmībhūta mārggem tu hetu vaikalyāt na utpadyante eva 
PVV_1.211–1.222,6–1.211–1.222,7	 kathañca nairātmya darśinaḥ mala utpattiḥ āśaṃkyate na tāvat hetu sākalyāt satva dṛṣṭeḥ hetu bhūtāyāḥ abhāvāt nairātmya darśana vat sattva darśanañca bhāvanayā utpannam hetuḥ iti ced kutas tasya bhāvanā kinnairātmyasya sa upadrava tvāt kiñcābhūta tvena bhrama hetu tvāt asvabhāvena upahantum śakya tvāt vā etat trayam asaṅgatam iti āha 
PVV_1.211–1.222,8–1.211–1.222,10	 nirupadrava bhūta artha svabhāvasya viparyayaiḥ na bādhā yatnava tve api buddheḥ tad pakṣa pātataḥ doṣa rāśeḥ udvejakasya prahāṇena nirupadravasya pramāṇa samvādi tvena bhūta arthasya satya arthasya anāropita tvena svabhāvasya prakṛteḥ nairātmyasya abhirucita viṣayasya viparyayeṣu ātma ādi a ākāreṣu abhyāse sa upadrava tva ādinā prayatnaḥ eva tāvat na sambhavati prekṣasya sambhavepi vā viparyayaiḥ 
PVV_1.211–1.222,11–1.211–1.222,15	 na bādhā nairātmyasya sā ātmībhūtasya svabhāvasya asti buddheḥ tatra doṣa prati na hi svabhāvaḥ sākṣātkṛtaḥ anyathā kartu śakyaḥ anena praṇītaḥ iti nirodha ākāraḥ darśitaḥ nanu yadi nairātmya sa ātma tva darśanayoḥ paraspara bhedāt bādhā tadā rāga pratighayoḥ api syāt iti āha ātma graha eka yoni tvāt kārya kāraṇa bhāvataḥ rāga pratidhayoḥ bādhāḥ bhede api na parasparam 
PVV_1.211–1.222,16	 ātma grahaḥ ekaḥ yoniṣkāraṇam yayoḥ tau tayoḥ bhāvaḥ tasmāt eka kāraṇa tvāt rāga pratidhayoḥ bhet api na parasparam bādhā rūpa rasayoḥ iva tathā kārya kāraṇa bhāvatopi na anyonyam bādhā tathā hi yadā ekasmin rāgaḥ tadā tad apakāriṇi dveṣaḥ yadā ca kvacid dveṣaḥ tadā tad apakāriṇi rāga upīti paraspara kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt na asti virodhaḥ cakṣuḥ ādi buddhīnām iva 
PVV_1.211–1.222,17–1.211–1.222,20	 nanu dveṣa ādi pratipakṣāḥ maitrī ādayaḥ na ca tān ucchindanti iti āha moha avirodhāt maitrī a ādeḥ nna atyantam doṣa nigrahaḥ tad mūlāḥ ca malāḥ sarve moha avirodhāt maitrī a ādeḥ maitrī karuṇa ādayaḥ moha avirodhinaḥ atas ca doṣa kāraṇā vaikalyāt na atyantam dveṣa ādi doṣāṇām nigrahaḥ maitrī ādeḥ āpāta viṣkambhana m ātrantu bhavati mohasya anapāyāt tad mūlāḥ ca malāḥ sarvve prasūyante 
PVV_1.211–1.222,21–1.211–1.222,26	 nanu sattva darśanam doṣa mūlam na mohaḥ iti āha sa ca sat kāya darśanam sa ca mohaḥ sat kāya darśanam nanu mohaḥ asaṃprakhyāna rūpaḥ sattva dṛṣṭiḥ tu viparīta artha pratipatti rūpā tat katham mohaḥ eva sattva darśanam iti āha vidyāyāḥ pratipakṣa tvāt caittattvena upalabdhitaḥ mithyā upalabdhiḥ ajñānam yukteḥ ca anyat yuktimat 
PVV_1.211–1.222,27	 vidyāyāḥ pratipakṣa tvāt vidyāyāḥ nairātmya dṛṣṭeḥ vvipakṣaḥ avidyā sa ca aprakhyāna mātram vā rūpa ādi vā na bhavati nirvvāṇepi tayoḥ bhāvāt kintu mithyā upalabdhiḥ ajñānam avidyā adharma anṛta vat vidyāyāḥ sat artha tvāt caittatvena upalabdhitaḥ ca caittatvena karaṇena upalabdhi rūpa tvāt ca āśraya ālambana ākāra kāla dravya samatā ādibhiḥ samam prayuktāḥ saṃprayuktāḥ iti saṃprayukta lakṣaṇam na ca asaṃprakhyānasya nīrūpasya ālambana ākāra yogaḥ iti mithyājñānam avidyā ukte arthe virodhāt bha gavatā pyuktam yāḥ kāścana loka vyavahāra upapattayaḥ sarvu āstāḥ ātma abhiniveśataḥ iti anena sattva dṛṣṭiḥ eva janma hetuḥ uktāḥ ātma abhiniveśa lakṣaṇa tvāt tasyāḥ atas anyat asaṃprakhyāna lakṣaṇam ajñānam ayuktam nirvvāṇepi tat sattvāt 
PVV_1.211–1.222,28–1.211–1.222,30	 nanu yadi avidyā dṛṣṭiḥ eva tathā ca dṛṣṭi saṃprayuktā avidyā iti saṃprayukta arthaḥ na syāt na sā tena eva samprayuktā kintu sakala kleśa anugatā avidyā sat kāya dṛṣṭiḥ tu tat eka deśaḥ tatas cagama avirodhaḥ iti āha vyākhyeyaḥ atra virodhaḥ yaḥ atra vidyā nirdeśe āgama virodha yaḥ prasajati sa sāmānya viśeṣa bhāvena bheda kalpanayā vyākhyeyaḥ samarthanīyaḥ yathā palāśa yuktam vanam iti dṛṣṭi svabhāvā avidyā prādhānyena kleśa hetuḥ iti upadarśanañca prayojanam 
PVV_1.211–1.222,31–1.211–1.222,34	 prakṛtam āha yatas ca evam ātma darśana prabhūtāḥ sarvu akleśāḥ tad virodhāt ca tad mayaiḥ virodhaḥ śūnyatā dṛṣṭeḥ sarva doṣaiḥ prasidhyati tayā sattva dṛṣṭyā virodhāt ca śūnyatā dṛṣṭeḥ nairātmya dṛṣṭeḥ tad mayaiḥ sattva dṛṣṭi hetukaiḥ sarvva doṣaiḥ vvirodhaḥ sidhyati śīta viruddhasya agneḥ iva tad kārye roma harṣa ādibhiḥ atas sa ātmībhūta nairātmyānām na punar doṣa leśa utpattiḥ anena niḥśaraṇate iti nirodha ākāraḥ nirddiṣṭaḥ doṣebhyaḥ sarvu athā niḥśaraṇāt 
PVV_1.211–1.222,35–1.211–1.222,37	 na akṣayaḥ prāṇi dharma tvāt rūpa ādi vat asiddhitaḥ sambandhe pratipakṣasya tyāgasya adarśanāt api syāt etat akṣayaḥ rāga ādiḥ prāṇi dharma tvāt rūpa ādi vat na yuktam etat asiddhitaḥ na hi prāṇī kaścid asti yat dharmāḥ rāga ādayaḥ siddhyanti sattve dṛṣṭau tu satyām kevalam upalabhyante iti pratītyasamutpāda mātram etat teṣām pratipakṣasya nairātmya darśanasya sambandhe saṃmukhībhāve tyāgasya āpāta viṣkambhaṇasya adarśanāt api sambhavat pratipakṣa tvena uccheda sambhavāt na akṣayitvam 
PVV_1.211–1.222,38–1.211–1.222,41	 syāt etat tāmra ādīnām agni yogāt drava avasthāyām naṣṭam api kāṭhinyam punar śīta samparkāt utpadyate tadvat naṣṭānām api doṣāṇām mārga sātmye punar kutaścid hetoḥ utpattiḥ syāt atra āha na kāṭhinya vat utpattiḥ punar doṣa virodhinaḥ sa ātma tvena anapāya tvāt anekāntāt ca bhasma vat na kāṭhinya vat utpattiḥ punar doṣāṇām doṣa virodhinaḥ nairātmyasya sa ātma tvena prakṛti tvena anapāyāt na hi avyāhate virodhini tad viruddhasya utpatti ragnau= iva śīta kāṭhinyam kādācid ka tvāt agni nivṛttau tad virodhinyāḥ drava tāyāḥ svarasa nirodhāt utpadyate anaikāntāt ca bhasma vat yathā bhasmani bhūte punar na kāṣṭhotpattiḥ tathā nairātmya sa ātma tāyām na punar naṣṭānām doṣāṇām utpattiḥ iti anaikāntika tā naṣṭa utpatteḥ 
PVV_1.211–1.222,42–1.211–1.222,46	 nanu ātma bhāvanayā api mokṣa usti tat kim nairātmya bhāvanayā yat āhuḥ ātmā mantavyaḥ ityādi atra āha yaḥ paśyati ātmānam tatra asya aham iti śāśvataḥ snehaḥ snehāt sukheṣu tṛṣyati tṛṣṇāḥ doṣān= tiraskurute yaḥ paśyati ātmānam tatra ātmani asya draṣṭuḥ aham iti śāśvataḥ anupāyi snehaḥ bhavati snehāt ātma snehāt sukheṣu tṛṣyati tṛṣṇāvān bhavati iti tṛṣṇā ca sukha sādhana tvena adhyavasitānām vastūnām doṣān aśuci tva ādīn tiraskurute pracchādayati doṣa tiraskaraṇāt 
PVV_1.211–1.222,47–1.211–1.222,50	 guṇa darśī paritṛṣyan mama iti tad sādhanāni upādatte tena ātma abhiniveśaḥ yāvat tāvat sa saṃsāre guṇa darśī śuci tveṣṭa tva guṇān paśyan paritṛṣyan mama iti mama idam sukham iti garddhamānaḥ tasya sukhasya sādhanāni garbha gamana ādīni upādatte tena ātma darśana mūla tvena janma ādeḥ ātma abhiniveśaḥ yāvat tāvat saḥ ātma darśī saṃsāraḥ eva 
PVV_1.211–1.222,51–1.211–1.222,57	 na kevalam janma prabandhaḥ tasya doṣāḥ api samastāḥ santi iti āha atmani sati para saṃjñā sva para vibhāgāt parigraha dveṣau anayoḥ saṃpratibaddhāḥ sarve doṣāḥ prajāyante ātmani sati tatas anyasmin para saṃjñā para buddhiḥ bhavati sva para vibhāgāt ca kāraṇāt sva parayoḥ yathākramam parigrahaḥ abhiṣvaṅgaḥ dveṣaḥ parityāgaḥ tau bhavataḥ anayoḥ anunaya pratiṣedhayoḥ saṃpratibaddhāḥ sarvve doṣāḥ rāga mātsarya īrṣyā ādayaḥ prajāyante yadi api ātmani snehavān tathā api atmīye sukha sādhane vairāgyāt na saṃsarati iti na etat yuktam yatas niyamena ātmani snihyan= tadīye na virajyate ātmani snihyan prīyamāṇaḥ tadīyaḥ ātmīye sukha sādhane niyamena na viraabhiṣvajati eva tat katham ātmīya virāgāt muktiḥ ātma snehasya ātmīya vairāgya virodhi tvāt 
PVV_1.223,0–1.224–1.226,5	 tam eva tyajati iti ced āha ne ca asti ātmani nirdoṣe sneha apagama kāraṇam snehaḥ sa doṣaḥ iti ced tatas kim tasya varjanam yadi api ātmā nirdoṣaḥ tathā api snehaḥ sa doṣaḥ iti ced tatas sa doṣa tvāt kim tasya snehasya varjanam aduṣite asya viṣaye na śakyam tasya varjanam adūṣitesya viṣayaḥ ātmani na śakyam tasya varjanam na hi snehaḥ sva guṇa doṣābhyām upādīyate tyajyate vā kintu viṣayasya viṣayaḥ ca nirdoṣaḥ iti katham asya varjanam kiñca prahāṇiḥ icchā dveṣa ādeḥ guṇa doṣa anubandhinaḥ tayoḥ adṛṣṭiḥ viṣaye icchā dveṣa ādeḥ guṇa doṣa anubandhinaḥ yathākramam viṣayasya guṇa doṣa anuvartinaḥ prahāṇiḥ prahāṇi upāyaḥ tayoḥ guṇa doṣayoḥ adṛṣṭiḥ viṣaye ananya upāya tā darśana artham upacāraḥ viṣaya guṇa doṣa adarśane eva icchā dveṣa ādi prahāṇi upāyaḥ iti arthaḥ 
PVV_1.224–1.226,6–1.224–1.226,10	 nanu adṛṣṭopi iti ādiḥ anicchā mātrāt tyajyamānaḥ dṛśyate iti āha na tu bāhyeṣu yaḥ kramaḥ na tu bāhyeṣu vastuṣu yaḥ kramaḥ anicchā mātra kṛta tyāga rūpaḥ saḥ āntareṣu api sneha ādiṣu yuktaḥ bāhya adhīnam bāhyam anicchayā tyaktum śakyam ātma darśana adhīnantu na śakya parihāram avikala hetutvena utpatteḥ kiñca na hi sneha guṇāt snehaḥ kintu artha guṇa darśanāt 
PVV_1.224–1.226,11–1.224–1.226,14	 kāraṇe avikale tasmin kāryam kena nivāryate na hi sneha guṇāt snehaḥ kriyate kintu arthasya viṣayasya guṇa doṣa darśanāt jāyate kāraṇe avikale tasmin viṣaya guṇe kāryam snehaḥ kena nivāryate na kenacid kā vā sa doṣa tā dṛṣṭā snehe duḥkha samāśrayaḥ kā vā sa doṣa tā dṛṣṭā snehe yena ayam varjayitavyaḥ duḥkhasya samāśrayaḥ ced doṣaḥ tathā hi ātmani snihyan tad sukha sādhaneṣu tṛṣṇāvān duḥkha bhūtam saṃsāram upādatte 
PVV_1.227,0–1.227,4	 tathā api na virāgaḥ atra sva tva dṛṣṭeḥ yatha ātmani tathā api duḥkha hetu tvepi na virogaḥ atra snehe yathā ātmani sva tva dṛṣṭeḥ duḥkha nidāna bhūtāyāḥ hetau= ātmani na virāgaḥ yadi duḥkha hetau virāgaḥ tathā sva tve dṛṣṭi dvāreṇa sarvvam duḥkham iti tasya hetau= ātmani eva sa yuktaḥ na ca asti etat na taiḥ vinā duḥkha hetuḥ ātmā ced te api tādṛśāḥ na taiḥ sneha buddhīndriya ādibhiḥ ātmīyaiḥ vvinā duḥkha hetuḥ ātmā ced tepi sneha ādayaḥ tādṛśāḥ ātmānam antareṇa na duḥkha hetavaḥ 
PVV_1.228,0–1.228,1	 nirdoṣam dvayam api evam vairāgyāt na dvayoḥ tatas duḥkha bhāvanayā syāt ced ahidaṣṭa aṅga hāni vat evam paraspara sāpekṣa tve nirdoṣam sneha ādiḥ ātmā ca vairāgyan na dvayoḥ api tatas kāryam tathā ca saṃsāraḥ doṣāḥ ca durvvārāḥ hetu sākalyāt pravṛttiḥ yadi sneha ādiṣu duḥkha bhāvanayā hāniḥ syāt ahidaṣṭasya aṅgasya hāni vat yathā ātmīyam api ahidaṣṭam aṅgam duḥkha vaśāt virajya tyajyate anupabhoga āśraya tvāt 
PVV_1.229–1.231,0–1.229–1.231,2	 ātmīya buddhi hānyā atra tyāgaḥ na tu viyaryaye upabhoga āśraya tvena gṛhīteṣu indriya ādiṣu sva tvadhīḥ kena vāryeta vairāgyam tatra tat kutas ātmīya buddhi hānyā tatra ahi daṣṭa aṅge tyāgaḥ na tu viparyaye ātmīya buddhi sattāyām yasmāt upabhogasya āśraya tvena kāraṇa tvena gṛhīteṣu indriya ādiṣu sva tve dhīra ātmīya tva buddhiḥ kena hetunā vāryeta na kenacid tad kutas tatra upabhoga sādhane svīya avayave vairāgyam yena tyajyate tatas yat tyajyate ātmīya buddhi hānyāḥ eva na ca evam sneha ādiṣu ātmīya buddhi hāniḥ asti yena eṣām tyāgaḥ syāt 
PVV_1.229–1.231,3–1.229–1.231,8	 pratyakṣam eva sarvasya keśa ādiṣu kalevarāt cyuteṣu sadhṛṇā buddhiḥ jāyate anyeṣu sa spṛhā etat ca pratyakṣam eva sarvu asya keśa ādiṣu kalevarāt cyuteṣu ātmīya buddhi viṣayeṣu sadhṛṇā buddhiḥ jāyate janasya anyatra acyuteṣu ātmīya buddhi viṣayeṣu sa spṛhā duḥkha bhāvanayā ātmīya buddhiḥ eva hīyate iti ced na yuktam idam samavāya ādi sambandha janitā tatra hi svadhīḥ samavāya ādi sambandha janitāḥ hi yasmāt tatra buddhi ādau svadhīḥ tathā ca ātmanaḥ sukha ādīnā samavāyaḥ sambandhaḥ śarīreṇa saṃyogaḥ śarīra āśritaiḥ rūpa ādibhiḥ saṃyukta samavāyaḥ śrotra indriyeṇa saṃyogaḥ cakṣuḥ ādibhiḥ saṃyogi saṃyogaḥ ātma sambandhaḥ

PVV_1.256,0–1.256,4	 anityāt prāha tena eva duḥkham duḥkhāt nirātma tām tena eva anitya duḥkha bhāvanāyāḥ śūnyatā bhāvanā anukūla tvena bhagavān anityāt anitya tvāt duḥkham saṃsāri skandhānām hānāt duḥkhāt duḥkha tvāt nirātmatām āha tat yathā rūpam bhikṣavaḥ nityam anityam vā anityam bhadanta yat anityam tat duḥkham sukham vā iti evam hetu phala bhāvanena ātma darśanam eva mukteḥ upāyaḥ iti kathitam tat eva ācāryeṇa uktam uktaḥ mārgaḥ tad abhyāsāt āśrayaḥ parivartate iti na asti virodhaḥ yaḥ punar ātma darśī saḥ aviraktaḥ eva aviraktaḥ ca tṛṣṇāvān sarva ārambha samāśritaḥ aviraktaḥ ca tṛṣṇāvān hāni upādāna lakṣaṇān karma prasava hetūn samāḥ 
PVV_1.257,0–1.257,1	 saḥ amuktaḥ kleśa karmabhyām saṃsārī nāma tādṛśaḥ ātmīyam eva yaḥ na icchet bhoktā api asya na vidyate saḥ amuktaḥ kleśa karmabhyām ātma darśana pravṛtti kāraṇakābhyām saṃsārī nāma prasiddhaḥ tat evam ātmani sati na ātmīya tyāgaḥ tathā amuktiḥ iti uktam bhavatu vā atmīya tyāgaḥ tathā āpi ātmīyam eva yaḥ na icchet tat mate asi a ātmīyasya bhoktā na vidyate bhogya apekṣa tvāt bhoktṛ tvasya 
PVV_1.258–1.163,0–1.258–1.163,2	 ātmā api na tadā tasya kriyā bhogau hi lakṣaṇam tasmāt anādi santāna tulya jātīya bījikām utkhāta mūlām kuruta satva dṛṣṭim mumukṣavaḥ bhoktṛ a bhāve ātmā api na asti iti prasaṅgāt kutas iti ced hiḥ yasmāt asya ātmanaḥ kriyā bhogau lakṣaṇam karttā bhoktā ca ātmā ucyate yadā ca ātmīyam eva na asti kimartham karma kartavyam kim vā bhoktavyam kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tva abhāvāt ātma abhāvaḥ eva svīkṛtaḥ syāt tasmāt satya ātmani ātmīyam tad sneha ādi sattve anucchedaḥ evam saṃsārasya tasmāt saṃsārāt udvijamānā mumukṣavaḥ utkhāta mūlām uddhṛta kāraṇām sattva dṛṣṭim kuruta 
PVV_1.258–1.163,3–1.258–1.163,5	 nanu kim asyāḥ mūlam iti āha anādi santānaḥ tulya jātīyaḥ pūrvva pūrvva sattva darśana svabhāvaḥ avidyā rūpaḥ bījam kāraṇam yasya āḥ tām sattva darśanam avidyā svabhāvam pūrvva pūrvvam uttarottarasya sattva darśanasya hetuḥ iti arthaḥ nanu uktam īśvareṇa āgame asti ātmā mokṣaḥ ca asya dīkṣā vidhinā iti tat kim atra cintyate tad kāraṇā vā dhī vidhiḥ tam bādhate katham ityādinā ukta tvāt atra āha 
PVV_1.258–1.163,6–1.258–1.163,10	 āgamasya tathā abhāva nibandhanam apaśyatām muktim āgama mātreṇa vadan na paritoṣa kṛt āgamasya tathā abhāvasya pratipādita artha samvādi tvasya nibandhanam hetum apaśyatām mumukṣūṇām āgama mātreṇa muktim vadan na paritoṣa kṛt bhavati dīkṣā akiñcitkarī nanu asti prāmāṇya nibandhanam āgamasya dīkṣā vidhi spṛṣṭasya anāroha dharmaka tva darśanam yathā hi bījam dīkṣā vidhi spṛṣṭam na prarohati tathā pumān api dīkṣitaḥ na punar bhavati iti āha 
PVV_1.258–1.163,11–1.258–1.163,16	 na alam bīja ādi saṃsiddhaḥ vidhiḥ puṃsām ajat mane taila abhyaṅga agni ha ādeḥ api mukti prasaṅgataḥ na alam śaktaḥ bīja ādiṣu saṃsiddhaḥ vidhiḥ dīkṣāyāḥ puṃsām ajat mane taila abhyaṅga agni dāha deḥ api saṃsārat mukti prasaṅgataḥ tailena abhyaktam bījam agninā ca spṛṣṭam na prarohati tathā puruṣopi taila abhyaṅga agni dāhābhyām na punar bhavet syāt etat dīkṣāyāḥ prāk pāpa guroḥ uttaram tulayā lāghavāt pāpa abhāva upalambhaḥ āgama prāmāṇya nibandhanam iti āha prāk guroḥ lāghavāt paścāt na pāpa haraṇam kṛtam mā bhūt gauravam eva asya na pāpam guru amūrttitaḥ 
PVV_1.258–1.163,17	 prāk guroḥ lāghavāt paścāt na pāpa haraṇam kṛtam dīkṣāyāḥ prāk guroḥ paścāt lāgha dīkṣayā na pāpa haraṇasya dīkṣitasya kintu gauravam eva asya kṛtam sat mā bhūt iti kasmāt na kalpyate lāghavam hi gaurava virodhi dṛśyamānam tad abhāvam eva gamayet na pāpa bhāvam pāpam eva guru iti ced na pāpam guru amūrttitaḥ mūrtta tva abhāvāt bhūrtta dharmaḥ hi gauravam katham pāpasya amūrttasya syāt 
PVV_1.258–1.163,18–1.258–1.163,25	 nanu tvad pakṣe api nairātmya darśane bhūtepi kasmāt na janma iti āha mithyājñāna tad udbhūta tarṣa sañcetana avaśāt hīna sthāna gatiḥ janma tatas tacchinna jāyate mithyājñānam duḥkhe viparyāsa matiḥ tad udbhūtaḥ tarṣaḥ mithyājñāna prabhavā tṛṣṇā tābhyām saṃprayukte cetane tad vaśa ādyāḥ hīna sthāna gatiḥ tad janma iti uktam atas tat chit ajñāna tṛṣṇā ācchedakaḥ nairātmya darśī na jātaye kāraṇa abhāvāt tat eva āha tayoḥ eva hi sāmarthyam jātau tanmātra bhāvataḥ tayā ujñāna tṛṣṇayoḥ hi sāmarthyam jātau janma nimittam tanmātreṇa bhāvataḥ te ca dīkṣitasya api staḥ iti sa jāyate 
PVV_1.264–1.270,0–1.264–1.270,3	 nanu karma api janma kāraṇam iṣṭam tat katham ajñāna tṛṣṇe eva ukte iti āha te cetane svayam karma iti akhaṇḍam janma kāraṇam gati pratītyoḥkaraṇāni āśrayaḥ tāni adṛṣṭataḥ adṛṣṭa nāśā āda gatiḥ tad saṃskāraḥ na cetanā te cetane mithyājñāna tad udbhūta ṛṣa saṃcetane svayam ātmanā pūrvvaśubha aśubha karma saṃskāra sahāye karma karma svabhāve iti akhaṇḍam anyūnam janma kāraṇam uktam iti na virodhaḥ syāt etat gati pratītyoḥ abhimata deśa gamanasya jñānasya ca karaṇāni indriyāṇi āśrayaḥ kāraṇam indriyebhyaḥ utpannena jñānena viṣayam paricchidya pravṛtteḥ tāni indriyāṇi ca adṛṣṭataḥ śubha ādi lakṣaṇāt dīkṣayā ca adṛṣṭa nāśāt tad kāryāṇām kāraṇānām anutpatteḥ vviṣayasya pariccheda tṛṣṇayoḥ abhāvāt agatiḥ janma sthānaḥ iti na asti punarbhavaḥ dīkṣitasya tad adṛṣṭañca ātma saṃskāraḥ na cetanā syāt dīkṣitasya api sā asti iti janma api syāta 
PVV_1.264–1.270,4–1.264–1.270,7	 atra āha sāmarthyam karaṇa utpatteḥ bhāva abhāva anuvṛttitaḥ dṛṣṭam buddheḥ na ca anyasyāḥ santi tāni nayanti kim buddheḥ bhāva abhāva anuvṛttitaḥ anvaya vyatireka anuvṛttyā karaṇānām ekasmāt deśāt apara deśa sambaddhānām utpatteḥ kāraṇāt sāmārthyam buddheḥ indriya jananam pratidṛṣṭam na anyasya saṃskāra rūpasya adṛṣṭasya tad anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāna anupalambhāt sā buddhiḥ ca asti deśa antara sambaddha karaṇa janikā dīkṣitasyā tad kintāni karaṇāni garbha sthānan na yanti gacchanti hetu avaikalyāt bhavitavyam 
PVV_1.264–1.270,8–1.264–1.270,11	 gamanena avaśyam dīkṣayā upahatāḥ buddhiḥ deśa antaram netum indriyāṇi aśaktā ced dhāraṇa preraṇa kṣobha nirodhāḥ cetanā vaśāḥ na syuḥ teṣām asāmarthye tasya dīkṣā ādi anantaram atha buddheḥ tadā abhāvāt na syuḥ sandhīyate malaiḥ nanu evantasya mumukṣoḥ dīkṣa anantaram buddheḥ asāmarthye teṣām indriyāṇām sva viṣaye vyavasthāpanam dhāraṇam tatra ayojanam preraṇam kṣobhaḥ vikāraḥ sva viṣayān nivartanam nirodhaḥ te buddhi nibandhana vṛttayaḥ na syuḥ atha buddheḥ tadā maraṇa kāle abhāvāt na syuḥ dhāraṇa preraṇa ādayaḥ 
PVV_1.264–1.270,12–1.264–1.270,15	 atra āha sandhīyate janyate malaiḥ mithyā jñānaiḥ mithyājñāna ātma sneha ādibhiḥ buddhiḥ maraṇa samayepī iti kutas buddhi abhāvaḥ buddheḥ teṣām asāmarthye jīvataḥ api syuḥ akṣamāḥ nirhrāsa atiśayāt puṣṭau pratipakṣa sva pakṣayoḥ doṣāḥ sva bīja santānāḥ dīkṣite api anivāritāḥ atha malāḥ api dīkṣayā upahata sāmarthyāḥ na buddhi sandadhati tadā teṣām malānām asāmarthye svīkriyamāṇe jīvatopi dīkṣitasya malāḥ buddhi sandhānam pratyakṣamāḥ syuḥ dīkṣā malānām bādhikā iti api mithyā tathā pratipakṣasya nairātmya bhāvanāyāḥ sva pakṣasya ayoni śoma naskārasya abhyāsāt puṣṭau satyām doṣāṇām yathākramam narhrāsāt apacayāt atiśayāt abhivṛddhe rdoṣāḥ svakīyāt bījāt tulya jātīya kāraṇāt santānaḥ yeṣām te dīkṣitepi doṣa bīje paripoṣavati anivāritāḥ 
PVV_1.264–1.270,16–1.264–1.270,19	 syāt etat ātmanā upi garbha gata karaṇa ādi janane vyāpāraḥ saḥ eva dīkṣayā niruddhaḥ iti na punar janma iti āha nityasya nirapekṣa tvāt krama utpattiḥ virudhyate kriyā āyām akriyā yāñca kriyayoḥ sadṛśa ātmanaḥ aikyañca hetu phalayoḥ vyatirekaḥ tatas tayoḥ nityasya anupakārya tayā nirapekṣa tvāt karaṇa ādīnām krameṇa utpattiḥ vvirudhyate sama tva hetu sadbhāvāt sakṛt utpāda prasakteḥ indriya ādeḥ kriyā āyām akriyā yāñca sadṛśa ātmanaḥ tulya rūpasya ātmanaḥ tayoḥ kālayoḥ te te virudhyete 
PVV_1.264–1.270,20	 yadi asau kārya karaṇa svabhāvaḥ tadā kāryāt eva kriyā virāmosya virudhyate evam akriyāyām api vācyam kiñca ātmanaḥ karma kartṛ tā hetu tvam bhoktṛ tvañca phalam te ca ātmanaḥ eka rūpasya rūpe iti hetu phalā bheda prasaṅgaḥ vyatirekaḥ bhedaḥ tatas ātmanaḥ tayoḥ kartṛ tu abhoktṛ tvayoḥ dharmayoḥ tatas na aikya prasaṅgaḥ iti ced 
PVV_1.271–1.276,0–1.271–1.276,4	 kartṛ bhoktṛ tva hāniḥ syāt sāmarthyañca na sidhyati evam kartṛ tu abhoktṛ tvā hāniḥ syāt ātmanaḥ atad svabhāva tvāt tad sambandhāt kartā bhoktā ca anupakṛtasya sambandhi tve ati prasaṅgāt upakṛta tvam veditavyam tat ca aśakya sādhanam yasmāt nityasya avyatireki tvāt sāmarthyañca na sidhyati nanu yadi ātmā na asti tadā anyena anubhūtam karma ca kṛtam anyaḥ smarati bhuḍatkte phalam iti syāt tathā ca atiprasaṅgaḥ iti āha anya smaraṇa bhoga ādi prasaṅgaḥ ca na bādhakāḥ asmṛteḥ kasya cit tena hi anubhūteḥ smṛta udbhavaḥ 
PVV_1.271–1.276,5	 anyasya smaraṇa bhoga ādi prasaṅgāḥ ca na bādhakāḥ bhavanti asmṛteḥ kasyacid smarttuḥ abhāvāt evam bhoga upi na asti bhoktra bhāvāt tena hi tasmāt smartra bhāvāt kāraṇāt viṣayāṇām anubhūteḥ sakāśāt smṛtiḥ eva smṛtam tasya udbhavaḥ vastu dharmaḥ hi eṣa yat anubhavaḥ paṭīyān smaraṇa bīja ādhāna dvāreṇa smaraṇam janayati śubha aśubha cetanāḥ ca saṃskārāḥ bhoga ākāram samvidam pravartayanti tat kim smartṛ bhoktṛ durgraheṇa tad tad ākāraḥ pratītyasamutpannaḥ buddhi prabandhaḥ eva kevalaḥ na tu saṃsārī nāma kaścid 
PVV_1.271–1.276,6–1.271–1.276,9	 yadi na asti ātmā katham sa kopa dṛṣṭiḥ saṃsāra pravṛttiḥ vvā iti āha sthiram sukham mama ahañcā ityādi satya catuṣṭaye abhūtān ṣoḍaśa ākārān āropya paritṛṣyati sthira makṣaṇikam sukham tri duḥkha tā viparītam mama iti ātmīyam aham iti ātma ahaṃkāraḥ ca iti duḥkha satyasya viparītāḥ ākārāḥ iti ādyān prati satyam caturaḥ kṛtvā ṣoḍaśa ākārān bhūtān prāk yathā ukta bhūta ākāra viparītān satya catuṣṭaye aropayati iti bhrāntiḥ eva sat kāya dṛṣṭiḥ sva bīja prabhavā āropya ca kiñcid sva sūkha sādhanañca manyamānaḥ tad artham paritṛṣyati tṛṣṇayā ca janma sthāna upāṃdānam iti saṃsāra pravṛttiḥ 
PVV_1.271–1.276,10–1.271–1.276,13	 mārga viparyayam saṃsāra hetum uktvā mārgam āha tatra eva tad viruddha artha tattva ākāra anurodhinī hanti sa anucarām tṛṣṇām samyak dṛṣṭiḥ su bhāvitāḥ tatra satya catuṣṭayaḥ eva myak dṛṣṭiḥ na īrātmya dṛṣṭiḥ tad viruddha artha tattva ākāra anu teṣām sthira sukha ādi ākārāṇām avidyā āropitānām viruddhaḥ arthaḥ tasya tattvāni bhūtāḥ ākārā anityā sukha ādayaḥ ṣoḍaśa ākārāḥ tān anuroddhum śīlam yasyāḥ sā tathā su bhāvitā sa ādara nirantara dīrgha kāla abhyāsa prāpta vaiśadyā hanti tṛṣṇām janma hetum sa anucarām mātsarya ādi parivārām 
PVV_1.271–1.276,14–1.271–1.276,17	 nanu tṛṣṇā kṣayepi karma dehayoḥ janma hetvoḥ bhāvāt janma kim na bhavati iti āha trihetoḥ na udbhavaḥ karma dehayoḥ sthitayoḥ api eka abhāvāt vinā bījam na aṅkurasya iva sambhavaḥ trihetoḥ tṛṣṇā karma deha hetoḥ janmanaḥ tṛṣṇāyāḥ kṣaye karma dehayoḥ sthitayoḥ api utpattiḥ na bhavati eka abhāvāt hetu sāmagrya vaikalyāt vinābījam kṣiti udaka ādi bhāvepi na aṅkurasya udbhavaḥ 
PVV_1.271–1.276,18–1.271–1.276,21	 nanu tri hetoḥ janmanaḥ eka abhāvepi ced anutpattiḥ tat kim karmmaṇaḥ dehasya vā kṣayaḥ na abhyasyate pare ca āhuḥ karma kṣayāt muktiḥ iti atra āha asambhavāt vipakṣasya na hāniḥ karma dehayoḥ aśakya tvāt ca tṛṣṇāyām sthitāyām punar udbhavāt asambhavāt vipakṣasya na hāniḥ karma dehayoḥ asti aśakya tvāt ca sati api vā vipakṣe tad abhyāsāt deha karma nivṛttiḥ aśakya kriyā tṛṣṇāyām sthitāyām tad pracitasya ātma grahavataḥ garbha sthāna parigrahe sati punar udbhavāt dehasya śarīriṇaḥ ca tṛṣṇayā eva pravṛttyā sarvu atra śubha aśubha pravṛtteḥ ca 
PVV_1.271–1.276,22–1.271–1.276,25	 evantarhi tṛṣṇā karma ca kṣapayitavyam mumukṣuṇā iti āha dvaya kṣaya artham yatne ca vyarthaḥ karma kṣartha śramaḥ dvaya kṣaya artham yatne kriyamāṇe karma kṣaye vyarthaḥ śramaḥ tṛṣṇā kṣaya mātrāt janma abhāva siddheḥ sat api karma anupayuktam iti alam tad kṣaya prayāsena na ca karma kṣayaḥ pratipakṣa abhāvāt śakyaḥ iti uktam santāpa kleśa upabhogāt pūrvva arjita karma kṣayaḥ aparasya ca akāraṇam tatas muktiḥ iti api mohaḥ 
PVV_1.277,0–1.277,2	 tathā hi phala vaicitrya dṛṣṭeḥ ca śakti bhedaḥ anumīyate karmaṇām tāpa saṃkleśāt na eka rūpāt tatas kṣayaḥ karmaṇām phala vaicitryasya nānā gati upabhogyāne kavidhā upakaraṇa sādhya vividha sukha duḥkha upabhoga prakārasya dṛṣṭeḥ ca śakti bhedaḥ sāmarthya nānā tvam anumīyate atas nānā prakāra phala janana sāmarthyāt kāraṇāt eka rūpāt phalāt tāpa saṃkleśāt na karmaṇām kṣayaḥ 
PVV_1.278,0–1.278,2	 sarvu eṣām karmaṇām tāpaḥ eva phalam iti ced phalam kathañcid tat janyam alpam syāt na vijātimat athā api tapasaḥ śaktyā śakti saṅkara saṃkṣayaiḥ tasya karmaṇaḥ janyam phalam kathañcid jugupsā ādibhiḥ alpam syāt na tu vijāti dānam dattvā hiṃsitvā vā jugupsuḥ tayoḥ phalam alpīyaḥ anubhavati kāraṇa tā na vāpādānāt na tu śubhasya duḥkham aśubhasya vā sukham phalam bhavitum arhati atha api tapasaḥ tāpa kleśa mātra phalena tāni hīyante tapaḥ śaktyā karmaṇām saṃkṣayeṇa vā janma abhāvaḥ 
PVV_1.279–1.281,0–1.279–1.281,2	 kleśāt kutaścid dhīyeta aśeṣam akleśa leśataḥ yat ca kiñcid avaśiṣṭam tat kleśāt kutaścid keśa ulluñcana ādeḥ kṣīyate karma kṣayāt ca muktiḥ atra āha hīyeta aśeṣam akleśa leśataḥ yadi tapasā karma kṣayaḥ aśeṣam karma hīyeta akleśataḥ vinā eva keśa ulluñcana ādi duḥkhāt karmaṇaḥ kṣīṇa tvāt yathā nāraka ādi duḥkham na bhavati tathā alpīyopi na syāt śakti sāṃkarya ipi leśataḥ santāpa kleśāt kevalāt karma hīyeta na duḥkha antara anubandhī saṃsāra prabandhaḥ tapasvinaḥ syāt 
PVV_1.279–1.281,3–1.279–1.281,5	 yadi iṣṭam aparam kleśāt tat tapaḥ kleśaḥ eva ced tat karma phalam iti asmāt na śakteḥ saṅkara ādikam tapasaḥ śaktyā śakti saṅkara saṃkṣayaḥ ca tadā vaktum śakyaḥ yadi syāt iṣṭam manyat tapaḥ na anyathā kleśaḥ eva ced tat tapaḥ tad kleśa rūpam tapaḥ karma phalam tapaḥ avaśeṣitasya karmaṇaḥ phalam iṣṭam iti asmāt karma phala bhūtāt tapasaḥ yuktam ādi śabdāt saṃkṣayaḥ ca 
PVV_1.279–1.281,6–1.279–1.281,9	 tasya mate tu utpitsu doṣa nirghātāt ye api doṣa virodhinaḥ tad je karmāṇi śaktāḥ syuḥ kṛta hāniḥ katham bhavet utpitsoḥ tṛṣṇā ādeḥ doṣasya nirghātāt yepi doṣa virodhinaḥ nairātmya abhyāsa ādayaḥ upāyāḥ tad je tṛṣṇā ādi doṣa prabhave karmaṇi kāraṇa vāraṇa dvāreṇa vyāhantum śaktāḥ na prāc janite tasya utpanna tvāt atas kṛtasya karmaṇaḥ hāniḥ 
PVV_1.279–1.281,10–1.279–1.281,12	 nanu yathā doṣebhyaḥ karma tathā karmaṇaḥ doṣāḥ ca bhavanti iti akṣīṇa karmaṇaḥ na syāt muktiḥ iti āha doṣāḥ na karmaṇaḥ duṣṭaḥ karoti na viparyayāt doṣāḥ na karmaṇaḥ bhavanti kintu doṣaiḥ duṣṭaḥ prāṇī karmakaraḥ bhavati na vipa na aduṣṭaḥ karma karoti nairātmya darśinaḥ tṛṣṇā bhāvāt kvacid pravṛtti nivṛtti asambhavāt 
PVV_1.282,0–1.282,2	 nanu karmaṇaḥ śubhāt sukham sukhāt abhilāṣaḥ abhilāṣāt ca rāgaḥ iti karmaṇaḥ doṣa janma iti āha mithyā vikalpena vinā na abhilāṣaḥ sukhāt api yaḥ ca sukhāt api abhilāṣaḥ rāga hetuḥ dṛśyate sa ca mithyā vikalpena vinā sthira sukha madīya ahaṃkāra vikalpanam antareṇa na bhavati iti āyoni śoma naskāraḥ eva doṣa hetuḥ na karma tatas sati api karmaṇi unmūlita ātma dṛṣṭayaḥ nirdoṣāḥ nirvvānti nirvvāṇañca duḥkha nirodha lakṣaṇam duḥkham parijñāya tat samudayam mārgabhāvanayā prahāya prāpyate na anyathā iti 
PVV_1.282,3–1.282,6	 catur satya prakāśakaḥ eva mumukṣūṇām upāsyaḥ iti tāyi tvam uktam tat evam anulomataḥ pramāṇa bhūtāye tyādi pañca padāni vyākhyāya pratilomataḥ liṅgalaiṅgika tvam darśayan= āha tāyāt tattva sthira aśeṣa viśeṣa jñāna sādhanam tāyāt catur satya prakāśa lakṣaṇāt liṅgāt tattva sthira aśeṣa viśeṣa jñānasya triguṇasya sugata tvasya sādhanam siddhiḥ tattvasya kṣaṇika nairātmyasya jñānāt praśastam 
PVV_1.283–1.284,0–1.283–1.284,1	 bodha artha tvāt gameḥ apunarāvṛttyā ca sthiram niḥśeṣam viśeṣa jñānam triguṇam sugata tvam bodha artha tvāt gameḥ gata śabdaḥ prakṛtiḥ na hi samvādinaḥ asākṣāt kṛtasya arthasya upadeśaḥ śakya kriyaḥ na ca anumānena jñātasya upadeśaḥ iti yuktam uktam kṣaṇika tva nairātmya ādi viṣayasya anumānasya bhagavat upadeśam antareṇa utpatti bīja abhāvāt agṛhīta upadeśānām abhāvāt na ca nitya parokṣasya arthasya sthairya ādi viparyaya adhyavasāyinaḥ kaścid niścayaḥ asti tasmāt pramāṇa samvādinaḥ parokṣa arthasya upadeśaḥ tad sākṣātkāra pūrvvakaḥ eva iti yuktam tāyi tvāt sugata tva anumānam bhagavataḥ sa ca bhagavān tāyaḥ sugata tvāt triguṇāt guṇa anukrameṇa 
PVV_1.283–1.284,2–1.283–1.284,3	 bāhya śaikṣā śaikṣa adhikaḥ tatas bāhya śaikṣā śaikṣebhyaḥ adhikaḥ ye laukika bhāvanā mārgeṇa vīta rāgāḥ bāhyāḥ atatva darśinaḥ tebhyaḥ tattva darśi tvāt adhikaḥ ye śaikṣāḥ abāhyāḥ parihāṇi dharmāṇaḥ tebhyaḥ apunarāvṛttyā ye ca aśaikṣāḥ śrāvakāḥ aprahīṇa kleśa vāsanā asākṣāt kṛta sarvu ākāra vaḥ tavaḥ tebhyaḥ niḥśeṣa pratītyai tasmāt sugata tvāt śāsanam śāstṛ tvam anumīyate 
PVV_1.283–1.284,4–1.283–1.284,7	 ki punar śāsanam iti āha para artha jñāna ghaṭanam tasmāt tad śāsanam tatas dayā para artha taṃtra tvam tad śāsanam kāraṇe kārya upacārāt para artham yat jñānam sugata tvam tad artham ghaṭanam vyāyāmaḥ buddha tva sādhana mārga abhyāsaḥ iti arthaḥ na hi upāyam antareṇa upeya sambhavaḥ tatas śāsanāt dayā para artha tantra tvam para artha pradhāna tvam jagat hita eṣitvam anumīyate iti arthaḥ 
PVV_1.283–1.284,8–1.283–1.284,10	 nanu na avaśyam kāruṇikasya mokṣa mārga abhyāsaḥ sva artha buddhyā api bāhyānām iva sambhavāt tat katham upāya abhyāsāt dayā anumānam iti āha siddhārthasyā avirāmataḥ siddhārthasya niṣpanna mokṣa lakṣaṇa ātma samvādasya api sugatasya khaḍga ādi vat para artha kriyā ataḥ a virāmataḥ anivṛtteḥ phala avasthāyān dayā sadbhāvāt hetu avasthāyām api tasya astitvam anumānañca 
PVV_1.283–1.284,11–1.283–1.284,16	 jagat hita eṣitvasya sugata tva śāstṛ tvatāyi tva sahitasya prāmāṇya sādhana tvam āha dayayā śreyaḥ ācaṣṭe yatas dayayā jagat hita eṣitvena śreyaḥ ācaṣṭe nirdayaḥ tu visamvādana abhiprāya upi brūyāt sadayopya bhūtam ajñaḥ vakti iti āha jñānāt satyam sa sādhanam jñānāt sugata tvāt bhūtam ācaṣṭe tat ca jñānam sa sādhanam vidyamāna upāya abhyāsam vidyamāna śāstṛ tvam iti arthaḥ 
PVV_1.285–1.287,0–1.285–1.287,1	 tat ca abhiyogavān vaktum yatas tasmāt pramāṇa tā tat ca satya catuṣṭayam vineyānām vaktum abhiyogaḥ sāda rasa tata pravṛttiḥ tadvān tāyī ca iti arthaḥ tasmāt kāruṇika tvāt sugata tvāt śāstṛ tvāt tāyi tvāt ca bhagavataḥ pramāṇa tā yathā upadarśita artha samvādaka tā anyaiḥ ajñāta catur satya artha prakāśaka tā vā anumīyate iti arthaḥ 
PVV_1.285–1.287,2–1.285–1.287,6	 evañca anumāna anumeya vyavahāre sthite prāmāṇyāt tāyi tvam hita eṣi tvāt upāya abhyāsāt ca sugata tvambhavati iti uktam kasmāt punar aneka guṇa sambhāra sambhavepi prāmāṇyena eva bhagavataḥ stutiḥ iti āha upadeśa tathā abhāva stutiḥ tad upadeśataḥ pramāṇa tatva sidhi artham upadeśasya tathā abhāvaḥ samvādaka tvam prāmāṇyam tena stutiḥ ācāryeṇa kṛtā tasya bhagavataḥ upadeśataḥ pramāṇasya tattvam lakṣaṇam tat sidhi artham bha ga vaḥ dde śanāyāḥ pramāṇa viniścayaḥ na utprekṣā mātreṇa iti ākhyātum iti arthaḥ 
PVV_1.285–1.287,7–1.285–1.287,10	 nanu nīla samaṅgī puruṣaḥ nīlam jānāti no tu nīlam iti bruvatā bhagavatā pratyakṣam darśitam anumānam na uktam katham āgamāt pratyetavyam iti āha anumāne api avāraṇāt prayoga darśanāt vā asya anumānepya vāraṇa ādiṣṭiḥ darśitāḥ śūnyāḥ para pravādāḥ ityādinā śābda ādeḥ eva niṣedhāt prayogasya para artha anumāna rūpasya darśanāt vāgame asya anumānasya nirdeśaḥ kṛtaḥ eva bhagavatā 
PVV_1.285–1.287,11–1.285–1.287,17	 tam eva prayogam āha yat kiñcid udaya ātmakam nirodha dharmakam sarvam tat iti ādau= anekadhā yat kiñcid udaya ātmakam tat sarvam nirodha dharmakam iti ādau= āgama vākye anekadhā svabhāva ādi liṅga jam aneka prakāram anumānam duśyate katham punar anena anumānam uktam iti āha anumāna āśrayaḥ liṅgam avinābhāva lakṣaṇam vyāpti pradarśanāt hetoḥ sādhyena uktañca tat sphuṭam 
PVV_1.285–1.287,18–ii.0,0	 anumānasya āśrayaḥ kāraṇam liṅgam vaktavyam anumāna nirdeśa artham anyathā aśakya tvāt kim lakṣaṇam iti āha avinābhāvaḥ sādhya avyabhicāri tvam tad lakṣaṇam yasya tat tathā sa ca avinābhāvaḥ liṅgam lakṣaṇam hetoḥ udaya dharmaka tvasya sādhyena nirodha dharmaka tvena vyāpteḥ pradarśanātyat kiñcit udaya dharmakam tyādinā sphuṭaḥ pravyaktaḥ darśitaḥ iti anumāna prāmāṇya nirdeśa upi bhagavat upajñam eva tat evam bhagavān eva pramāṇa bhūtaḥ tāyī mumukṣubhiḥ upāsyaḥ na itaraḥ iti darśana arthamā cā rye ṇa tasya stutiḥ uktā iti yuktam prathama paricchedena pramāṇa sāmānya lakṣaṇam vyavasthāpya viśeṣa lakṣaṇam ākhyātum dvitīya pariccheda ārambhaḥ 
PVV_2.1–2.2,0–2.1–2.2,2	 vipratipattayaḥ ca atra saṃkhyā lakṣaṇa gocara phala viṣayāḥ santi tatra saṃkhyā vipratipatti nirākaraṇa artham āha mānam dvividham viṣaya dvaividhyāt mānam dvividham yat tad pramāṇam avisamvādi tvāt ajñāta artha prakāśaka tvāt sāmānya lakṣaṇam uktam tat dvividham pratyakṣa anumāna bhedena kasmāt viṣayasya sva lakṣaṇa sāmānya lakṣaṇa rūpa tayā dvaividhyāt śābda ādikam api hi pramāṇam bha vat sa viṣayam vaktavyam viṣayaḥ ca sva sāmānya lakṣaṇāt atiriktaḥ na asti tatas tad viṣaya tve pratyakṣa anumāna tā eva na api sāmānya viśeṣa ātmakaḥ ekosti viṣayaḥ paraspara viruddhayoḥ aikātmya ayogāt 
PVV_2.1–2.2,3–2.1–2.2,4	 nanu katham viṣaya dvaividhya siddhiḥ na pratyakṣān na api anumānataḥ yathākramam sva lakṣaṇa sāmānya lakṣaṇa tvāt anayoḥ dvābhyām dvaya siddhiḥ iti ced nanu pratyakṣasya sāmānya aviṣaya tve sādhya sādhana sambandha āgrahaṇāt anumānam eva na syāt sāmānya viṣaya tve ca pratyakṣa tvāt eva tad siddheḥ vviphalam anumānasya prāmāṇya kalpanam 
PVV_2.1–2.2,5	 atra ucyate pratyakṣam api sva lakṣaṇam viṣayīkuḥ vvat tad sambhavi vijātīya vyāvṛtti upakalpitam sāmānyam pṛṣṭha vikalpena niścinvat tat viṣayam api niścaya viṣayeṇa ca pratyakṣa viṣaya vyavasthā evantarhi sva lakṣaṇa viṣaya tā na syāt iti ced na sajātīya vyāvṛtta tvena api tatas niścayāt dve ca vyāvṛttī sva lakṣaṇe staḥ niścite ca pratyakṣa balāt na ca evam api anumānasya vaiyarthya na hi sāmānyam iti eva pratyakṣa viṣayaḥ parokṣe tasya apravṛtteḥ na ca yat ekadā aparokṣam tat sarvadā tathā sva lakṣaṇam kadācid aparokṣam api anyadā parokṣam evam sāmānyam api tatas aparokṣe sāmānye gṛhītāyām vyāptau parokṣe tasmin= anumāna vṛttiḥ iti na kaścid virodhaḥ tasmāt pratyakṣa tvāt vā viṣaya dvaividhya siddhiḥ pratyakṣa anumānābhyām vā iti ubhayathā api upapannam 
PVV_2.1–2.2,6–2.1–2.2,8	 viṣaya dvaividhyam eva kasmāt iti āha śakti aśaktitaḥ artha kriyāyām śakti aśaktitaḥ artha kriyāyām sva lakṣaṇasya artha kriyā śakta tvāt vijātīya vyāvṛtti upakalpitasya ca sāmānyasya aśakta tvāt viṣaya dvaividhyam na hi ekasya viruddhau= imau dharmau yujyete yadi anartha kriyā kāri sāmānyam keśoṇḍuka jñāna pratibhāsi keśa ādī api sāmānyam syāt 
PVV_2.1–2.2,9–2.1–2.2,11	 keśa ādiḥ nna arthaḥ nartha adhimokṣataḥ na keśādiḥ arthaḥ sāmānya rūpaḥ anartha adhimokṣataḥ yatra hi vyavahartṝṇām artha adhyavasāyaḥ saḥ arthaḥ sva lakṣaṇam sāmānyam vā syāt yatra punar artha buddhiḥ eva na asti sa katham sāmānyam ucyatām sadṛśā sadṛśa tvāt ca viṣaya aviṣaya tvataḥ śabdasya anya nimittānām bhāve dhīḥ sat asatvatas 
PVV_2.1–2.2,12	 tathā tadṛśā sadṛśa tvāt ca viṣaya dvaividhyam sadṛśam sāmānyam sarva vyakti sādhāraṇa tvāt asadṛśam sva lakṣaṇam sarvu atas vyāvṛtta tvāt anayoḥ ca anyonya vyavaccheda rūpa tvāt na rāśi antaram tatas yadi kalpyamānam sadṛśam tadā sāmānyam eva tat atha asadṛśam sva lakṣaṇam eva iti dvaividhyam eva viṣayasya tathā śabdasya viṣaya aviṣaya tvataḥ ca dvaividhyam śabdasya viṣayaḥ sāmānyam aviṣayaḥ sva lakṣaṇam na ca śabda viṣaya aviṣayābhyām anyosti saru u asya saṃgrahāt dvaividhyam eva tathā viṣayāt anyaṣān nimittānām manaskāra vat sādguṇya saṃketa grahaṇānām bhāve grāhikāyāḥ dhiyaḥ sāmānye sattvāt sva lakṣaṇe ca abhāvāt viṣaya dvaividhyam yatra viṣaya vyatirikta nimitta sadbhāve bhavati buddhiḥ tad sāmānyam yatratu na bhavati tat sva lakṣaṇam prakāra antarañca na sambhavati iti buddhi viṣaya aviṣaya tve sāmānya sva lakṣaṇa tā eva iti dvaividhyam eva viṣayasya 
PVV_2.3,0–2.3,2	 tat eva artha kriyā sāmarthya ādikam sva lakṣaṇa ādau yojayan= āha artha kriyā samartha yat tat atra parama artha sat anyat saṃvṛtisat proktam te sva sāmānya lakṣaṇaḥ artha kriyāyām jñāna ādikāyām svarūpa upadhānena samartham yat tat atra vastu vicāraḥ parama artha evam yat asadṛśam śabda aviṣayaḥ anya nimitta bhāve jñāna abhāvaḥ ca tat parama artha sat atas anyat aśaktam sadṛśam śabda viṣayaḥ anya nimitta bhāve buddheḥ vviṣayaḥ ca tat saṃvṛtisat kalpanā mātra vyavahārya tvāt te parama artha saṃvṛtī sva sāmānya lakṣaṇe 
PVV_2.4,0–2.4,1	 aśaktam sarvam iti ced bīja ādeḥ aṅkura ādiṣu dṛṣṭā śaktiḥ sva lakṣaṇa sāmānya lakṣaṇe iṣṭe sarvvam artha kāri tvena iṣṭam aśaktam na kiñcid karttum samartham iti ced bīja ādeḥ kāraṇa abhimatasya aṅkura ādau kārya saṃmate dṛṣṭā śaktiḥ janana lakṣaṇā bīja anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyī aṅkuraḥ dṛśyate idam eva kāraṇasya śakta tvam yat prāc adṛṣṭasya tad bhāvaḥ eva bhāvaḥ 
PVV_2.4,2–2.4,3	 matā sā ced saṃvṛtyā sā śaktiḥ saṃvṛtyā matā ced kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ hi vyavahāra mātrataḥ siddhaḥ na paramārthataḥ na tāvat pratyakṣam tad grahaṇa samartham bīja aṅkura grāhiṇoḥ pratyakṣayoḥ sva viṣaya mātra vyavasthāpanāt kena anvaya vyatireka grahaṇam krameṇa dvayoḥ gṛhītayoḥ tad bala bhāvinā smaraṇena grahaṇam iti ced 
PVV_2.4,4	 nanu kena anvaya vyatirekau gṛhītau na pratyekam bīja aṅkura jñānābhyām sva sva viṣaya grahaṇāt na api dvābhyām jñānayoḥ jñeyayoḥ ca sāhitya abhāvāt asāhitye bīja aṅkura mātrasya grahaṇam na anvaya vyatirekayoḥ krama grahaṇam eva kārya kāraṇa bhāva grahaṇam tat tu ghaṭa kulālayoḥ api asti iti ced na ca kramopi kenacid śakya grahaṇaḥ pratiyogya vedanāt pūrva apara grahaṇam atas eva na asti sva jñānena vartamāna tā grahaṇāt ca kārya kāle ca kāraṇam pūrvvam ucyate tadā ca tat eva na asti tat etat mṛtasya ārogyam atha yadā eva bījam tadā eva aṅkurāt pūrvvam na tu paścāt asya pūrvva tvam sambhavati 
PVV_2.4,5	 nanu evam pūrvvatayā pratibhāsosya prāptaḥ na ca etat asti aṅkura sāhityam pūrvva tvam tat ca gṛhyate eva iti ced tādṛśam pūrvva tvam anyeṣām api asti iti tepi kāraṇāni syuḥ kiñca pūrvva tvam vartamāna kālāt prāc bhāvi tvam ucyate tat yadi vastunaḥ rūpam tadā vartamānam kadāpi na syāt vartam āna tā tad prāk bhāvi tvayoḥ vvirodhāt syāt etat aṅkura vartam āna tāyāḥ prāc bhāvi tvam pūrvva tvam tat ca bījasya vartamāna tvena aviruddham iti na tasya abhāvaḥ evantarhi bīja grahaṇe pūrvvata agrahaṇam prāptam na ca bīja svarūpam iva pūrvvatām api tad grāhiṇi jñāne kaścid upalabhate 
PVV_2.4,6–2.4,8^1	 nanu āpekṣikam idam pūrvva tvam pratiyoginaḥ apratītau katham pratīyatām yadi evam vastunaḥ na idam kevalam bhāva antara apekṣayā vyavahriyate iyātam na hi vastu rūpam sati vastu ninā asti yat ca asti tena vastu rūpa avabhāsini jñāne pratibhāsitavyam eva anyathā jñāna jñeyayoḥ vviṣaya viṣayitā eva na syāt tasmāt na adhyakṣāt kārya kāraṇa tā grahaḥ atas ca na anumānāt api na hi sarvvadā parokṣe anye anumāna vṛttiḥ vyāpti grahaṇa pūrvvaka tvāt tasya na api pratyakṣa bala bhāvi smaraṇam tad grahaṇa pravaṇam 
PVV_2.4,6–2.4,8^2	 na hi tat svatantram pramāṇam kintu pramāṇa vyāpāra vyavasthāpakam yadi yathā anubhavam pravartate na anyathā na ca kārya kāraṇa bhāva anubhavaḥ bhūtaḥ iti uktam atas smaraṇa tvam api asya na asti anūbhūta vikalpanasya smaraṇa tvāt tatas vikalpa mātram etat na tatas vastu vyavasthā iti saṃvṛttyā eva avicārita ramaṇīyayā kārya kāraṇa bhāva vyavahāraḥ na paramārthataḥ astu yathā tathā astu yathā tathā sāṃvṛtam api kārya kāraṇa bhāvam āśritya sādhya sādhana ādi vyavahāra samvāda sampratyayāt samāptaḥ loka vyavahāraḥ sāṃvyavahāri kañca pramāṇam tāvatā eva sustham 
PVV_2.5,0–2.5,1	 sā asti sarvatra ced buddheḥ na anvayavyatirekayoḥ sāmānya lakṣaṇe adṛṣṭeḥ cakṣu ūru upādi buddhi vat sārtha kriyā sa sva lakṣaṇe sāmānyepi asti ced na sāmānya lakṣaṇe astu tāvat anyasya kāryasya buddheḥ api anvaya vyatirekayoḥ adṛṣṭeḥ antyam hi bhāvānām kāryam buddhiḥ sā api yat anvaya vyatirekau na anuvidhatte tasya kutas artha kriyā pratyakṣam tāvat na sāmānya viṣayam sva lakṣaṇa mātrasya pratibhāsanāt ghaṭaḥ ityādi vikalpa buddhiḥ tu sāmānya avasāyāt tad viṣayāḥ sā api samayā bhoga ādi mātrāt utpatteḥ na sāmānya anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyinī cakṣu ūrūpādi buddhi vat cakṣu ūrūpa ādi ja buddheḥ cakṣuḥ ādi anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānam iva sāmarthye sati bhāvāt eka apāyepya bhāvāt ca na evam sāmānya buddhiḥ ābhoga mātrāt utpatteḥ 
PVV_2.6,0–2.6,1	 etena samaya ābhoga ādi antaraṅga anurodhataḥ ghaṭa utkṣepaṇa sāmānya saṃkhyā ādiṣu dhiyaḥ gatāḥ etena sāmānyasya jñāna mātra kārya īpi a sāmarthya kathanena samaya ābhoga ādeḥ antaraṅgasya anurodhataḥ ghaṭaḥ avayavi dravyam utkṣepaṇam karma sāmānyam saṃkhyā guṇaḥ samavāyaḥ ādi śabdāt saṃyoga vibhāga ādayaḥ teṣu yāḥ dhiyaḥ vikalpikāḥ bhavanti tāḥ gatāḥ vyākhyātāḥ na hi rūpa ādi vyatiriktam dravyam apara apara deśi janya hasta ādi kṣaṇāt bhinnam karma vyakti vyatireki sāmānyam pratyakṣa buddha avabhāsate vikalpabuddhiḥ astu kalpikā sā ca saṃketa saṃskāra prabodha mātra bhāvinī na artha adhīnā iti na teṣām sāmarthyam samarthayati 
PVV_2.7,0–2.7,5	 nanu yadi artha nirapekṣāṇām anya nimittānām bhāve yatra buddhiḥ tad sāmānyam tadā taimirika buddhi pratibhāsinaḥ keśādayopi sāmānyam stuḥ teṣu api dhiyaḥ artha nirapekṣa cakṣuḥ ādi mātra nimitta tvāt iti āha keśa ādayaḥ na sāmānyam anartha abhiniveśataḥ keśa ādayaḥ taimirika pratibhāsinaḥ na sāmānyam anartha abhiniveśataḥ na hi teṣu viṣaya buddhiḥ vyavahāriṇām viṣaye ca sāmānya cintā iyam yadi jñeya tvena adhyavasāya abhāvāt na sāmānyam tadā abhāva upyanupalabdhi viṣayaḥ sāmānyam na syāt tatas ca anupalabdhiḥ anumānam na bhavet iti āha jñeya tvena grahāt doṣaḥ na abhāveṣu prasajyate na abhāveṣu sāmānya rūpa tva abhāva doṣaḥ prasajyate jñeya tvena grahāt yadi api abhāve artha rūpa tāyāḥ adhyavasāyaḥ na asti jñeya tayā tu asti lokasya tat ca jñe yad artha kāri tat sāmānyam eva 
PVV_2.8–2.9,0–2.8–2.9,3	 yadi tu teṣām api tathā abhāve apratiṣedhāt teṣām taimirika gamyānām keśa ādīnām api tathā abhāve jñāna antareṇa jñeya tve samāna rūpatā iṣyate tadā apratiṣedha ādiṣṭam eva asmākam taimirika jñāna gamyāḥ keśa ādayaḥ iti yadā buddhi antareṇa parāmṛśyante tadā keśa ādayaḥ jñeya tvena sāmānyam iṣṭāḥ eva yadi taimirika dṛṣṭāḥ keśa ādayaḥ na vastu tadā sphuṭa ābhatā na syāt iti āha 
PVV_2.8–2.9,4–2.8–2.9,14	 sphuṭa ābhatā jñāna rūpa tayā artha tvāt jñāna rūpa tayā jñāna ākāra tayā keśa ādīnām artha tvāt sva lakṣaṇa tvāt sphuṭa ābhatā yadi jñāna ākāra tayā keśa ādayaḥ sva lakṣaṇantadā sāmānyam katham iti āha keśa ādi iti matiḥ punar sāmānya viṣayā keśādi iti punar vvikalpikā matiḥ taimirika upalabdha keśa ādi adhyavasāyinī sāmānya viṣayā ayam arthaḥ taimirika dṛṣṭam keśa ādi sāmānya rūpeṇa vyavasyantī vikalpikā buddhiḥ adhyavasāyena viṣayeṇa sāmānya viṣayā taimirika dhīḥ tu sva lakṣaṇa viṣayāḥ buddhi ākārasya sva lakṣaṇa tvāt kintarhi nirvviṣayam iti āha keśa pratibhāsam anarthakam taimirika keśa pratibhāsam jñānam anartha kamba āhya keśa abhāvāt jñāna rūpa tayā artha tve sāmānye ced prasajyate nanu jñāna rūpa tayā artha tve keśa ādi iti vikalpa buddhi pratibhāsini sāmānye sva lakṣaṇa tā prasajyate ced 
PVV_2.10,0–2.10,7	 tathā iṣṭa tvāt adoṣaḥ tathā jñāna ākāra tayā sāmānyasya api sva lakṣaṇa tāyāḥ iṣṭa tvāt adoṣaḥ kathantarhi sāmānya rūpa tā iti āha artha rūpa tvena samāna tā artha rūpa tvena adhyavasīyamāna jñeya rūpa tvena samāna tā na tu buddhi ākāra tvena katham punar artha rūpa tvena api samāna ta iti āha sarvatra sama rūpa tvāt tad vyāvṛtti samāśrayāt sarvu atra vyaktiṣu tad vyāvṛtti samāśrayāt vijātīya vyāvṛtti āśrayeṇa dṛśya vikalpya ekatva adhyavasāyāt upakalpitasya sāmānyasya sama rūpa tvāt sādhāraṇa rūpa tvāt artha tvena sāmānyam ucyate jñāna ākārasya sāmānyasya saṃprati vyatiriktasya ca pūrvvam pratiṣedhāt 
PVV_2.11,0–2.11,5	 rūpa ādi svabhāvam eva aviśeṣeṇa sāmānyam kinneṣyate iti āha na tat vastu abhidheya tvāt sāphalyāt akṣa saṃhateḥ tad sāmānyam na vastu rūpa ādi svabhāvam abhidheya tvāt śabda dharma vat sāmānyam śabda jñāna gocaraḥ na ca śabda viṣayaḥ vastu kasmāt iti āha sāphalyāt akṣa saṃhateḥ yadi śabda viṣayaḥ vastu bhavet tadā rūpa ādi śabdāt eva artha ādeḥ api rūpa ādi pratītau na kiñci d akṣaiḥ na ca evam tatas vastu viṣayeṇa indriya jñānena śabdasya na tulya viṣaya tā tathā ca avastu tā eva śābda jñāna avabhāsinaḥ sāmānyasya na rūpa āditā nanu rūpa ādayaḥ na śabdasya viṣayaḥ kintarhi nāma nimitte viprayukta saṃskāra saṃjñe te vijñānāt vyatirikte vai bhā ṣi kaḥ syeṣṭe tadā api nāma ādi vacane vaktṛ śrotṛ vācya anubandhini nāma ādi vacanaḥ iṣyamāṇe kintad nāma ādikam vaktari śrotari arthe vā sambaddham asambaddham eva vā kvacid sarvu athā vaktṛ

PVV_2.12,5	 na hi devadatte pratipādite tat pitari pravṛttiḥ nimittasya artha sārūpyāt pravṛttiḥ ced sambhāvyate etat kintu na syāt sarvvadāḥ na hi yama lakayoḥ niyamena bhrāntyā a nyatra pravṛttiḥ kadācid tatra api darśanāt tathā ādeśa bhrāntiḥ ca na syāt vaktṛ śrotra ādi sambandhini niyata deśe nāma ādau pratipādite tad anya deśe ghaṭa ādau sārūpyāt api na yu ktā pravṛttiḥ
