PVV_2.25,0–2.25,2	 kiñca jātiḥ jātimataḥ rūpāt bhinnā abhinnāḥ vā na jātiḥ jātimat vyakti rūpam yena apara āśrayam siddham pṛthak ced kārya tvam hi apekṣā iti abhidhīyate tatra na tāvat jātiḥ jātimat eva vyakti rūpam yena kāraṇena apara āśrayam ananyā anuyāyi siddham na hi ekasyāḥ vyakte rūpam anyatra asti sarvvānuyāyi ca sāmānyam iṣṭam vyakteḥ sakāśāt pṛthak ced sāmānyam asya idam sāmānyam iti bhāvika sambandha anupapattiḥ apekṣā lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ ced nanu apekṣā iti kāryatvam ucyate tad sāmānyasya nityasya asambhavi 
PVV_2.26,0–2.27,2	 niṣpatteḥ apara adhīnam api kāryam sva hetutaḥ sambadhyate kalpanayā kim akāryam kathañcana kāryam api niṣyatteḥ nitya tvāt apara adhīnam sarvu atra nirāśaṃsam vastutas na kvacid sambaḥ kevalam kalpanayā kāraṇa ātmani sambadhyate yat tu kathañcana sāmānyam akārya kvacid sambhatsyate anya tve tad asambaddham siddhā atas niḥsvabhāva tā jāti prasaṃgaḥ abhāvasya na tasmāt vyakteḥ sakāśāt anya tve tat sāmānyam asambaddham atas asya niḥsvabhāva tā vyaktibhyaḥ tattva anya tvābhyām vyavasthāpayitum aśakyatvāt yadi api niḥ svabhāvā jātiḥ tathā api na abhāvasya śaśaviṣāṇa ādeḥ api jāteḥ jāti rūpa tāyāḥ prasaṅgaḥ na hi yaḥ yaḥ abhāvaḥ sa jātiḥ ucyate kintu sāmānyam yat tat niḥsvabhāvam 
PVV_2.27,3–2.27,5	 nanu niḥsvabhāva tve katham sāmānyam iti āha apekṣā bhāvataḥ tayoḥ apekṣā bhāvataḥ tayoḥ śābaleyāgo vyāvṛttyoḥ parasparam apekṣā bhāvataḥ tad vyāvṛttiḥ eva sāmānyam na śaśa viṣāṇa ādiḥ na hi tad apekṣā kvacid asti atad vyāvṛttiḥ tu niḥsvabhāva api anugāmi pratyaya hetuḥ sāmānyam abhāva tvam iva prāc abhāva ādiṣu padārtha tvam iva dravya ādiṣu 
PVV_2.28,0–2.28,1	 tasmāt arūpāḥ rūpāṇām māśrayeṇa upakalpitā tad viśeṣa avagāha arthaiḥ jātiḥ śabdaiḥ prakāśyate tasmāt vastutas jātiḥ arūpāḥ niḥsvabhāvāḥ rūpāṇām śābaleya ādīnām na āśrayeṇa upa jātiḥ śabdaiḥ tad viśeṣa avagāha arthaiḥ te ca te viśeṣāḥ ca tad viśeṣāḥ teṣām avagāhaḥ pravṛtti viṣaya tvena vyāpanam saḥ arthaḥ prayojanam yeṣām taiḥ sakṛt eka kārya aneka pratipatti artham tad āśrayeṇa upakalpitā jātiḥ atad vyāvṛtti lakṣaṇā śabdaiḥ abhidheyāḥ 
PVV_2.29–2.30,0–2.29–2.30,4	 yadi jātiḥ niḥsvabhāvā katham svabhāva viśiṣṭā vyavasīyate iti āha tasyām rūpa avabhāsoyam tatvena arthasya vā grahaḥ bhrāntiḥ sā tasyām jātau rūpasya svabhāvasya avabhāsaḥ yaḥ ta tvena jāti svabhāvena vā arthasya jāteniḥsvabhāva tvāt viśeṣa ātmaka tva abhāvāt kintarhi bhrānteḥ bbījam iti āha anādika ālīna darśana abhyāsa nirmitā 
PVV_2.29–2.30,5–2.29–2.30,8	 anādi kālī nānām anādi kālikānām tathābhūta adhyavasāya jñānānām abhyāsena yadi anya vyāvṛttiḥ sāmānyam kintasya rūpam iti āha arthānām yat ca sāmānya manya vyāvṛtti lakṣaṇam yat niṣṭhāḥ te ime śabdāḥ na rūpam tasya kiñcana arthānām viśeṣāṇām yat ca sāmānya manya vyāvṛtti lakṣaṇam yad niṣṭhāḥ yat viṣayāḥ te sāṃketikāḥ śabdāḥ tasya rūpam svabhāvaḥ na kiñcana vastutas kalpita tvāt 
PVV_2.31–2.32,0–2.31–2.32,4	 nanu buddhi ākāraḥ sa svabhāvaḥ saḥ eva tarhi sāmānyambhaviṣyati iti āha sāmānya buddhau sāmānyena arūpāyām avīkṣaṇāt artha bhrāntiḥ apīṣyeta sāmānyam sā apiḥ sāmānya buddha avarūpāyām grāhya rūpa rahitāyām api sāmānyena vijātīya vyāvṛtti upakalpita abhedena ākāreṇa bhedeṣu artheṣu īkṣaṇāt sāmānyam api yat vyavasthāpyate sā api artha vivecakaiḥ na hi buddhi ākāraḥ sāmānyam uktam sva lakṣaṇa tvāt abhiplavāt artha rūpa tayā tatvena abhāvāt ca na rūpiṇī niḥsvabhāva tayā avācyam kutaścid vacanāt matam 
PVV_2.31–2.32,5	 artha niṣṭhatayā tu sāmānye gṛhyamāṇe artha bhramaḥ tathā buddhi ākārasya artha rūpa tvena vyaktiṣu abhiplavāt abhisambandhāt tattvena artha rūpa tvena abhāvāt ca na tathābhūta bāhya viṣayavatī sāmānya buddhiḥ atas ca tatas ca niḥsvabhāva tayā sāmānyam bheda abhedābhyām avācyam vyaktibhyaḥ svabhāvam hi bhinnam abhinnam vā syāt kutaścid sāmānyāt bhedena vacanāt yadi vastu sāmānyam matam 
PVV_2.33,0–2.33,1	 yadi vastuni vastūnām avācya tvam kathañcana na eva vācyam upādāna bhedāt bheda upacārataḥ yadi evam vyakteḥ api bheda abhedābhyām vācyam syāt yasmāt na vastūnām avācya tvam yathā hi sāmānyam svarūpavat tvāt sāmānya antarāt bhedena ucyate tathā vyakteḥ api tattva anya tvābhyām yathāsambhavamucyeta tasmāt yat kutaścid api vastunaḥ tatva anya tvābhyām avācyam tat avastu iti sa viśeṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ athavā nirvviśeṣaṇe hetau na asiddhiḥ yata sā amānyā antarāt api sāmānyam bhedena na eva vācyam upādānasya karkaśā baleya ādeḥ bhedāt tad āśraya utpanna buddhi ālambanā aśva tvagotva ādīnām bhedasya upacārāt 
PVV_2.34,0–2.34,2	 kiñca atīta anāgatepi arthe sāmānya vinibandhanāḥ śrutayaḥ niviśante sat asat dharmaḥ katham bhavet atīta anāgatepi arthe sāmānya nibandhanā sāmānya āśrayāḥ śrutayaḥ niviśante vyavatiṣṭhante āsīt ghaṭaḥ bhaviṣyati ityādayaḥ tathā ca asataḥ ghaṭasya sāmānyam dharmaḥ iti uktam syāt tat ca sāmānyam sat asataḥ atīta ādeḥ dharmaḥ katham bhavet na hi taikṣṇyam śaśa viṣāṇasya bhavati 
PVV_2.35,0–2.35,2	 upacārāt tat iṣṭam ced varttamāna ghaṭasya kā pratyāsattiḥ abhāvena yā paṭa ādau na vidyate atha upacārāt tat asat dharma tvam iṣṭam sāmānyasya na vastutas iti ced sati ghaṭe tad dharmatā dṛṣṭeḥ asati api tasmin sā kalpyate iti arthaḥ nanu sāmānya sambandhinaḥ api ghaṭasya abhāvena atīta ādi ghaṭa lakṣaṇena kā pratyāsattiḥ upacāra nibandhanam asti yā paṭa ādau na vidyate yat abhāvāt ghaṭa sambandhitā sāmānyasya paṭe na upacaryate sādṛśyam pratyāsattiḥ ita ced tat na sat asataḥ sādṛśya abhāvāt prāk tādṛś āsīt iti ced yadā āsīt na tadā tad upacāraḥ sambandhasya sattvāt yadā yana asti tadā api na sādṛśyam sati ca kiñcid upacaryeta na asati 
PVV_2.36,0–2.36,2	 kiñca buddheḥ askhalitā vṛttiḥ mukhya āropitayoḥ sadā siṃhe māṇavake tadvat ghoṣaṇā api asti laukikī mukhya āropitayoḥ arthayoḥ burgrāṃhikāyāḥ askhalitā dṛḍhā vṛttiḥ tantrāt avṛttiḥ ca sadā yathā siṃhe māṇavake ca siṃha buddheṃraskhalitā skhalitā ca vṛttiḥ iti laukikī api ghoṣaṇā asti na kevalam prāmāṇikī na ca atīta anāgata ghaṭa ādi buddhiḥ skhalantī jāyate yena atīta anāgata vyakti dharma tā sāmānyasya āropitā syāt 
PVV_2.37,0–2.37,1	 yatra rūḍhyā asat arthopi janaiḥ śabdaḥ niveśitaḥ sa mukhyaḥ tatra tad sāmyāt gauṇonyatra skhalat gatiḥ tasmāt yatra viṣaye asat arthaḥ vācya rahitopi śabdaḥ rūḍhyā vācaka tvena janaiḥ nive saṃketitaḥ sa mṛkhyaḥ tatra arthe tad sāmyāt tad viṣaya sādṛśyāt anyatra sa śabdaḥ skha dṛḍha tayā pratyaya haituḥ gauṇaḥ tatas ca sat artha viṣaya tvam mukhya tvam asat artha viṣaya tvañcāmukhya tvam iti mukhyā gauṇa lakṣaṇam apāḥ tam saṃketa vaśena niyama abhāvāt 
PVV_2.38,0–2.38,1	 yathā bhāvepya bhāva ākhyām yathākalpanam eva vā kuryāt aśakte śakte vā pradhāna ādi śrutim janaḥ yathā bhāvepi putra ādau tad kārya asamartha tvāt asat kalpe abhāva ākhyām śaśa viṣāṇam bandhyā sutaḥ iti ādikām janaḥ kuryyāt tatra bhāvepya mukhyaḥ abhāva śabdaḥ abhāve tu mukhyaḥ tathā yathā kalpanam eva sām khyāḥ dyabhimate vastutas a śakte pradhāna ādau śakte vā puruṣa ādau= aneka kārya samarthe tad sāmyāt pradhāna ādi śrutim janaḥ kuryyāt sa pradhāna śabdaḥ abhāṃvaḥ eva mukhyaḥ bhāve ca amukhyaḥ tasmāt sat asat artha viṣaya tā mukhya gauṇa viṣaya tā iti vyabhicāri lakṣaṇam 
PVV_2.39,0–2.39,4	 yathā saṃketam eva tu śabda vṛttiḥ iti yukttam na ca etat vastu viṣaya tve nyāyyam tathā hi śabdebhyaḥ yādṛśī buddhiḥ naṣṭe anaṣṭepi dṛśyate tādṛśi eva śabdebhyaḥ yādṛśī yādṛśa ākārā buddhiḥ naṣṭe viṣaye tādṛśī eva anaṣṭepi viṣaye avyāpta tā indriyasya dṛśyate na hi śabda janitā ghaṭa buddhiḥ nimīlita nayanasya naṣṭe anaṣṭe vā ghaṭe viśiṣyate tulya ākāra tvāt vyāpta indriyasya tu śabdam śrṛṇvataḥ yā spaṣṭā buddhiḥ sā pratyakṣā eva na śabda kṛtā tasmāt avastu viṣayā eva śābdī buddhiḥ sat arthānām na etat śotrādi cetasām sat arthānām vastu viṣayāṇām tu śrotra ādi indriya jātānām cetasām na etat viṣaya sada sattā kālayoḥ sāmyam śabda buddheḥ iva artha abhāve indriya buddheḥ anutpatteḥ 
PVV_2.40,0–2.40,4	 nanu naṣṭe anaṣṭepi vastuni ye śābdaḥ cetasī jāyete sāmānya mātra grahaṇāt sāmānyam cetasoḥ dvayoḥ tābhyām samānya mātrasya grahaṇāt tayoḥ dvayoḥ cetasoḥ sāmānyam sāmyam grāhya pratibhāsa kṛtam asti etat ca ayuktam yasmāt tasya api kevalasya prāk grahaṇam vinivāritam tasya api sāmānyasya kevalasya vyakti śūnyasya grahaṇam prāgnivā atad samāna tā avyaktī ityādinā 
PVV_2.41,0–2.41,2	 bhinnam sāmānyam niṣidhya abhinnam api niṣeddhum āha paraspara viśiṣṭānām aviśiṣṭam katham bhavet tathā dvi rūpa tāyām vā tat vastu ekam katham bhavet paraspara viśiṣṭānām viśeṣāṇām aviśiṣṭam abhinnam rūpam katham bhavet avaśyam hi vyaktīnām bhedaḥ kathañci daṅgīkarttavyaḥ sattva rajaḥ tamasām iva prakṛti caitanyayoḥ iva vā anyathā sāmānyam eva na syāt bhinnānām abhinnasya rūpasya tattvāt ye ca bhinna svabhāvāḥ te na abhinnā bhavitum arhanti viruddha tvāt atha ekasya api samānam asamānañca dve rūpe tathā dvi rūpa tāyām tat vastu ekam katham bhavet anyaḥ hi samānāt asamānaḥ svabhāvaḥ atas ca dve vastunī syātām na tu ekam dvi rūpam 
PVV_2.42,0–2.42,5	 atha dvayoḥ ekam tat rūpam sāmānyam tābhyām tat anyat eva syāt yadi rūpam samam tayoḥ yadi tayoḥ dvayoḥ samam samānam rūpam tadā tābhyām eva anyat eva tat syāt pṛthak bhūtam eva sāmānyam bhaviṣyati kaḥ doṣaḥ iti ced āha tayoḥ iti na sambandhaḥ vyāvṛttiḥ tu na duṣyati tayoḥ tad sāmānyam iti na sambandhaḥ upakārya upakāraka tva abhāvāt tathā asambandhe ati prasaṅgāt asmad mate tu vyāvṛttiḥ sāmānyam na duṣyati atad kārya vyāvṛtteḥ avastu tvāt anyathā anyān anya tva pakṣa uktaḥ doṣaḥ 
PVV_2.43,0–2.43,4	 tasmāt samāna tā eva asmin sāmānye avastu lakṣaṇam yatas samāna tvena avastu tā tasmāt samāna tā eva asmin sāmānye avastu lakṣaṇam yat sāmānyam tad avasthiti vyāpti siddheḥ bhede abhede ca vastu tva ayogāt prakāra antarasya ca abhāvāt kiñca kāryañcet tat anekam syāt naśvarañca na tat matam sāmānyam kāryam akāryam vā syāt sambandhinīnām vyaktīnām kāryañcet prativyakti sāmānya uktau= anekam syāt ekañca sāmā nyam iṣṭam aneka tve sāmānya rūpa tā nāśaḥ naśvarañca na tad sāmānyam matam kāryatvāt naśvarañca tat prāpnoti kāryatvasya nāśi tvena svabhāvasya vyāpteḥ 
PVV_2.44,0–2.44,5	 kiñca vastu mātra anubandhi tvāt vināśasya na nityatā vastu mātra anubandhi tvāt nāśasya vastunona nityatā syāt anitya tā virahe tu vastu virahopi vyāpya abhāvasya vyāpaka abhāva niyata tvāt atha dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ tadā asambandhaḥ ca jātīnām akārya tvāt arūpa tā akārya tvāt jātīnām sva vyaktibhiḥ saha sambandhaḥ ca na syāt kārya kāraṇa bhāva abhāve tasya idam iti sambandhasya anutpattiḥ iti uktam kārya tvam hi apekṣā iti abhidhīyate iti atra antare akārya tvāt jātīnām a rūpatā niḥsvabhāva tā utpadyamānam hi sa svabhāvam bhavet na itarat niyāmaka abhāvena svabhāva abhāva prasaṅgāt 
PVV_2.45,0–2.45,2	 śābda pratyayasya avastu viṣaya tāyām upapatti antaram āha yat ca vastu balāt jñānam jāyate tat apekṣate na saṅketam na sāmānya buddhiṣu etat vibhāvyate yat ca jñānam indriya jam vastunaḥ rūpa ādeḥ bbalāt jāyate tat na saṃketam apekṣate bāla badhira ādeḥ api bhāvāt sāmānya buddhiṣu tu etat saṃketa anapekṣa tvam na vibhāvyate saṃketa grahaṇa smaraṇa apekṣa tvāt tasmāt na vastu bala bhāvinyastāḥ tathā tve sati indriya artha sannipāte kṣepā yogāt 
PVV_2.46,0–2.46,1	 yāpya bheda anugā buddhiḥ kācid vastu dvaya īkṣaṇe saṅketena vinā sārtha pratyāsatti nibandhanā yā api saṃketena vinā vastu dvaya īkṣaṇe śāvaleyam dṛṣṭvā bāhuleyam paśyataḥ abheda anugamāt saḥ eva ayam iti abhedam adhyavasyantī buddhiḥ utpadyate śāvaleya karka darśane tu na utpadyate sā arthānām śāvaleya ādīnām asati api sāmānye yā pratyāsattiḥ ekabuddhi ādi kārya tvam tad nibandhanā 
PVV_2.47,0–2.47,2	 sāmānyam vinā eka kārya tā eva na syāt iti āha pratyāsattiḥ vinā jātyā yatheṣṭā cakṣuḥ ādiṣu jñāna kāryeṣu jātiḥ vā yayā anvā iti vibhāgataḥ pratyāsattiḥ vinā jānyā cakṣuḥ ādiḥ yeṣām viṣaya āloka manaskārāṇām teṣu jñāna kāryeṣu jñāna hetuṣu jāti ādi vinā rūpa jñāna eka kārya janaka tvam pratyāsattiḥ yathā iṣṭā yathā vā śāvaleyāt bāhuleya ādīnām karkā ādīnāñca tulye bhede yathā pratyāsatyā jāti antaram vinā eva vibhāgataḥ jātiḥ anveti śāvaleya bāhuleya ādiṣu eva go tvam samavetam na karkā ādiṣu sā eva anugāmi pratyaya nibandhanam āḥ tām alam jātyā 
PVV_2.48,0–2.48,6	 itas ca na vastu sāmānyam kathañcid api vijñāne tad rūpa anava bhāsataḥ dṛśya tvena abhimatasya tad rūpasya su agrāhiṇi vijñāne kathañcid api anavabhāsataḥ nanu santi api indriyāṇi na upalabhyante tatas atra anupalambhāt asatvam na na hi indriyāṇi sva grāhiṇi jñāne pratyavabhāsamāna tvāt santīṣyante kintarhi satsu api viṣaya manaskāra ādiṣu kadācid pravartate jñānam kadācid na iti vyabhicāra balāt ati indriyāṇi kānicid indriya vyapadeśyāni vyavasthāpyante yadi nāma indriyāṇām syāt draṣṭā bhāseta tad vapuḥ rūpava tvāt yadi tu ati indriyāṇām atīndriya darśī draṣṭā nāma syāt bhāseta rūpava tvāt teṣām indriyāṇām vapuḥ 
PVV_2.49,0–2.50,1	 na jātīnām kevalānām adarśanāt vyakti grahe ca tat śrabda rūpāt anyat na dṛśyate jātīnāntu duśya abhimatānām kevalānām vyakti svarūpa vyatiriktānām adarśanāḥ eva vyakti grahe tasyāḥ vyakteḥ śabdasya gauḥ ityasya rūpāt anyat sāmānyam na dṛśyate jñāna mātra artha karaṇepi a yogyamat eva tat tad ayogya tayā arūpam tat hi avastuṣu lakṣaṇam atas eva adṛśyamāna tvāt jñāna mātrasya arthasya artha kriyāyāḥ karaṇepyayogyam eva tat antyāḥ hi iyam bhāvānām artha kriyā yat uta sva jñāna jananam tatra api ayogya tayā tad sāmānyam arūpam niḥsvabhāvam hiḥ yasmāt sarvva artha kriyāyām aśakta tvam avastuṣu lakṣaṇam sarva sāmarthya rahitam hi avastu iṣyate 
PVV_2.51,0–2.51,2	 tathā ca sāmānyam iti na vastu yathā ukta viparītam yat tat sva lakṣaṇam iṣyate yathā uktāt sāmānyāt viparītam yat tat sva lakṣaṇam ucyate idañca vaiparītyam anabhidheya tvam tatvā anya tvābhyām vācya tvam asat artha pratyaya aviśiṣṭa pratibhāsa viṣaya tvam asādhāraṇa tvam saṃketa smaraṇa anapekṣa pratipattika tvam anya rūpa vivikta svarūpa pratibhāsavat tvam artha kriyā akṣama tvañca etat yuktam sva lakṣaṇam iṣyate etad viparyayasya avastu tva sādhanasya sāmānya lakṣaṇa tvāt 
PVV_2.51,3–2.51,5	 yat ca atad kārya vyavaccheda lakṣaṇam uktam sāmānyam trividham tat ca bhāva abhāva ubhayāśrayāt sāmānyam tat ca trividham boddhavyam bhāva abhāva ubhayāśrayāt kiñcid bhāva upādānam sāmānyam yathā rūpa ādīn bhāvān āśritya kṛtaka tva ādi śabda vācyam liṅgam abhāva upādānam yathā upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya asataḥ anupalabdhiḥ anutpattimat tva ādi ca tad hi abhāva āśrayam sāmānyam liṅgam ubhaya āśrayam anupalabdhi mātraṃjñeya tva ādi ca bhāva abhāva sādharaṇa tvāt 
PVV_2.52,0–2.52,1	 yadi bhāva āśrayam jñānam bhāve bhāva anubandhataḥ na ukta uttara tvāt dṛṣṭa tvāt atīta ādiṣu ca anyathā yadi kiñcid sāmānyam bhā tat jñānam tad bhāve bhāva viṣayam prāpnoti bhāva anubandhataḥ bhāva anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānāt na etat yuktam na tat vastu abhidheya tva ādinā ukta uttara tvāt niṣiddham hi sāmānyasya vastu tvam anantaram eva prapañcena iti anumāna bādhita tvam pratijñāyāḥ dṛṣṭa tvāt atīta ādiṣu ca anyathā vastu vyatirekeṇa eva āsīt ghaṭaḥ bhaviṣyati ca iti sāmānya buddhiḥ utpadyate iti asiddha tā api bhāva anubandhate iti hetoḥ 
PVV_2.53,0–2.53,3	 bhāva dharma tvahāniḥ ced bhāva grahaṇa pūrvakam tat jñānam iti adoṣoyam vastu vinā sāmānya buddhi utpāde bhāvadha sāmānyasya prasajyate ced bhāvasya rūpa ādeḥ grahaṇa pūrvvakam tasya sāmānyasya sādhāraṇa bāhya rūpa tayā a dhyavasita buddhi ākāra lakṣaṇasya adhyavasāyena jñānam iti ayam avastu dharma tva lakṣaṇaḥ adoṣaḥ doṣaḥ na bhavati na hi sāmānyam rūpa ādiḥ iva bhāva rūpa tayā jñāna viṣayaḥ iti bhāva dharmaḥ iṣṭam meyam tu ekam sva lakṣaṇām kintu bhāva vāsanā prabodha prasūta vikalpa kalpita tvāt paramārthataḥ meyam tu ekam tasya eva rūpa buddhi utpādaka tvāt 
PVV_2.54,0–2.54,4	 tasmāt artha kriyā siddheḥ sat asat tā vicāraṇāt sāmānyasya tu kalpita tvāt sāmarthya abhāvāt svalakṣaṇam ekam prameyam tasmāda artha kriyā arthibhiḥ sat asat tābhyām tasya eva vicāraṇāt asattvam api sva lakṣaṇasya eva vicintyate yadi ekam eva prameyam tad ācāryeṇa prameya dvaividhyam yat uktam na sva sāmānya lakṣaṇābhyām anyat prameyam asti iti tat virudhyate iti āha tasya sva para rūpābhyām gateḥ meya dvayam matam tasya sva lakṣaṇasya pratyakṣatas sva rūpeṇa anumānataḥ para rūpeṇa sāmānya ākāreṇa gateḥ meya dvayam matam na tu bhūta sāmānyasya sattvāt 
PVV_2.55,0–2.55,3	 ayathā abhiniveśena dvitīyā bhrāntiḥ iṣyate yā ca dvitīyā para rūpeṇa gatiḥ ayatha abhiniveśena bhrāntiḥ iṣyate sā anumānam yathā artha usti yathā vā su a ākāraḥ tathā na abhiniviśate kintu su a ākāram bāhyam sādhāraṇa tayā manyate gatiḥ ced para rūpeṇa na ca bhrānteḥ pramāṇatā nanu anumānam para rūpeṇa gatiḥ ced tadā bhrāntiḥ eva na ca bhrānteḥ pramāṇatā iṣyate mṛgatṛṣṇā ādeḥ iva 
PVV_2.56,0–2.56,6	 atra ucyate abhiprāya avi saṃvādāt api bhrānteḥ pramāṇatā gatiḥ api anyathā dṛṣṭāḥ bhrānteḥ api pramāṇa tā abhiprāyasya artha kriyā arthibhiḥ jñāna gocara tayā abhiprāya viṣayīkṛtasya artha kriyā samarthasya arthasya saṃvādāt artha kriyā arthinaḥ hi tad sādhana samartha artha prāpakam pramāṇam icchanti anyathā para rūpeṇa gatiḥ api kācid abhipreta artha samvādikā dṛṣṭā iti pramāṇam eva nanu anumānam vastu eva gṛhṇat pramāṇam astu kim bhrāntiḥ iṣyate iti āha pakṣaḥ ca ayam kṛta uttaraḥ pakṣaḥ ca ayam prāk eva na tat vastu abhidheya tvāt ityādinā kṛta uttaraḥ 
PVV_2.57,0–2.57,2	 nanu bhrāntam api yadi anumānam pramāṇam tadā sarvvā eva bhrāntiḥ pramāṇam syāt iti āha maṇi pradīpa prabhayoḥ maṇi buddhyā abhidhāvatoḥ mithyājñāna aviśeṣepi viśeṣa urtha kriyām prāti maṇi pradīpayoḥ ye prabhe tayoḥ maṇi buddhyā maṇiḥ eva ayam iti adhyavasāyena tad grahaṇa artham dhāvataḥ mithyājñānasya bhrānta tvasya aviśeṣepi viśeṣaḥ artha kriyām prati maṇi prabhāyāṃm api adhyavasāyī maṇi sādhyām artha kriyām prāpnoti

PVV_2.59–2.60,3–2.59–2.60,5	 kathantat pratyetavyam iti āha tasya adṛṣṭa ātma rūpasya gateḥ anyorthaḥ āśrayaḥ tad āśrayeṇa sambandhī yadi syāt gamakaḥ tadā tasya sāmānyasya sva lakṣaṇa viśeṣeṇa sva lakṣaṇa vivekena adṛṣṭa ātma rūpasya gateḥ pratīteḥ tasmāt anyaḥ arthaḥ liṅga bhūtaḥ āśrayaḥ siddhi nimittam yadi tatas pratyetavyena anagni vyavaccheda ādinā tad āśrayeṇa ca dharmiṇā sambandhī sambandhavān syāt tadā na anyathā anane sādhya pratibandhaḥ anvaya vyatireka rūpaḥ pakṣa dharma tā ca liṅgasya uktā

PVV_2.103,0–2.103,1	 sāmānya āśraya saṃsiddhau sāmānyam siddham eva tat tad asiddhau tathā asya eva hi anumānam pravartate tasmāt sāmānyasya anitya ādeḥ āśrayasya varṇṇa ādeḥ pratyakṣāt saṃsiddhau siddham eva yadi tu abhyāsa ādi abhāvāt anurūpa niścaya abhāvāt ajñānam tadā pratyakṣāt tat asiddhau= asya eva hi varṇṇa ādeḥ tathā nitya tvena tat avyabhicāri liṅgadanu mānam pravartate 
PVV_2.104,0–2.104,2	 kasmāt punar gṛhītepya parijñānam iti āha kvacid tad aparijñānam sadṛśa apara sambhavāt bhrānteḥ apaśyataḥ bhedam māyā golaka bheda vat kvacid anitya tā ādau gṛhītā ipi anurūpa niścaya abhāvāt aparijñānam pūrvvakṣaṇa vināśa kāle tad sadṛśasya aparasya sambhavāt bhāva śūnya antarā lakṣaṇa abhāvāt saḥ eva ayam iti bhrānteḥ sthairya grāhiṇyāḥ kṣaṇānām bhedam a aniścicanvataḥ puṃsaḥ dṛṣṭāntam āha māyā golaka bheda vat māyākāra darśitau golakau bhinnau= adhyakṣeṇa gṛhītvā api sādṛśyāt lāghavāt ca vipralabdha buddhiḥ eka tvena adhyavasyati yathā tathā sthira adhyavasāyaḥ 
PVV_2.105,0–2.105,2	 nanu yadi kvacid nāśaḥ dṛśyeṃta tadā asya ahetukasya svabhāva tvāt kṣaṇa kṣayiṣu bhāveṣu ekatā buddheḥ bhrānta tvam bhavet iti āha tathā hi aliṅgam ābālam asaṃśliṣṭa uttara udayam paśyan paricchinatti eva dīpa ādim nāśinam janaḥ tathā hi dīpa ādi ādi śabdāt turaṅga disantāna viccheda kāle asaṃśliṣṭa uttara udayam aghaṭitaḥ uttarasya udayaḥ janma yasmin tam ekasya svarasa nirodhi tve aparasya kāraṇa abhāvāt anutpattau nāśinam adhyakṣataḥ paśyan= aliṅgaṅgama kaliṅga rahitam ābālam bāla paryantam janaḥ paricchinatti eva tatas prāk api sataḥ svarasa nirodhāt sadṛśa apara aparakṣaṇa pracaye saḥ eva ayam iti buddhi bhrāntiḥ eva 
PVV_2.106,0–2.106,2	 yathā bhāva svabhāva bhūtāyām api śaktau phale adṛśaḥ anānantaryatas mohaḥ viniścetuḥ apāṭavāt bhāvasya bīja ādeḥ svabhāva bhūtāyām api aṅkura ādi janikāyām śaktau phale a ṅkura ādau adarśanāt viniścetuḥ punsaḥ apāṭavāt mohaḥ aśakta bhramaḥ tathā kṣaṇikeṣu bhāveṣu sadṛśa apara apara utpatteḥ bhāva śūni akṣaṇā darśanāt ca sthira bhramaḥ 
PVV_2.107,0–2.107,1	 tasya eva vinivṛti artham anumāna upavarṇanam vyavasyanti īkṣaṇāt eva sarva ākārān mahā ādhiyaḥ tasya ekatva bhramasya eva nivṛtti artha samvādi liṅga jasya kṣaṇika tā viṣayasya anumānasya upavarṇṇanam niścaya āropa manasā urbbādhya bādhaka bhāvataḥ iti nyāyāt ye tumahā dhiyaḥ viparīta vyavasāya anākrānta pratyakṣāḥ yoginaḥ te padārthasya īkṣaṇāt eva niścinvanti

PVV_2.109,0–2.109,1	 yathā codanam ākhyāḥ ca saḥ asati bhrānti kāraṇe pratibhāḥ pratisandhatte sva anurūpāḥ svabhāvataḥ yathā ācaḥ yathā saṃketam ākhyāḥ śabdāḥ ca pravartante yatra vyāvṛttau yaḥ śabdaḥ viniveśitaḥ sa ca tasyām niścitāyām pravartate sa bhāvaḥ asati bhrānti kāraṇe yathābhyāsam sva anurūpāḥ sva vyāvṛtti samucitāḥ pratibhā niścaya buddhīḥ svabhāvataḥ pratisaṃdhatte utpādayati tasmāt abhyāsavatām īkṣaṇā devān ityādi niścayaḥ anyeṣāntu sthira āropaṇa artham anumānam iti sthitam etat

PVV_2.111,0–2.111,2	 nanu prāk paścāt abhāvayoḥ vyavadhāyakaḥ sattā sambandhaḥ anitya tā na pradhvaṃsa abhāvaḥ iti āha yasya ubhayānta vyavadhi sattā sambandha vācinī anitya tā śrutiḥ tena tāvantau= iti kau smṛtau yasya nai yā yi kā deru bhayasya prāk paścāt abhāvasya antarasya yaḥ vyavadhāyakaḥ sattā sambandhaḥ tad vācinī anityatā śrutiḥ iṣṭā tena vādinā tāvantau= iti kausmṛtau 
PVV_2.112,0–2.112,1	 prāk paścāt api abhāvaḥ ced saḥ eva anitya tā na kim ṣaṣṭhī ādyayogāt iti ced antayoḥ sa katham bhavet prāgbhāvaḥ paścāt abhāvopi ced saḥ eva prāc abhāvaḥ paścāt abhāvaḥ anitya tā kinneṣyate sattā viśeṣaṇa tvena api tad abhyupagamasya iṣṭa tvāt paṭasya ghaṭe ca abhāvaḥ iti ṣaṣṭi ādi vibhakti ayogāt pradhvaṃsa abhāvaḥ na anitya tā na hi bhāva abhāvayoḥ saṃyoga ādiḥ kaścid sambandha usti yaḥ ucyeta ṣaṣṭi ādibhiḥ iti ced evantarhi antayoḥ sa ṣaṣṭi ādi yogaḥ katham bhavet abhāvayoḥ vyavadhi bhūtā sattā ityādi 
PVV_2.113,0–2.113,4	 kiñca sattā sambandhayoḥ dhrauvyāt antābhyām na viśeṣaṇam sattā tad sambandhe para mate dhrauvyādantābhyām prāc pradhvaṃsa abhāvābhyām na viśeṣaṇam syāt anta dvaya viśiṣṭā sattā tad sambandhaḥ vā iti na hi niṃtyasya sarva kāla vyāpinaḥ anta sambhavaḥ aviśeṣaṇam eva syāt antau ced kārya kāraṇe kārya kāraṇe antau= abhimate iti ced tadā tābhyām sattā sambandhayoḥ aviśeṣaṇa 
PVV_2.114,0–2.114,1	 asambandhāt na bhāvasya prāgabhāvam sa vā aṃchati tad upādhi samākhyāne tepyasya ca na sidhyataḥ yasmāt sa nai yā yi kā dirbhauvasya asambandhāt prāgabhāvam sambandhinam na vāñchati tathā ca tad upādhi samākhyāne prāc abhāva viśeṣaṇam kārya kāraṇam iti samākhyānam vyapadeśaḥ yayoḥ te tathā te kārya kāraṇepyasya na sidhyataḥ yasya hi prāc abhāvaḥ sa bhavan kāryam syāt na ca tad sambandhaḥ bhāvasya iti kārya abhāvaḥ kārya abhāvāt ca kāraṇa abhāvaḥ tad utpādakasya kāraṇa tvāt

PVV_2.120–2.121,0–2.120–2.121,4	 vismṛta tvāt adoṣaḥ ced tatas eva anidarśanam dṛṣṭe tad bhāva siddhiḥ ced pramāṇāt na aprasiddhaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ sa ced siddhaḥ kim anumānena gṛhītasya api vismṛta tvāt punar anumāna pratīta avadoṣaḥ ced tatas vismṛta tvāt eva anidarśanam na hi gṛhīta vismṛtasya dṛṣṭānta tā pūrvva pratyayena dṛṣṭe artha pramāṇāt viśeṣa dṛṣṭa anumāna ādyaḥ eva prāk dṛṣṭaḥ saḥ eva ayam iti tad bhāvasya pūrvvasya siddhiḥ ced iṣyate nanu ayam tad bhāvaḥ kim anya vastuni sādhyate uta tatra eva anya vastuni tattva ārope viparyāsaḥ tad siddha repramāṇa tā pratyakṣa itarayoḥ aikyāt eka siddhiḥ dvayoḥ api 
PVV_2.120–2.121,5	 tatra anya vastuni vartamāne tattvasya atīta vastu ātmakasya ārope svīkriyamāṇe viparyāsaḥ ayathārtha tvam syāt na hi anyasya ani ātma tvam asti tad aśakya prāpaṇam upadarśayat apramāṇam syāt atha tatra eva tad bhāva siddhiḥ iti dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ tadā tad siddheḥ eka siddheḥ vviśeṣa dṛṣṭasya anumānasya apramāṇa tā gṛhīta grāhi tvāt na hi ekasya nirbhāgasya kiñcid agṛhītam nāma tathā hi pratyakṣa itarayoḥ adhyakṣa anumāna viṣaya yauḥ aikyāt dvayoḥ api pratyakṣe anumāne ca ekasya arthasya siddhiḥ 
PVV_2.122,0–2.122,2	 tatas ca dṛṣṭānta grāhiṇā eva abhraṣṭa smṛti saṃskāreṇa pratyakṣeṇa siddha tvāt viphalam anumānam pratyakṣa saṃskāra bhraṃśe tu na adṛṣṭāntam anumānam asti tasmāt sandhīyamānam ca anyena vyavasāyam smṛtim viduḥ tad liṅga apekṣaṇāt no ced smṛtiḥ na vyabhicārataḥ anyena atīta darśanena eka viṣaya tayā sandhīya mānam ghaṭyamānam param vyavasāyaṃsmṛtim viduḥ u vidvāṃsaḥ gṛhīta artha vikalpena smṛti tvam tat ca iha avikalam tasya pratipattavyasya cihnam avyabhicāri liṅgam ntad apekṣaṇāt nocet viśeṣa dṛṣṭam anumānam smṛtiḥ sā tu liṅga nirapekṣyāḥ na etat yuktaṃvyabhicāra tas tathā hi yadi liṅgantri rūpanta dā vyāpti grahaṇa viṣaya tvena eva tad siddheḥ vyartham anumānam atha na trirūpanta dāḥ nāvya bhicāra niścayaḥ tasmāt viśeṣa dṛṣṭasya apramāṇa tvāt ekatra aneka vṛtteḥ api tri eka saṃkhyā apohana abhāvaḥ nirastaḥ tasmāt sthitam etat mānam dvividham meya dvaividhyāt iti 
PVV_2.123,0–2.123,2	 idānīm avasara prāptām pratyakṣasya lakṣaṇa vipratipattim nirākarttum āha pratyakṣam kalpanā apoḍham pratyakṣeṇa eva sidhyati pratyātma vedyaḥ sarveṣām vikalpaḥ nāma saṃśrayaḥ yat tat pratyakṣam iti prasiddhaṃtat kalpanāyāḥ apoḍham draṣṭavyam kalpanā artha rahitam iti arthaḥ tat ca etat īdṛśam pratyakṣeṇa eva sva samvedanena eva sidhyati kalpanā rahitasya arthasya rūpasya samvedanasya aparokṣa tvāt yadi tu kalpanā svabhāva tvam asya syāt tathā eva prakāśeta vikalpasya aparokṣa tvāt tathā hi pratyātma vedyaḥ sarvu eṣām prāṇinām vikalpaḥ nāma śabda saṃsargavān sa yadi syāt upalabhya eva bhavet 
PVV_2.124,0–2.125,2	 tasmāt saṃhṛtya sarvatas cintām stimitena antarātmanā sthitopi cakṣuṣā rūpam īkṣate sākṣa jā matiḥ saṃhṛtya ākṛṣya sarvvatas vikalpanīyāt cintām stimitena sarvva avikalpa vigamāt adhikṣiptena antarātmanā cetasā sthitaḥ api puruṣaḥ cakṣuḥ vvijñānena rūpa jā nirvvikalpā matiḥ sarva samviditā eva santi eva indriya dhiyaḥ kalpanāḥ tāḥ tu na upalabhyante iti api asat tathā hi punar vikalpayan kiñcid āsīt me kalpanā īdṛśī vetti ca iti na pūrvva ukta avasthāyām indriyāt gatau vikalpa avasthāyāḥ ūrdhvam punar vvikalpayan pumān āsīt me kalpanedṛśī iti vā iti na indrit pannāyām gatau buddhau saṃhṛtya ityādinā pūrvvamukta avasthāḥ yasyāḥ tasyāḥ kalpanām vā iti yadi sā tatra syāt atad saṃskārasya smṛtiḥ jāyate tasmāt na asti iti niścīyate

PVV_2.154,0–2.154,4	 syāt etat viśiṣṭa pratītiḥ vviśeṣaṇa pratīti pūrvvikā yathā daṇḍi pratītiḥ viśiṣṭa pratītiḥ ca śāvaleya ādiṣu gauḥ iti viśeṣaṇañca śāvaleya ādiṣu go tvam eva iti anumānataḥ jāti siddhiḥ iti āha anumānañca jāti ādau vastunaḥ na asti bhedini anumānam vastunaḥ śābaleya ādeḥ bhedini jāti ādau na asti na hi vyakti vyatiriktam viśeṣaṇam upalabhyate śṛṅga ādi ava yava sanniveśaḥ eva tu abhinnaḥ viśeṣaṇam astu tathā ca nābhimata siddhiḥ dṛṣṭānta asiddhim api āha sarvu atra vyapadeśaḥ hi daṇḍa ādeḥ api sāṃvṛtāt 
PVV_2.154,5	 sarvu atra puruṣa ādau daṇḍī ityādi vyapadeśa upi hi na daṇḍa ādeḥ vvastunaḥ kintu sāṃvṛtāt daṇḍa sva lakṣaṇasya vyupadeśe hetu tve sarvu atra puruṣe syāt sambandhini eva anyatra iti ced tarhi sambandhaḥ daṇḍaḥ kāraṇam daṇḍi vyapadeśasya sambandhaḥ ca saṃyoga ādiḥ na asti iti param kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ pariśiṣyate tasya nimitta tve yathā daṇḍī puruṣaḥ tathā puruṣī daṇḍaḥ iti api syāt samāna tvāt nimittasya tasmāt kalpita viśeṣaṇa bhāva niyamaḥ daṇḍaḥ sambandhī sāṃvṛtaḥ eva viśeṣaṇam

PVV_2.157,0–2.157,3	 kiñca mālā ādau ca mahatva ādiḥ iṣṭaḥ yaḥ ca aupacārikaḥ mukhyā viśiṣṭa vijñāna grāhya tvāt na aupacārikaḥ mahatī prāsāda mālā iti katham vyapadeśaḥ mahatvam parimāṇam guṇaḥ tasya mālāyām na sattvam na hi prāsāda mālā kiñcid iti uktam na api saṃyoga lakṣaṇe prāsāde mahat tvam nirguṇa tvā guṇānām kāṣṭha ādiṣu dravyeṣu prāsāda ārambhakeṣu mahattva sattvāt vṛkṣeṣu kusuma sambhavāt vana saṃkhyā lakṣaṇam kusumitam iti yathā ucyate tathā prāsāda mālā yaḥ ca iṣṭaḥ sa ca ayuktaḥ kāṣṭha ādiṣu api tādṛśasya mahattvasya abhāvāt kiñca mahān parvvataḥ iti mukhya mahat tva grāhaka jñānena askhalat vṛtti tvāt aviśiṣṭena jñānena grāhya tvāt prāsāda mālā maha tva ādiḥ aupacārikaḥ na yuktaḥ na hi māṇavakaḥ iva siṃha buddhiḥ mahat tva buddhiḥ ca mālāyām skhalati

PVV_2.228–2.229,0–2.228–2.229,3^1	 kiñca svatas vastu antarā bhedāt guṇa ādeḥ bhedakasya ca agrahāt eka buddhiḥ syāt paśyatā upi para aparam guṇa ādi bheda grahaṇāt nānātva pratipad yadi astu nāma tathā api eṣām bhavet sambandhi saṃkaraḥ vastunaḥ svatas vastu antarāt bheda abhāvāt vadanti hi svatas hi na gauḥ nāgaurggo tva yogāt gauḥ tathā svatas hi śuklaḥ na aśuklaḥ śukla tva yogāt śuklaḥ ityādi bhedakasya ca guṇa ādeḥ agrahāt padārthaiḥ saha tatas ca parāparam artha jātam paśya padārtha tva buddhiḥ syāt na hi dravyāṇām anyonyasya bhedakāḥ guṇa jāti ādayaḥ taiḥ saha gṛhyante yena bheda buddhiḥ syāt dravye gṛhīte paścāt guṇa ādīnām bhedānām viśeṣāṇām nānā tva grahaṇam dravyāṇām yadi iṣyate astu nāma paścāt guṇa ādi grahaṇam tathā api eṣām guṇa karmma sāmāni ādīnām sambandhinaḥ sāṃkaryam syāt svatas hi dravyam bhedāt na upalabhyate 
PVV_2.228–2.229,3^2	 paścāt upalabhyamānaiḥ tu guṇa ādibhiḥ saṃbandhi tayā avagataiḥ bhedena tat vyavasthāpanīyam tatas ca ekatra eka dravye guṇa ādayaḥ sambandhi tayā pratīyeran bhinna deśānām guṇānām bhinna deśeṣu yojanāt na sambandhi sāṃkaryam iti ced na deśa bhedasya api viśeṣaṇa tvāt sa upyekasya iti syāt ekasya viruddha dharma ayogāt pratīyamāna arthāḥ paścāt pratīyamānairūpa ādhibhiḥ bhinnāḥ vyavasthāpyante iti ced nanu evam api svatas arthānām bheda abhāvāt bheda nibandhanaiḥ ca upādhibhiḥ saha vedanā bhāvāt na adhyakṣa siddhā bheda vyavasthitiḥ syāt kintu viruddha upādhi sambandhāni atha anupapattyā kalpanīyāḥ tathā ca pratyakṣa virodhaḥ 
PVV_2.228–2.229,4	 atha dṛṣṭerthe paścāttanam adhyakṣam upādhi grāhakam tān yojayet bheda grāhakam katham adṛśyamāne yojana upādhīnām pratyakṣa kṛtāḥ vikalpa kṛtā eva tu syāt tathā ca vyaktam na bheda darśanam syāt vikalpa viṣayasya asphuṭa tvāt ṛṣṭe arthe paścāt upādhiḥ pratīyamānaḥ tasya eva dṛṣṭaḥ iti ced tasya iti kim ucyate na tāvat anekāsu upādhi grahaṇāt pūrvvam aneka tvasya apratīteḥ ekam ced katham upādhibhiḥ bhedanīyam anavadhṛta eka aneka bhāvam vastu mātram tat iti ced tatra tarhi deśa bhedāt aya upi upādhayaḥ paścāt upalabhyamānāḥ yojyante tad anantaram dṛṣṭa tvāt tatas ca anivāryaḥ sambandhi saṃkara prasaṅgaḥ 
PVV_2.230,0–2.231,2	 sām khya matepi śabda ādīnām aneka tvāt siddhoneka grahaḥ sakṛt sanniveśa graha ayogāt agrahe sanniveśinām śabda ādīnām sukha duḥkha moha ātmaka tayā aneka tvāt śabda ādi grahe sakṛt aneka grahaḥ na hi aṅguli agrahaṇe muṣṭi grahaṇam yadi pratyakṣam avikalpam tadā katham dharmma dharmmyādi grahaṇam iti āha sarvatas vinivṛttasya vinivṛttiḥ yatas yatas tat bheda unnīta bhedā sā dharmmiṇaḥ aneka rūpa tā sarvvataḥ parasmāt vinivṛttasya arthasya yatas yatas parasmāt vinivṛttaḥ taiḥ bhedaiḥ vyāvṛttibhiḥ unnītā sā aneka rūpa tā dharmmi dharmma ātmaka tayā dharmmiṇaḥ arthasya sarvvaṃtaḥ vyāvṛtte pratyakṣeṇa gṛhīte vastuni tad vyāvṛtti anukāriṇaḥ vikalpāḥ pratyakṣa dṛṣṭa tvena dharmmi dharmma bhāvam vyavasthāpayanti iti pratyakṣa kṛtaḥ saḥ ucyate na tu pratyakṣa pratibhāsamāna tvāt 
PVV_2.232,0–2.232,2	 tathā hi te kalpitāḥ rūpa bhedāt nirvvikalpasya cetasaḥ na vicitrasya citra ābhāḥ kādācid kasya gocaraḥ te dharmi dharma ādayaḥ rūpa bhedāt buddhi ākāra viśeṣā vijātīya vyāvṛtti āśrayeṇa kalpitā vicitra ābhāḥ vastu bala bhāvi tvāt kādācid kasya vicitrasya dharmmi dharmma bheda pratibhāsa rahitasya nirvvikalpasya cetasaḥ pratyakṣasya na gocaraḥ pratyakṣam hi vastu sāmarthya utpannam tad ākāram anukuryāt na vikalpitam 
PVV_2.233,0–2.233,2	 bhavatu vā vastu eva sāmānyam tathā api na asau śabda vikalpa viṣayaḥ iti āha yadi api asti sita tva ādi yādṛś indriya gocaraḥ na sobhidhīyate śabdaiḥ jñānayoḥ rūpa bhedataḥ yadi api sita tva ādi sāmānyam asti paṭa ādau dharmmiṇi yādṛś sita tva ādi viśat ākāraḥ indriyasya gocaraḥ saḥ indriya jñāna gocaraḥ arthaḥ abhidhīyate na śabdaiḥ jñānayoḥ indriya śabda janitayaḥ rūpasya ākārasya sphuṭa asphuṭa tvena bhedataḥ

PVV_2.236,0–2.236,2	 yat api ucyate paraiḥ śābda indriya jñānayoḥ yādi na eka viṣaya tvam tadā viṣāṇa ādimantam artham gauḥ iti śabdāt pratītya kāla antare vyakti viśeṣam dṛṣṭavataḥ ayam asau śabdāt prāk mayā pratītaḥ gauḥ iti pratyabhijñānam eka tā adhya vasāyi yat utpadyate tat na syāt iti tatra āha vṛtteḥ dṛśya aparāmarśena abhidhāna vikalpayoḥ darśanāt pratyabhijñānam gavā ādīnām nivāritam abhidhāna vikalpayoḥ dṛ śyasya adhyakṣa viṣayasya aparāmarśena viṣayīkaraṇena vṛtteḥ paścāt darśanāt saḥ eva ayam śabda nirdiṣṭaḥ gauḥ iti pratya bhijñānam gavā ādīnām yat iṣyate tat nivāritam boddhavyam indriya śabda jñānayoḥ bhinna ākāra tvena eva viṣayat tva abhāvāt katham tad eka tā vyavasāyi vastu viṣayam syāt 
PVV_2.237,0–2.237,1	 anvayāt ca anumānam yat abhidhāna vikalpayoḥ dṛśye gavā ādau jāti ādeḥ tat api etena dūṣitam yat ca dṛśye gavā ādau= aneka tra abhinna ākārayoḥ abhidhāna vikalpayoḥ anvayāt anuvṛttena abhidhāna vikalpayoḥ dṛśya tva aparāmarśena hetunā dūṣitam boddhavyam na hi anvayinau= api śabda vikalpau vastu spṛśataḥ tat katham tābhyām vastunaḥ sāmānyasya siddhiḥ 
PVV_2.238,0–2.238,3	 yadi na asti sāmānyam tathā katham astu pratyabhijñānam iti āha darśanāni eva bhinnāni api ekām kurvanti kalpanām pratyabhijñāna saṃkhyātām svabhāvena iti varṇitam darśanāni indriya jñānāni eva bhinnāni nānā akṣaṇa viṣayāṇi anekāni api svabhāvena pratyabhijñāna kāraṇa svarūpeṇa sva kāraṇa prasūtena kalpanā ātmeka tva adhyavasāyinīm pratya pratyabhijñāna nāmnā prasiddhām kurvanti iti varṇṇitam prāk tasmāt sthitam etat pratyakṣam anirdeśya tvāt avikalpam iti uktam indriya pratyakṣam  
PVV_2.239,0–2.239,2	 mānasam ākhyātum āha tat ca indriya jñāna anantaram iṣṭam tena saha eka viṣayam bhinna viṣayam vā syāt ubhayathā api tu doṣaḥ iti āha pūrvva anubhūta grahaṇe mānasasya apramāṇa tā adṛṣṭa grahaṇa indha ādeḥ api syāt artha darśanam pūrvva anubhūtasya indriya jñāna gṛhītasya grahaṇe mānasasya svīkriyamāṇe apramāṇa tā syāt ajñāta artha prakāśasya pramāṇa tvāt indriya jñāna adṛṣṭasya grahaṇe punar iṣyamāṇe andha ādeḥ api syāt arthasya rūpa ādeḥ darśanam 
PVV_2.240,0–2.240,2	 indriya jñāna anubhūta viṣaya tvepi dvau vikalpau saḥ arthaḥ kṣaṇikaḥ na vā kṣaṇika tvāt atītasya darśane ca na sambhavaḥ vācya makṣaṇika tve syāt lakṣaṇam sa viśeṣaṇam prathama pakṣaḥ indriya jñāna viṣayasya arthasya pūrvva kālasya saha bhuvaḥ vā kṣaṇika naṣṭasya mānasena darśane darśanasya ca na sambhavosti akṣaṇika tve vai adhigata artha adhigantṛ tvādapramāṇam syāt atha mānasam adhigata artha adhigantṛ pramāṇam iṣyate tadā api mānasasya sa viśeṣaṇam lakṣaṇam vācyam syāt yathā adhigata viṣaya tvepi kalpanā apoḍham abhrānta mānasam pratyakṣam iti

PVV_2.404–2.405,0–2.404–2.405,3	 atha tādṛśam vastu eva utpannam dṛśyate iti na jñāna ākāraḥ iti āha tasya tad bāhya rūpa tve kā prasanna īkṣaṇe akṣamā bhūtam paśyan= ca tad darśī kathañca upahata indriyaḥ śodhitam timireṇa asya vyaktam cakṣuḥ atīndriyam paśyataḥ anyākṣa dṛśya irthe tat avyaktam katham punar tasya maṇḍalasya tad bāhya rūpa tve abhyupagamyamāne prasanna īkṣaṇe draṣṭari kā akṣamā dveṣaḥ yena asmai na ātmānam upadarśayet yat vastupahata indriyeṇa dṛśyate tad anupahata indriyeṇa sutarām dṛśyate bhūtam satyam ca paśyan tad darśī maṇḍaladarśī katham upahata indriyaiḥ aparaiḥ adṛśyam maṇḍalam paśyataḥ asya manda cakṣuṣṭvena naṣṭasya timireṇa vyaktam cakṣuḥ śodhitam iti upahasati kintu taimirikasya atīndriya artha darśana kṣamam tat cakṣuḥ anyasya ataimirikasya akṣa dṛśye arthe pradīpe katham punar avyaktam asphuṭam yat atīndriyam paśyati tat sarvvam dṛśyam sutarām paśyati

PVV_iii.0,0–3.1,2	 pratyakṣam ākhyāya avasara prāptam anumānam idānīm vaktavyam tat ca dvividham sva artham parārthañca tatra sva artham idānīm vaktavyam etat pūrvaka tvāt para arthasya tad liṅge vipratipattayaḥ santi iti tāsām nirākaraṇena tad vyavasthāpana artham āha pakṣa dharmaḥ tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ hetuḥ pakṣaḥ dharmi dharma samudāya unumeyaḥ tad eka deśa tvāt upacāreṇa dharmī pakṣaḥ uktaḥ tasya dharmaḥ anena pakṣa dharma tvam uktam dharmi dharmaḥ hetuḥ iti anumāne saru u asya dharmmi dharmmaḥ hetuḥ syāt iti upacāra āśrayaṇam tathā cākṣuṣa tva ādiḥ śabde dharmiṇi na hetuḥ tad aṃśena pakṣasya dharmeṇa sisā dhayiṣitena vyāptaḥ hetuḥ boddhavyaḥ dvividhā ca iyam vyāptiḥ vyāpaka vyāpya dharma tayā tatra vyāpye sati vyāpakasya avaśyambhāvaḥ tasya vyāptiḥ vyāpyasya ca vyāpakaḥ eva sati bhāvaḥ nāma tasya vyāptiḥ ābhyām yathākramam anvaya vyatirekau= uktau vyāpya sadbhāve vyāpakasya satva niyamasya anvaya rūpa tvāt vyāpaka abhāve vyāpya abhāvasya ca vyatireka rūpa tvāt 
PVV_3.1,3–3.1,10	 tridhā eva saḥ tridhā eva tri prakāraḥ eva kārya svabhāva anupalambha bhedena sa hetuḥ yathā agniḥ atra dhamāt vṛkṣa vyavahāra yogyoyam śiṃśapā tvāt na iha pradeśe ghaṭaḥ upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdheḥ iti saṃkhyā niyamaḥ uktaḥ kasmāt punar trividhaḥ eva hetuḥ iti āha avinā abhau= a niyamāt avinā abhā= asya sādhya avyabhicāri tvasya trividhaḥ eva hetau niyamāt niyata tvāt saṃyogi ādiṣu ca abhāvāt sati eva avinā abhāve hetu tvam sa ca vyāptyā kathitaḥ anena saṃkhyā niyama kāraṇam uktam hetavaḥ uktāḥ ke punar hetvābhāsāḥ iti āha hetvābhāsāḥ tatas apare hetu vat ābhāsantaḥ iti hetvābhāsāḥ hetu pratirūpakāḥ tatas trividhāt hetoḥ apare anye saṃyogi ādayaḥ avinā abhāve sati hetu tvam sa ca tādātmyāt tad utpatteḥ ca ye tu tad vikalāḥ te avinā abhāva virahāt hetvābhāsāḥ iti arthaḥ 
PVV_3.2aba,0–3.2aba,2	 yadi tad utpattyā gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ tadā dhūma tva viśeṣa vat sāmānya dharmāḥ pārthiva tvādayopi gamakāḥ syuḥ tathā agneḥ sāmānya dharma vat cāndana tvāt ayopi viśeṣa dharmma agamyāḥ syuḥ sarvu athā kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt iti āha kāryam svabhāvaiḥ yāvadbhiḥ avinābhāvi kārya vat kārya svabhāvaiḥ yāvadbhiḥ vviśiṣṭaiḥ ddhūmavatu a ādibhiḥ avinābhāvi vinā na bhavati iti kāraṇe kāraṇa viṣaye avadhāritam taiḥ eva viśiṣṭaiḥ svabhāvaiḥ hetuḥ na sādhāraṇaiḥ pārthiva tva ādibhiḥ agnim antareṇa api teṣām bhāvāt tathā kāraṇe adhikaraṇe yāvadbhiḥ svabhāvaiḥ agni tva ādibhiḥ sāmānya dharmaiḥ avinā bhāvi kārya dhūma ādi niścitam teṣām sāmanya dharmāṇām hetuḥ na viśeṣa dharmāṇām ca andana tva ādīnām tāni antareṇa api dhūma ādeḥ darśanāt yadi dhūma tva viśeṣitam pārthiva tvam hetuḥ kriyate tadā iṣṭam eva vyabhicāra abhāvāt yadi ca kāraṇa gata cāndana tva ādi viśeṣa janitaḥ dhūmasya viśeṣaḥ śakyaḥ niścetum tadā ca andana tva ādayaḥ gamyāḥ iṣyante na hi kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ sattā mātreṇa gabhya gamaka bhāva nimittam kintu niścaya apekṣaḥ sa ca yāvat niścīyate tathā agamya gamaka bhāvaḥ 
PVV_3.2aba,3	 bhāvopi svabhāvopi hetuḥ svabhāve sādhye kīdṛśe hetoḥ bhāvaḥ kevalaḥ bhāva mātram tat anuroddhum anuvarttitum śīlam asya iti bhāva mātra anurodha tasmin yasya sattā mātreṇa yaḥ dharmaḥ avaśyam bhavati na hetu antaram apekṣate tasmin sādhye svabhāva ākhyaḥ hetuḥ na anyatra yathā vastra tvam rāge evañca vidhi sādhana tvam kārya svabhāvayoḥ darśitam 
PVV_3.2cada,0–3.2cada,5	 idānīm tṛtīya hetoḥ pratiṣedha phala tvam āha apravṛttiḥ pramāṇānām pramāṇa nivṛtti rūpā anupalabdhiḥ asati sat vyavahāra atikrānta tvāt asat aviśiṣṭe deśa kāla svabhāva viprakṛṣṭe sumeru u ādau sat jñāna śabda vyavahārāṇām pravṛtti pratiṣedhaḥ apravṛttiḥ tad phalāḥ etat ca apravṛtti phala tvam dṛśya adṛśya anupalabdhyoḥ sādhāraṇaṃjñāna pūrvaka tvāt sat jñāna śabda vyavahārasya jñāna abhāve tad abhāvasya nyāya prāpta tvāt dṛśya anupalabdheḥ phala antaram āha kācid pramāṇa nivṛttiḥ asat jñānam abhāva jñānam tad phalāḥ katham iti āha hetu bheda vyapekṣayā hetuḥ anupalambhaḥ tasya bhedaḥ viśeṣaṇam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta viṣaya tvam tasya vyapekṣayā kāṃkṣayā upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta anupalabdhiḥ iti arthaḥ 
PVV_3.2cada,6	 nanu yadi anupalabdhyā abhāvaḥ sādhyate tadā upalabdhi abhāvopi tatas eva iti anavasthānāt abhāva apratipattiḥ syāt dṛṣṭāntaḥ ca na syāt anyasya abhāva sādhanasya abhāvāt anupalabdheḥ ca anavasthā prāpta tvāt atha padārtha antara upalabdhiḥ eva anupalabdhiḥ tayā adhyakṣa siddhyā abhāvaḥ sādhyate tasmāt na doṣaḥ yadi evam artha antarāt api kinnābhāvaḥ sādhyate tat api hi anupalabdhi rūpam pratyakṣa siddhañca kaḥ vā anya upalambha abhāvena sambandhaḥ 
PVV_3.2cada,7–3.2cada,9	 ucyate eka jñāna saṃsarggi vastu antaram tad upalabdhiḥ ca anupalabdhiḥ vvivakṣita upalabdheḥ anya tvāt abhakṣā sparśanīya vat saḥ eva abhāvaḥ tad atiriktasya vigrahavataḥ abhāvasya abhāvāt tasmāt tādātmyam abhāva anupalambhayoḥ sambandhaḥ evam tarhi anupalabdhi siddhiḥ eva abhāva siddhiḥ kim sādhyate satyam na abhāvaḥ sādhyaḥ siddha tvāt asya kintarhi viṣaya upadarśanena viṣayī vyavahāraḥ sādhyate yathā go vyavahāra viṣayaḥ ayam sāsna ādi samudāya ātmaka tvāt 
PVV_3.3,0–3.3,2	 sā ca prayoga bhedāt anupalabdhiḥ caturvvidhā katham iti āha viruddha kāryayoḥ siddhiraḥ  hetu  bhāyoḥ dṛśya ātmanā urabhāva artha anupalabdhiḥ caturvvidhāḥ viruddhañca kāryañca viruddha kārye kāryañca pratyāsatteḥ vviruddhasya eva boddhavyam tayoḥ dṛśya ātmanoḥ hetu bhāvayoḥ kāraṇa svabhāvayoḥ ca dṛśya ātmanoḥ yathākramam siddhiḥ upalabdhiḥ asiddhiḥ anupalabdhiḥ ca 
PVV_3.3,3–3.3,4	 viruddha upalabdhiḥ yathā na atra śīta sparśaḥ agneḥ vyāpya vyāpakayoḥ vastutaḥ tādātmyāt vyāpaka viruddha upalabdhiḥ api anena eva uktā bhavati yathā na atra tuṣāra spararśaḥ agneḥ viruddha kārya upalabdhiḥ yathā na atra śīta sparśaḥ dhūmāt kāraṇa anupalabdhiḥ yathā na atra dhūmaḥ anagneḥ svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ yathā na atra dhūma unupalabdheḥ anena vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ api uktāḥ yathā na atra śiṃśapā vṛkṣa abhāvāt caturvvidhā api anupalabdhiḥ abhāva arthā pratiṣedha phalāḥ tatra svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ svayam eva pratiṣedhya abhāva rūpa tayā siddhā abhāva vyavahāra sādhanī itarāḥ tu niṣedhya abhāva avyabhicāriṇyaḥ tad abhāvam abhāva vyavahārañca sādhayanti tasya asiddha tvāt 
PVV_3.4,0–3.4,2	 yadi viruddha kārya upalabdhyā abhāva siddhiḥ tadā viruddha kāraṇa upalabdhyā api kim na sādhyate iti āha tad viruddha nimittasya yā upalabdhiḥ prayujyate nimittayoḥ viruddha tva abhāvaḥ hi vyabhicāravān tad viruddha nimittasya niṣedhya viruddha kāraṇasya yā upalabdhiḥ prayujyate yathā na śīta sparśaḥ tra kāṣṭhāt iti sā niṣedhyasya viruddhasya ca ye nimitte tayoḥ vviruddha tva abhāve vyabhicāriṇī anaikāntikī virodhe tu nimittayoḥ iṣyate eva yathā na asya roma harṣa ādi viśeṣāḥ santi sannihita dahana viśeṣa tvāt romaharṣa tada bhāvayoḥ vvirodhaḥ tad kāraṇayoḥ ca śīta dahanayoḥ iti yuktā iyam anupalabdhiḥ tathā niṣedhya viruddha kāraṇa kāya palabdhiḥ yathā na roma harṣa yukta puruṣa vān ayam pradeśa udhūmāt iti ukta aṣṭavidhā anupalabdhiḥ 
PVV_3.5,0–3.5,2	 anayā diśā aparāḥ api boddhavyāḥ iṣṭam viruddha kāryepi deśa kāla ādi apekṣaṇām anyathā vyabhicārī syāt bhasma iva aśīta sādhane virupaddha kārye viruddha kārya upalabdhau= api viṣaye nirdeśāt deśasya sannihitasya kālasya varttamānasya kvacid atīta apekṣaṇam iṣṭam anyathā vyabhicāri syāt liṅgam udāharaṇam āha bhasma iva aśītasya śīta abhāvasya sādhane yathā na āsīt kvacid śīta sparśaḥ na asti vā atra bhasmanaḥ iti bhasma anaikāntikam deśa viśeṣye atīta kāla apekṣayā tu syāt hetuḥ na āsīt atra śīta sparśaḥ bhasmanaḥ iti 
PVV_3.6,0–3.6,2	 nanu hetunā yaḥ samagreṇa kārya utpāda unumīyate artha antara anapekṣa tvāt sa svabhāva unuvarṇṇitaḥ hetunā samagreṇa yaḥ kārya utpāda unumīyate sa kasmin hetau= antarbhavati iti āha sa svabhāva hetuḥ anuvarṇṇitaḥ na hi samagrāt hetoḥ kārya sambhava unumīyate kintarhi kārya arjana yogya tvam tat ca artha antara anapekṣa tvāt hetu sākalya mātrā anubandhyā iva iti tasmin sādhye hetu sākalyam svabhāva hetuḥ eva 
PVV_3.7,0–3.7,2	 kasmāt punar kāryam eva na anumīyate iti āha sāmagrophala śaktīnām pariṇāma anubandhini anaikāntika tā kārye pratibandhasya sambhavāt kārye anumeye anaikāntika tā hetu sākalyasya kīdṛśe sāmagryāḥ phalañca tāḥ uttarakṣaṇam śaktayaḥ ca tāsām pariṇāmaḥ kārya utpāda anuguṇaḥ tāratamya yogī kṣaṇa prabandhaḥ tad anubandhini tad apekṣiṇi atas eva pratibandhasya sambhavāt iti uktam 
PVV_3.8,0–3.8,2	 na khalu kāryam hetavaḥ militāḥ iti eva bhavati kim tu eṣām viśeṣam apekṣate atra antare ca śakti vyāghātaḥ mantra tantra ādinā vaikalyañca sambhavati iti kāryasya avaśya bhāvāt na tad anumānam eka sāmagrī adhīnasya rūpa āde rasataḥ gatiḥ hetu dharma anumānena dhūma indhana vikāra vat yā ca rasataḥ madhura ādikāt rūpa ādeḥ ādi śabdāt gandhasya sparśasya ca ekasāmagrya rasa ādinā saha ekasāmagraya āyattasya gatiḥ sā katham iti āha hetu dharma anumānena rasa kāraṇasya dharmaḥ rasa ādi sahacara rūpa janaka tvam tad anumānena rasāt rūpa ādi gatiḥ na hi kāryam rasaḥ kāraṇam antareṇa kāraṇañca asya rasa sahakāri rūpa janakam puñjāt puñja utpatteḥ atas tasmin= anumite anumitam eva rūpam dhūma indhana vikāra vat dhūmāt hetu dharma anumānena indhana vikārasya aṅgārādeḥ ddhūma sahacarasyaḥ vā anumānam 
PVV_3.9,0–3.9,3	 etat eva sphuṭayannāḥ śakti pravṛttyā na vinā rasaḥ sā eva anya kāraṇam iti atīta eka kālānām jāyate kārya liṅgataḥ rasa hetoḥ śakti pravṛttyā śakti ābhimukhyena vinā na rasaḥ utpadyate sā eva rasa hetoḥ śakti pravṛttiḥ anyasya rūpa ādeḥ kāraṇam itara samāna kāla rūpa ādi janaka tvena rasa hetoḥ atītasya hetoḥ eka kālānām rasa sahacarāṇām ca rūpa ādīnām gatiḥ tasya rasa rūpa hetoḥ kāryāt rasāt liṅgāt jātāḥ evam pipīlika utsaraṇa ādi darśanāt varṣa pipīlikā ādi kṣobha hetoḥ bhūta pariṇāma viśeṣasya anumānāt varṣa anumānam kārya liṅga jam veditavyam nadī pūra ādeḥ vvarṣa kārya tvam vyaktam eva 
PVV_3.10,0–3.10,1	 hetunā yaḥ asamagreṇa kārya utpādaḥ anumīyate tat śeṣa vat asāmarthyāt dehāt rāga anumāna vat yaḥ punar hetunā asamagreṇa kārya utpādaḥ kārya utpādana yogya tvam anumīyate tad śeṣa vat ana ekānti kam asāmarthyāt samartham hi kārya utpādana yogyam na ca vyagrāṇām samartha tā dehāt buddhīndriya ādeḥ ca hetoḥ rāga anumāna vat deha ādīnām kathañcid rāga hetu tva ipi na ayoni śomanaskāra rahitānām kāraṇa tvam sahitānām eva hetu tvāt tatas kevalāt dehāt rāga anumānam anaikāntikam 
PVV_3.11,0–3.11,2	 tathā vipakṣe adṛṣṭi mātreṇa kārya sāmānya darśanāt hetu jñāna pramāṇa āmam vacanāt rāgita ādi vat vipakṣe adṛṣṭi mātreṇa kārya sāmānyasya kvacid dharmiṇi darśanāt hetu jñān aṃyat pramāṇa ābham sandigdha vipakṣa vyāvṛttikam tat vacanāt rāgita ādi vat yathā vacanasya vīta rāge adarśanāt kvacid darśanāt rāga anumānam anaikāntikam na hi rāga vacanayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ siddhaḥ vaktu kāma tā hetu tvāt tasya sā ca vīta rāgasya karuṇayā saṃbhavati yadi api vaktari rāgaḥ dṛśyate tathā api kvacid vaktu kāma tāsa tvepi rāga abhāve vacana abhāva asiddheḥ na tad kāryatā siddhiḥ upala khaṇḍāt vaktu kāma tā nivṛtteḥ eva vacana abhāvaḥ na tu rāga abhāvāt tatas vīta rāgāt sandigdhosya vyatirekaḥ 
PVV_3.12,0–3.12,1	 na ca adarśana mātreṇa vipakṣe avyabhicāritā saṃbhāvya vyabhicāri tvāt sthālī taṃḍula pāka vat na ca vipakṣe hetoḥ adarśana mātreṇa sādhya abhāva prayukta sādhana abhāva niścaya rahitena sādhya avyabhicāritā sādhyate sambhāvya vyabhicāra tvāt yadi vipakṣāt hetu nivṛtti niścayaḥ evam vyabhicāra śaṅkā nirāsaḥ sa tu na asti iti tasya api abhāvaḥ sthālī taṇḍula pāka vat sthālī antargatānām taṇḍulānāṃpākasya iva anumānam tad itareṣām pāka adarśanāt śeṣavat 
PVV_3.13,0–3.13,2	 kim punar śeṣavat iti ucyate iti āha yasya adarśana mātreṇa vyatirekaḥ pradarśyate tasya saṃśaya hetu tvāt śeṣavat tat udāhṛtam yasya liṅgasya adarśana mātreṇa vipakṣevī atirekaḥ pradarśyate na tu kāraṇa vyāpaka nivṛttyā tasya saṃśaya hetu tvāt sādhya aniścāyaka tvāt śeṣavat tat udāhṛtam sandigdha vipakṣa vyāvṛttika tvam śeṣavat ucyate pratibandha abhāvāt iti arthaḥ 
PVV_3.14,0–3.14,1^1	 hetoḥ triṣu api rūpeṣu niścayaḥ tena varṇitaḥ asiddha viparīta artha vyabhicāri vipakṣataḥ sūtram uktam asya ayam arthaḥ yaḥ guṇaḥ sa dravya āśrayī tat yathā rūpa ādiḥ apākaja anuṣṇā śīta sparśa śya guṇaḥ tasmāt tasya āśraya bhūtena dravyeṇa bhavitavyam na ca ayam dṛṣṭānām pṛthivī ādīnām guṇaḥ teṣām pāka ja an uṣṇa aśīta sparśa ādi guṇa tvāt tatas yasya ayam guṇaḥ sa vāyuḥ bhaviṣyati iti ukte vaiśeṣikeṇa tatra ācārya di gnāḥ gena uktam yadi adarśana mātreṇa dṛṣṭebhyaḥ sparśasya pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate na ca sā upi yuktaḥ iti dṛśya adṛśya samudāyasya sāmānyena niṣedhāt 
PVV_3.14,0–3.14,1^2	 yat etat uktam tat virudhyate iti vā rti kaḥ kā raḥ darśayan= āha dṛṣṭa ityādi yadi adṛṣṭyā nivṛtiḥ syāt tadā adṛṣṭena darśanāt kāraṇāt apāka jasya anuṣṇa aśīta sparśasya dṛṣṭā ayuktiḥ dṛṣṭeṣu pṛthivī ādiṣu asaṅga tiryām varṇitā vai śe ṣi kaiḥ yasyāḥ ācāryeṇa ayukta tvam uktam sā syāt avirodhinī yuktā eva syāt iti arthaḥ vāyu prakaraṇe pṛthivī ādibhyaḥ yadi sparśa ādeḥ guṇa tvam siddham syāt tatas vāyu dravya anumānam syāt sā eva tu asiddhā svātantryeṇa pratīteḥ sparśa aviśeṣa usmākam vāyuḥ ācāryeṇa tu sparśa vyatiriktam vāyum abhyupagamya ayukta tvam uktam pare 
PVV_3.14,2	 tena pratibandhasya avaśya abhyupagantavya tvena hetoḥ triṣu api pakṣa dharma anvaya vyatirekeṣu niścayaḥ ācārya di gnāḥ ge na vārṇṇitaḥ katham uktaḥ iti āha asiddhasya viparīta arthasya viruddhasya vyabhicāriṇaḥ anaikāntikasya vipakṣeṇa tatra asiddhatva vipakṣeṇa pakṣa dharma tvasya niścayaḥ uktaḥ viruddha vipakṣeṇa anvayasya anaikāntika vipakṣeṇa vyatirekasya 
PVV_3.15,0–3.15,2	 na hya sati pratibandhe vipakṣāt vyatirekaḥ śakya niścayaḥ uktaḥ ca niścayaḥ tatas pratibandha upya ācāryeṇa iṣṭaḥ iti pratīyate anyathā vyabhicāri vipakṣeṇa vaidharmya vacanam ca yat yadi adṛṣṭi phalam tat ca tad anuktepi gamyate pratibandha aniṣṭau vyabhicāriṇaḥ anaikāntikasya vipakṣeṇa vaidharmyasya vyatirekasya vacanam yat ācāryasya eṣa tāvat nyāyaḥ yat u bhayam vaktavyam viruddha anaikāntika pratipakṣeṇa iti ubhayam anvaya vyatirekau tat ca yadi adṛṣṭi phalam adarśana mātra phalam tad adarśana mātram anuktepi vyabhicāri vipakṣeṇa vyatirekaḥ gamyate hetu trairūpya nirddeśāt eva vipakṣe adarśana mātrasya gata tvāt tasmāt vaidharmya vacanena vipakṣe hetu abhāvaḥ kathyate sa ca adarśana mātreṇa na sidhyati 
PVV_3.16,0–3.16,2	 na asti iti vacanāt eva sidhyati iti ced na ca na asti iti vacanāt tat na asti eva yathā yadi na asti sa khyāpyate ca ayam uktau na iti gatiḥ tadā na ca na asti iti vacanāt eva tad sādhanam vipakṣe na asti eva iti yuktam tat api hi anupalambham eva khyāpayati sa ca sarvu asmāt vipakṣāt hetu abhāva pratītau= aśaktaḥ kathantarhi iti āha yathā yena prakāreṇa sādhya sādhanayoḥ pratibandhaḥ sati sādhya abhāvena sādhanam vipakṣe na asti sa nyāyaḥ yadi khyāpyate vyabhicāri vipakṣeṇa vaidharmya uktyā tadā na asti iti gamyate na anyathā 
PVV_3.17,0–3.17,3	 kiñca yadi adṛṣṭau nivṛttiḥ syāt śeṣavat vyabhicāri kim vyatireki api hetuḥ syāt na vācyā asiddhi yojanā yadi adṛṣṭau vipakṣāt hetoḥ nivṛttiḥ syāt śeṣavat sandigdha vipakṣa vyatirekaṃvyabhi kim iṣṭamā cā rye ṇa evañca sarasāni etāni phalāni rūpa aviśeṣāt iti sarvu asya tādṛś rūpasya pakṣīkṛta tvāt na vyabhicāra darśanam vipakṣe ca adarśanam asti iti prāptam adarśana mātrat vyatireka vādinaḥ hetu tvam asya vyatireki api hetuḥ syāt na idam nirātmakam jīvat śarīram aprāṇa ādimatva prasaṅga ādi ti bau ddham prati sā ātmakasya kasyacid asiddheḥ anvaya abhāvāt nirātmakebhyaḥ ca paṭa ādibhyaḥ nivṛtteḥ prāṇādiḥ vyatirekī sa hetuḥ syāt adarśanāt vyatireka siddheḥ aniṣṭaḥ ca ācāryeṇa 
PVV_3.17,4	 kiñca vādi prativādinoḥ asiddhasya anyatara asiddhasya sandigdhasya āśraya asiddhasya sandigdha āśraya asiddhasya asiddhasya ca nirāsam pakṣa dharma tva niścayena pratipādyāṃnvayavyatireka niścaya vacanena sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ hetoḥ anvayasya vyatirekasya ca viparītāyāḥ asiddheḥ caturvvidhāyāḥ yojanā ācāryeṇa sa pakṣe sannasan= iti evamādiṣu api yathāyogam udāhāryyam ityādinā nirdiṣṭā sā api na vācyā adarśanasya vyatireka niścaya hetu tve sandigdha vyatirekasya hetu tvāt 
PVV_3.18,0–3.18,2	 api ca viśeṣasya vyavaccheda hetu tā syāt adarśanāt pramāṇa antara vādhā ced na idānīt na asti tādṛśaḥ viśeṣasya asādhāraṇasya śrāvaṇa tva ādeḥ nitye anitye ca adarśanāt ubhayatas vyāvṛtteḥ śabde dharmiṇi dvaya vyavacchedana hetu tā syāt pramāṇa antara bādhā ced anyonya vyavaccheda rūpayoḥ eka pratiṣedhasya apara vidhinā antarīyaka tvāt ubhaya vyavaccheda unumāna bādhitaḥ na idānīm bādha saṃbhave na asti tādṛśaḥ evam tarhi adṛṣṭeḥ abhāva niścayaḥ na asti iti vaktavyam yathā śrāvaṇa tvena ubhaya vyāvṛtta tayā niścitena prasādhyamānasya ubhaya vyavacchedasya pramāṇa antareṇa bādhā 
PVV_3.19,0–3.19,1	 tathā anyatra api saṃbhāvyam pramāṇa antara bādhanam dṛṣṭā ayuktiḥ adṛṣṭeḥ ca syāt sparśasya avirodhanī tathā anyatra api vipakṣāt hetoḥ vyatirikepi saṃbhāvyam pramāṇa antara bādhanam adarśana mātrasya nimittasya samāna tvāt tathā dṛṣṭā ayuktiḥ adṛṣṭeḥ ca syāt sparśasya avirodhinī dṛṣṭeṣu pṛthivī ādiṣu apākajasya anuṣṇa aśīta sparśasya ayuktiḥ yoga abhāvaḥ adṛṣṭeḥ adarśanāt vai śe ṣi kaḥ syeṣṭā anupalambhāt vyāptyā nivṛttyā niścaya ādā cāryeṇa pratikṣiptā ca yadi adarśana mātraṇe dṛṣṭebhyaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate na ca sā upi yukta pavasavaḥ ityādinā avirodhīnaḥ virodha rahitā syāt evamā cā ryī yaḥ kaścana pratibandham anabhyupagacchan virodhāt upālabdhaḥ 
PVV_3.20,0–3.20,2	 saṃprati parān pratyāha deśa ādi bhedāt dṛśyante bhinnāḥ dravyeṣu śaktayaḥ tatra eka dṛṣṭyā na anyatra yuktaḥ tad bhāva niścayaḥ deśa ādi bhedāt deśa kāla sahakāri bhedāt dṛśyante bhinnāḥ nānā prakārāḥ dravyeṣu tatra ekasmin deśa ādau= ekasya dravyasya śakti viśeṣavataḥ dṛṣṭyā anyatra deśa ādautasya śakti viśeṣavataḥ dravyasya bhāva niścayaḥ na yuktaḥ pratibandham antareṇa na hi ekatra yathā oṣadhayaḥ dṛṣṭāḥ tathā eva anyatra api tāḥ śakyante vyavasthāpayitum kṣetra ādi viśeṣāt viśiṣṭatara rasa vīrya ādi darśanāt 
PVV_3.21,0–3.21,2	 kiñca ātma mṛd cetana ādīnām yaḥ abhāvasya aprasādhakaḥ saḥ eva anupalambhaḥ ki hetu abhāvasya sādhakaḥ ātma mṛd cetana ādīnām yaḥ abhāvasya aprasādhakaḥ ātmanā unupalabhyamānasya ca yaḥ anupalambhaḥ abhāvasya aprasādhakaḥ vai śe ṣi kaḥ sye ṣṭaḥ tathā mudaḥ cetanāyāḥ svabhāva bhūtāyāḥ yaḥ anupalambhaḥ abhāva aprasādhakaḥ cā rvvā kaḥ syeṣṭaḥ tathā kṣīra ādau dadhi ādi abhāvasya yonupalambhaḥ aprasādhakaḥ iṣṭaḥ sām khya sya saḥ eva anupalambhaḥ kim kasmāt vipakṣe hetu abhāvasya iṣṭaḥ vai śe ṣikā dibhiḥ yathā ghaṭa ādau prāṇa ādi matva abhāvaḥ vaiśeṣikasya vaktṛ tva abhāvaḥ vipakṣe cā rvvā kaḥ sya saṃghāta tvā abhāvaḥ vā vipakṣe sām khya syānupalambha ādiṣṭaḥ uktaḥ pareṣān ca nyāya vyāghātaḥ paraspara virodhaḥ ca 
PVV_3.22,0–3.22,2	 yasmāt adarśana mātrat na vyatireka siddhiḥ tasmāt tanmātra sambandhaḥ svabhāvaḥ bhāvam eva vā nivartayet kāraṇam vā kāryam avyabhicārataḥ tasmāt tanmātra sambandhaḥ tad sādhanam kevalam tanmātram tena sambaddhaḥ hetu sattā mātreṇa kāraṇa antara apekṣā rahitena sambandhaḥ yasya iti arthaḥ svabhāvaḥ vyāpakaḥ dharmaḥ nivarttamānaḥ bhāvam vyāpyam eva vā nivarttayet yathā vṛkṣa tvam śiṃśapām vṛkṣa viśeṣa tvāt śiṃśapāyāḥ kāraṇam vā nivarttamānam kāryam nivarttayati avyabhicārataḥ na hi vyāpyam kāryam ca vyāpakena kāraṇena vinā bhavataḥ tad svabhāva tvāt tad adhīna tvāt ca iti 
PVV_3.23,0–3.24,2	 tādātmya tad utpattī avaśya āśrayaṇīye anyathā eka nivṛtya anya vinivṛttiḥ katham bhavet na aśvavān iti saṃdehe kim na vā paśu saṃśayaḥ anya sādhyasya nivṛtyā anyasya sādhanasya vinivṛttiḥ katham bhavet svatantra tvāt na hi martyaḥ aśva rahitaḥ iti gorahitā upi bhavati tathā sannidhānāt tathā ekasya katham anyasya sannidhiḥ gomān iti eva martyena bhāvyam aśvavatā api kim tathā sannidhānāt ekasya hetoḥ katham anyasya sādhyasya sannidhiḥ gomān iti eva gavāśvasya parasparam apratibaddha tvāt eka bhāve na anya bhāvaḥ tathā śiṃśapā avṛkṣa ādau= api syāt yasmāt kāraṇa vyāpaka nivṛttyā kārya vyāpaka nivṛttiḥ darśanīyāḥ vipakṣe 
PVV_3.25,0–3.25,1	 tasmāt vaidharmya dṛṣṭānte na iṣṭaḥ vaśyam iha āśrayaḥ tad abhāve ca tat na iti vacanāt api tad gatiḥ tasmāt vaidharmya dṛṣṭānte na iṣṭaḥ avaśyam iha āśrayaḥ vastu bhūtaḥ dharmī tasya kāraṇa vyāpakasya sādhyasya abhāve ca tad kārya vāyapyam sādhanam na iti vacanāt api tasya sādhya abhāve sādhana abhāvasya gatiḥ vastuni vastu nivṛttiḥ sandigdhā vastu sambandha avirodhāt avastuni tu vastu sattā virudhyate nivṛttiḥ tu yuktāḥ atas sa dharmiṇam antareṇa api voṅmātra topi gamyate eva 
PVV_3.26,0–3.26,2	 yatas tad bhāva hetu bhāvau hi dṛṣṭānte tad avedinaḥ khyāpyete viduṣām vācyaḥ hetuḥ eva hi kevalaḥ tad bhāva hetu bhāvau dṛṣṭānte khyāpyete tasya sādhanasya bhāvaḥ tādātmyam sādhyasya hetu bhāvaḥ ca khyāpyate vaidharmya dṛṣṭānte sādhya nivṛttyā sādhana nivṛtti kathanena tayoḥ tādātmya tad utpatti bandham ajānataḥ yāhi anya nivṛttyā itara nivṛttiḥ sā vastu bhūtam āśrayam antareṇa api śakyate nirdeṣṭum ye tu pratibandham vidanti teṣām viduṣām na dṛṣṭāntaḥ tatra darśanīyasya pratibandhasya siddha tvāt yasmāt dṛṣṭānte pratibandhaḥ kathyate 
PVV_3.27,0–3.27,2	 tena eva jñāta sambandhe dvayoḥ anyatara uktitaḥ artha apatyā dvitīyepi smṛtiḥ samupajāyate tena eva kāraṇena jñāta sambandhe hetau sādharmya vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntayoḥ anyatarasya uktitaḥ a rthā sāmarthyena dvitīyepi smṛtiḥ samupajāyate iti na tasya nirdeśaḥ karttavyaḥ tathā hi yat kṛtakam tat anityam yathā ghaṭaḥ iti tādātmye nirjñāte nitya tva abhāve kṛtaka tva abhāvaḥ sāmarthyāt ākāśa ādau gamyate tathā vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntena tādātmye kathite sāmarthyāt anvayaḥ ghaṭa ādau gamyate evam sādhana bhāve sādhyasya avaśyam bhāvaḥ yadi sādhya abhāve hetu abhāvaḥ tathā sādhya abhāve hetu abhāvaḥ tadā bhavati 
PVV_3.28,0–3.28,2	 yadi sādhana bhāve avaśyam sādhya bhāvaḥ evam kārya anupalambhayoḥ api yojyam hetu svabhāva abhāvotaḥ pratiṣedhe ca kasyacid hetuḥ yukta upalambhasya tasya ca anupalambhanam yatas kāraṇa vyāpaka nivṛttibhyām kārya vyāpya nivṛttiḥ atas hetoḥ svabhāvasya vyāpakasya abhāvaḥ kasyacid kāryasya vyāpyasya ca pratiṣedhe abhāve abhāva vyavahāre ca hetuḥ tathā tasya pratiṣedhyasya yukta upalambhasya upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupa pratiṣedhe pratiṣedha vyavahāre hetuḥ tasya svayam eva abhāva rūpa tvāt 
PVV_3.29,0–3.29,1	 iti iyan trividha uktā api anupalabdhiḥ anekadhā tad tad viruddha ādi agati gati bheda prayogataḥ iti nirdiṣṭa krameṇa iyam anupalabdhiḥ kāraṇa vyāpaka svabhāva anupalabdhi bhedena trivi bahu prakārā tad tad viruddha ādi agati gati bheda prayogataḥ te ca kāraṇa vyāpaka svabhāvāḥ teṣām viruddha ādayaḥ ca tad tad viruddha ādayaḥ ādi śabdāt viruddha kārya ādayaḥ ca teṣām yathākramam agati gatayaḥ kāraṇa vyāpaka svabhāvānām anupalabdhayaḥ teṣām viruddha ādīnām upalabdhayaḥ ca tāsām anyonyam bhedaḥ nānātvam tasya prayogataḥ śabdasya abhidhā vyāpārāt yathā uktaṃprāc sā eṣā aneka prakārā api trividha anupalabdhiḥ saṃgṛhīta iti arthaḥ 
PVV_3.30,0–3.30,2	 uktam artha ślokābhyām saṃgṛhṇan= āha kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt vā svabhāvāt vā niyāmakāt avinā abhauva niyamaḥ adarśanāt na na darśanāt kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt tad utpatteḥ vvā niyāmakāt sādhanasya sādhya avyabhicāra kāraṇāt svabhāvāt tādātmyāt vā niyāmakāt avinā abhāva niyamaḥ sādhya avyabhicāri tva niyamaḥ sādhanasya vipakṣe hetoḥ adarśanāt na sa pakṣe darśanāt darśana adarśanayoḥ vyabhicāriṇī api hetau sambhavāt niyama hetu abhāvāt ca 
PVV_3.31,0–3.31,1	 avaśyaṃbhāva niyamaḥ anyathā parasya kaḥ paraiḥ artha antara nimitte vā dharme vāsasi rāga vat anyathā tādātmya tad utpattyoḥ avyabhicāra nibandhanayoḥ asvīkāre parasya sādhyasya paraiḥ sādhanaiḥ kaḥ avaśyaṃbhāva niyamaḥ na kaścid utpādakāt anyorthaḥ artha antaram tad nimitte asvabhāva bhūte kaḥ avaśyambhāva niyamaḥ vāsasi rāga vat yathā artha antara nimittasya rāgasya vastre na avaśyaṃbhāva niyamaḥ 
PVV_3.32,0–3.32,1	 artha antara nimittaḥ he dharmaḥ syāt anyaḥ eva saḥ paścāt bhāvāt na hetu tvam phalepi ekānta tā kutas vastra utpādakāt artha antara nimittaḥ rāga dravya kāraṇaḥ hi dharmaḥ rāgaḥ prāk utpannāt vastrāt anyaḥ eva syāt bhinna kāla tvāt bhinna hetuka tvāt ca ittham api yadi eka tvaṃviśvam ekam bhavet tatas ca saha utpatti nāśau syātām sarvatra sarvvam ca upayujyate ekatva abhimānaḥ tu sadṛśa apara apara utpatteḥ bhrāntyā tasya ca artha antara nimittasya dharmasya vastra utpādāt paścāt bhāvāt na hetu tvam vastram prati atas kāraṇa tayā api na asya anumānam rāga utpattau vastram sahakāri kāraṇam atas kārya tayā rāga anumānam ced phalepi kāraṇāt anumīyamāne ekānta tā ku na hi avaśyam kāraṇāni kāryavanti bhavanti 
PVV_3.33,0–3.33,2	 yadi darśana adarśane na anvaya vyatirekabuddhi hetuḥ ddhūma ugnit na vyabhicarati iti na syāta pratipattiḥ iti āha kāryam dhūmaḥ hutabhujaḥ kārya dharma anuvuttitaḥ tasya abhāve tu sa bhavan hetumat tām vilaṃghayet kāryam dhūmaḥ hutabhujaḥ kārya dharmasya kāraṇa anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyi tvasya trividha darśana adarśana niścitasya anuvṛttitaḥ sa dhūmaḥ tasya agneḥ abhāve tu bhavan hetumat tām vilaṃgha krāmayet 
PVV_3.34,0–3.34,1	 nityam sattvam asat tvam vā ahetoḥ anya anapekṣaṇāt apekṣātaḥ ca bhāvānām kādācid kasya sambhavaḥ ahetu tve ca dhūmasya nityam sattvam ākāśasya iva syāt asattvam śaśa viṣāṇa ādeḥ iva ahetoḥ anya apekṣaṇa abhāvāt apekṣātaḥ ca bhāvānām kādācid kasya sambhavaḥ tatas yadi ahetuḥ bhāvaḥ tadā nityam syāt asat eva vā syāt hetu abhāvāt tasmāt dhūmasyakādācitka tva darśanāt hetumatvam agni anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāna darśanāt tad kāryatvañca yaḥ ca yasya kāryam sa tam na vyabhicarati tad adhīna svarūpa tvāt 
PVV_3.35,0–3.35,2	 atas ca agni svabhāvaḥ śakrasya mūrdhā yadi agniḥ eva saḥ atha anagni svabhāva ūsau dhūmaḥ tatra katham bhavet agni svabhāvaḥ śakrasya mūrddhā valmīkaḥ yadi agniḥ eva sa tadā na hi vahni svarūpa tām vihāya anyat vahne rūpam atha anyathā pratīyamāna tvāt anagni svabhāva ūsau tadā dhūmaḥ vahneḥ janya svabhāvaḥ tatra śakra mūrdhni katham bhavet na hi vahni janyonyasmāt bhavitum arhati tad adhīna tvāt tatas śakra mūrdhnaḥ dhūma utpattiḥ iti bhrāntiḥ eṣā vahneḥ eva tad deśa vartinaḥ anupalakṣitāt utpattiḥ 
PVV_3.36,0–3.36,2	 kiñca dhūma hetu svabhāvaḥ hi vahniḥ tad śakti bhedavān adhūma hetoḥ dhūmasya bhāve sa syāt ahetukaḥ dhūma hetu svabhāvaḥ tad śakti bhedavān dhūma janana śakti viśeṣa yuktaḥ vahniḥ pratītaḥ adhūma hetoḥ adahanāt dhūmasya bhāve sa dhūmaḥ ahetukaḥ syāt hetum pramāṇa niścitam antareṇa eva utpādāt ahetu tve ca nityam sattvam asat tvam vām syāt iti uktam 
PVV_3.37,0–3.37,2	 syāt etat śālūka ādi sva bījāt vijātīyāt ca gomaya ādeḥ dṛśyate tat katham avahneḥ ddhūma utpāde ahetu tu a prasaṅgaḥ iti āha anvaya vyatireka ādyaḥ yasya dṛṣṭa unuvartakaḥ svabhāvaḥ tasya tad hetuḥ atas bhinnāt na sambhavaḥ anvaya vyatirekāt yaḥ svabhāvaḥ yasya anuvarttakaḥ apekṣakaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ taṃsya svabhāvasya tat anuvarttyamānam hetuḥ atas bhinnāt vijātīyāt na saṃbhavaḥ kasyacid yat hi śālūka ādi sva bīja prabhavam yat ca vijātīya prabhavam tayoḥ sadṛśa tva pratītau= api na tādṛśa tvam rasa vīrya vipāka bhedāt yadi tu hetu bhedepya bhedaḥ viśva ātmakam dravyam syāt iti ādi uktaṃprasajyeta 
PVV_3.38,0–3.38,1	 svabhāvepya vinābhāvaḥ bhāva mātra anurodhini tad abhāve svayambhauvasya abhāvaḥ syāt abhedataḥ svabhāvepi hetau= a vinā bhāvaḥ kva sādhye bhāva mātra anurodhini sādhana svarūpa mātra anuvarttini vyāpake yathā kṛtaka tvasya anitya tve yatas tasya vyāpakasya abhāve bhāvasya vyāpyasya kṛtaka tva ādeḥ svayam abhāvaḥ syāt abhedate aikātmyāt vastutas 
PVV_3.39,0–3.40,1	 yadi yaḥ eva kṛtakaḥ saḥ eva anityaḥ bheda abhāvāt tadā pratijñā artha eka deśaḥ hetuḥ syāt iti āha sarve bhāvāḥ svabhāvena sva svabhāva vyavasthiteḥ svabhāva para bhāvābhyām vyāvṛtti bhāginaḥ yatas sarvve bhāvāḥ svabhāvena sva svabhāva vyavasthiteḥ ātma ātmīya rūpa vasthita tvāt svabhāva para bhāvābhyām sajātīyāt vijātīyāt ca vyāvṛtti bhāginaḥ yasmāt na kenacid miśrāḥ tasmāt vyāvṛttiḥ arthānām yatas ca tad nibandhanāḥ jāti bhedāḥ prakalpyante tad viśeṣa avagāhinaḥ tasmāt yatas yatas asvarūpāt arthāt vyāvṛttiḥ arthānām tad nibandhanāḥ tad tad vyāvṛtti nimittā jāti bhedāḥ tad viśeṣa avagāhinaḥ tad sva lakṣaṇa āśrayāḥ kalpyante śabdaiḥ svavācya tayā 
PVV_3.41,0–3.41,2	 yatas śabdaḥ kāścid artha kriyāḥ kurvan= atad kāriṇaḥ aśabdāt akṛtakāt nityādeḥ ca vyāvṛttaḥ iti tad tadvayava= cheda pratipādana artham śabda kṛtaka anitya tva ādyāḥ jātayaḥ ananya śabda vācya tayā kalpyante tasmāt viśeṣaḥ yaḥ yena dharmeṇa saṃpratīyate na sa śakyaḥ tatonyena tena bhinnā vyavasthitiḥ tasmāt svabhāva abhedepi kṛtaka tva anitya tva ādīnām yena dharmeṇa nāmnā anityaḥ iti anena yaḥ viśeṣaḥ nityāt vyāvṛttiḥ saṃpra sa viśeṣaḥ śakyaḥ tatas anitya śabdāt anyena kṛtaka śabdena pratyetum tena kāraṇena sādhya sādhanayoḥ bhinnā vyavasthitiḥ yadi api śabdaḥ eva kṛtakaḥ anityaḥ ca tathā api aśabda vyāvṛtta tayā niścitaḥ dharmī kṛtaka tayā ca hetuḥ anitya tayā ca asiddhaḥ sādhyaḥ tatas dharmi sādhya sādhanānām bhedaḥ kalpitaḥ na tu tāni eva kalpitāni teṣām sattvāt tatas kalpita dharmiṇi kalpitāt sādhanāt kalpitasya sādhyasya siddhim ācakṣāṇaḥ pratyākhyātaḥ tasmāt na pratijñā artha eka deśaḥ hetuḥ sādhya sādhanayoḥ bhinna vyavaccheda rūpa tvāt 
PVV_3.42,0–3.42,2	 kasmāt punar vyavacchedaḥ śabda liṅgābhyām pratipādyate iti iṣyate na tu vastu eva vidhi rūpeṇa iti āha ekasya artha svabhāvasya pratyakṣasya sataḥ svayam konyaḥ bhāgaḥ na dṛṣṭaḥ syāt yaḥ pramāṇaiḥ parīkṣyate ekastha artha svabhāvasya svayam ātmanā pratyakṣasya sataḥ konyaḥ bhāgaḥ na dṛ nirṇṇīyate yadi pramāṇa antaraiḥ śabda antaraiḥ ca vastu eva viṣayīkarttavyaṃtadā tat pratyakṣeṇa śabda antareṇa ca dṛṣṭam eva iti vyarthāni pramāṇāni syuḥ 
PVV_3.43,0–3.44,2	 tvad matepi pratyakṣeṇa dṛṣṭe dharmiṇi pramāṇa antara vaiphalyam syāt na iti āha no ced bhrānti nimittena saṃyojyeta guṇa antaram śuktau vā rajata ākāraḥ rūpa sādharmya darśanāt dṛṣṭe sarvathā vastuni no ced bhrānti nimittena sādṛśya ādinā saṃyojyeta āropyeta guṇa antaram dharmma antaram asat eva śuktau vā śuktau= iva rūpa sādharmya darśanāt bhrānti nimittāt rajata ākāraḥ tadā sarvu athā vastu niścayāt pramāṇa antara śabda antara vaiphalyam syāt etat eva āha tasmāt dṛṣṭasya bhāvasya dṛṣṭaḥ eva akhilaḥ guṇaḥ bhrānteḥ na niścayaḥ iti sādhanam saṃpravarttate tasmāt dṛṣṭasya bhāvasya dṛṣṭaḥ eva akhilaḥ guṇaḥ dharmaḥ tathā api bhrānteḥ vviparīta ākāra āropikāyāḥ na niścīyate iti āropita vyavaccheda artham sādhanam śabda antarañca saṃpravarttate 
PVV_3.45,0–3.45,2	 na kevalam pratyakṣāt vastu grahe sādhana antara śabda antara vaiphalyam kintu anumānāt api iti āha vastu grahenumānāt ca dharmasya ekasya niścaye sarva grahaḥ hi apohe tu na ayam doṣaḥ prasajyate vastu grahenumānāt ca dharmasya ekasya kṛtaka tva ādeḥ pratyaya bheda abheditva ādi kṛte niścaye sya anitya tva ādeḥ grahaḥ syāt eka rūpa tvāt kṛtaka tva ādi sādhana antara vaiyarthyam apohe tu anya vyavacchede śabda liṅga viṣaye svīkriyamāṇe na ayam pramāṇa antara ādi vaiphalyaṣaḥ prasajyate na khalu pratyagra dṛṣṭam vastu antaram śabda liṅgā kintu anya vyavacchedaḥ ekasmin= ca vyavacchede siddhepya siddham vyavaccheda antaram liṅga antarataḥ śabda antarataḥ ca sādhyate iti na kaścid doṣaḥ 
PVV_3.46,0–3.46,1	 tasmāt apoha viṣayam liṅgam iti prakīrtitam anyathā dharmiṇaḥ siddhau kim atas sādhakam param tasmāt ācāryeṇa apoha viṣayam liṅgam iti prakīrtitam liṅgam upalakṣaṇam śabdaḥ ca anyathā yadi vastu viṣayam liṅgam tadā dharmmiṇaḥ sarva ātmanā pratyakṣataḥ siddhau kim atas dharmiṇaḥ parama siddham asti yat prasādhakam liṅgampramāṇam syāt 
PVV_3.47,0–3.47,1	 kvacid sāmānya viṣayam dṛṣṭe jñānam aliṅga jam katham anya apoha viṣayam tanmātra apoha gocaraḥ nanu kvacid nīlā dau= asamāropitaḥ anyaḥ viparīta aṃśaḥ yasmin tasmin pratyakṣeṇa dṛṣṭe yat jñānam aliṅga jam vikalpakam sāmānya viṣayam bhavati tad āropa abhāvāt katham anya apoha viṣayam āha tanmātrasya ānīla mātrasya apohaḥ vijātīyāt vyāvṛttiḥ vyavacchedaḥ sa gocaraḥ yasya tat tathā nīla vikalpasya ānīla vyavacchedaḥ eva viṣayaḥ iti arthaḥ 
PVV_3.48,0–3.49,2	 kasmāt evam iti āha niścaya āropa manasoḥ bādhya bādhaka bhāvataḥ samāropa viveke asya pravṛttiḥ iti gamyate niścaya āropamanasoḥ bāṣya bādhaka bhāvataḥ samāropasya viveke vyavacchede asya niścayasya pravṛttiḥ iti gamyate tasmāt yāvantoṃ aśasamāropāḥ niścayāḥ tad nirāsataḥ tāvantaḥ eva śabdāḥ bhinna vyavaccheda gocarāḥ yāvantaḥ aśasya dharmasya samāropāḥ tasya nirāsa nimittam viniścayāḥ śabdāḥ ca tāvantaḥ eva tena te niścayāḥ śabdāḥ ca bhinna vyavaccheda gocarāḥ 
PVV_3.50,0–3.50,1	 anyathā vastu viṣayīkurutaḥ ekena vā dhiyā ekatra na anyaḥ viṣaya uḥ ti iti syāt paryāyatā anyathā yadi śabda niścayau sarva ātmanā vastu viṣayīkurutaḥ tat ekena śabdena buddhyā vā vikalpikayā vyāpte sarva ātmanā viṣayīkṛte vastuni ekatra na anyaḥ apratipannaḥ viṣaya uḥ ti iti paryāyatā śabdānām syāt vikalpā nāñca eka viṣaya tā bhavet 
PVV_3.51,0–3.51,2	 nanu dravyāt upādhayaḥ parasparañca bhinnāḥ tad nimittāḥ vikalpāḥ śabdāḥ ca teṣu tad ādhāre vā dravye varttante iti āha nānā upādhi viśiṣṭasya bhedinorthasya grāhikāḥ upakāra aṅga śaktibhyaḥ abhinna ātma niścaya grahe yasya api nai yā yi kā dermate nānā upādheḥ dravya tva ādi aneka dharma viśiṣṭha syātas eva upāghi bhedāt bhedinorthasya vidhi rūpeṇa dhīḥ tasya api matena nānā prakārāṇām upādhīnām upakārasya aṅgam yāḥ śaktayaḥ tābhyaḥ abhinna ātmanaḥ upādhimataḥ dravyasya niścaya jñānena grahe 
PVV_3.52,0–3.52,2	 sarva ātmanā kṛte grāhe kaḥ bhedaḥ syāt aniścitaḥ tayoḥ ātmani sambandhāt eka jñāne dvaya grahaḥ sarvu ātmanā kṛte sati upakāryasya upādhi ka lāpasya madhye kaḥ bhedaḥ upādhi viśeṣaḥ syāt aniścitaḥ yathā dravyam ekam upādhim upakaroti tathā parān api tatas eka upādhi upakāraka tve vidhi rūpeṇa gṛhyamāṇe sarvvā upādhi upakāraka tvam gṛhyeta tathā ca sarvvā upādhi grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ na hi yat sa apekṣam yat rūpam tad agrahaṇe tat gṛhītum śakyam nanu dhūma apekṣam vahneḥ kāraṇa tvam na ca tad grahe dhūma grahaḥ na etat yuktam tathā hi 
PVV_3.52,3–3.52,4	 kim punar kāraṇa tvam iṣṭam vahneḥ yadi avidyamāna tvāt dhūmāt pūrvva kāla bhāvitāḥ dhūmāsāhityam varttamāna kāla sattā na tat dhūma apekṣam sva kāraṇāt tathā utpatteḥ dhūmam antareṇa eva ca bhāvāt na ca tad grahe dhūma grahaḥ viruddha tvāt na hi dhūma grahaṇe tasmāt prāk bhāvi tvasya tat asā ahityasya ca grahaṇam atha dhūmasya ayam hetuḥ iti niścaya viṣaya tvam kāraṇa tvam iṣṭantadā asti eva īdṛśa kāraṇa tvasya grahe dhūma pratītiḥ ubhaya prati iti ākāra tvāt asya niścayasya dvaya anvaya vyatireka grahaṇa sāpekṣa tvāt ca nanu ca gṛhīta tad utpatteḥ agni mātra darśanāt kāraṇa tva pratītiḥ na ca tadā dhūmaḥ 
PVV_3.52,5^1	 siddhāntī na ca tatra pratyakṣāt kāraṇa tvasya pratītiḥ kintu agni rūpa mātrasya anyathā sarvu asya tad darśinaḥ kāraṇa tva pratīti prasaṅgaḥ kintu vyāpti graha sāpekṣā ānumānikī tad pratītiḥ tathā hi gṛhīta tad utpatteḥ eva iyam bhavati na anyasya tad utpatti grahe ca yat evam rūpam tat etat kāraṇam iti gṛhītā vyāptiḥ anumāna pratītau ca dhūma kāraṇam vahniḥ iti vyavaccheda dvayam anyonya sāpekṣam pratīyate eva iti alam tad prasaṅgena na hi anutkhātita kāryaḥ kāraṇa tva niścayaḥ atyantam abhyāsāt ca vyāpti graha saṃskārasya prabuddha tvāt apekṣā na asti iti atatva vivekinām na anumāna tva prabodhaḥ 
PVV_3.52,5^2	 na hi anumānam aham iti utpannam anumānam ucyate kintu trirūpa liṅga jam anumeya viṣayam kāraṇa tva jñānañca tādṛśam eva dravyantu yena eva rūpeṇa ekam upādhim upakaroti tena eva aparān api iti ekopodhi upakāraka tve gṛhyamāṇe na aneka upādhi upakāraka tvasya grahaṇāt sarvvā upādhi grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ paraspara sāpekṣa tvāt tatas ca tayoḥ upādhi kalāpa tad upakāraka tvayoḥ ātmani sambandhāt dravyasya sambandhāt ekasya upādhi upakāraka tvasya jñāne dvayasya grahaḥ syāt eka niyatā pratītiḥ na bhavet iti arthaḥ 
PVV_3.53,0–3.53,3	 atha dravyāt upādhi upakārikāḥ śaktayaḥ bhinnāḥ eva dravya grahaṇe tāsām agrahaṇāt na sarvvā upādhi grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ iti āha dharma upakāra śaktīnām bhede tāḥ tasya kim yadi na upakāraḥ tatas tāsām tathā syāt anavasthitiḥ dharmāṇām upādhīnāu pakārasya nimitta bhūtānām śaktīnām dravyāt bhede svīkriyamāṇe tāḥ śaktayaḥ tasya dravyasya kim kasmāt yadi na upakāraḥ tatas dravyāt tāsām śaktīnām upakāram antareṇa sambandhe ati prasaṅgāt atha tāsām śaktīnām dravyeṇa upakāraḥ kriyate svarūpeṇa tadā śakti upakāra tvasya grahaṇāt śaktīnām grahaḥ tad grahāt ca sarvvā upādhi graha prasaṅgaḥ tad avasthaḥ syāt etat śaktīḥ api bhinnābhiḥ śaktibhiḥ upakaroti tathā syāt anavasthitiḥ tathā hi yāḥ tāḥ śakti upakārikāḥ śakti apaḥ tāḥ dravyasya upakāra dvārāt yadi iṣṭāḥ tadā asvarūpeṇa upakāraka tve sarvvā upādhi graha prasaṅga bhayāt anyāḥ śaktaye eṣṭavyāḥ tathā ca anavasthā vyaktā 
PVV_3.54,0–3.54,2	 uktam artham saṃgṛhṇan= āha eka upakārake grāhye adṛṣṭāḥ tasmin na santi te sarva upakārakam hi ekam tad grahe sakala grahaḥ ekasya upādheḥ upakārake dravye grāhye abhimate tatas eka upādhi upakāraka dravya svabhāvāt apare upādhi antarāṇām upakārakāḥ upakāra śakti bhedāḥ dṛṣṭe tasmin= eka upādhi upakārake dravye adṛṣṭāḥ ye te na santi ekam eva hi rūpam sarvvā upādhi upakārakamatas tasya eka upādhimatas grahe sakala upādhi grahaḥ syāt 
PVV_3.55,0–3.55,1	 yadi bhrānti nivṛtti artham gṛhītepi anyat iṣyate tad vyavaccheda viṣayam siddhantadvat tatas aparam sarvu ātmanā vikalpena gṛhītepi vastuni bhrāntyā tathā na niścayaḥ iti yadi pramāṇa antaram iṣyate tad bhrānti nivarttakam pramāṇa antaram vyavaccheda viṣayam siddham bhrama āropita tva apoha viṣaya tvāt tatas bhrānti nivarttakāt aparam yat pūrvvam utpannam vastu viṣayam iṣṭam tadvat apoha viṣayam siddham 
PVV_3.56,0–3.56,3	 kasmāt iti āha tad vipakṣa samāropa viṣaye yadi niścayaiḥ niścīyate na yat rūpam tat teṣām viṣayaḥ katham avidyamāna ani asamārope viṣaye vṛtteḥ vikalpaḥ hi vyavaccheda viṣayam niścinvan tad vipakṣa samāropa viṣaye na bhavati kintu tad vyavaccheda niścaya āropamanasā urbbādhya bādhaka bhāvataḥ iti uktam api ca niścayaiḥ eka ākāra pravṛttaiḥ yat rūpam na niścīyate tad teṣām viṣayaḥ katham ucyate niścitañcā pratipannam ca iti vipratisiddham yadi kṛtaka tva niścaye anitya tva ādi api niścitam katham tasya apratipattiḥ kṛtaka tvasya api vā mā abhūt 
PVV_3.57,0–3.57,2	 evantarhi pratyakṣa gṛhīte vastuni niścaya aniścayau na syātām iti āha pratyakṣeṇa gṛhītepi viśeṣa īṃśa vivarjite yad viśeṣa avasāya isti pratyayaḥ sa pratīyate pratyakṣeṇa gṛhītepi viśeṣe sva lakṣaṇe sarvvatas vyāvṛtteṃ aśaiḥ bhāgaiḥ vvivarjite yasya viśeṣasya vyavacchedasya avasāya isti pratyayaḥ sahakārī prakaraṇa abhyāsa pāṭava ādiḥ sa pratīyate na itaraḥ na khalu asmad mate pratyakṣam niścaya ātmakam na api anubhava mātra adhīnaḥ niścayaḥ yena sarvu athā niścaya prasaṅgaḥ kintu yatra vyavacchede abhyāsāt ayaḥ sahakāriṇaḥ pratyakṣasya santi sa niścīyate na anyaḥ iti yuktaḥ vibhāgaḥ 
PVV_3.58,0–3.58,1	 tatra api ca anya vyāvṛttiḥ anya vyāvṛttaḥ iti api śabdāḥ ca niścayāḥ ca eva nimittam anurundhate tatra api ca anya apohepi śabda vikalpa viṣaye anya vyāvṛttiḥ anya vyāvṛttaḥ iti api bhinna viṣayāḥ iva pravartante na te vyāvṛtti vyāvṛttayoḥ vvāstava bheda nibandhanāḥ kintarhi saṃketam eva bheda vyavahāra vyasthāpakam vakṣyamāṇa nimittam anurundhate anuvarttante yadi goranyā ago vyāvṛttiḥ tadā yathā gaura goḥ aśvādeḥ vyāvṛttaḥ tathā ago vyāvṛtteḥ api vyāvṛttaḥ tatas ca aśva ādi vat goragauḥ eva syāt yaḥ hi ago vyāvṛtteḥ vyāvṛttaḥ saḥ agauryatha āśvādiḥ gauḥ ca tathā iti syāt tathā ago vyāvṛttiḥ api na prāpnoti sarvu asya eva ago tvāt goragoḥ anya tve hi tasmāt vyāvṛttiḥ syāt yadā tu gauḥ eva na asti tadā kasya kasmāt vyāvṛttiḥ tasmāt na vyāvṛtti vyāvṛttayoḥ vvastutaḥ bhedaḥ 
PVV_3.59,0–3.59,2	 tatas ca dvayoḥ eka abhidhāna ipi vibhaktiḥ vyatirekiṇī bhinnam artham iva anveti vācyate sa viśeṣataḥ dvayoḥ vyāvṛtti vyāvṛttayoḥ ekasya arthasya abhidhāna ipi vastutas vibhaktiḥ ṣaṣṭhī ādiḥ vyatirekaḥ vācya bhedaḥ tadvatī vyāvṛttasya vyāvṛttiḥ iti bhinnam iva artham anveti anugacchati vācaka tvena vācyasya leśa viśeṣataḥ alpa bhedāt sa aṅketikāt abhinna īpi arthe 
PVV_3.60,0–3.60,2	 kimartham saṃketa bhedaḥ kaḥ ca vācya viśeṣaḥ iti āha bheda antara pratikṣepa apratikṣepau tayoḥ dvayoḥ padam saṅketa bhedasya jñātṛ vāñcha anurodhinaḥ bheda antarasya pratipādyamānāt vyavacchedāt anyasya vyavacchedasya pratikṣepaḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyasya svabhāvaḥ apratikṣepaḥ tad sambhavaḥ tau tayoḥ dvayoḥ vyāvṛtti vyāvṛtta śabdayoḥ saṃketa bhedasya jñātṛ vāñcha anurodhinaḥ padam kāraṇam jñātā hi kadācid gauḥ a naśva tvam niṣkṛṣṭa dharma antara sambandha yogya tvam jijñāsate tadā go tvam asya iti ucyate na tu go tvam asya śuklam iti yadā tu vyāvṛttiḥ eva aniṣkṛṣṭa dharma antara sambandha yogyā jijñāsitā bhavati tadā vyāvṛtta śabda saṃketaḥ yathā gaurayam iti dharmma antara sāmānādhikaraṇyañca gauḥ śuklaḥ ityādi 
PVV_3.61,0–3.61,1	 bhedoyam a iva sarvatra dravya bhāva abhidhāyinoḥ śabdayoḥ na tayoḥ vācye viśeṣaḥ tena kaścana bhedoyam a iva saṃketa kṛtaḥ dharma antara pratikṣepa apratikṣepa pratipatti phalaḥ dravya bhāva ārddharmi dharma vācinoḥ śabdayoḥ na vāstavaḥ tena tayoḥ vvācye niścaya viṣaye na kaścid viśe bheda antara pratikṣepa apratikṣepābhyām ekasya eva pratyāyanāt

PVV_3.89,0–3.90,1	 kasmāt evam iti āha samāna bhinna ādi ākāraiḥ na tat grāhyam kathañcana bhedānām bahu bhedānām tatra ekasmin= ayogataḥ samāna bhinna ādi ākāraiḥ sāmānya ākāra dharmi dharma bheda ākāra sāmānādhikaraṇyā ādi ākāraiḥ ca tat sva lakṣaṇam kathañcana grāhyam na bhavati kim kāraṇam iti āha bhedānāṃdharmāṇām kṛtaka tva ādīnām bahu bhedānām aneka prakārāṇām tatra sva lakṣaṇaḥ ekasmin naḥ tad rūpam sarvatas bhinnam tathā tad pratipādikā na śrutiḥ kalpanā vā asti sāmānyena eva vṛttitaḥ tasmāt tasya sva lakṣaṇasya rūpam sarvvatas sajātīya vijātīyāt bhinnam tathā tena sarvu atas bhinnena rūpeṇa tad pratipādikā śrutiḥ kalpanā vā na asti sāmānyena eva kalpitena rūpeṇa śabda vikalpayoḥ vṛttitaḥ 
PVV_3.91,0–3.91,2	 kim punar sva lakṣaṇam eva śabdaiḥ na ucyate iti āha śabdāḥ saṃketitam prāhuḥ vyavahārāya sa smṛtaḥ tadā sva lakṣaṇam na asti saṅketaḥ tena tatra na śabdāḥ saṃketitam artham āhuḥ na yam kañcid sa saṃketaḥ vyavahārāya saṃketitam artham śabdāt uccaritāt pratipadyeyam iti saṃketa grahaṇam tadā vyavahāra kāle ca sva lakṣaṇam saṃketa viṣayaḥ na asti tena tatra sva lakṣaṇe saṃketaḥ yuktaḥ

PVV_3.94,0–3.94,1	 tad kāriṇām a tad kāri bheda sāmye na kim kṛtaḥ tadvat doṣasya sāmyāt ced aḥ tu jātiḥ alam parā kiñca yām artha kriyām uddiśya śabda niyogaḥ tad kārim arthānām atat kāribhyaḥ yaḥ bhedaḥ vyavacchedaḥ tat eva sāmyam sāmānyam anya apohaḥ sādhāraṇa tvāt tatra kim saṃketaḥ na kṛtaḥ sāmānya vat apohopi sādhāraṇaḥ anartha kriyā kārī sva lakṣaṇa sambandhāt tad upalabhya rūpaḥ caḥ tadvat doṣasya jātimati saṃketa viṣaye ānantyāt saṃketa akaraṇasya sāmyāt ced aḥ tu doṣaḥ samāna tvāt dvayoḥ asta jātiḥ parā alam anupayuktā jātim abhyupetya api vijātīya vyavacchedaḥ a vaśya āśrayaṇīyaḥ yadi gauḥ aśva ādibhyaḥ na vyavacchinnaḥ tadā aśvaḥ eva syāt yaḥ ca ekasya vyavacchedaḥ sa saru u asya saḥ eva saṅketa viṣayaḥ astu kim pramāṇa bādhita jāti svīkāreṇa atas eva tadvat doṣa upi na sambhavati abhyupagamya tu sāṃpratam āpāditam kiñca
