PVV_3.148–3.156,10–3.148–3.156,14	 ananyatve anvaya abhāvāt anya tvepi anapāśrayāt ananya tve ekatra vyaktau tadātmanaḥ sataḥ sāmānyasya anyatra vyakti antare anvayāḥ darśana asambhavāt katham sāmānya buddhiḥ anya tvepi jāteḥ anapāśrayāt ukta yuktyā aśrayatva abhāvāt na vyaktiṣu apūrvvāsu tad nibandhanā dhīḥ syāt api ca sāmānyam sva āśraya gatam vā kalpyate sarvu agatam vā ākāśa ādi vat tatra prathama pakṣam dūṣayitum āha na yāti na ca tatra āsīt asti paścāt na ca aṃśa vat jahāti pūrvvam na ādhāram aho vyasana santatiḥ 
PVV_3.148–3.156,15	 eka vyakti sthitam sāmānyam vyakti antaram utpadyamānam niṣkriya tvāt na yāti na vyakti utpatti deśe prāk āsīt vyakti mātra niṣṭha tvāt asti ca paścāt utpatteḥ sāmānyam sāmānya śūnyāyāḥ vyakteḥ sthiti anupagamāt na ca aṃśa vat na hi sāmānyam sa avayavam yena kvacid ekena avayavena samavetam sat avayava antaraiḥ utpadyamāna vyaktibhiḥ sambadhyate na ca pūrvva utpannam ādhāram jahāti utpitsu vyakti antareṇa sambandha artham anyatra sthitasya apara sambandhaḥ tad deśa āgamanam kila na yujyate iti aho sva āśraya gata sāmānya vādinām 
PVV_3.148–3.156,16–3.148–3.156,19	 kiñca anyatra varttamānasya tatonya sthāna janmani sva sthānāt acalatonyatra vṛttiḥ ayuktimat anyatra pūrvvasthitāyām vyaktau varttamānasya sāmānyasya svasmāt sthānāt āśrayāt acalataḥ tatas pūrvvavyakteḥ anyatra sthāne janma yasya tatra dravye vṛttiḥ itya na hi vyakti antara sthitasya vyakti antaram anāgacchataḥ tena saha anutpadyamānasya ca tad sambandhaḥ yuktaḥ 
PVV_3.148–3.156,20–3.148–3.156,23	 tathā yatra asau varttate bhāvaḥ te na saṃbadhyata ipi na tad deśinañca vyāpnoti kim api etat mahā adbhutam yatra deśe asau śāvaleya ādiḥ bhāvaḥ varttate tena deśena sāmānyam na sambadhyate sva vyakti niṣṭha tvāt tasya tad deśinam sāmānya sambandha rahitaḥ deśaḥ yasya tam viśeṣañca vyāpnoti kim api mahā adbhutam etat durbuddhi vilapiteṣu 
PVV_3.148–3.156,24–3.148–3.156,26	 vyakti avaikatra vyaktā atha sarvagā jātiḥ iṣyate sarvatra dṛśyeta abhedāt sā api na vyakti apekṣiṇī atha sarvu atra gāḥ jātiḥ iṣyate tadā ekatra eva deśe vyaktyā vyaktā sā jātiḥ sarvu atra deśe dṛśyeta abhedāt eka vyakti vyaktam rūpam sarvu atra vidyamānam abhinnam iti upalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ vyaṅgya vyañjaka bhāvaḥ ca ayuktaḥ iti uktam bhavatu vā tathā api na sā jātiḥ vyakti apekṣiṇī 
PVV_3.148–3.156,27–3.148–3.156,34	 tathā hi vyañjakasya apratītau na vyaṅgyam samyak pratīyate viparyayaḥ punar kasmāt iṣṭaḥ sāmānya tadvatoḥ vyañjakasya pradīpa ādera pratītau na vyaṅgyam ghaṭa ādiḥ saṃpratīyate iti tāvat sthitam sāmānya tadvatoḥ punar kasmāt viparyayaḥ iṣṭaḥ yadi vyaktiḥ sāmānyasya vyañjikā tadā vyakteḥ grahe sāmānyam na gṛhyeta iha tu sāmānyasya vyaṅgyasya prāk grahaṇam tatas tad viśiṣṭa tvena vyaktiḥ gahyate iti kim iṣyate vyañjaka agrahe vyaṅgyā grahṇāt kiñca pācaka ādiṣu abhinnena vinā api arthena vācakaḥ yadi sāmānyam eva abhinna abhidhāna hetuḥ na vyaktayaḥ tadā pācaka ādiṣu abhinnena arthena pācaka tva ādi sāmānyena vinā eva tvad matepi pācaka ādi śabdaḥ katham vācakaḥ pratyayaḥ ca anuyāyī karma pacana ādi tad hetuḥ iti ced āha 
PVV_3.157–3.173,0–3.157–3.173,4	 bhedāt na hetuḥ karma asya na jātiḥ karma saṃśrayāt bhedāt na hetuḥ karma ādi karma api prativyakti ekasyām api pauru vāparyeṇa bhinnam eva tat katham vyakti vat eka abhidhāna hetuḥ karma sāmānyam hetuḥ ced āha asya karmaṇaḥ jātiḥ nābhinnā abhidhāna hetuḥ tasyāḥ karma saṃśrayāt karmaṇi samaveta tvāt tatra eva abhidhāna hetu tā syāt na dravye atha karma sāmānyam karmaṇi sambaddham tat ca dravyaḥ iti paramparayā tad sambaddham tad nimittaḥ śabdaḥ dravye varttate iti āha śruti antara nimitta tvāt karmaṇaḥ na nimitta tā asaṃbaṃdhāt na sāmānyam na ayuktam śabda kāraṇāt atiprasaṃgāt 
PVV_3.157–3.173,5	 śruti antarasya pācaka ādi śabdāt anyasya pākaḥ iti ādi śabdasya nimita tvāt karmaṇaḥ dravye pācaka śabda vṛttau na asti nimitta tā paraṃparayā api tathā anitya tvāt sthiti abhāvāt ca karmaṇaḥ tasmin nivṛtte pācaka ādi pratipattiḥ nna syāt apacati apitad vi apadeśaḥ dṛśyate nitya tvāt karma sāmānyam pācaka vyapadeśe hetuḥ ced āha asambandhāt dravyeṇa karma sāmānyasya na sambandhaḥ sākṣāt tatra asamavāyāt na api paraṃparayā karmaṇā tad samavetasya naṣṭa tvāt samavāyinā sāmānyena sambandha abhāvāt nasāmānyam śabdasya pācaka ādeḥ kāraṇa anna ayuktam kiṃtu ayuktam eva atiprasaṅgāt karma tvasya sambandha vyatirekeṇa vyapadeśa hetu tve sarvu atra tathā tva prasaṅgaḥ 
PVV_3.157–3.173,6–3.157–3.173,11	 apacati api puruṣe atīta anāgatam karma tad vyapadeśa nimittam iti ced āha karma api na asat jñāna abhidhānayoḥ anaimittika tā āpatteḥ na karma āsat api jñāna abhidhānayoḥ hetuḥ anaimittika tāyāḥ āpatteḥ hetum vinā bhavataḥ ahetuka tva prasaṅgāt atīta anāga tañca karma avidyamāna tvāt asat eva pāka ādi nirvarttikā śaktiḥ pācaka ādi vyapadeśa hetuḥ iti ced āha na ca śaktiḥ ananvayāt 
PVV_3.157–3.173,12–3.157–3.173,15	 śaktiḥ hi dravyāt abhinnā bhinnā vā pratipannāḥ abhinnā ced tadā dravya vadananvayān na ca anvayinaḥ anvayi śabda hetu tāḥ atha bhinnā tadā anupakārakayoḥ sambandha anupapatteḥ dravyeṇa upakriyamāṇā śaktiḥ tad sambandhinī iti vaktavyam atra api dravyam śakti antareṇa svayam eva asamartha svabhāva tayā śaktim upakaroti iti vācyam ādye anavasthā dvitīye tu kāryam eva kin na karoti iti alam śakti svīkāreṇa sāmānyam pācaka tva ādi yadi prāk eva tat bhavet vyaktam sattā ādi vat no ced na paścāt aviśeṣataḥ kriyā upakāra apekṣasya vyañjaka tve avikāriṇaḥ atiśaye vā hi api asya kṣaṇika tvāt kriyā kutas 
PVV_3.157–3.173,16	 abhinna abhidhāne nimittam sāmānyam eva pācaka tva ādi yat i iṣyate tadā pāka ādi kriyātaḥ prāk eva tat pācaka tva ādi sāmānyam dravya utpattau= eva vyaktam bhavet no ced prāk avyaktam na paścāt api vyaktam syāt aviśeṣatas viśeṣa abhāvāt nitya eka rūpasya sāmānyasya kriyāyāḥ karmaṇaḥ pāka ādi na upakāraḥ tad apekṣasya dravyasya pācaka tva ādi sāmānya vyañjaka tve ca iṣyamāṇe avikāriṇaḥ sthirasya dravyasya apekṣā na asti atiśaye vā prāk avasthātaḥ svīkriyamāṇe kṣaṇika tvam syāt kṣaṇika tvāt utpatti anantara vināśi tvāt kriyā karma kutas sambhavati utpatti anantaram sthitau hi karma kuryāt sā ca kṣaṇikasya na asti iti na tena upakāropi 
PVV_3.157–3.173,17–3.157–3.173,19	 tulye bhede yayā jātiḥ pratyāsattyā prasarpati kvacid na anyatra sā eva astu śabda jñāna nibandhanam vastu bhūta sāmānya vādinā upi vyaktīnām tulye bhede parasparam eka artha karaṇa ādikayā yayā pratyāsattyā kvacid vyaktau śāvaleya bāhuleyayoḥ jātiḥ sā eva pratyāsattiḥ abhinnasya śabda jñānasya nibandham astu kim pramāṇa antara bādhita jāti svīkāreṇa 
PVV_3.157–3.173,20–3.157–3.173,23	 sām khyā prāhuḥ na nivṛttim vihāya asti yadi bhāva anvaya uparaḥ ekasya kāryam anyasya na syāt atyanta bhedataḥ yadi nivṛttim vijātīya vyavacchedam vihāya bhāvānām satva rajaḥ tamaḥ sāmya avasthā svabhāva prakṛti ātmanā advayaḥ eka rūpaḥ anvayaḥ aparaḥ na asti tat ekasya kāryam aṅkuraḥ anyasya kṣiti ādeḥ na syāt bīja kṣiti ādīnām atyantabhe aṅkura kārakam yat rūpam bījasya tat ced kṣiti ādeḥ nna asti na syāt asau tad kārakaḥ astitve ca eka rūpa anvayaḥ 
PVV_3.157–3.173,24–3.157–3.173,29	 siddhāntavādi āha yadi eka ātma tayā anekaḥ kāryasya ekasya kārakaḥ ātmā ekatra api vā asti iti vyarthāḥ syuḥ sahakāriṇaḥ yadi eka ātma tayā anekaḥ bīja śalila ādiḥ kāryasya aṅkurasya ekasya kārakaḥ tadā aṅkura kārakaḥ ātmā anuyāyī ekatra api bīje anyatra vā asti iti vyarthāḥ sahakāriṇaḥ ekatra vidyamānena eva tena ātmanā kārya utpatteḥ na apaiti abhinnam tat rūpam viśeṣāḥ khalu a pāyinaḥ eka apāye phala abhāvāt viśeṣebhyaḥ tad udbhavaḥ 
PVV_3.157–3.173,30	 sahakāriṇām abhāvepi bīja satve abhinnam tat pradhānam karttṛ rūpam na apaiti nitya tvāt vyakti satvāt ca viśeṣāḥ khalu nūnam apāyinaḥ na pradhānam ekasya sahakāriṇaḥ viśeṣasya apāyepi phalasya abhāvāt viśeṣebhyaḥ tasya kāryasya udbhavaḥ niścīyate na pradhānāt viśeṣasya anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānāt sāmānyasya viparyayāt 
PVV_3.157–3.173,31–3.157–3.173,36	 sa pāramārthikaḥ bhāvaḥ yaḥ eva artha kriyā kṣamaḥ sa ca na anveti yonvā iti na tasmāt kārya sambhavaḥ saḥ eva pāramārthikaḥ bhāvaḥ yortha kriyā kṣamaḥ viśeṣa urtha kriyā kṣamaḥ na anveti parasparam bhedāt yaḥ anveti pradhāna ākhyaḥ bhāvaḥ na tasmāt kāryasya yadi eka rūpān anugamaḥ tadā viśeṣeṣu api kecid janayanti na aparaḥ iti kutoyaṃvibhāgaḥ iti āha tena ātmanā api bhede hi hetuḥ kaścid na ca aparaḥ svabhāva uyam abhede tu syātām nāśa udbhavau sakṛt 
PVV_3.157–3.173,37	 yena eka rūpa anvaye sahakāri vaikalya prasaṅgaḥ tena kāraṇena ātmanā sva rūpeṇa bīja jala śilā anala ādīnām bhedepi kaścid kṣiti śalila bīja ādiḥ aṅkurasya hetuḥ na śilā anala ādiḥ hi yasmāt svabhāva uyam aṅkura janana śaktaḥ tad itaraḥ ca pramāṇa dṛṣṭaḥ bīja ādīnām śilā ādīnān ca na atra paryanuyoga avatāraḥ kutas utpannaḥ iti ced sva sva hetoḥ sā upi kasmāt tad janakaḥ iti ced sva hetoḥ tatra api praśne tat eva uttaram anādiḥ ca hetu phala paraṃpara eka rūpa anugamāt viśeṣāṇām abhedetu svīkriyamāṇe sakṛt ekasya nāśodbha viśeṣa antarayoḥ yathāsaṃbhavam nāśaḥ janmani ca tad aparasya viśeṣasya tad abhinna rūpa tayā nāśa udbhavau syātāḥ 
PVV_3.157–3.173,38–3.157–3.173,40	 bheda upi tena na evam ced yaḥ ekasmin vinaśyati tiṣṭhati ātmā na tasya atas na syāt sāmānya bheda dhīḥ atha parasparam viśeṣāṇām ekāntena nābhedaḥ kintarhi bhedaḥ viśeṣa rūpa tayā tena bhedena evam sakṛt nāśa udbhava prasaṅgaḥ na ced yadi ekasmin viśeṣe vinaśyati tiṣṭhati ātmā anuyāyī pradhāna ākhyaḥ tadā sa tasya viśeṣasya ātmā na bhavati na hi yasmin vinaśyati yaḥ na naṣṭaḥ sa tasya svabhāvaḥ viruddha dharma adhyāsa lakṣaṇa tvāt abhedasya atas parasparam sarvu athā bhedāt na syāt sāmānya bheda dhīḥ anvayi sāmānyam ananvayī bhedaḥ ucyate yadā ca sāmānyam bhedāt bhinnam tadā anugāmi vyakti svarūpam na sāmānyam na ca tad ātmakaḥ bhedaḥ atas tat buddhiḥ api na bhavet 
PVV_3.157–3.173,41–3.157–3.173,44	 nanu anya nivṛttau= api samānam etat bhāve naśyati anya nivṛttiḥ naśyati na vā yadi naśyati na syāt vyakti antare tad buddhiḥ atha na naśyati tadā atyanta bhedāta sāmānya bheda buddhiḥ na syāt iti āha nivṛtteḥ niḥsvabhāva tvāt na sthāna āsthāna kalpanā upaplavaḥ ca sāmānya dhiyaḥ tena api adūṣaṇā nivṛtteḥ niḥsvabhāva tvāt na sthāna āsthānayoḥ sthiti nivṛttyoḥ kalpanā yuktāḥ kalpitā hi anya nivṛttiḥ niḥsvabhāvā sā kim bhāvāt bhinnā abhinnā vā iti na yuktā kalpanā na hi śaśa viṣāṇam bhinnam abhinnam vā iti yuktam kalpiyitum upaplavaḥ mithyā tvañca sāmānya dhiyaḥ viṣaya abhāvāt tena na api adūṣaṇā

PVV_3.175,0–3.175,4	 paryāyeṇa atha karttṛ tvam sa kim tasya eva vastunaḥ atha kāraka eka svabhāva anugamāt sahakāriṇām paryāyeṇa karttṛ tvam sa paryāyaḥ tasya anvayinaḥ ekasya vastunaḥ kim kasmāt yuktaḥ na hi ekam vastu kārya kurvvata paryāyeṇa na karoti iti yuktam vyapadeṣṭum tena eva kriyamāṇa tvāt sahakāriṇām bahūnām paryāyeṇa kriyā sambhāvyate teṣu ca ekasya kārakam rūpam anyatra na asti iti na te kuryuḥ sarvu eṣān ca sva hetu vala āyātaḥ eka kārya kārakaḥ svabhāvaḥ asmābhiḥ iva sām khyaiḥ rneṣyate kiñca atyanta bheda abhedau tu syātām tadvati vastuni tadvati sāmānya viśeṣavati vastuni svīkriyamāṇe atyantam ekāntena sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ bheda abhedaḥ syātām sāmānya svarūpa tvāt bhedasya sāmānyam eva bhavet na bhedaḥ bheda ātma tvāt sāmānyasya bhedaḥ eva bhavet sāmānyam 
PVV_3.176–3.184aba,0–3.176–3.184aba,5	 atha tayoḥ kathañcana bheda upyasti iti ced āha anyonyam vā tayoḥ bhedaḥ sadṛśā sadṛśa ātmanoḥ tayoḥ sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ sadṛśā sadṛśa ātmanoḥ sādhāraṇā sādhāraṇa svarūpayoḥ anyonyam bhedaḥ eva vā bhavet na kathañcid eka tvam etat eva sphuṭayitum pūrvvapakṣayati tayoḥ api bhavet bhedaḥ yadi yena ātmanā tayoḥ bhedaḥ sāmānyam iti etat yadi bhedaḥ tad ātmanā bhedaḥ eva 
PVV_3.176–3.184aba,6	 na sarvu ātmanā abhedaḥ tayoḥ sāmānya viśeṣoḥ api kathañcid bhedaḥ anyathā sāmānya viśeṣa bhāva anupapattiḥ atra āha yena ātmanā sva rūpeṇa sādhāraṇena ca asādhāraṇena ca tayoḥ sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ bhedaḥ sāmānyam viśeṣaḥ iti etat vyavasthāpyate tena ātmanā sādhāraṇa asādhāraṇena yadi bhedaḥ tadā bhedaḥ eva tayoḥ syāt bhinna lakṣaṇa tvāt 
PVV_3.176–3.184aba,7–3.176–3.184aba,11	 tathā ca syāt niḥsāmānya viśeṣa tā bheda sāmāni ayoḥ yadvat ghaṭa ādīnām parasparam tathā ca niḥsāmānya viśeṣa tā samānya viśeṣa rūpa tā abhāvaḥ sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ abhitayoḥ syāt yadvat ghaṭa ādīnām viśeṣāṇām parasparam na sāmānya viśeṣa tā viśeṣaḥ sva lakṣaṇa rūpam anugāmi sāmānyam tat eva anugāmi viśeṣaḥ ucyate yadi tu tayoḥ bhedaḥ eva na sāmānya viśeṣa bhāvaḥ syāt yam a ātmānam puraskṛtya puruṣoyam pravartate tad sādhya phala vān chāvān bheda abhedau tad āśrayau cintyate sva ātmanā bhedaḥ 
PVV_3.176–3.184aba,12	 api ca ayam vyavahārī puruṣaḥ yam arthasya ātmānam svabhāvam puraskṛtya pravṛtti viṣaya tvena āgraham kṛtvā tad sādhya phala vān chāvān artha sādhya phala samīhā yuktaḥ sana pravarttate tad āśrayau tad artha viṣayau bheda abhedau śāstra kāraiḥ cinti ete na tu artha kriyā anupayukta sāmānya viṣayau teṣāñca artha kriyā kāriṇām puruṣa pravṛtti viṣayāṇām arthānām sva ātmanā sva rūpeṇa bhedaḥ 
PVV_3.176–3.184aba,13–3.176–3.184aba,16	 katham tarhi ekabuddhi śabda viṣaya tā iti āha vyāvṛttyā ca samāna tā asti eva vastu na anveti pravṛtti ādi prasaṅgataḥ vijātīyāt vyāvṛtyā ca sā samāna tā asti eva sva svabhāva niyatantu sva lakṣaṇam vastu na anveti sarvu atra pravṛtti ādi prasaṅgataḥ agniḥ api śalila svabhāvaḥ eva iti śalila arthī tatra api pravartteta tasmāt sthitam etat na kiñcid kim api anveti iti 
PVV_3.176–3.184aba,17–3.176–3.184aba,20	 etena eva yadāhrīkāḥ kim api ayuktam ākulam pralapanti pratikṣiptam tat api ekānta sambhavāt etena sām khya mata nirākaraṇena eva ahrīkā di ga mba rāyatsyāt uṣṭraḥ dadhi ti kim api ayukta tayā heya upādeya viṣaya apariniṣṭhānāt ākulam pralapanti tat api pratikṣiptam ekāntasya bhedasya sambhavāt ākula tvam eva ākhyātum āha 
PVV_3.176–3.184aba,21–3.176–3.184aba,24	 sarvaṃsya ubhaya rūpa tve tad viśeṣa nirākṛteḥ coditaḥ dadhi khāde ti kim uṣṭram na abhidhāvati sarvu asya vastunaḥ ubhayarupa tve sva para rūpa tve sati tad viśeṣasya dadhyeva dadhinā uṣṭra auṣṭraḥ eva uṣṭraḥ na dadhīti asya bhedasya nirākṛteḥ dadhi khāda iti coditaḥ niyojyaḥ kim uṣṭram prati na abhidhāvati atha arasti atiśayaḥ kaśicat yena bhedena varttate 
PVV_3.176–3.184aba,25–3.176–3.184aba,29	 saḥ eva viśeṣaḥ anyatra na asti iti anubhayam param atha asti dadhnaḥ sakāśāt uṣṭrasya atiśayaḥ viśeṣaḥ kaścid yena viśeṣeṇa coditena bhedena pratiniyamena dadhi śabdāt dadhnī eva uṣṭra śabdāt uṣṭraḥ eva pravarttate evantarhi sa viśeṣaḥ eva anyatra asambhavī uṣṭraḥ viśeṣaḥ dadhi lakṣaṇaḥ anyatra vastuni na asti iti sarvvam vastu anubhayam na sva para rūpam kintu param eva parasmāt kiñca sarvvātma tve ca sarvu eṣām bhinnau syātām na dhī dhvanī bheda saṃhāra vādasya tad abhedāt asambhavaḥ 
PVV_3.176–3.184aba,30	 sarvu eṣām bhāvānām sarvu ātma tve ca bhinnau dhī dhvanī na syātām eka viṣaya tvāt tayoḥ dhī dhvanyoḥ abhedāt bheda saṃhāra vādasya asambhavaḥ syāt uṣṭrāt bhinnam dadhi iti bheda vyavahāraḥ dadhyeva uṣṭraḥ iti ca tad ātma tā upasaṃhāra vyavahāraḥ ca buddhi śabdayoḥ abhedāt na syāt na hi buddhi śabdayoḥ bheda vyavahāraḥ yuktaḥ tad nibandhana tvāt tasya tad abhāvepi bhāve ca atiprasaṅgāt bheda pratītyoḥ bhāvāt tādātmya upasaṃhāraḥ ca katham tad adhīna tvāt tasya 
PVV_3.184cd–3.200,0–3.184cd–3.200,2	 dravya abhāvāt abhāvasya śabdāḥ rūpa abhidhāyinaḥ na āśaṅkyāḥ eva siddhāḥ te atas vyavat cheda vācakāḥ uktam tāvat bhāva ādi śabdānām vyavaccheda viṣaya tvam yepi abhāva ādi śabdāḥ abhāvasya svarūpa abhāvāt tepi rūpa abhidhāyinaḥ vastu vācakāḥ na aśaṅakyāḥ eva sambhavat vastu vācyam syāt na vā iti cintyeta api yatra tu vastu eva na asti tatra kā cintā atas te abhāva ādi śabdāḥ vyavacchedasya bhāva vyāvṛtteḥ vvācakāḥ siddhāḥ tasmāt sthitam etat svabhāva hetoḥ vvastutas sādhya ātmaka tvepi na pratijñā artha eka deśaḥ hetuḥ sādhya sādhana dharmi dhvani vikalpānām bhinna vyavaccheda viṣaya tvāt na ca sādhya ādīnām kalpita tvam bhedasya kalpanāt śabda tvena niścitaḥ dharmī sattvena ca hetuḥ kṣaṇika tvena niścitaḥ sādhyaḥ iti akalpitāḥ eva dharmya ādayaḥ iti uktam 
PVV_3.184cd–3.200,3–3.184cd–3.200,6	 sa ca ayam svabhāvaḥ hetuḥ upādhi bheda apekṣaḥ vā svabhāvaḥ kevalaḥ athavā ucyate sādhya sidhi artham nāśe kāryatva sattva vat kvacid upādhi bhedaḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣaḥ bhinnaḥ abhinnaḥ vā tad apekṣaḥ kevalaḥ viśeṣaṇa rahitaḥ śuddha ūthavā sādhya sidhi artham ucyate nāśe kāryatva sattva vat nāśe sādhye kārya tvam bhinna viśeṣaṇa apekṣaḥ svabhāvaḥ tad janmani apekṣita para vyāpārasya kāryatvāt evam pratyaya bheda bhedi tva ādayaḥ draṣṭavyāḥ utpattimatvam punar abhinna viśeṣaṇam utpattyā svabhāva bhūtayā kalpita bhedayā viśeṣaṇāt sattvantu kevalam nāśaḥ eva sādhye svabhāvaḥ viśeṣaṇa anupādānāt 
PVV_3.184cd–3.200,7–3.184cd–3.200,9	 sattā svabhāvaḥ hetuḥ ced sā sattā sādhyate katham bhedena ananvayāt soyam vyāhataḥ hetu sādhyayoḥ nanu sattā svabhāvaḥ hetuḥ ced abhimataḥ sāmānya rūpaḥ viśeṣasya ananvayāt tadā pradhāna ākhyā sarvu avyakti vyāpinī katham sādhyate acetana tva ādi hetoḥ atha bhedānām parasparam atyantam bhedena ananvayāt na sādhyate tadā soyam bhedānām ananvayaḥ hi hetu sādhyayoḥ vyāhitaḥ 
PVV_3.184cd–3.200,10–3.184cd–3.200,14	 artha ananvayinaḥ sādhya tā na yuktā tathā sādhana tā api tat katham sattvam sādhanam tasmāt sattā sāmānyam sādhyañca sādhanañcān anvayāt syāt atra āha bhāva upādāna mātre tu sādhye sāmānya dharmiṇi na kaścid arthaḥ siddhaḥ syāt aniṣiddhañca tādṛśam bhāvaḥ sattā sā upādānam viśeṣaṇam yasya sa bhāva upādānaḥ saḥ eva kevalaḥ tanmātram tasmin sādhye sāmānya dharmiṇi sāmānya dharmavati na kaścid arthaḥ pradhāna siddhi lakṣaṇaḥ sām khya sya siddhaḥ syāt satva mātra viśeṣaṇasya dharmiṇaḥ sādhanāt aniṣiddhañca tādṛśam sādhyam bhedānām satvasya iṣṭa tvāt 
PVV_3.184cd–3.200,15–3.184cd–3.200,17	 upātta bhede sādhyesmin bhavet hetuḥ ananvayaḥ sattāyām tena sādhyāyām viśeṣaḥ sādhitaḥ bhavet atha eka sukha ādi ātmakam iti apradhāna viśeṣaṇa viśeṣitam sattvam sādhyam tadā upātta bhede sattve bhavet hetuḥ ananvayaḥ anvaya rahitaḥ pradhānasya kvacid anvaya asiddheḥ sāmānyam eva punar kinna sādhyate sāmānye sādhye siddha sādhana doṣāt sattāyām sādhyāya āmiṣṭāyām tena vādinā viśeṣaḥ eva abhimataḥ sādhitaḥ bhavet 
PVV_3.184cd–3.200,18–3.184cd–3.200,23	 atra ca ananvaya doṣaḥ uktaḥ asmākantu aparāmṛṣṭa tad bhede vastu mātre tu sādhane tanmātra vyāpinaḥ sādhyasya anvayaḥ na vihanyate aparā muṣṭaḥ anadhyavasitaḥ tasya vastunaḥ bhedaḥ yasmin tasmin vastu mātre nitya tvasya anvayaḥ na vihanyate atas sādhana tvam sattvasya yuktam nanu dhūmāt agni sādhanepi samānam etat tathā hi yadi dhūmāt agni sattā mātram sādhyate tadā siddha sādhya tā atha parvvate asti iti sādhyate tadā anvayā siddhiḥ na etat asti na hi pakṣā yoga vyavacchedaḥ tam agnim viśeṣīkaroti anagni vyāvṛttasya sādhanāt sattā sādhane tu tat sattva viśeṣaḥ eva pradhāna ākhyaḥ sādhyaḥ 
PVV_3.184cd–3.200,24–3.184cd–3.200,27	 kiñca na asiddhe bhāva dharma usti vyabhicāryu bhaya āśrayaḥ dharmaḥ viruddhaḥ abhāvasya sā sattā sādhyate katham sattāyām sādhanam acetana tvādi iṣṭam sadbhāva dharmaḥ abhāva dharmaḥ ubhaya dharmaḥ vā bhavet tatra sādhanāt prāc asiddhe bhāve bhāva dharmaḥ na asti iti asiddhā asau ubhaya āśrayaḥ bhāva abhāva dharmaḥ ca vyabhicārya naukāntikaḥ na hi ubhaya dharmaḥ ekāntena eka sattām gamayati amūrta tvam iva vastu tām abhāvasya tu dharmaḥ viruddhaḥ asattva sādhanāt tatas trividha doṣa duṣṭa tvāt sādhanasyasā sattā katham sādhyate 
PVV_3.184cd–3.200,28–3.184cd–3.200,31	 sādhana pakṣetu sattā dharmiṇi siddha tvāt na asiddhāḥ anitya tā vyāpti prāpteḥ virodha vyabhicārau ca apāḥ tau tasmāt siddhaḥ svabhāvaḥ gamakaḥ atas gamyaḥ tasya vyāpakaḥ siddhaḥ svabhāva niyataḥ sva nivṛttau nivartakaḥ vyāpya svabhāvaḥ sādhya ātma tayā siddhaḥ niścitaḥ gamakaḥ tasya vyāpyasya vyāpakaḥ svabhāvaḥ siddhaḥ gamyaḥ vyāpakasya tatra bhāvaḥ eva vyāpyasya ca tatra eva bhāvaḥ iti ubhaya dharma rūpāyāḥ vyāpteḥ siddha tvāt 
PVV_3.184cd–3.200,32–3.184cd–3.200,36	 atas ca ayaṃvyāpakaḥ sva nivṛttau tasya vyāpyasya nivarttakaḥ anena sādharmya vaidharmya prayogau= uddiṣṭau udāharaṇam āha anitya tve yathā kāryam akāryam vā avināśini ahetu tvāt vināśasya svabhāvāt anubandhitā anitya tve sādhye kārya hetuḥ yathā yat kṛtakam tat anityam tathā ghaṭaḥ kṛtakaḥ ca śabdaḥ iti sādharmya prayogaḥ akāryam akārya svabhāvaḥ vā avināśini nāśābhāvaḥ iti anitya tva nivṛttau kṛtaka tva nivṛttiḥ yathā ākāśe kṛtakaḥ ca śabdaḥ iti vaidharmya prayogaḥ katham punar gamyate sattva mātra anubandhinī naśvaratā iti āha ahetu tvāt ahetu kṛta tvāt vināśasya svabhāvāt vastu sattā mātreṇa anubandhitāḥ 
PVV_3.184cd–3.200,37–3.184cd–3.200,40	 kasmāt evam iti āha sa apekṣāṇām hi bhāvānām na avaśyam bhāviteṃkṣyate bāhulyepī iti ced tasya hetoḥ kvacid asambhavaḥ sa apekṣāṇām bhāvānām hi yasmāt avaśyaṃbhāvitāḥ na īkṣyate rāgasya iva vāsasi tatas ca kaścid ghaṭaḥ na vinaśyet api vināśakānām hetūnām bāhulyāt avaśyam iti ced bāhulyepi tasya nāśakasya hetoḥ kvacid ghaṭa ādau= asambhavaḥ syāt tad vyāghātakānām api bāhulyāt 
PVV_3.184cd–3.200,41–3.184cd–3.200,46	 etena vyabhicāri tvam uktam kārya avyavasthiteḥ sarveṣām nāśa hetūnām hetum at nāśa vādinām etena nāśa hetūnām pratirodha sambhavena hetum at nāśa vādinām matena nāśa hetūnām mudgara ādīnām sarvu eṣām nāśe kārye anumāpayitavye vyabhicāri tvam uktam boddhavyam kāryā vināśa hetoḥ vināśasya utpatti niyama abhāvāt katham punar vvināśasya ahetu ta iti āha asāmarthyāt ca tad hetoḥ bhavati eva svabhāvataḥ yatra nāma bhavati asmāt anyatra api svabhāvataḥ 
PVV_3.184cd–3.200,47	 asāmarthyāt ca tad hetoḥ vvinaśvarasya vā bhāvasya vināśaḥ kriyate nāśa hetunā tatra vinaśvarasya svayam eva vināśāt alam nāśa hetunā avinaśvarasya nāśam karttum na kaścid samarthaḥ ca śabdāt kriyā pratiṣedhaḥ syāt tathā hi abhāvaḥ yadi paryudāsaḥ bhāva antaram kapāla ādikam tadā tasya mudgara ādi hetuteṣyate eva tat utpādepi ghaṭasya na kiñcid iti prāgvat upalabdhi ādi prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt abhāvam karoti bhāvam na karoti iti syāt tathā ca ākarttuḥ ahetu tā eva tasmāt vināśa hetoḥ ayogāt eva vināśaḥ svabhāvataḥ sva hetoḥ bhavati asmāt iti bhāvaḥ hetuḥ yatra nāma vināśaḥ bhavati iti mudgarāt kapāla utpattau loka abhimānaḥ tatra vināśaka ayogāt sva hetoḥ eva vinaśvara svabhāvatayā utpatteḥ dvitīye kṣaṇe na bhavati iti vaktavyam tasmāt ahetu tva vyavasthānāt anyatra api yatra visadṛśa anutpattyā vināśa utpatti abhimānaḥ na asti tatra api svabhāvataḥ sva hetoḥ eva vinaśyati iti vināśaḥ eka kṣaṇa sthāyī bhāvaḥ jāyate 
PVV_3.184cd–3.200,48–3.184cd–3.200,51	 tathāvidhe ca bhāva mātra anurodhini vināśe satvam hetuḥ avyabhicāraḥ kāryasya kāraṇe tad adhīna tvāt iti uktam tat eva āha yā kācid bhāva viṣayā anumitiḥ dvividhā eva sā sva sādhye kārya bhāvābhyām sambandha niyamāt tayoḥ yā kācid bhāva viṣaya anumitiḥ sā dvividhā eva kārya bhāvābhyām hetubhyām kāraṇa vyāpaka viṣayā bhavantī tayoḥ kārya svabhāvayoḥ eva sva sādhye sambandhasya niyamāt anyasya tu sādhye anāpatteḥ atad ātma tvāt ca na avi abhicāra niyamaḥ 
PVV_3.184cd–3.200,52–3.184cd–3.200,55	 anupalabdheḥ api upalabdhi nivṛtti mātra lakṣaṇāyāḥ prāmāṇyam ākhyātum āha pravṛtteḥ buddhi pūrva tvāt tad bhāva anupalambhane pravarttitavyam na iti uktā anupalabdheḥ pramāṇa tā sat jñāna śabda vyavahārāṇāṃpravṛtteḥ buddhi pūrvvaka tvāt tasyāḥ buddheḥ bhāva anupalambhane kāraṇa abhāvāt pravartitavyam na iti sāmarthyāt sidhyati na hi kāraṇa abhāvam kāryam yuktam atas anupalabdheḥ upalabdhi nivṛttiḥ upāyāḥ pravṛtti niṣedhe sādhye pramāṇa tā uktā cā rye ṇa na piśāca ādikam ghaṭa ādikam sat iti vaktavyam anupalabdheḥ iti sat vyavahāra pratiṣedha mātram sādhyate na tu asattva vyavahāraḥ 
PVV_3.184cd–3.200,56–3.184cd–3.200,59	 yatra tarhi pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ śāstrasya nivṛttiḥ tasya abhāvaḥ eva sādhayitum yuktaḥ iti āha śāstra adhikāra asambaddhāḥ bahava ūrthāḥ atīndriyāḥ aliṅgāḥ ca kathanteṣām abhāva unupalabdhitaḥ śāstra adhikāre asambaddhā anena śāstra viṣaya tvam āha bahavaḥ arthāḥ aniyata kāraṇa upanipāta janyāḥ sūkṣmāḥ durllakṣa bhedāḥ manaḥ vṛttayaḥ janminām deśa phala vyavahitāḥ vā anutpannāḥ dravya viśeṣāḥ atīndriyāḥ anena pratyakṣa aviṣaya tām āha liṅgāt ca ananumeya tām āha teṣām arthānām pratyakṣa anumāna śāstra nivṛtti lakṣaṇāyāḥ anupalabdhitaḥ sādhayitum yuktaḥ sati api anupalambhe teṣām sattva sambhavāt 
PVV_3.184cd–3.200,60–3.184cd–3.200,64	 atas īdṛśī anupalabdhiḥ sat asat niścaya phalā na iti syāt vā apramāṇa tā pramāṇam api kācid syāt liṅga atiśaya bhāvinī sataḥ asat niścaya phalā na iti apramāṇa tā vā asyāḥ syāt sattva pratiṣedhe sādhye kācid tu anupalabdhiḥ lliṅga jā pratītiḥ asmin= eva sādhye pramāṇam api liṅga viśeṣa prabhavāḥ yathā uktam prāk hetu bheda vyapekṣayā iti upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta anupalabdhi liṅga jā iti arthaḥ svabhāva jñāpaka ajñānasya ayam nyāya udāhṛtaḥ 
PVV_3.184cd–3.200,65	 yat punar uktam apramāṇam anupalabdhiḥ iti yasya kasyacid svabhāvasya jñāpakasya liṅgasya ca ajñānasya anupalabdheḥ ayam nyāya udāhṛtaḥ na hi svabhāvaḥ na upalabhyataiti eva na asti deśa kāla svabhāva viprakṛṣṭānām adarśanepi sattva avirodhāt tatas na asti virakta cetaḥ iti ādya yuktam na ca kāraṇam iti eva kāryāṇi avyavadhānataḥ bhavanti tatas na asti dāna hiṃsā virati cetanānām abhyudaya hetu tā phala anantarya abhāva āditi a yuktam

PVV_3.219–3.223,15–3.219–3.223,20	 yatas ca sattva dṛṣṭiḥ avidyā mohaḥ nidānam doṣāṇām atra eva abhidhīyate satkāya dṛṣṭiḥ anyatra atas eva mohaḥ avidyā doṣāṇām nidānam abhidhīyate bhagavatā avidyāḥ hetukāḥ iti punar anyatra pradeśe satkāya dṛṣṭiḥ doṣa nidānam abhidhīyate nanu anyepi indriya viṣayāḥ yoni śoma naskāra ādayaḥ doṣa hetavaḥ tad kim avidyā sat kāya dṛṣṭiḥ eva abhihite iti āha tad prahāṇe prahāṇataḥ tasya mohasya sat kāya dṛṣṭi lakṣaṇasya prahāṇe doṣāṇām prahāṇataḥ prādhānyāt saḥ eva uktaḥ na itaraḥ iti arthaḥ 
PVV_3.224,0–3.225,1	 veda pramāṇyam nirācikīrṣan paramatam utthāpayati girām mithyātva hetūnām doṣāṇām puruṣa āśrayāt apauruṣeyam satya artham iti kecid pracakṣate girām vācām mithyātvaṃsya hetūnām doṣāṇām ajñāna visamvāda abhiprāya ādīnām vā puruṣasya āśrayāt āśrayaṇa tvāt apauruṣeyam vākyam mithyātva hetoḥ puruṣa doṣasya abhāvāt satya artham iti kecid jai mi nī yāḥ pracakṣate girām satya tva hetūnām guṇānām puruṣa āśrayāt apauruṣeyam mithyā artham kim na iti anye pracakṣate tān eva prati girām satya tvasya hetūnām dayā dharma paratva ādīnām guṇānām puruṣasya āśrayāt apauruṣeyam vākyam satya tā hetoḥ puruṣa guṇasya abhāvāt mithyā artham kim na bhavati iti anye sau ga tāḥ pracakṣate 
PVV_3.226,0–3.226,2	 kiñca artha jñāpana hetuḥ hi saṅketaḥ puruṣa āśrayaḥ girā ām apauruṣeya tvepi ataḥ mithyātva sambhavaḥ saṅketam antareṇa apauruṣeyāt api vākyāt artha pratīteḥ abhāvāt artha jñāpana hetuḥ iha saṅketaḥ svīkartavyaḥ sa ca puruṣa kṛta tvāt puruṣa āśrayaḥ atas saṃketasya puruṣa āśraya tvāt girā ām apauruṣeya tvepi mithyātvasya sambhavaḥ saṃketa vaśena vācaḥ artham bruvate sa ca doṣa āśrayeṇa puruṣeṇa kriyate iti tāsām na visaṃvāda śaṅkā nirāsaḥ pauruṣeya vākya vat iti vyartham apauruṣeya tva kalpanam 
PVV_3.227,0–3.227,2	 atha śabda arthayoḥ sambandhaḥ na pauruṣeyaḥ kintu svābhāvikaḥ tatas na mithyātva sambhavaḥ tadā sambandha apauruṣeya tve syāt pratītiḥ a saṃvidaḥ sambandha apauruṣeya tvepīṣyamāṇe syāt arthānām pratītiḥ a saṃvidaḥ avidyamāna saṅketa pratīteḥ puṃsaḥ na ced śabda arthayoḥ sāṃketikaḥ vācya vācaka tā sambandhaḥ kintu svābhāvikaḥ tadā agṛhīta śaṅkā ita upi śrutāt śabdāt artham pratipadyeta iti 
PVV_3.227,3–3.227,5	 atha saṃketāt satopi tasya sambandhasya abhivyakti pradīpa ādi vat ghaṭa ādeḥ atas na agṛhīta vyañjakasya vyaṅgya pratītiḥ tadā saṃketāt tad abhivyaktau= asamartha ani akalpanā saṃṅketāt tasya sambandhasya abhivyakta aviṣyamāṇāyām saṃketāt anyasya sambandhasya kalpanā asamarthā sambandha vyavasthāpanāya saṃketāt eva vācya vācaka bhāvasya kalpitasya ghaṭamāna tvāt hasta saṃjñā ādeḥ iva artha pratipādanasya 
PVV_3.228,0–3.228,4	 kiñca vācā kim ekena arthena saha vācya vācaka sambandhaḥ atha anekaiḥ tatra girām eka artha niyame na syāt artha antare gatiḥ girām ekasmin= arthe vācakatayā niyame sati saṃketa vaśāt anyatra arthe na syāt gatiḥ dṛśyate ca vivakṣātaḥ aneka artha abhidhānam aneka artha abhisambandhe viruddha vyakti sambhavaḥ anekaiḥ arthaiḥ vvācaka tva abhisambandhe viruddhasya arthasya vyakteḥ pratīteḥ sambhavaḥ syāt agniṣṭomaḥ svargasya sādhanam iti viparyaya upyavasīyeta tatas ca apravṛttiḥ eva syāt svargīrthinaḥ 
PVV_3.229,0–3.229,2	 atha aneka artha abhidhāyī api śabdaḥ puruṣeṇa saṅketāt abhimata artha abhidhāyi tvena niyamyate tadā apauruṣeya tāyāñca vyarthā syāt parikalpanā vācyaḥ ca hetuḥ bhinnānām sambandhasya vyavasthiteḥ apauruṣeya tāyāñca vyarthā parikalpanā syāt tad abhyupagamepi puruṣa svātantrya abhyupagamāt tadā arthebhyaḥ bhinnānām śabdānām taiḥ saha sambandhasya vyavasthiteḥ hetuḥ ca vācyoyena avyabhicāraḥ na hi śabda arthayoḥ tādātmyam bhedāt na api tad utpattiḥ artham antareṇa api vivakṣātaḥ śabda utpatteḥ anyathā ca avyabhicāra abhāvāt 
PVV_3.230,0–3.230,2	 uktam artham saṃgṛhṇāt na āha asaṃskārya tayā puṃbhiḥ sarvu athā syāt nirarthatā saṃskāra upagame mukhyam gaja snāna nibham bhavet yadi saṅketa nirapekṣāṇām svatas eva vācaka tvam śabdānām tadā apuṃbhi saṅketa dvāreṇa niyamya tayā sarvu athā nirarthatā syāt puruṣa saṅketa nirapekṣāt śabdāt arthaṃpratīteḥ abhāvāt etad doṣa bhayāt saṃskārasya upagame svīkāre idam apauruṣeya tvam mukhyam anupacaritam gajasnānam bhavet gajaḥ hi snāne paṅkam apanīya punar tena ātmānam limpati tathā apauruṣeya tvam sambandhasya svīkṛtya api punar saṅkete puruṣa apekṣā iti vyaktam sāmyam 
PVV_3.231–3.236aba,0–3.231–3.236aba,5	 sambandhi nām a nitya tvāt na saṃbandhā isti nityatā tathā sambandhinām arthānām anitya tvāt saṃbandhe nityatā na asti na hi āśraya apāye bhavati āśritam kiñca nityasya anupakārya tvāt akurvāṇaḥ ca na āśrayaḥ arthaiḥ atas sa śabdānām saṃskāryaḥ puruṣaiḥ dhiyā nityasya sambandhasya anupakārya tvāt akurvvāṇaḥ anupakurvvāṇaḥ śabdaḥ arthaḥ ca āśrayaḥ yuktaḥ yatas svābhāvika sambandha anupapattiḥ atas sambandhaḥ arthaiḥ saha śabdānām puruṣaiḥ vyavahartṛbhiḥ artha pratipādana abhiprāya anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānam āśritya dhiyā kalpikayā saṃskāryaḥ vyavasthāpyaḥ 
PVV_3.231–3.236aba,6–3.231–3.236aba,10	 atha anityaḥ eva sambandhaḥ tadā sambandhinām nāśe sambandhasya naṣṭa tvāt nirarthakaḥ śabdaḥ syāt athavā arthaiḥ eva saha utpāde na svabhāva viparyayaḥ śabdeṣu yuktaḥ vācyaiḥ arthaiḥ eva saha sambandhasya utpādaḥ iṣyate tadā utpādaḥ iṣyamāṇepi pūrvvam arthena saha sambandhasya vinaṣṭa tvāt artha sambandha rahita ātmasu śabdeṣu svabhāvasya sambandha vikalasya viparyayaḥ sambandha yogī na yuktaḥ na hi nityasya pūrvva apara eka svabhāvasya anyathātvam yuktam anyathā nitya tā hāni prasaṅgāt 
PVV_3.231–3.236aba,11–3.231–3.236aba,16	 asmad mate tu sambandhe na ayam doṣaḥ vikalpite vikalpite kalpanā nirmite sambandhe ayam svabhāva anyatva prasaṅga doṣaḥ na bhavati na hi kalpanāk lṛptaḥ dharmaḥ svabhāvam vastutas spṛśati nitya tvāt āśraya apāyepya nāśaḥ yadi sammataḥ nityeṣu āśraya sāmarthyam kim yena iṣṭaḥ sa ca āśrayaḥ sambandhasya nitya tvāt āśrayasya vācyasya apāyepya nāśaḥ yadi jāteḥ iva sammataḥ tadā nityeṣu jāti sambandha ādiṣu āśrayasya vācyasyāḥ vācakasya ca kim sāmarthyam upakāra viśeṣa ādhāya kaṃyena sāmarthyena sa vācyadira āśrayaḥ iṣṭaḥ na hi anupakāryam āśrita m ati prasaṅgāt nityasya ca upakārāsambhavaḥ bheda abheda kalpanāyām ayukta tvāt 
PVV_3.231–3.236aba,17–3.231–3.236aba,23	 atha nityasya api jāti sambandha ādeḥ āśrayeṇa abhivyakti lakṣaṇaḥ upakāraḥ kriyate na ca avyakti hetuḥ kārakaḥ dīpa ādi vat ghaṭa ādeḥ iti āha jñāna utpādena hetūnām sambandhāt sahakāriṇām tad utpādana yogya tvena utpattiḥ vyaktiḥ iṣyate ghaṭa ādiṣu api yukti jñaiḥ jñāna utpādena hetūnām dīpa ādīnām sahakāriṇām sambandhāt tad utpādana yogya tvena jñāna utpādana samartha tvena utpattiḥ ghaṭa ādiṣu api bhāveṣu yukti jñaiḥ nyāya vidbhiḥ vyaktiḥ iṣyate anyathā jñāna utpādana yogyasya svabhāvasya anutpattau jñāna utpādanam na syāt aviśeṣe avikāriṇām vyañjakaiḥ svaiḥ kutas korthaḥ vyaktāḥ taiḥ te yatas matāḥ nityānām jāti sambandha ādīnām avikāriṇām kutaścid aviśeṣe viśeṣa asambhave svaiḥ vyañjakaiḥ āśraya abhimataiḥ korthaḥ svabhāvānyathātva ādiḥ kutas na kaścid yatas arthāt kṛtāt taiḥ vyañjakaiḥ te jāti ādayaḥ vyaktāḥ matāḥ 
PVV_3.236bc–3.246,0–3.236bc–3.246,3	 kiñca sambandhasya ca vastu tve syāt bhedāt buddhi citra tā tābhyām abhede tau= eva na atonyāḥ vastunaḥ gatiḥ yadi sambandhasya vastu tvanta dā vastu tve sati bhedaḥ abhedaḥ vā abhyupagantavyaḥ tatra bhedāt buddheḥ citra tā syāt vācya vācakau sambandhaḥ ca iti tritayam dṛśyeta na ca īkṣyate atha dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ tadā tābhyām abhede sambandhasya tau vācya vācakau= eva syātām na tu sambandhaḥ nāma kaścid atha sambandhaḥ na bhinnaḥ na api abhinnaḥ atas bheda abhedābhyām anyā vastunaḥ gatiḥ na asti anyonya vaccheda ātmaka tvāt anayaḥ rāśi antara asambhavān na anyaḥ prakāra usti vastunaḥ 
PVV_3.236bc–3.246,4–3.236bc–3.246,9	 tasmāt bhinna tvāt vastu rūpasya sambandhaḥ kalpanā kṛtaḥ sat dravyam syāt para adhīnam sambandhonyasya vā katham bhinna tvāt vastunoḥ sambandhinoḥ rūpasya sambandhaḥ śleṣa lakṣaṇaḥ kalpanayā kṛtaḥ na vāstavaḥ anyathā sat dravyam sambandha ākhyam para adhīnam sambandha āyattam katham syāt bhinnayoḥ sambandhinoḥ śleṣa lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ parasparam amiśra svabhāva tvāt saru u asya tathā api sambandha iti prasaṅgāt kiñca varṇṇāḥ nirarthakāḥ santaḥ 
PVV_3.236bc–3.246,10	 ayam sambandhaḥ varttamānaḥ varṇṇeṣu pada ādiṣu vā varttata tatra varṇṇāḥ santaḥ pratyekam teṣām artha pratipādaka tva abhāvāt nānā prayoktṛ prayuktebhyaḥ artha apratipatteḥ ca vyatikrama prayuktebhyaḥ ca saraḥ rasa ityādibhyaḥ tulyā syāt pratipattiḥ tad samudāyasya ca asambhavaḥ krameṇa upalambhāt na ca samudāyaḥ nāma samudāyibhyaḥ bhinnaḥ anupalambha bādhita tvāt teṣāñca vācaka tvāt ekasmāt api pratītiḥ syāt pratyekam na ced vācakāḥ samuditebhyopi tebhyaḥ na syāt pratītiḥ tadā api anyasya abhāvāt 
PVV_3.236bc–3.246,11	 atha krameṇa varṇṇeṣu gṛhīteṣu tad saṃskāra sahāyena adhyakṣeṇa gṛhīta ādantya varṇṇāt artha pratītiḥ tat kim antyaḥ eva varṇṇaḥ vācakaḥ na anye tathā tet vyartham teṣām uccāraṇam savveṣu pratīteṣu artha pratītiḥ iti ced kim antya varṇṇa grāhikayā buddhyā sarvu atra grahaṇam anya ani abuddhyā eva ced tāḥ kim buddhayaḥ antya varṇṇa buddhi kāle bhavanti yena tadā artha pratītiḥ ucyate anya anya kāle eva iti ced yadi tābhiḥ vvācakāḥ varṇṇāḥ gṛhyante ekaika varṇṇa grahaṇepi artha pratītiḥ syāt vācakeṣu sarvu aṣu gṛhīteṣu pratītiḥ iti ced tadā tu na pratyekam vācakaḥ tat atiriktaḥ ca samudāyaḥ na asti 
PVV_3.236bc–3.246,12	 pratyekam samarthāḥ sthiti bīja ādayaḥ aṅkura janane na ca kevala ajanayanti iti ced ye samarthāḥ na teṣām kṣaṇika tvāt pṛthak bhāvaḥ iti asamānam samuditāḥ eva tu samarthāḥ na tu evam varṇṇānām kvāpi samudāyaḥ krama upalabhya tvāt tadā ced pratipādakāḥ avācakāḥ eva pūrvva varṇṇa grahaṇa saṃskāra īpi kim antya varṇṇa buddhau sarvve pratibhānti na vā na tāvat upalabhyante tatas tat upadarśam api vyartham sarvu eṣu kramāt pratīteṣu smṛtiḥ samudāya viṣayā bhavati iti ced kimvarṇṇānām samudāya usti pratītaḥ vā yaḥ smaryate kevalam kalpyate kalpitasya vācaka tva abhyupagame na vivādaḥ tasmāt na varṇṇe sambandha vṛttiḥ 
PVV_3.236bc–3.246,13–3.236bc–3.246,18	 pada vākya ādiṣu tarhi syāt iti ced pada ādi parikalpitam avastuni katham vṛttiḥ sambandhasya asya vastunaḥ na hi krama uccāritebhyaḥ varṇṇebhyaḥ vyatiriktam pada ādikam upalabhyate kevalam kalpanā buddhyā krama uccāritānām varṇṇānām samudāyaḥ kalpitaḥ padam padānāñca samudāyaḥ kalpitaḥ vākyam ucyate tat ca kalpita tvāt avastu avastuni na hi śaśa viśāṇasya nīla ādi ḥ ddharmaḥ yuktaḥ tat evam na sambandhaḥ nityaḥ anityaḥ vā yuktaḥ iti sthitam apauruṣeya tā āpi iṣṭā karttṛṇāma smṛteḥ kila santi asya api anuvaktāraḥ iti dhik vyāpakam tamaḥ 
PVV_3.236bc–3.246,19	 veda vākyānām apauruṣeya tā api kenaci nmī mām sa kaḥ pravareṇa iṣṭā karttṛṇāma smṛteḥ liṅgāt kila akṣamāyām kila śabdaḥ asya api arthasya nyāyāt dūram āyātasya anuvaktāraḥ paṇḍitaṃmanyāḥ santi tasya eva tāvat īdṛśam prajñā skhalitam katham vṛttam iti sa vismaya anukampannaḥ cetaḥ tat api apare anuvadanti iti nirdaya ākrānta bhuvanam dhik avya apakantamaḥ tathā hi karttuḥ smaraṇam asiddham smaranti saugatāḥ mantrāṇām kartṝn aṣṭaka ādīn kā ṇādā śca vi dhā tāḥ ram mithyā tad smaraṇañcet ku mā rasa mbha vā deḥ api kā li dā sa ādi karttṛ smaraṇam mithyā iti tat api apauruṣā iyam tatra ekam smaraṇam apramāṇam anyat ca anyathā iti na atra vibhāga kāraṇam bahūnām saṃpratipatti vipratipattayaḥ ca na pramāṇa itara lakṣaṇe samvāda satvena sidhyataḥ tatas ca asmṛta karttṛkam iti aśakya niścayam sandigdha vipakṣa vyāvṛttika tvāt 
PVV_3.236bc–3.246,20–3.236bc–3.246,22	 yathā ayam anyatas aśrutvā na imam varṇa pada kramam vaktum samarthaḥ puruṣaḥ tathā anyopī iti kaścana yadā api vedān adhīyānaḥ yathā ayam idāni intanaḥ māṇavakaḥ anyatas upādhyāyāt aśrutvā mucyamānam varṇṇa padayoḥ kramamānupūru vī viśiṣṭām veda ākhyām vaktum asamarthaḥ vedaka pāṭhaka tvāt tathā anyaḥ upādhyāyaḥ tat upādhyāya upīti anādiḥ eṣa kramaḥ itikaści nmī mām sa kaḥ sarvu asya eva veda pāṭhaḥ para upadeśāt iti nitya tā eva vedānām 
PVV_3.236bc–3.246,23–3.236bc–3.246,26	 tatra api āha anyaḥ vā racitaḥ granthaḥ sampradāyāt ṛte paraiḥ dṛṣṭaḥ kaḥ abhihitaḥ yena sopyevam na anumīyate anyaḥ vā veda āditaraḥ kāvya ādiḥ granthaḥ racitaḥ kavi prabhṛtibhiḥ saṃpradāyāt ṛte upadeśāt vinā paraiḥ adhyetṛbhiḥ abhihitaḥ kaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ na kaścid yena para upadeśe asati aśakya adhyayana tvena sa upi kāvya ādiḥ evam nityam na anumīyate tatra api hetuḥ ayam siddhaḥ eva atha puruṣeṇa tad karaṇa avirodhāt sandigdha vyatireka tā asya hetoḥ tadā vedepi duṣṭa tvam asyāḥ katham nivāryam 
PVV_3.236bc–3.246,27–3.236bc–3.246,30	 api ca yat jātīyaḥ yatas siddhaḥ saḥ aviśiṣṭa ugni kāṣṭha vat adṛṣṭa hetuḥ api anyaḥ tad bhavaḥ saṃpratīyate yat jātīyaḥ yad dravya samāna jātīyaḥ yaḥ padārthaḥ yatas hetoḥ siddhaḥ anvaya vyatirekābhyām niścitaḥ sa tad jātīya tvena aviśiṣṭaḥ anyaḥ adṛṣṭa hetuḥ api tad hetuka tvena saṃpratīyate kim iva agni kāṣṭha vat kāṣṭha kārya tvena vahneḥ niścita tvāt vahni darśanāt adṛṣṭam api kāṣṭham anumīyate na ca vaidika pauruṣeya vākyānām kaścid bhedaḥ sarvu eṣām durbhaṇa tva ādīnām mantra ādi sāma arthya anāñca sādhāraṇa tvāt 
PVV_3.236bc–3.246,31–3.236bc–3.246,34	 idānīm veda karaṇa samartha puruṣa adarśanam bhās ra tādiṣu api samānam tatas asati avāntara bhede bhedāt hetu upanyāsaḥ na yuktaḥ sati tu vastutas tatra apradarśya ye bhedam kārya sāmānya darśanāt hetavaḥ pravitanyante sarve te vyabhicāriṇaḥ tatra sādhanīkṛte vastuni avāntara bhede bhedam apradarśya kārya sāmānyasya vijātīya vyāvṛtti mātrasya darśanāt ye hetavaḥ yad veda adhyayanam tad veda adhyayana pūrvvakam na karaṇa pūrvvakam yathā yaḥ pathika agniḥ sa jvālā pūrvvakaḥ na vāraṇi nirmathana pūrvvakaḥ ityādayaḥ pravitanyante vistāryante sarvva te vyabhicāriṇaḥ anaikāntikāḥ na hi veda adhyayanam iti eva adhyayana pūrvvakam kṛtvā karaṇa pūrvvakasya api adhyayanasya upapatteḥ araṇi nirmathanasya ca vahneḥ bhāva avirodhāt 
PVV_3.236bc–3.246,35–3.236bc–3.246,38	 bhavatu vā sarvu athā anāditā siddhyet evam na apuruṣa āśrayaḥ tasmāt apauruṣeya tve syāt anya upya nara āśrayaḥ evam veda adhyayanam adhyayana pūrvvatāsāḥ dhanam tathā api sarvu athā anāditāḥ veda adhyayanasya sidhyet ḍimbhaka pāṃśu krīḍā ādīnām iva na apuruṣa āśrayaḥ puruṣa āśrayaṇa abhāvaḥ tu na sidhyet ḍimbhaka pāṃśu krīḍā ādayaḥ hi darśana pūrvvakāḥ anādayaḥ ca na ca apauruṣeyāḥ ḍimbhakaiḥ eva kriyamāṇa tvāt evam śabdāḥ api adhyetṛbhiḥ eva kriyante na tu svayam ātmānam dhvanayanti yena apauruṣeyāḥ syuḥ anādiḥ tādṛś karaṇa kramaḥ puruṣa paraṃparāyāḥ anādeḥ āgata tvāt atha anādi tvā deva apauruṣeya tā iti āha tasya anādi tvāt apauruṣeya tve sādhye syāt anyaḥ pyapauruṣeyaḥ anara āśrayaḥ iti prasaṅgaḥ 
PVV_3.236bc–3.246,39–3.236bc–3.246,45	 tam eva āha mleccha ādi vyavahārāṇām nāstikya vacasām api anādi tvāt tathā abhāvaḥ mleccha ādeḥ vyavahārāṇām mātṛ vivāha mukti prāpaṇa māraṇa ādīnām nāstikyavaca para loka karma phala ādi apavādi nām anādi tvāt tathā abhāvaḥ apauruṣeya tvam syāt yadi pauruṣeyāḥ katham anādayaḥ iti āha pūrva saṃskāra santateḥ pūrvva saṃskārāt anādeḥ santateḥ santānena pravṛtteḥ 
PVV_3.236bc–3.246,46–3.236bc–3.246,48	 atha anādi tvāt mleccha ādi vyavahārāṇāñca apauruṣeya tā astitvāha tādṛśe apauruṣeya tve kaḥ siddhepi guṇaḥ bhavet tādṛśe mleccha ādi vyavahāra sādhāraṇe apauruṣeya tve siddhepi kaḥ guṇaḥ avisamvādaka lakṣaṇaḥ bhavet pauruṣeya vākyānām visamvāda adarśanādapauruṣeya tvam iṣṭam sa ca tasmin= api sati mleccha ādi vyavahārāṇām iva duṣpariharaḥ 
PVV_3.247,0–3.247,5	 atha veda vākyānām eva anādi tvāt apauruṣeya tvam tadā artha saṃskāra bhedānām darśanāt saṃśayaḥ punar arthasya saṃskāraḥ vyākhyānam tasya bhedānām vikalpānām prakṛti pratyaya aneka artha tvāt rūḍheḥ nirukta ādibhyaḥ ca yathāpratibham puṃsān darśanāt saṃśayaḥ artha niścaya abhāvaḥ kasya ca apauruṣeya tvam iṣṭam kimvarṇṇānām uta pada vākyānām iti āha anya aviśeṣāt varṇṇānām sādhane kim phalam bhavet anyaiḥ lokikaiḥ varṇṇaiḥ vaidikānām aviśeṣāt pratyabhijñāyamāna tvena eka tvāt apauruṣeya tvasya sādhane kim phalam bhavet tathā tve laukikānām artha vyabhicārāt 
PVV_3.248–3.250,0–3.248–3.250,2	 vākyam bhinnam na varṇebhyaḥ vidyate anupalambhataḥ aneka avayava ātma tve pṛthak teṣām nirarthatā atad rūpe ca tādrūpyam kalpitam siṃhatā ādi vat vākyam padañca varṇṇebhyaḥ bhinnam na vidyate anupalambhāt tat katham asya apauruṣeya tvam sādhyam abhinnam ced tadā aneka avayava ātma tve vākyasya teṣām avayavānām pṛthak pratyekam nirarthaka tā iti pada ātmakam anarthakam eva syāt tatas ca ātad rūpe avācaka rūpe tādrūpyam vācaka tvam kalpitam kalpanā buddhi nirmitam māṇavaka ādau= iva siṃhatā ādi tatas pauruṣeyam eva vācaka tvam syāt iti prastuta kṣatiḥ 
PVV_3.248–3.250,3–3.248–3.250,9	 atha pratyekam avayavānām sārthaka tvam tadā pratyekam sārthaka tvepi mithyā aneka tva kalpanā eka avayava gatyā ca vākya artha pratipad bhavet pratyekam sārthaka tvepi mithyā aneka tvasya aneka avayava ātmakasya kalpanā ekasmāt artha pratīteḥ tathā ekasya avayavasya gatyā vākya arthasya pratipad pratītiḥ bhavet ekasya api vācaka tvāt tad samudāyaḥ vācakaḥ iti ced sa kintebhyaḥ bhinnaḥ sa ca pratyuktaḥ avayavāḥ militāḥ samudāyaḥ iti ced sa ca na sambhavati eva tat yadi pratyekam vācaka tvam eva tadā eṣām pratyekam vācaka tve ca ekasmāt api syāt artha pratītiḥ atha sakṛt śrutau ca sarveṣām kāla bhedaḥ na yujyate eka avayava gatyā artha pratipatteḥ avayava antara vaiphalya doṣāt sarvva avayavānām sakṛt śrutiḥ iṣyate tadā sarvu eṣām avayavānām sakṛt śrutau ca abhimatāyām avayava śravaṇasya kāla bhedaḥ dṛśyeta ca 
PVV_3.251–3.260,0–3.251–3.260,1	 atha anavayavam ekam varṇṇebhyaḥ vyatiriktam sphoṭa rūpam vākyam tat ca kramavadbhiḥ d niyata anupūrvvīkaiḥ dhvanibhiḥ krameṇa vyajyate vyakti anukrameṇa eva ca krama vat pratīyate tad rūpā vibhāgena nāda rūpāṇām varṇṇānām grahaṇāt varṇṇa vibhāga vat ca lakṣyate vastutas tathā rahitam api iti kecid ekatvepi hi abhinnasya kramaśas gati asambhavāt 
PVV_3.251–3.260,2–3.251–3.260,5	 tat eka tva ipi hi abhinnasya anavayavasya sphoṭa rūpasya vākyasya prathama dhvaninā api vyakta tvāt krama pratīteḥ asambhavāt sakṛt pratīti prasaṅgaḥ yadi prathama vyaktau na pratītiḥ aparāsu api na syāt tad eka vyañcaka tvāt vyaktīnām kiñca vākyantat nityam anityam vā syāt anityam yatna sambhūtam pauruṣeyam kathat na tat nitya upalabdhi nitya tve api anāvaraṇa sambhavāt 
PVV_3.251–3.260,6	 yadi anityam pauruṣeyam katham na tat yatna sambhavāt ghaṭa ādi vat nitya tva īpyu bhavet vākyānām anāvaraṇa sambhavāt āvaraṇa ayogāt yadi nityam kadācid upalabhyate tadā tasya anāvṛta svabhāva tā abhyupagantavyā tādṛśam nityam upalabhyeta abhimata kālaḥ iva āvṛta svabhāve tu sarvvadā anupalambhaḥ syāt tasmāt kāla bhedena upalabhya anupalabhya svabhāva tvāt ekasya nāśāt anyasya udayaḥ iti syāt tathā ca nitya tva kṣatiḥ 
PVV_3.251–3.260,7–3.251–3.260,10	 eka svabhāvaḥ eva śabdaḥ param aśrutiḥ vvikala tvāt ced kasyacid sahakāriṇaḥ kāmam anya pratīkṣā uktiḥ niyamaḥ tu virudhyate kasyacid sahakāriṇaḥ jñāna janakasya vaikalyāt aśrutiḥ iti ced kāmam anyasya sahakāriṇaḥ upakārakasya pratīkṣā apekṣaṇam astu niyamaḥ pūrvvāpara eka svabhāvatā āvaraṇantu śabdānām virudhyate na hi eka svabhāvaḥ param apekṣate ca iti kṣamam upakārakasya apekṣaṇīya tvāt upakāra antarasya ca svabhāva antara lakṣaṇa tvāt 
PVV_3.251–3.260,11–3.251–3.260,14	 api ca śabdāḥ avyāpinaḥ vyāpinaḥ vā syuḥ tatra sarvatra anupalambhaḥ syāt teṣām avyāpitā yadi sarveṣām upalambhaḥ syāt yugapad vyāpitā yadi yadi avyāpitā teṣām sarvu atra deśe aanupalambhaḥ syāt na hi eka deśa sthitaḥ śailaḥ sarvu atra upalabhyate yogyatā atiśaya lābhāt vyañcakebhyaḥ dṛśyate eva iti ced evantarhi sarvvaiḥ sarvu adeśa sthaiḥ upalabhyeta tathā vyāpitā yadi sarvu eṣām śabdānām yugapad upalambhaḥ syāt vyāpi tvāt sarvu eṣām sarvu atra bhāvāt 
PVV_3.251–3.260,15–3.251–3.260,18	 atha vyāpi tvā ipi yaḥ eva abhivyaktyā saṃskṛtaḥ saḥ eva upalabhyate na itaraḥ saṃskṛtasya upalambhe ca kaḥ saṃskarttā avikāriṇaḥ indriyasya syāt saṃskāraḥ śṛṇuyāt nikhilañca tat saṃskṛtasya ca upalambhe ca svīkriyamāṇe nitya tvāt avikāriṇaḥ kaḥ saṃskarttā nāma na hi anupakurvvan saṃskarttā anupakāryaḥ vā saṃskāryaḥ atha indriyam anitya tvāt saṃskārya tatas saṃskṛtaḥ eva paśyati na anyaḥ iti vibhāgaḥ satyam indriyasya syāt saṃskāraḥ kintu tad indriyam nikhilam ca śabda grāmam śṛṇuyāt na tu eka śabdam 
PVV_3.251–3.260,19–3.251–3.260,23	 saṃskāra bheda bhinna tvāt ekārtha niyamaḥ yadi aneka śabda saṃghāte śrutiḥ kalakale katham saṃskārasya śabda viṣayasya bhedāt pratiniyamāt bhinna tvāt indriya saṃskārāṇām ekasmin= arthe śabde niyamaḥ śrutiḥ yat īṣyate tadā aneka śabda saṃghāte kalakale śrutiḥ anekeṣām śabdānām katham na aneka śabda grāhi syāt atha dhvanayaḥ kevalam tatra śrūyante ced na vācakāḥ 
PVV_3.251–3.260,24–3.251–3.260,27	 dhvanibhyaḥ bhinnam asti iti śraddheyam avivakṣitam tatra kalakale dhvanayaḥ śabda vyañjakāḥ kevalam śrūyante na vācakāḥ śabdāḥ dhvanibhyaḥ śrūyamāṇebhyaḥ bhinnam śabda rūpam asti iti yat kiñjididam atiśraddheyam śraddhā vaśāt yadi etat aṅgīkriyate na tu pramāṇa balāt kiñja sthiteṣu anyeṣu śabdeṣu śrūyate vācakaḥ katham 
PVV_3.251–3.260,28–3.251–3.260,29	 kalakale dhvani mātram yadi śrūyate na śabdaḥ tadā bahūnām vyāharttṝṇām tūṣṇīmbhāvāt anyeṣu api eṣu śabdeṣu sthiteṣu ekasmin puruṣe vyāharati katham vācakaḥ śrūyateka lakalaiḥ va dhvani mātra śrutiḥ tadā api syāt atha vācakasya ulabdhi pratyaya bhāvāt upalabdhiḥ tadā kalaka lepi syāt viśeṣa abhāvāt yadi ca indriyāṇām saṃskāra viśeṣāt śabda viśeṣa upalabdhi pratiniyamaḥ tadā

PVV_3.251–3.260,35–3.251–3.260,37	 yaiḥ kaiḥ api doṣaiḥ dhvanayaḥ avācakāḥ sammatāḥ te doṣāḥ vyajyamānepi vācakesmin bhavanti tathā hi yathā pratyekam avācaka tvāt vācaka tve vā dhvani antara vaiphalyāt sāhitya abhāvāt ca dhvanayaḥ avācakāḥ tathā dhvanibhiḥ pratyekam vācaka an abhivyakteḥ abhivyaktau vā dhvani antare vaiphalyāt sāhitya abhāvāt ca na abhivyajyeta śabdaḥ anabhivyaktaḥ ca kam artha pratipādayet varṇṇa ānupūrvī vākyam ced na varṇṇānām abhedataḥ teṣāñca na vyavasthānam krama antara virodhataḥ 
PVV_3.251–3.260,38	 varṇṇānām ānupūrvvī paripāṭi viśeṣaḥ vākyam tat ca upalabhyate eva iti ced mānupūrvyāyāḥ abhedataḥ na hi varṇṇebhyaḥ bhinnā ānupūrvvī pratīti viṣayaḥ tatas ca varṇṇāḥ eva vākyam iti syāt teṣāñca loka vedayoḥ na viśeṣaḥ iti sarvu atra prāmāṇyam atha aprāmāṇi am vā syāt atha viśeṣa anupūrvvīkā varṇṇāḥ eva veda vākyam na itaraḥ iti āha teṣā varṇṇānām na vyavasthāna krama niyamaḥ krama antarasya laukikasya virodhataḥ tathā hi varṇṇa vat ānupūrvvī nityāḥ na ca varṇṇāḥ bahavaḥ santi samāna jātīyāḥ vai eka tvāt varṇṇasya tatas ca agniḥ iti eva ākāra gakāra nakārāṇām ānupūrvvī viśiṣṭaḥ syāt nagam iti anyathā na bhavet kṛtakānām api bījāṅtkura patra ādīnām ṛtu saṃvatsara ādīnām viśiṣṭa ānupūrvī na anyathā bhavati kimpunar nityānām 
PVV_3.251–3.260,39–3.251–3.260,41	 sā ca iyam ānupūrvvī varṇṇānām deśa kāla krama abhāvaḥ vyāpti nitya tva varṇṇanāt deśa kṛtā vā pipīlikānām iva paṃktī syāt kāla kṛtā vā bīja aṅkura ādīnām iva dvayoḥ api deśa kāla kramayoḥ abhāvaḥ varṇṇānām vyāpti nitya tvayoḥ vvarṇṇanāt anyonya deśa parihāreṇa vṛttiḥ hi deśapaurvāparya tat ca sarvu agānām asambhavi tathā anyonya kāla parihāreṇa vṛttiḥ kālapaurvāparyañca nityānām asambhavi 
PVV_3.261–3.272,0–3.261–3.272,5	 atha ānupūrvvī samarthana artham anitya tā avyāpita iṣyate anitya avyāpita āyāñca doṣaḥ prāk eva kīrttitaḥ anitya avyāpita āyāñca doṣaḥ prāk eva uktaḥ anitya tve pauruṣeya tā avyāpi tve ca sarvu atra upalabdhiḥ ca na syāt vyakti krama upi vākyam na nitya vyakti nirākṛteḥ vyāpārāt eva tad siddheḥ karaṇānām ca kārya tā iti nitya vyāpinām api śabdānām vyakteḥ abhivyakte pratiniyata deśa kālāyāḥ kramaḥ vākyam na yuktaḥ nityasya vyakti nirākṛteḥ jñāna utpādana hetūnām ityādinā tasmāt karaṇānām vyāparā devateṣām varṇṇānām siddheḥ kārya tā eṣām yuktā na vyaṅgyatā 
PVV_3.261–3.272,6–3.261–3.272,9	 kiñca sva jñānena anya dhī hetuḥ siddherthe vyañcakaḥ mataḥ yathā dīponyathā vā api kaḥ viśeṣaḥ sya kārakāt siddhe vidyamāne arthe sva jñānena kāraṇena anyasya jñāna hetuḥ vyañjakaḥ mataḥ ghaṭasya yathā anyathā vā api iti yadi vyaṅgyaḥ prāk siddhaḥ na bhavet tadā asya vyañjakasya kārakāt hetoḥ kaḥ viśeṣaḥ na kaścid apūrvva pratipatti hetu tva aviśeṣāt 
PVV_3.261–3.272,10–3.261–3.272,15	 tathā karaṇānām samagrāṇām vyāpārāt upalabdhitaḥ niyamena ca kārya tvam vyañcake tad asambhavāt karaṇānām samagrāṇām vyāpārāt niyamena upalabdhitaḥ ca kāryatvam eva varṇṇānām vyañcake dīpa ādau tasya vyaṅgya upalabdhi niyamasya asambhavāt na hi dīpaḥ iti eva ghaṭa pratītiḥ karaṇa sāmagryantu kāryam avaśyam bhāvayati iti karaṇa sāmagrye niyata upalambhasya kārya tā eva tad rūpa āvaraṇanām ca vyaktiḥ te vigamaḥ yadi abhāve karaṇa grāma sāmarthyam kim nu tat bhavet 
PVV_3.261–3.272,16	 teṣām varṇṇānām rūpasya stimita vāyavīya avayava saṃyoga rūpāṇām āvaraṇānām prayatna preritena vāyunā vigamaḥ yadi vyaktiḥ te mī mām sa kaḥ syeṣṭā tadā pūrvva avasthā tyāge na atiśayaḥ na vyaktiḥ anitya tva āsakteḥ upalambha āvaraṇa vigamaḥ vā śabda ālambanam jñānam vā vyaktiḥ syāt iti atra āha kāryam vyaktiḥ aśakyā yasmāt āvaraṇa vigame abhāve nīrūpe karaṇa grāmasya kim nu tat sāmarthyam bhavet kvacid karttavye sāmarthyam syāt na tu karttavya abhāve yadi sa mastaka ātvarya sambhavepi śabdānām na kārya tā tadā 
PVV_3.261–3.272,17–3.261–3.272,19	 śabda aviśeṣāt anyeṣām api vyaktiḥ prasajyate tathā abhyupagame sarvu akārakāṇām nirarthatā śabdāt aviśeṣāt anya vyāpāra antarāt upalabhyamāna tva niyamena anyeṣām ghaṭa ādīnām api vyaktiḥ prasajyeta kārya tā na syāt tathā abhyupagame ca sarvu eṣām kārakāṇām vyañcaka abhimatānām nirarthaka tā utpādakam hi kāraṇabhiṣyate na tu vyañjakam śabdānām iva 
PVV_3.261–3.272,20–3.261–3.272,22	 sādhanam pratyabhijñānam sat prayoga ādi yat matam anudāharaṇam sarvu abhāvānām kṣaṇa bhaṅgataḥ yat ca nitya tva siddhaye varṇṇānām pratyabhijñānam sat prayogaḥ ādi śabdāt uccāryamāṇa tva ādi sādhanam matam san= ā iva hi prayujyate yathā vā asya ādi cchidāyām tatas prayogāt prayogepi vidyamāna tvāt varṇṇāḥ nityāḥ eva tad anudāharaṇam dṛṣṭānta vikalaṃsarvveṣa ambhāvānām kṣaṇa bhaṅgataḥ 
PVV_3.261–3.272,23–3.261–3.272,28	 dūṣyaḥ kuhetuḥ anyā upi anayā eva diśā paraiḥ ucyamānaḥ kuhetuḥ anyā upi dūṣyaḥ atha buddhiḥ abhivyaktiḥ vvarṇṇānām sā ca kramavatī vākyam iṣṭam tadā vākyasya apauruṣeya tvena iṣṭa tvāt buddhiḥ apauruṣeyī syāt tatra buddheḥ apuruṣa āśraye bādha abhyupeta pratyakṣa pratīta anumitaiḥ samam buddheḥ apuruṣa āśraye puruṣān āśrayaṇebādhāḥ kaiḥ iti āha abhyupeta pratyakṣa pratīta anumitaiḥ eka kālam eva buddheḥ apuruṣa āśraya tvasya abhyupetena puruṣa guṇa tva abhyupagamena pratyakṣa pratītena ca puruṣa kārya tvena tad prayatnakāḥ ryatvena vā kādācid katva anumitena kāryatvena ca bādhā 
PVV_3.261–3.272,29–3.261–3.272,32	 varṇṇānām ānupūrvvī vākyam syāt iti āha ānupūrvyāḥ ca varṇṇebhyaḥ bhedaḥ sphoṭena cintitaḥ kalpanā āropitā sā syāt katham vā apuruṣa āśrayāḥ varṇṇebhyaḥ ānupūrvyā bhedaḥ ca sphoṭena cintitena ekatvena hi abhinnasya kramaśas ityādinā cintitaḥ na hi varṇṇebhyaḥ vyatiriktā ānupūrvvī kācid upalabhyate abheda pakṣe ca saraḥ rasaḥ iti ādau pratipatteḥ bheda abhāva prasaṅgaḥ prakāra antarasya ca abhāvaḥ tasmāt vastu bhūta ānupūrvyā ayogāt kalpanā āropitā sā syāt tathā ca apuruṣa āśrayāḥ 
PVV_3.261–3.272,33–3.261–3.272,36	 katham punar avagamyate dhvaniḥ avaśyam anityaḥ iti āha sattā mātra anubandhi tvāt nāśasya anitya tā dhvaneḥ avināśāt saḥ eva asya vināśaḥ iti ced katham anyorthoni asya nāśoḥ tu kāṣṭham kasmāt na dṛśyate sattā mātra anubandhi tvāt nāśasya dhvaneḥ anitya tā na khalu asatām anyasmāt nāśa utpattiḥ sva hetoḥ eva tu vinaśvara svabhāva tayā utpannāḥ bhāvāḥ vinaśyanti vināśaḥ hi kriyamāṇaḥ bhāvāt vyatiriktaḥ vā bhavet avyatireka pakṣe bhāvaḥ eva kriyate iti syāt tat ca aśakya kriyam utpanna tvāt vyatirekepi agneḥ sakāśāt artha antarasya vināśa ākhyasya utpattau kāṣṭhasya darśanambhavet avināśāt 
PVV_3.261–3.272,37	 saḥ eva agni janmā arthaḥ asi avināśaḥ tena adarśanam iti ced katham anyorthonyasya vināśaḥ yuktaḥ evam hi ati prasaṅgaḥ syāt kāṣṭhe agni kṛtaḥ svabhāvaḥ vināśaḥ na sarvvaḥ iti ced kāṣṭha vināśayoḥ kaḥ sambandhaḥ na āśraya āśrayi bhāvaḥ niṣetsyamāna tvāt kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ ced agneḥ api sa vināśaḥ syāt tasya api kāryatvāt tasmāt na bhāva antaram arthasya nāśaḥ astu vā nāśaḥ kāṣṭhañcet apracyuta prācīna svabhāvam kasmāt na dṛśyate 
PVV_3.261–3.272,38	 nanu yosau= artha antara svabhāvaḥ vahni kṛtaḥ sa kāṣṭhasya nāśaḥ nāśa rūpa tayā pratīteḥ vināśaḥ ca abhāvaḥ yaḥ ca abhāvaḥ sa kāṣṭha virodhi rūpaḥ eva kriyate na ca ayam artha antara tvāt ghaṭa vat virodhi rūpa tā kurttum aśakyaḥ na hi ghaṭa vat artha antara tvāt dhūmaḥ agni kāryaḥ na bhavati tasmāt yathā antara rūpa upi dhūmaḥ agninā kriyate tathā virodhi rūpopi vināśīkriyeta yayoḥ ca paraspara parihāreṇa virodhaḥ tayoḥ eka bhāvaḥ eva aparasparasya adarśanam iti katham agni kṛtasya artha antarasya vināśa saṃjñitasya virodhinaḥ bhāve kāṣṭhasya darśanam ucyate 
PVV_3.261–3.272,39–3.261–3.272,40	 atra ucyate yosau= artha antara svabhāvaḥ nāśaḥ tena saha kāṣṭhasya kaḥ virodhaḥ yadi saha anavasthāna lakṣaṇaḥ sambhāvyatas eva tad bhāvayoḥ nivartti anivarttaka bhāva darśanāt agni śītayoḥ iva kintu bhāva antarasya yadi kāṣṭha vināśaka tvam sa ca nāśaḥ kimartha antara nivṛttiḥ artha antara tve tulyaḥ prasaṅgaḥ nivṛttiḥ ca niḥsvabhāvāḥ na tatra hetu vyāpāraḥ iti vakṣyate paraspara parihāra sthiti lakṣaṇaḥ ced virodhaḥ evam api atiprasaṅgaḥ yathā kāṣṭhāt bhinnam abhimata padārtha antaram tathā anyat api ghaṭa ādikam iti tat api kāṣṭhasya vināśaḥ syāt nanu yaḥ eva kāṣṭhasya nāśa rūpa tayā virodhi rūpa tayā ca sva hetubhiḥ kriyate saḥ eva nāśaḥ na tu yaḥ kaścid arthaḥ iti katham atiprasaktiḥ 
PVV_3.261–3.272,41	 tat api ayuktam paraspara parihāreṇa hi virodhī nāśaḥ iṣṭam sa ca paraspara parihāraḥ abhimata padārtha vat ghaṭa ādīnām api iti na viśeṣaḥ atha yaḥ eva kāṣṭha nivṛtti rūpaḥ saḥ eva tad nāśaḥ na anyaḥ kim idam nivṛtti rūpa tvam kāṣṭhāt anya tvam nivṛtti mātra ātmaka tvam vā anya tvañced tad itarasya api samānam nivṛtti mātra ātmaka tvañca bhāva antarasya ayuktam svabhāva aviśeṣava tvāt yat utpattau yat nivṛttiḥ sa virodhī nāśaḥ ca iti ced anyā tarhi vināśāt nivṛttiḥ tatra ca samānaḥ sarvvaḥ eva prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt kāṣṭham svarasa nirodhitayā nivarttate agni kāṣṭha ādi sāmagrayāḥ tu aṅgāra ādikam jāyate iti yuktam artha antara svabhāve tu sati nāśe kāṣṭham kasmāt na dṛśyate iti anivāryaḥ prasaṅgaḥ 
PVV_3.261–3.272,42–3.261–3.272,47	 tad parigrahataḥ ced na tena anāvaraṇam yatas vināśasya vināśi tvam tena vināśa ākhyena bhāva antareṇa parigraha tovaṣṭabdha tvāt kāṣṭhā darśanam iti ced bhāva antareṇa kāṣṭhasya anāvaraṇam yatas tatas kāṣṭhasya aparigrahaḥ na hi nāśaḥ vastu āvaraṇam avināśi tva prasaṅgāt na ca pūrvvāpara eka svabhāvasya varaṇam yuktam iti uktam kiñca syāt utpatteḥ tatas punar kāṣṭhasya darśanam bhāva antara bhūtasya nāśasya yadi utpattiḥ iṣyate tadā utpatti liṅgāt vināśi tvam nāśasya syāt ghaṭa ādi vat tatas kāṣṭha nāśasya nāśāt punar kāṣṭha darśanam bhavet hantṛ ghāte caitrāpunarbhavaḥ yathā atra api evam iti ced hantuḥ nna amaraṇa tvataḥ 
PVV_3.261–3.272,48	 nanu caitrasya hantuḥ vyāghāte kṛte caitrasya punarbhāvaḥ na asti yathā tathā atra api kāṣṭha nāśa nivṛttyā na kāṣṭha punarbhāvaḥ iti ced na hantuḥ amaraṇa tvataḥ na hi hantā maraṇam caitrasya kintu anyaḥ eva indriya āyuḥ nirodhaḥ yena hantṛ maraṇe caitra punar ujjīvana prasaṅgaḥ yadi tu indriya ādi nirodha nivṛttiḥ syāt syāt eva ujjīvanam tat ca tvad mate prāptam nirodhasya utpatti bhāvayoḥ iṣṭaḥ 
PVV_3.273,0–3.274,1	 ananya tve vināśasya syāt nāśaḥ kāṣṭham eva tu tasya asatvāt ahetu tvam na atonyā vidyete gatiḥ atha na bhāvāt bhinnaḥ nāśaḥ kintarhi abhinnaḥ ananya tve vināśasya nāśaḥ kāṣṭham eva tu syāt tasya kāṣṭhasya agni sannidhānāt prāk eva sa tvāt ahetu tvam na aśaka abhimatasya na atas bheda abheda prakārāt anyā gatiḥ utpattimatosti dvidhā api ca nāśa hetu ayogaḥ ahetu tvepi nāśasya nitya tvāt bhāva nāśayoḥ sahabhāva prasaṅgaḥ ced asataḥ nitya tā kutas ahetu tvepi nāśasya nitya tvāt ākāśa ādi vat bhāva nāśayoḥ anyonya abhāva svabhāvayoḥ sahabhāva prasaṅgaḥ ced nanu nāśasya asataḥ nīrūpa tvāt nitya tā kutas vastu hi nityam anityam vā syāt yat tu na kiñcid tat katham ucyatām 
PVV_3.275,0–3.275,1	 asatve abhāva nāśi tva prasaṅga upi na yujyate nāśena yasmāt bhāvasya na vināśanam iṣyate atas ca anitya tvāt asatve nāśasya abhāva nāśi tvasya prasaṅga upi na kāṣṭha ādeḥ nāśena hetunā nāśanam na iṣyate yadi hi nāśena nāśaḥ kriyate iti iṣyate tadā nāśa abhāve vastu nāśaḥ na syāt kintu sva hetutaḥ eva bhāvāḥ eka kṣaṇa sthiti dharmāṇaḥ utpannāḥ dvitīye kṣaṇe na bhavanti na tu nāma kaścid bhavati yasya nitya tva anitya tvayoḥ doṣa avakāśaḥ 
PVV_3.276,0–3.276,2	 kathantarhi idānīm ahetukaḥ nāśaḥ bhavati iti ucyate iti āha naśyan bhāvaḥ para apekṣaḥ na tasya jñāpanāya sā avasthā ahetuḥ uktā asyāḥ bhedam āropya cetasā naśyan bhāvaḥ eva kṣaṇa sthiti dharma tayā sva hetoḥ utpatteḥ dvitīye kṣaṇe abhavat na parā kāraṇa antara nirapekṣaḥ iti tasya kāraṇa antara anapekṣa nāśi tvasya jñāpanāya bhāvānām avasthā ahetuḥ uktāḥ ahetukaḥ vināśaḥ bhavati ityādi vacasā eva asyāḥ avasthāyāḥ dharmiṇaḥ sakāśāt bheda antara pratikṣepeṇa cetasā vikalpa kena bhedamā na tu vastutas nāśaḥ nāma kaścid bhāvāt bhinna svabhāvaḥ bhavati 
PVV_3.277,0–3.277,1	 svatopi bhāve abhāvasya vikalpaḥ ced ayam samaḥ na tasya kiñcid bhavati na bhavati eva kevalam sva topya bhāvasya bhāve ayantatva anyatva vikalpaḥ samaḥ ced tathā hi yadi bhāvāt bhinna upyabhāvaḥ jñātaḥ bhāvaḥ kim iti na dṛśyate abheda tu bhāvaḥ eva nāśaḥ iti katham naṣṭaḥ atra āha na tasya bhāvasya kiñcid vināśaḥ anyovā bhavati kintarhi saḥ eva kevalam na bhavati vyavaharttavya eka rūpa tvāt tasya tatra ca bheda abheda vikalpān avatāraḥ 
PVV_3.278,0–3.278,3	 bhāve hi eṣa vikalpaḥ syāt vidheḥ vastu anurodhataḥ hi yasmāt bhāve vikalpaḥ eṣa bheda abheda ātmakaḥ syāt vidheḥ vvastu anurodhataḥ nāśaḥ tu prasajya pratiṣedha rūpaḥ niḥsvabhāva tvāt bheda abheda vikalpa akṣamaḥ yadi ca prasajya pratiṣedha ipi vastu antara vidhiḥ tadā paryudāsāt na bhidyeta ubhayatra api vidheḥ prādhānyāt paryudāsaḥ vā na sidhyet eka nivṛttau= apara vidhāne sa syāt nivṛtti a siddhau tu katham yuktaḥ na bhāvaḥ bhavati iti uktam abhāvaḥ bhavati iti na yadā ca bhāva nivṛttiḥ vināśa arthaḥ tadā abhāvaḥ bhavati ityādi vākyena bhāvaḥ na tyuktam abhāvasya bhāva ayogāt atas ca hetuḥ api nāśasya na kaścid 
PVV_3.279,0–3.280,1	 apekṣeta paraḥ kāryam yadi vidyeta kiñcana yat akiñcitkaram vastu kim kenacid apekṣyate yasmāt paraḥ kāraṇa abhimataḥ apekṣya tayadi kiñcana kāryam vidyeta anyathā yat akiñcitkaram vastu tat kenacid kim apekṣyate etena ahetuka tvepi hi abhūtvā nāśa bhāvataḥ sattā nāśi tva doṣasya pratyākhyātam prasañcanam etena nāśasya niḥsvabhāva tva kathanena ahetuka tvepi satya bhūtvā nāśasya ghaṭa ādau= iva pratyākhyātam na hi abhāvaḥ nāma kaścid bhavati yasya abhūtvā bhāvāt sattvam nāśitvam vā syāt 
PVV_3.281,0–3.281,1	 yathā keṣāñcid eva iṣṭaḥ pratighaḥ janminām tathā nāśa svabhāvaḥ bhāvānām na anutpattimatām yadi nanu yathā janminām buddhi ādīnām madhye keṣāñcid eva ghaṭa ādīnām pratighaḥ sva deśe vastu antara utpatti vyāghātaḥ iṣṭaḥ na buddhi ādīnām tathā yadi satām utpattimatām eva nāśaḥ svabhāvaḥ syāt na anutpattimatām śabda ākāśa ādīnām tadā katham uktam sattā mātra anubandhi tvāt nāśasya anitya tā dhvaneḥ iti 
PVV_3.282,0–3.282,2	 atra āha svabhāva niyamāt hetoḥ svabhāva niyamaḥ phale na anitye rūpa bheda usti bhedakānām abhāvataḥ hetoḥ svabhāvasya viśiṣṭa kārya utpādana yogya tāyāḥ niyamāt phale kārye svabhāvasya pratigha apratigha ādeḥ niyamaḥ tatas nitya tva abhimata anāñca hetum antareṇa svabhāva niyama ayogāt hetuḥ eṣṭavyaḥ kṛtake punar anitye vā bhāve rūpasya naśvarān aśvarasya bhedaḥ na asti kasmāt iti āha nitya anitya svabhāva tayā kṛtakasya bhedakānām hetūnām abhāvataḥ na hi kaścid eva hetuḥ anityam janayatinā aparaḥ sarvu eṣām kṛtakānām artha kriyā kāri tvāt tasya ca anitya tā vyāpteḥ 
PVV_3.283,0–3.283,1	 pratyākhyeyā atas eva eṣām sambandhasya api nitya tā sambandha doṣaiḥ prāk uktaiḥ śabda śaktiḥ ca dūṣitāḥ atas sarvu abhāva kṣaṇika tva sādhakāt pramāṇāt eva eṣām śabdānām artha sambandhasya api sambandhasya vastu tve kṣaṇika tvāt yā ca śabda śaktiḥ yogya tā ākhyā artha pratipatti āśrayaḥ varṇṇyate sā ca śabdāt vyatiriktā eva iti tadvat anityāḥ atha bhinnā tādṛśī ca sambandha doṣaiḥ sambandhi nām a nitya tvāt na sambandha ityādinā prāk uktaiḥ dūṣitā iti na punar ucyate 
PVV_3.284,0–3.284,2	 na tāvat apauruṣā iyam vacanam asti iti uktam bhavatu vā tathā api nā apauruṣeyam iti eva yathā artha jñāna sādhanam dṛṣṭaḥ anyathā api vahni ādiḥ aduṣṭaḥ puruṣa āgasā na apauruṣā iyam iti eva vacanam yathā arthasya avisamvādinaḥ jñānasya sādhanam yasmāt puruṣasya āgasā doṣeṇa aduṣṭopi vahni ādiḥ nīlotpala ādau= anyathā apardṛṣṭaḥ 
PVV_3.285,0–3.285,2	 kiñca na jñāna hetu tā eva syāt tasmin= akṛtake mate nityebhyaḥ vastu sāmarthyāt na ca janma asti kasyacid tasmin śabde akṛtake mate jñāna hetu tā eva na syāt na hi nityebhyaḥ vastu kārya janma aśakteḥ kasyacid jñānasya anyasya vājanma asti krama ākramayoḥ vyāpakayoḥ nityāt nivṛtteḥ tat vyāpyasya sāmarthyasya abhāvāt 
PVV_3.286,0–3.286,2	 tasmāt vikalpa vāsanā udbhūtāḥ samāropita gocarāḥ jāyante buddhayaḥ tatra kevalam na artha gocarāḥ tatra anitya ātmani uccarite śabde anādi antena vikalpane citta santatau= āropitāyāḥ vāsanāyā vikalpikā buddhayaḥ jāyante samāropita gocarāḥ kalpita artha viṣayāḥ na artha gocarāḥ na sva lakṣaṇa viṣayāḥ tathā artha tve śabda pramāṇa antara vaiphalyasya ukteḥ 
PVV_3.287–3.288,0–3.287–3.288,4	 nanu mithyātvam kṛtakeṣu eva dṛṣṭam iti akṛtam vacaḥ satya artham vyatirekasya virodhi vyāpanāt yadi hetau= asambhave bhāvaḥ tat tasya api śaṅkyate viruddhānām padārthānām api vyāpaka darśanāt mithyātvam artha śūnya tvam kṛtakeṣu eva vākyeṣu dṛṣṭam iti akṛtam vacaḥ satya artham syāt tadā kaḥ doṣaḥ kasmāt evam iti āha paraḥ akṛtaka tvasya sādhanasya virodhinā kṛtaka tvena sādhya viparyayasya mithyātvasya vyāpanāt atra āha vipakṣān mithyā tvāt akṛtakasya hetoḥ asaṃbhave asaṃbhava nimittam hetau bādhaka pramāṇe a nukte tasya akṛtaka tvasya api mithyātve vipakṣe bhāvaḥ śaṃkyate bādhaka pramāṇa adarśanāt nanu mithyātvam kṛtakeṣu dṛṣṭam tat akṛtakeṣu virodhiṣu katham syāt iti āha viruddhānā hi vyāpyānām padārthānām ekasya vyāpakasya darśanāt yathā prayatna anantarīyaka tvayoḥ ekena kṛtaka tvena anitya tvena vā vyāptiḥ 
PVV_3.289,0–3.289,3	 kiñca na asattā siddhiḥ iti uktam sarvatonupalambhanāt asiddha āyāma sattāyām sandigdhā vyatirekitā sarvvataḥ vipakṣāt hetoḥ asattāyāḥ anupalambhāt pratibdham antareṇa na siddhiḥ iti uktam na ca adarśana mātreṇa vipakṣe avyabhicārita ityādinā asiddhā vipakṣāt vyatirekitā sandigdhā kasmāt punar vyatireka niścaya apekṣā na hi sādhana tayā upāttaḥ dharmam iti eva sādhanam 
PVV_3.290,0–3.290,2	 kintarhi anvayaḥ vyatirekaḥ vā sattvam vā sādhya dharmiṇi tad niścaya phalaiḥ jñānaiḥ siddhyanti yadi sādhanam anvayaḥ sa pakṣevyatirekaḥ vipakṣāt sādhya dharmiṇi satvam vā tad niścaya phalaiḥ anvaya ādi niścaya prayojanaiḥ jñānaiḥ pramāṇa ātmabhiḥ yadi sidhyanti tadā sādhanam bhavati niścita trairūpyasya eva hetu tvāt 
PVV_3.291,0–3.291,2	 yat api vyatirekī hetuḥ iti uktam tat ca ayuktam iti āha yatra sādhya vipakṣasya varṇṇate vyatirekitā saḥ eva asya sa pakṣaḥ syāt sarvaḥ hetuḥ ananvayī yatra dharmiṇi sādhya vipakṣasya mithyātvasya sādhana avipakṣa vyatirekāt vyati yat kṛtakam na bhavati tat mithyārthañca na bhavati iti saḥ eva sādhya sādhana viparyaya nivṛtti darśana viṣayaḥ dharmī sa pakṛtaka tvasya hetoḥ viparyaya niṣedhena vidheḥ eva pratipādanāt yatra ca sādhya sādhana sattava niścayaḥ saḥ eva pakṣaḥ atas sarvvaḥ hetuḥ ananvayī na kevala vyatirekī 
PVV_3.292,0–3.292,4	 nanu pakṣasya vedasya katham sa pakṣatā sa pakṣa lakṣaṇa yogāt evam tarhi sarvvaḥ pakṣaḥ sa pakṣaḥ syāt bhavati eva kim anyena iti ced anyasya api lākṣaṇikam tat katham tyajyatām kiñca samaya tve hi mantrāṇām kasyacid kārya darśanam kiñcid kārya kāriṇaḥ mantrāḥ apauruṣeyāḥ ca iti vyāhatam tathā hikasyacit satya tapaḥ prabhāvataḥ puṃsaḥ samaya tve saṃketa tve mantrāṇām abhyupagamyamāne kāryasya mantra prayoga nispādya tvena iṣṭasya sādhanam siddhiḥ syāt kenacid śakti viśeṣavatā mad praṇītam mantram evaṃprayuñjānasya ayam arthaḥ setsyati iti samayasya kṛta tvāt siddhiḥ syāt kavi samaya ādi vat kāvya apāṭhakasya artha siddhiḥ atha api bhāva śaktiḥ syāt anyathā api aviśeṣataḥ atha api bhāva śaktiḥ yayā abhimata siddhiḥ evantar hi anyathā prayuktepi mantre syāt abhimatam aviśeṣatas varṇṇa ātmakasya mantrasya
