PVV_3.319,0–3.319,1	 prasiddhaḥ lokavādaḥ ced tatra koti indriya artha dṛś aneka artheṣu śabdeṣu yena arthoyam vivecitaḥ agniḥ dāha ādi samarthaḥ tasmin ghṛta ādi prakṣepaḥ ca havanam iti prasiddhaḥ lokavādaḥ tatas na anya artha kalpanā iti ced tatra loke rāga ādimati kaḥ atīndriya artha dṛś asti ṣu aneka artha abhidhāna yogyeṣu śabdeṣu ayam abhimata ūrthaḥ vivecitaḥ vācya tayā viśeṣaṇa vyavasthāpitaḥ yadi dāhaka dravye ghṛta prakṣepasya svargeṇa sambandhaḥ śva māṃsa bhakṣaṇena ca na asti iti kena api dṛṣṭam syāt syāt ayam artha vivekaḥ tad darśī tu rāga ādima tvāt kaścid neṣṭaḥ iti na asti viparīta kalpanā nirāsaḥ 
PVV_3.320,0–3.320,2	 na ca loka prasiddha anusārāt veda artha vyavasthā tathā hi svarga uḥ vaśya ādi śabdaḥ ca dṛṣṭaḥ rūḍha artha vācakaḥ śabda antareṣu tādṛkṣu tādṛśyeva astu kalpanā svarga urvaśya ādi śabdaḥ ca ārūḍha artha vācakaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ manuṣya atiśāyi puruṣa viśeṣa niketaḥ atimānuṣa sukha adhiṣṭhānaḥ nānā upakāraṇaḥ svargaḥ tad sthā apsarāḥ u rvva śī ti prasiddhaḥ loka vādaḥ tam ullaṃdhya duḥkhena asambhinnā niratiśayā prītiḥ svargaḥ urvvaśī ca araṇiḥ pātrī vā iti aprasiddha artha kalpanā iti śabda antareṣu agnihotra ādiṣu tādṛkṣu sarvva artha yogyeṣu tādṛśi eva aprasiddha arthā eva kalpanāḥ tu nyāyasya tulya tvāt 
PVV_3.321,0–3.321,2	 kiñca prasiddhaḥ ca nṛṇām vādaḥ pramāṇam sa ca na iṣyate tatas ca bhūyortha gatiḥ kim etat dviṣṭha kāmitam prasiddhaḥ ca nṛṇām vādaḥ eva na tu anyathā kācid sa puruṣa pravarttita tvāt pramāṇam na iṣyate bhavatā bhūyas punar tatas janavādāt arthasya gatiḥ iti kim etat dviṣṭha kāmitam lokavādaḥ apramāṇa tvāt dviṣṭhaḥ saṃprati kāmyate iti vyaktaḥ virodhaḥ 
PVV_3.322,0–3.323,2	 atha prasiddhim ullaṃdhya kalpane na nibandhanam prasiddheḥ apramāṇa tvāt tad grahe kim nibandhanam atha lokasya prasiddhim ullaṃdhya śva māṃsa bhakṣaṇa ādi artha kalpane na nibandhanam asti tasyāḥ grahe kim nibandhanam vicārakasya na kiñcid kiñca utpāditā prasiddhyā eva śaṅkā śabda artha niścaye yasmāt nānā artha vṛtti tvam śabdānām tatra dṛśyate prasiddhyā eva śabda artha niścaye viparīta artha kalpanāyā śaṅkā utpāditā yasmāt nānā artha vṛtti tvam śabdānām gavākṣa prabhṛtīnām tatra prasiddhau dṛśyate 
PVV_3.324,0–3.324,2	 tathā anyathā sambhava abhāvāt nānā śakteḥ svayam dhvaneḥ avaśyam śaṅkayā bhāvyam niyāmakam apaśyatām nānā śakteḥ aneka artha pratipādana yogyasya dhvaneḥ svayam ātmanā anyathā sambhavasya eka artha pratipādana yogyatā sambhavasya asambhavāt avaśyam artha antara śaṅkayā bhāvyam katham iti āha niyāmakam apaśyatām aneka arthasya śabdasya eka vṛtti niyama kāraṇam apaśyatām puṃsām 
PVV_3.325,0–3.325,2	 kiñca eṣa sthāṇuḥ ayam mārgaḥ iti vakti iti kaścana anyaḥ svayam bravīmi iti tayoḥ bhedaḥ parīkṣyatām svayam artha pratipādana śūnyaḥ netā anabhimata artha dyotaka tvena pratipādayan karttuḥ nnabhidyate tasya api evam vyāpāra tvāt yathā kenacid kaścana panthānam pṛṣṭhe āha na aham jāne kintu sthāṇuḥ eṣa vakti ayam mārgaḥ iti anyaḥ punar pratyāha aham svayam bravīmi ayam mārgaḥ iti tayoḥ evam vādinoḥ pratipādaka tvasya bhedaḥ ekaḥ nirabhiprāya vacanam vaktṛ tvena vyapadiśati anyaḥ tu na iti vacana vaidagdhyam eva anayoḥ bhidyate na upadeśa pravṛtti nivṛttī tathā svayam artha pratipādayatā upi veda artha viśeṣa abhidhāyinaḥ abhidadhat karttaṃva vācaka tāyāḥ 
PVV_3.326,0–3.326,2	 atha tad artha pratipādane yogyāḥ eva śabdāḥ nanu evam sarvu atra yogyasya eka artha dyotane niyamaḥ kutas jñātāḥ vā ati indriyāḥ kena vivakṣā vacanāt ṛte sarvu atra arthe yogyasya śabdasya eka artha dyotene niyamaḥ kutas jātaḥ puruṣaḥ ced niyāmakaḥ na bhavati syāt etat pratiniyatāḥ eva arthāḥ teṣām na te puruṣeṇa niyamyante evam api jñātāḥ vai atīndriyāḥ pratiniyatā arthāḥkena puruṣeṇa rāga ādimatā vivakṣāyāḥ prakāśakāt vacanāt pratipādanāt ṛte na hi vedeṣu kasyacid vivakṣā asti tad avagatim antareṇa ca pratiniyata artha tā na śakyāḥ boddhum na hi śabdāḥ svayam sva artha niyamam kathayanti saṃketam antareṇa sa ca pauruṣeyaḥ na ca artha niyama avagamam vinā saṃketa karaṇam artha niyama pratītiḥ ca vinā saṃketam na asti iti vyaktam itaretara āśraya tvam 
PVV_3.327,0–3.328,2	 api ca vivakṣā niyame hetuḥ saṅketaḥ tad prakāśanaḥ apauruṣeye sā na asti tasya sā ekārtha tā kutas vivakṣā arthasya niyame hetuḥ saṃketaḥ tad prakāśanaḥ artha niyama bodhanaḥ apauruṣeye ca vede sā vivakṣā na asti puruṣa prayojya tvāt tasyāḥ tatas tad prasādhyā sā ekārtha tā vedasya kutas atha svabhāva niyamenyatra na yojyeta tayā punar saṅketaḥ ca nirarthaḥ syāt vyaktau ca niyamaḥ kutas svabhāvataḥ śabdāḥ kvacid arthe niyatāḥ tadā svabhāva niyame anyatra arthe vācaka tvena tayā vivakṣayā na yojyeta na hi svabhāvena pratiniyata aviṣayonyathā kartum śakyate saṃketaḥ ca nirarthaḥ syāt svabhāva pratiniyame sati na hi cakṣuḥ indriyam rūpa grahaṇa pratiniyatam tatra saṅketam apekṣate saṅketāt vācaka tāya avyakta aviṣyamāṇāyām niyamaḥ kutas ayam eva asya śabdasya arthaḥ iti niyamaḥ na yujyate puruṣa adhīna saṅketa apekṣāyām 
PVV_3.329,0–3.329,2	 tathā hi yatra svātantryam icchāyāḥ niyamaḥ nāma tatra kaḥ dyotayet tena saṅketaḥ na iṣṭām eva asya yogyatām yatra puruṣasya svātaḥ ntryam icchāyāḥ tatra niyamaḥ nāma kaḥ saṅgataḥ tena icchā adhīna tvena saṃketaḥ na iṣṭām eva yogya tām uddyotayet anabhimatām api vyañjayet iti arthaḥ tat evam apauruṣeya tvam āgama lakṣaṇam bruvāṇā mī mām sa kāḥ pratikṣiptāḥ 
PVV_3.330,0–3.330,2	 saṃprati bṛ ddha mī mām sa kānām matam dūṣayitum utthāpayati yasmāt kila īdṛśam satyam yathā agniḥ śītanodanaḥ vākyam veda eka deśa tvāt anyat api aparaḥ avravīt yathā vaidikam vākyam agniḥ himasya bheṣajam iti satyam śīta nodana tvena vahneḥ pramāṇa siddha tvāt tathā annyat api vākyam agniṣṭomena juhuyāt svarga kāmaḥ ityādi veda eka deśa tvāt satyam iti aparaḥ mī mām sa kaḥ abravīt uktavān kila śabdaḥ akṣamāyām 
PVV_3.331,0–3.331,1	 rasavat tulya rūpa tvāt eka bhāṇḍe ca pāka vat śeṣavat vyabhicāri tvāt kṣiptam nyāya videdṛśam īdṛśam anumānam śeṣavat anaikāntikam vyabhicāri tvāt nyāya vid ācārya di gnāge na pratikṣiptam rasavat tulya rūpa tvāt svādita phalena tulya rūpa tvāt phala antarasya tādṛś rasa anumāna vat eka bhāṇḍa antarga tvāt dṛṣṭa pāka taṇḍula anumāna vat na hi etādṛśasya hetoḥ sādhya pratibandha usti viparyaya bādhaka pramāṇāt iti vipañcitam prāk 
PVV_3.332–3.334,0–3.332–3.334,3	 dṛśyate ca bahutara viṣaye visamvādaḥ vedasya katham ekasatya tayā sarvu atra tathātvam tathā ca nityasya puṃsaḥ kartṛ tvam nityān bhāvān atīndriyān aindriyān viṣamam hetum bhāvānām viṣamām sthitim nivṛttim ca pramāṇābhyām anyat vā vyasta gocaram viruddham āgama apekṣeṇa anumānena vā vadat virodham asamādhāya śāstra artham ca apradarśya saḥ satya artham pratijñānānaḥ jayet dhāṣṭaryena bandhakīm 
PVV_3.332–3.334,4	 paraiḥ anādheya viśeṣasya puṃsaḥ ātmanaḥ krama janmasu karma ādiṣu kartṛ tvam vadat śāstram tathā nityān bhāvān diś kāla ākāśa ādīn artha kriyā rahitān sataḥ vadat vastutas atīndriyān guṇa karma sāmānya ādīn aindriyān pratyakṣān vadat tathā bhāvānām viṣamam hetum prāc ajanakam vadat tathā viṣamām sthitim nispannānām bhāvānām āśraya vaśena sthitim vadat nivṛttiñca viṣamām svatas anaśvara svabhāvānām anya kṛtām nivṛttim vadat anyat vāvastu vyasta gocaram pramāṇā pratyakṣa anumānābhyām nirasta avakāśam vadat āgama apekṣeṇa āgama siddha liṅga trairūpyeṇa anumānena ca viruddham agni hotra snāna ādeḥ pāpa śamanam vadat na hi rāga ādi prabhavaḥ dharmaḥ tad apanayanam antareṇa snāna ādeḥ nivṛttim arhati evamvidha visamvāda bhājam artham vadat śāstram virodham prāmāṇikam asamādhāya aparihyatya pravṛtti kāma ucitam śāstra artham anuguṇa upāyam puruṣa artha lakṣaṇañcā pradarśya sa jara nmī mām sa kaḥ eka deśa samvāda darśanāt satya artham pratijānānaḥ dhā sākṣāt dṛṣṭa vyalīkām sva patim sva śīla prāmāṇya udbhāvanena bhrāntam āvedayantīm jayet 
PVV_3.335,0–3.335,2	 kiñca sidhyet pramāṇam yadi evam apramāṇam atha iha kim na hi ekam na asti satya artham puruṣe bahu bhāṣiṇi yadi evam dṛṣṭa eka deśa samvādasya avayava tvāt anyat api pramāṇam sidhyet atha iha nyāye kim apramāṇam śāstram bhaviṣyati na hi bahu bhāṣiṇi puruṣe satya artham ekam vace na asti kintu asti eva tena eva dṛṣṭāntena tat vacanam pramāṇam syāt 
PVV_3.336,0–3.337,2	 na ayam svabhāvaḥ kāryam vā vastūnām vaktari dhvaniḥ na ca tad vyatiriktasya vidyatevyabhicāritā na ayam dhvaniḥ vvastūnām svabhāvaḥ kāryam vā yasmāt vaktari dhvaniḥ bhavati na hi vastunaḥ svabhāvonyatra dharmiṇi varttate kāryamvā anyatas bhavitum arhati na ca tat vyati kārya svabhāvābhyām aparasya avyabhicāritā vidyate iti niveditam syāt etat pravṛttiḥ vācaka anāñca vācya dṛṣṭi kṛtā iti ced paraspara viruddha arthā katham ekatra sā bhavet vācakānām śabdānām pravṛttiḥ vvācya dṛṣṭi kṛtā abhidheya darśana āgatā tatas paraṃparayā tat kāryatā eva eṣām iti ced evam tarhi sā śabda pravṛttiḥ ekatra vastuni paraspara viruddha arthāḥ 
PVV_3.338,0–3.338,2	 yadi yathā vastu eva śabdaḥ tadā vastutas eka rūpeṇa śabde nityaḥ kim ayam anityaḥ vā ityādi śabda sandarbhaḥ na bhavet vastubhiḥ na āgamāḥ tena kathañcid na antarīyakāḥ pratipattuḥ na sidhyanti kutas tebhyaḥ artha niścayaḥ tena pratibandha abhāvena vastubhiḥ saha na antarīyakāḥ āgamā pratipattuḥ artham śabdāt pratipadyamānasya kathañcid na sidhyanti tat kutas tebhyaḥ āgama artha niścayaḥ 
PVV_3.339,0–iv.0,1	 tasmāt na tad nivṛttyā api bhāva abhāvaḥ prasidhyati tena asat niścaya phalā anupalabdhiḥ na sidhyati yasmāt pravarttamānāt āgamāt na asti artha siddhiḥ tsmāt tasya āgamasya nivṛttyā api pramāṇa traya nivṛtti lakṣaṇā api anupalabdhiḥ arthānām asat niścaya phalā na sidhyati tatas yuktam uktam sat asat niścaya phalā na iti syāt vā apavasava sat vyavahāra sādhane ca adhikṛte vyavasthitā iti avasthitam sva artha anumānam vyākhyāya para artha anumānam vyākhyātum āha tatra para artha anumānam sva dṛṣṭa artha prakāśanam iti ācāryīyalakṣaṇam svena dṛṣṭaḥ sva dṛṣṭaḥ sva dṛṣṭaḥ ca asau= arthaḥ ca iti tri rūpaḥ hetuḥ tasya prakāśanam vacanam anumāna hetu tvāt iti arthaḥ 
PVV_4.1,0–4.1,2	 nanu trirūpa liṅga ākhyānam iti eva astu kim sva dṛṣṭa grahaṇena iti śaṅkāyām para mata nirāsa artha tām asya darśayitum āha parasya pratipādya tvāt adṛṣṭopi svayam paraiḥ dṛṣṭa sādhanam iti eke tad kṣepāya ātma dṛś vacaḥ parasya para artha anumānena pratipādya tvāt sādhana vādinā svayam adṛṣṭā upi pramāṇena prativādibhiḥ āgamāt dṛṣṭa sādhanam liṅgam iti eke sām khyāḥ te hi sukha ādīnām utpattimatvāt anityāt acetana tvam rūpa ādīnām iva bauddham pratyāhuḥ na hi asate utpattimatvam sataḥ ca niranvaya vināśaḥ anitya tvam hetuḥ sāṃkhya asiddhaḥ bauddhasya punar āgamāt siddhaḥ tāvatā eva hetuḥ iti manyante tasya para matasya kṣepāya pratiṣedhāya ātma adṛṣṭa vacanam sūtre na prativādi mātra siddhasya hetu tvam kintu ubhaya siddhasya evati arthaḥ 
PVV_4.2,0–4.2,2	 na ca āgamāt prativādinā upi sādhana siddhiḥ yuktā iti vaktum āha anumāviṣaye na iṣṭam parīkṣita parigrahāt vācaḥ prāmāṇyam asmin hi na anumānam pravartate anumānasya vastu bala pravṛttasya viṣaye yasmāt anumāna jñānam utpadyate sa ca trirūpaḥ hetuḥ tatra pratipādye vācaḥ āgama ātmikāyāḥ prāmāṇyam na iṣṭam artha pratibandha abhāvāt iti uktam 
PVV_4.2,3	 kiñca pramāṇa antara samvādāt parīkṣitasya pramāṇa upapannasya āgama arthasya parigrahāt svīkārāt na iṣṭam vacana prāmāṇyam yadi vacanam iti eva pramāṇanta dā pratijñāpadāt eva sādhyasya siddheḥ niṣphalam hetu dṛṣṭanta ādi vacanam syāt pramāṇa antara samvāda apekṣā ca na bhavet samvāda jñānasya eva artha bhāva anuvidhāyi tvāt tasmin= āgama arthe prāmāṇyam vacanasya tu viparyayāt yadi tu āgamaḥ iti eva pramāṇam tadā pramāṇa antara samvāda apekṣā na syāt hi yasmāt asmin= āgama arthe pramāṇa pratipādita tvāt niścite anumānam na pravṛrttate yadi hi āgama arthaḥ sandihyeta tadā tad niścaya arthā pramāṇa antara vṛttiḥ apekṣyeta 
PVV_4.3,0–4.3,1	 bādhanāya āgamasya ukteḥ sādhanasya param prati sopramāṇam tadā asiddham tat siddham akhilantataḥ yadi ca āgamasya sukha ādi caitanya pratipādakasya bādhanāya sādhanasya utpattimatu ā ādeḥ sām khye na param bauddham pratyuktiḥ tatas kāraṇāt saḥ āgamaḥ apramāṇam tadā na hi pramāṇasya bādhaḥ yuktaḥ tatas āgama aprāmāṇyāt tena āgamena sākṣāt pāraṃparyābhyām siddham utpattimatu a ādi sādhyam ca ācaitanyam akhilam idam asiddham 
PVV_4.4,0–4.4,1	 tat āgamavataḥ siddham yadi kasya kaḥ āgamaḥ bādhyamānaḥ pramāṇena sa siddhaḥ katham āgamaḥ sa ca sukha ādi utpattimatva pratipādakaḥ āgamaḥ ca tad āgamaḥ tadvataḥ tad sambandhinaḥ bauddhasya siddham utpattimat tva ādi liṅgam iti ced kasya puruṣasya kaḥ āgamaḥ sambandhī na tāvat avayavat āgamopi puruṣasya sahaja sambandhena sambaddhaḥ na api yukti upapanna yata upādhinā pratyakṣa anumāna vat sambandhaḥ tathā hi pramāṇena utpattimatu ā ādi liṅga jena anumānena āgama pratipāditasya sukha ādi caitanyasya bādhanāt bādhyamānaḥ āgamaḥ hetuḥ sa yena yukti samvāda upādhinā api puruṣeṇa sambandham anubhavet 
PVV_4.5,0–4.5,2	 syāt etat sukha ādīnām acaitanyam tena eva āgamena pradeśa antare darśitam atas abādhya tvāt pramāṇāt asmāt sādhana vidhiḥ yuktaḥ iti āha tad viruddha abhyupagamaḥ tena eva ca katham bhavet tad anya upagame tasya tyāga aṃgasya apramāṇatā tasmāt caitanyāt pratipāditāt viruddhasya ācaitanyasya abhyupagamaḥ tena caitanya pratipādakena eva ca āgamena katham bhavet sambhave vā viruddha artha abhidhāyi tvena apramāṇāt āgamāt hetu siddhiḥ ayuktā eva āgama pratītena utpattimat tva ādinā tasmāt āgama ukta ca etanya asya ācaitanyasya upagame svīkāre vā prativādīnā kriyamāṇe tasya āgamasya tyāgāṃ abhyupagatā syāt yadā eva āgama prāmāṇyasya bādhake hetau= ādriyate tadā eva tatra saṃśayitaḥ na ca apramāṇāt hetu siddhiḥ 
PVV_4.6,0–4.6,2	 kiñca tat kasmāt sādhanam na uktam sva pratotiḥ yat udbhavāḥ yuktyā yayā āgamaḥ grāhyaḥ parasya api ca sā na kim ayamvādī tāvat svayam pratītam eva ācaitanyam parasmai pratipādayati va ca sādhanam antareṇa eva pratītiḥ tatas pratipādayituḥ svasya pratītiḥ caitanya viṣayāḥ yasmāt sādhanāt udbhavaḥ yasya aḥsā yat udbhavāḥ tad sādhanam svāgama ādikam kasmāt pratipādyam prati na uktam svayam pratipanna sāmarthyam eva sādhanam vaktum ucitam tathā niryuktikasya āgamasya aprāmāṇyāt yayā yuktyā upapannaḥ āgamaḥ sādhana tvena gāhyaḥ vādinā sā yuktiḥ parasya pratipādyasya api kinna sādhanayena tat parityajya anyat apramāṇa siddham utpatti ādi ucyate 
PVV_4.7,0–4.7,2	 atha yoga bala jena pratyakṣeṇa sukha ādīnām acaitanyam pratītam na tat anyathā pratipādayitum parasya śakyate iti para upagatam sādhanam ucyate nanu tathā api na akasmikaḥ buddhi sukha ādya caitanya viṣayasya niścayaḥ tad sākṣāt kāri pratyakṣa tad sādhana yoga anuṣṭhānayoḥ sādhya sādhana bhāva avadhāraṇañca avaśya karttavyam tat niścayam antareṇa yoga anuṣṭhāna ayogāt tathā ca prākṛtasya sataḥ prāk yaiḥ pratipatti akṣa saṃbhavau sādhanaiḥ sādhanāni artha śakti jñānesya tāni alam 
PVV_4.7,3	 prākṛtasya arvvāc darśanasya sataḥ yaiḥ sādhanaiḥ sukha ācaitanya ādi viṣayam tat grāhi pratyakṣa tad sādhanayoḥ sambandhañca niścitya pravṛttasya upāye pratipattuḥ anuṣṭhānasya tad phalasya akṣasya pratyakṣasya ācaitanya ādi viṣaya grāhiṇaḥ sambhavau bhavataḥ tāni sādhanāni arthasya upāya abhyāsasya śakteḥ acaitanya grāhi pratyakṣa janikāyāḥ jñāne karttavye asya pratipādyasya alam samarthāni tatasyāni eva sādhanāni ucyantām kim svayam adṛṣṭa sādhya pratipādana sāmarthyena uttima tva ādinā uktena 
PVV_4.8,0–4.8,2	 syāt etat pratyakṣasya ācaitanya ādi viṣayasya yoga ādi abhyāsena saha sādhya sādhana sambandhaḥ viprakṛṣṭātvāt sāmānya ākāreṇa api na pratīyate tatosya anupadarśanam iti āha vicchinna anugamāḥ yepi sāmānyena api agocarāḥ sādhya sādhana cintā asti na teṣu artheṣu kācana yepi vicchinnaḥ viprakṛṣṭaḥ anugamaḥ sambandhaḥ yeṣām te pratyakṣa tad upāya ādayaḥ sāmānyena aviśeṣa ākāreṇa api agocarāḥ teṣu artheṣu idam sādhanam idam sādhyam iti ca sādhya sādhana cintā kācana na asti tatas arvvāk darśanasya abuddhi viṣayīkṛtayaḥ rūpayoḥ upaya upeyayoḥ ekatra anuṣṭhānau= aparatra niṣpādanam iti kutas 
PVV_4.9,0–4.9,2	 kiñca apramāṇakāt āgamāt icchā mātreṇa pratipādyaḥ hetum kurvvan punar icchayā tam eva pariharan hetu tad ābhāsayoḥ icchā adhīna tām svīkuryāt iti ākhyātum āha puṃsām abhiprāya vaśāt tattva atattva vyavasthitau luptau hetu tad ābhāsau tasya vastu asamāśrayāt puṃsām abhiprāya vaśāt icchā anurodhāt tattvāyoḥ hetu tad ābhāsa tvayoḥ vyavasthi viṣyamāṇāyām hetu tadābhāsau luptau syātām avyavasthita tvāt tasya puruṣa abhiprāyasya vastu asaṃśrayāt yathāvastu pravṛtti niyama abhāvāt 
PVV_4.10,0–4.10,2	 api ca san= arthaḥ jñāna sāpekṣaḥ na āsan jñānena sādhakaḥ satopi vastu asaṃśliṣṭā asaṃgatyā sadṛśī gatiḥ san= arthaḥ jñāna sāpekṣaḥ sādhya sādhakaḥ pratītaḥ yathā dhūma ādiḥ na āsannarthaḥ jñānena pratīti mātreṇa sādhakaḥ sādhyasya yathā kalpitaḥ dhūmaḥ atha ācaitanyam vastutosti eva tat yathā kathañcid parasmai pratipādanīyam atas para abhyupagataḥ hetuḥ kriyate iti āha sa topya caitanyasya vastu asaṃśliṣṭā vastu bhūta liṅga apratibaddhā gatiḥ asaṅgatyā asataḥ pratītyā sadṛśī samyak pratīta tva abhāvat anyetu asat gatyā doṣavat pratītyā sadṛśī iti vyācakṣate teṣām sa topya vastu kṛtā pratipattiḥ asat pratipattim na atiśete apratyaya tvāt iti viniścaya granthena saha eka vākyatā na syāt 
PVV_4.11,0–4.11,2	 kiñca liṅgam svabhāvaḥ kāryam vā dṛśya adarśanam eva vā sambaddham vastutassiddham tat asiddham kim ātmanaḥ liṅgam sādhya artha sa na anyat vyabhicārāt tat ca svabhāvaḥ kāryam manupalabdhiḥ eva anyasya pratibandha abhāvāt iti uktam tad utpatti ādikam yadi triṣu hetuṣu antarbhūtam tadā vastutas paramārthataḥ siddham pratipādyasya kim kasmāt ātmanaḥ sām khya sya vādinaḥ asiddham utpattimatu ādi svabhāva hetuḥ syāt sa ca dharmi grāhakāt pramāṇāt anyatas vā śiṃśapātva vat kṛtaka tva ādi vat arthān prativādinaḥ iva vādinā upi sidhyet 
PVV_4.12,0–4.12,4	 atha trividhe hetau na antar bhavati utpatti ādi tadā pareṇa api anyatas gantum ayuktam pareṇa prativādinā api trividhāt hetoḥ anyatas hetoḥ acaitanyam gantum pratyetum ayuktam yadi para abhyupagama siddham asādhanam tadā prasaṅga hetuḥ ahetuḥ syāt iti āha para kalpitaiḥ prasaṅgaḥ dvaya sambandhāt eka apāyeni ahānaye para kalpitaiḥ sādhanaiḥ prasaṅgaḥ kriyate yathā sāmānyasya para upagata aneka vṛtti tvāt aneka tvam āpādyate na tu ayam pāramārthikaḥ hetuḥ trairūpya abhāvāt yadi ayam na hetuḥ tadā kim artham ucyate iti āha dvayoḥ sādhya sādhanayoḥ sambandhāt vyāpya vyāpaka bhāvāt sphāritāt ekasya sādhyasya apāye anyasya sādhanasya hānaye yathā ca anekaṃsāmānyam tasmāt na aneka vṛtti iti viparyaya prayoge sādhya abhāve sādhana abhāvaḥ kathyate prasaṅga viparyayotra maulaḥ hetuḥ sādhya sādhanya vyāpti grāhaka pramāṇa smārakaḥ tu prasaṅge prayogaḥ iti arthaḥ bhinna deśa kāla ādiṣu anekāsu vyaktiṣu vṛttasya tad atad deśa tva ādi viruddha dharma adhyāsāt aneka tva siddheḥ aneka vṛtta tva aneka tvayoḥ vyāpti siddhiḥ boddhavyā 
PVV_4.13,0–4.13,3	 uktam sva dṛṣṭa grahaṇasya sāphalyam artha grahaṇasya idānīm vaktavyam adṛṣṭa artha prakāśanam iti atra sūtre yat upāttam tad artha grahaṇam śabda kalpanā āropita ātmanām aliṅga tva prasiddhi artham arthāt arthasya siddhitaḥ tad artha grahaṇam śabdena kalpanayā ca āropitaḥ ātmā yeṣām pakṣa sa pakṣa anyatara tva ādīnām teṣām aliṅga tva prasiddhi artham boddhavyam kasmāt punar kalpitasya aliṅga tvam iti āha arthāt vastu bhūtāt liṅgāt arthasya sādhyasya siddhitaḥ 
PVV_4.14,0–4.14,3	 kalpanā āgamayoḥ karttuḥ icchā mātra anuvṛttitaḥ vastunaḥ ca anyathā bhāvāt tad kṛtāḥ vyabhicāriṇaḥ kalpanāyāḥ āgamasya śabdasya ca karttuḥ puruṣasya icchā mātrasya anuvṛtti tonurodhāt vastunaḥ ca anyathā bhāvāt karttuḥ icchā anuvṛtteḥ tābhyām śabda kalpanābhyām kṛtāḥ hetavaḥ vyabhicāriṇaḥ na aikāntikāḥ uktam artha grahaṇa prayojanam sva dṛṣṭa artha prakāśana śabdena trirūpa liṅga vacanam iṣṭam na pakṣa vacanam api iti vaktavyam 
PVV_4.15,0–4.15,3	 yadi sākṣāt pāramparyeṇa vā pakṣa vacanam sādhya prattipattau= upayujyate tadā ucyeta kintu etat na asti iti āha arthāt artha gateḥ śaktiḥ pakṣa hetu abhidhānayoḥ na arthe tena tayoḥ nna asti svatas sādhana saṃsthiti sākṣāt tāvata pakṣa abhidhānasya hetu abhidhānasya ca pratipādye arthe śaktiḥ na vidyate kim kāraṇam iti āha arthāt vacana pratipādyāt artha sādhyasya gateḥ na vacanāt tena sākṣāt artha pratipādaka tva abhāvena tayoḥ pakṣa hetu abhidhānayoḥ svatas svarūpeṇa sādhana saṃsthitiḥ sādhana tva vyavasthāḥ nāstiyataḥ ca pakṣa vacanam sākṣāt arthe na pramāṇam 
PVV_4.16,0–4.17,2	 tat pakṣa vacanam vaktuḥ abhiprāya nivedane pramāṇam saṃśaya utpatteḥ tatas sākṣāt na sādhanam tat tasmāt pakṣa vacanaṃvaktuḥ abhiprāya nivedane pramāṇam śabda prāmāṇyamā cā ryaḥ sya vadataḥ abhimatam iti boddhavyam tad pakṣa vacanāt sādhyertha saṃśaya utpatteḥ aniścayāt na sākṣāt sādhanam arthasya tat paraṃparayā sādhya sādhanāt pramāṇam pakṣa vacanam vaktuḥ abhiprāya nivedane pramāṇantarhi syāt iti āha sādhyasya eva abhidhānena pāraṃparyeṇa na api alam śaktasya sūcakam hetu vacaḥ aśaktam api svayam pāramparyeṇa api pakṣa vacana malam samartham na sādhya siddhau sādhyasya eva kevalasya abhidhānāt na hi pakṣa vacasā sādhakam kiñcid ucyate sādhya mātrasya eva abhidhānāt trirūpasya hetoḥ vvacaḥ vacanantu svayam sākṣāt siddhau= aśaktam api śaktasya trirūpa liṅgasya sūcakam pratipādakam iti sādhanam ucitam 
PVV_4.18,0–4.18,3	 nanu ācāryasya pakṣa vacanam asādhana tvena iṣṭam iti katham jñāyate iti āha hetu artha viṣaya tvena tad aśakta uktiḥ īritā śaktiḥ tasya api ced hetu vacanasya pravṛrttanāt hetoḥ arthaḥ sādhyaḥ sa viṣayosya iti hetu artha viṣayaḥ tatvena sādhya artha upadarśaka tvena tasya pakṣa vacanasya sādhya sādhanam pratyaśaktasya uktiḥ īritāḥ nirdiṣṭa ācāryeṇa tatra anumeya nirdeśaḥ hetu artha viṣayaḥ mataḥ iti anena granthena tatas jñāyate pakṣa vacanam asādhanam iṣṭam ācāryasya iti nanu tasya pakṣa vacanasya api sādhya siddhau śaktiḥ asti tad sādhakasya hetu vacanasi aprava na hi anuddiṣṭerthe sādhana prastāvaḥ tatas sādhana prastāvanā hetu tvena pakṣa vacanasya sādhaka tvam asti iti ced evam 
PVV_4.19,0–4.19,3	 tad saṃśayena jijñāsoḥ bhavet prakaraṇa āśrayaḥ tasya sādhya saṃśayena jijñāsā tasya añca satyām sādhanam ucyate iti jijñāsoḥpuṃsaḥ saṃśayaḥ jijñāsā ca prakaraṇasya sādhana prastāvasya āśrayaḥ nimittam iti bhavet sādhanam pakṣa vacana vat nanu saṃśaya jijñāse pratipādya pravartite pakṣa vacanantu vā ādi pravartitam tat katham tad samudāyasya sādhanasya vādinā nirdeśa saṃbhavaḥ iti āha vipakṣa upagamepi etat tulyam iti anavasthitiḥ 
PVV_4.19,4	 evantarhi vipakṣasya sādhya viruddhasya dharmasya upagame para abhiprāyeṇa nitya śabdaḥ iti sādhya nirdeśa kṛte pārśva sthānām tathā saṃśaya nirāsa artham yat kṛtakam tat anityam yathā ghaṭaḥ kṛtakaḥ ca śabdaḥ iti punar vādinā eva ucyate tadā nitya tva pratijñāyāḥ tat anitya tva avi abhicāri kṛtaka tva hetu pravarttaka tvam tulyam iti nitya tva pratijñāpi anitya pratijñāvat sādhanam syāt iti anavasthitiḥ sādhana avayavānām 
PVV_4.20,0–4.20,2	 yatas ca pakṣa vacanasya sādhya siddhau sākṣāt pāramparyeṇa vā sāmarthyam na asti tatas antaraṅgam tu sāmarthyam triṣu rūpeṣu saṃsthitam tatra smṛti samādhānam tad vacasi ā iva saṃsthitam antaraṅgam sāmarthyam tu śabdaḥ avadhāraṇe bhinnakramaḥ ca iti triṣu eva pakṣa dharmatā ādiṣu rūpeṣu saṃsthitam tatra trirūpa liṅge sādhya sādhana śakti smṛteḥ samādhānam āropaṇam trirūpa liṅga pratipādaka vacanaḥ eva saṃsthitam atas tat eva pāramparyeṇa sādhya siddheḥ aṅga tvāt pramāṇan na pakṣa vacanam 
PVV_4.21–4.22,0–4.21–4.22,3	 nanu akhyāpite hi viṣaye hetu vṛtteḥ asaṃbhavāt viṣaya khyāpanāt eva siddhau ced tasya śakta tā uktam atra akhyāpite apratipādite sādhanasya viṣaye sādhye hetoḥ vṛtteḥ eva hi asambhavāt tasya pakṣa vacanasya viṣaya khyāpanāt eva sādhyasya siddhau pāramparyeṇa śakta tā iti ced uktam atra saṃśaya jijñāsayoḥ api sādhana pravṛrttaka tvāt sādhana tva prasaṅgaḥ iti 
PVV_4.21–4.22,4–4.23,2	 kiñca vinā api asmāt kṛtakaḥ śabdaḥ īdṛśāḥ sarve anityāḥ iti proktā ipi arthāt tad nāśadhorbhavet asmāt pakṣa vacanāt vinā api kṛtakaḥ śabdaḥ īdaśāḥ ye kṛtakāḥ te sarvve anityā pakṣa dharma tā vyāpti vacane proktā ipi arthāt tasya śabdasya nāśadhīḥ bhavet anitya tva avi abhicāri kṛtaka tvam śabde varttamānam anitya tām tatra gamayati eva iti niṣphalam pakṣa vacanam tasmāt anuktau= api pakṣasya siddheḥ apratibandhataḥ triṣu anyatama rūpasya eva anuktiḥ nyūna toditā pakṣasya anuktau= api sādhya siddheḥ apratibandhataḥ avirodhāt tri pakṣa dharmatā ādiṣu rūpeṣu anyatamasya ekasya anuktiḥ nyūna toditā sādhana doṣaḥ na tu pakṣa ādya vacanam 
PVV_4.24,0–4.24,2	 yadi ca pratijñā sādhanam iṣyate tadā sādhya nirdeśaḥ pratijñā iti pratijñā lakṣaṇam ati vyāpi syāt asiddhasya hetoḥ dṛṣṭāntasya ca asiddhasya sādhya tvam sādhana tvañca asti iti pratijñā artham syāt yasya tu mate pratijñā na sādhanam sādhya uktim vā pratijñām sa vadan doṣaiḥ na yujyate sādhana adhikṛteḥ eva hetvābhāsā prasaṅgataḥ sa sādhyoktim sādhya nirdeśam pratijñām vadan= anantara uktaiḥ doṣaiḥ na yujyate sādhanā sādhana tvena adhikāra deva pratijñā arthasya hetvābhāseṣu aprasaṅgataḥ 
PVV_4.25,0–4.25,2	 yasmāt aviśeṣa uktiḥ api eka jātīye saṃśaya āvahā anyathā sarvu asādhya ukteḥ pratijñātvam prasajyate aviśeṣa uktiḥ sāmānya abhidhānam api eka jātīye saṃśaya āvahā tattva artha śaṅkā upa adhikā na sarvu atra iti nyāyaḥ tatas asādhanam eva sādhyam pratijñā na tu asiddha hetu dṛṣṭānta ādikam tasya sādhana tvena iṣṭa tvāt anyathā yadi evam na abhyupagamyate tadā sarvu asyāḥ sādhya ukteḥ ghaṭam karoti iti ādeḥ pratijñātvam prasajyate jñāpaka hetu adhikārāt tad sādhyasya eva pratijñātvam na kāraka hetu sādhyasya iti ced yadi evam asādhana bhūta sādhya nirdeśaḥ pratijñā na sādhana nirdeśaḥ iti siddham 
PVV_4.26,0–4.26,2	 syāt etat siddha ukteḥ sādhana tvāt ca parasya api na duṣyati idānīm sādhya nirdeśaḥ sādhana avayavaḥ katham parasya api siddha ukteḥ siddhārtha pratipādaka tvāt sādhana tvāt ca pratijñā tvam iṣṭam atas hetvābhāsa ādi pratijñātva prasaṅgena na duṣyati hetvābhāsa ādyasiddha tvāt asādhanam aṃsa adhana tvāt ca na pratijñā idānīm asmin= abhyupagame sādhya nirdeśaḥ asiddha tvāt sādhana avayavaḥ katham na hi pratijñā arthaḥ siddhaḥ tad artham eva sādhana upanyāsāt asiddhaḥ ca na sādhanam hetvābhāsa vat 
PVV_4.27,0–4.27,2^1	 yā ca sva yūthyānām pūrvva pakṣa parihāra uktiḥ sa ābhāsokya ādi upakṣepa parihāra viḍambanā asambaddhā tathā hi eṣa na nyāyyaḥ iti sūcitam pakṣa vacanam sādhanam sa ābhāsa artha tvāt iti ced na pratyakṣeṇa anekāntāt pratyakṣam sa ābhāsam api na kasyacid pramāṇasya sādhanam  vacana ātma tve sati sābhāsa tvāt sādhana tvam iti ced na dūṣaṇena anekāntāt dūṣaṇam sa ābhā saṃvacana ātma tvepi na sādhanam itisā api sa ābhāsa uktiḥ ādiḥ yasya tausā bhāsa ukti ādī upakṣepa parihārau tau= eva viḍamvanā ayukta tayā atas eva āha asambaddhā tathā sābhāsa tvasya viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa bhāvāt eva ahetu tvāt asambandhaḥ pūrvvapakṣaḥ tatas tam anumatya pratyakṣeṇa anekānta tā pādanam aśobhanam punarvacana ātma tvam viśeṣaṇam paroktam apratikṣipya dūṣaṇa ābhāsena anekānta tā pādanam ca ayuktam 
PVV_4.27,2^2	 tat eva hi hetoḥ vviśeṣaṇam upayuktam yat vipakṣāt hetum vyāvarttayati na ca vacana ātma tvā asādhana tvayoḥ kaścid virodhaḥ yena asādhanāt vacana ātma tva nivṛtteḥ vviśeṣaṇa sāphalyam syāt tathā hi eṣa vipakṣāt avyāvarttaka hetu viśeṣaṇa upanyāsaḥ na nyāyyaḥ iti varṇṇi taṃprāk veda nitya tā sidhyarthaṃmadhyayana pūrvvakam iti ukte bhārata adhyayanena anekānta tām āpāditām pratiṣeddhum veda adhyayana tve satī iti viśeṣaṇam mī mām sa kena upanyastam tat api kṛti pūrvvakam bhārata adhyayana vat syāt na kaścid virodhaḥ tatas vipakṣāt avyāvarttakam viśeṣaṇam ayuktam iti uktam prāk 
PVV_4.28,0–4.28,2	 nanu yadi pakṣa vacanam asādhanam sāmarthya gamyā abhidheyañca tadācā rye ṇa pakṣa lakṣaṇam kṛtam kimartham iti āha gamya artha tvepi sa adhya ukteḥ asaṃmohāya lakṣaṇam tad catur lakṣaṇam rūpa nipāteṣu svayam padaiḥ sādhya vyāpta pakṣa vacana sāmarthyāt gamya artha tvepi sādhya ukteḥ pakṣa vacanasya lakṣaṇam uktam asaṃmohāya vipratipatti nirākaraṇena sādhya pratipatti artham tathā hi ātma artha tvam sādhyam api sām khyāḥ asādhyam ācakṣate para artha tvam asādhyam api sādhyam iti santi vipratipattayaḥ tat ca sādhyam catur lakṣaṇam uktam sva rūpeṇa eva nirdeśyaḥ svayam iṣṭaḥ anirākṛtaḥ pakṣaḥ iti atra lakṣaṇa catuṣṭaya pratipādakaiḥ rupa nipāteṣu svayam padaiḥ yathākramam

PVV_4.46,0–4.46,2	 nanu kaiścid prakaraṇaiḥ icchā bhavet sā gamyate ca taiḥ balāt tava iccheyam iti vyaktam īśvara ceṣṭitam kaiścid prakaraṇaiḥ vvivāda ādibhiḥ icchā vādinaḥ kasmiścid dharme bhavet taiḥ eva ca prakaraṇaiḥ sā icchā gamyate pareṇa api na tu tasya dharmiṇaḥ dharmaḥ iti eva vādinā iṣyate tatas dhami dharma tva ādi sandigdha vipakṣa vyatireki tvāt śeṣavat svayam anicchataḥ ca vādinaḥ sādhanasya balāt tava iccheyam iti yat ucyate vyaktam idam īśvaram iti upahasati 
PVV_4.47,0–4.47,2	 kiñca vadan= a kārya liṅgām tām vyabhicāreṇa bādhyate anāntarīyake ca arthe bādhitenyasya kā kṣatiḥ tām icchām akārya liṅga jām kāryā itara liṅgām anumeya tvena vadan paraḥ vyabhicā na hi anyaḥ akāryaḥ anyam na vyabhicarati iti niyamosti api ca sādhyasa anitya tvasya ānantarīyake arthe ākāśa guṇa tva ādau bādhita tvepi anyasya sādhyasya kā na hi anitya tvam ākāśa guṇa tvanāntarīyakam yena tad abhāve tat api na syāt kṛtaka tvantu anitvatyatā avyabhicārī iti tasmāt na anumānam anaikāntikam 
PVV_4.48,0–4.48,1	 uktañca na āgama apekṣam anumānam sva gocare siddham tena su siddha tat na tadā śāstram īkṣyate anumāviṣaye na iṣṭam vācaḥ prāmāṇya mityādinā uktam prāk vastu bala pravṛttam anumānam na āgama apekṣam svasya gocare sādhyaḥ iti tasmāt tena vastu bala pravṛttena āgamānapekṣiṇā anumāne yat siddham su siddhantat tadā ca na śāstram īkṣyate bādhitam na vā iti vastu bala pravṛtta anumānena tad apekṣā bhāvāt tadā anukāle śāstrasya anāśrayaṇāt 
PVV_4.49,0–4.49,1	 vāda tyāgaḥ tadā syāt ced na tadā anabhyupāyataḥ upāyaḥ hi abhyupāye ayam anaṅgam sa tadā api san vāda tyāgaḥ syāt ced na vāda tyāgaḥ sisādhayiṣita eka dharmāt aparasya śāstra abhyupetasya tadā sādhana upanyāsa kāle sādhya tayā anabhyupāyataḥ asvīkārāt nanu śāstra abhyupagamāt yadā vādaḥ kriyate tadā śāstra artha bādhanāt vāda tyāgaḥ syāt eva iti āha śāstrasya abhyupāye ayam vicāra aupāyaḥ tatas tadā vicāra kāle san= api abhyupagamaḥ anaṅgam śāstra artha grahaṇe gṛhītasya tyāgaḥ syāt na vicārāt prāk grahaṇam abhyupagamāt nyāyyam 
PVV_4.50,0–4.50,2	 kadā tarhi śāstreṇa bādhā iṣyate iti āha tadā viśuddhe viṣaya dvaye śāstra parigraham cikīrṣoḥ sa hi kālaḥ syāt tadā śāstreṇa bādhanam śāstra upadarśite viṣaya dvaye pratyakṣa parokṣe rūpa nairātmya ādau tadā pramāṇa pravṛttyā viśuddhe nirṇṇīte sati paścāt atyanta parokṣe svarga ādau śāstreṇa śāstra āśrayaṇena anumānam cikīrṣoḥ sataḥ sa hi kālaḥ abhyugamya yadi śāstra bādhaḥ na bhavet atas tadā śāstreṇa bādhanam sādhya sādhana ādeḥ iṣyate 
PVV_4.51,0–4.51,2	 tat api karamāt śāstra bādha iṣyate iti āha tad virodhena cintāyāḥ tad siddha artheṣu ayogataḥ tṛtīya sthāna saṃkrāntau nyāyyaḥ śāstra parigrahaḥ tasya śāstrasya virodhena tad siddheṣu artheṣu liṅga ādiṣu asiddha kalpeṣu gamaka cintāyāḥ ayogataḥ yasmāt pratyakṣa parokṣa arthayoḥ na āgama adhikāraḥ tasmāt tṛtī atīndriye viṣaye vicāra saṃkrāntaḥ śāstra parigrahaḥ nyāyyaḥ prakāra antara abhāvāt 
PVV_4.52,0–4.52,1	 tatra api sādhya dharmasya na antarīyaka bādhanam parihāryam na ca anyeṣām anavasthā prasaṅgataḥ tatra śāstre parigrahepi tadā sādhayitum ārabdhasya sādhya dharmasya yat na antarīya sambaddham yathā kṣaṇika tvasya nairātmyam tasya bādhanam parihāryam vastutas tāt ātmyāt anayoḥ nairātmya bādhane kṣaṇika tva bādhana prasaṅgāt na tu anyeṣām sādhyasya akāraṇa avyāpaka bhūtānām dharmāṇām bādhanam parihāryam anavasthā prasaṅgataḥ na hi śāstra darśita sambhava dharma vyāpti liṅgasya dṛṣṭānte darśayitum śakyate yena kaścid āgama āśrayaḥ hetuḥ avatiṣṭheta 
PVV_4.53,0–4.53,2	 nanu śāstram anapekṣya na vādaḥ karttavyaḥ iti vastu bala pravṛttā anumānepi śāstra apekṣā iti āha kena iyam sarva cintāsu śāstram grāhyam iti sthitiḥ kṛta idānīm asiddhāntaiḥ grāhyaḥ dhūmena na analaḥ sarvvāsu parokṣa atyanta parokṣa artha cintāsu śāstram grāhyam iti kena iyam sthitiḥ kṛtā na etat anumanyante vidvān saḥ idānīm aviduṣām asmin= abhyupagame asiddhāntaiḥ siddhānta viśeṣa āśraya rahitaiḥ gopālaka ādibhiḥ ddhū mena liṅgena na analaḥ grāhyaḥ 
PVV_4.54,0–4.54,2	 na ca kasyacid siddhānta sambandhaḥ yuktaḥ tathā hi sambandhaḥ bhavan sahajaḥ vā bhavet aupādhikaḥ vā dvayam api niṣeddhum āha riktasya janta ūḥ jjātasya guṇa doṣam apaśyataḥ vilabdhāḥ vata kena amī siddhānta viṣamagrahāḥ riktasya tucchasya siddhānta rahitasya jantoḥ jātasya anena sahaja sambandha abhāva nimittam uktam guṇa doṣam prāmāṇya aprāmāṇya nibandhanam apaśyataḥ anena aupādhika sambandha nimitta abhāvaḥ uktaḥ kena anartha paṭīyasā siddhāntāeva viṣama grahāḥ duṣparihāra tvāt ime vilabdha avata yeṣu svāmi tvena jantavaḥ vyavaharanti na hi karṇṇa nāśam iva siddhāntaḥ prāṇa sahajaḥ na api doṣa ūrjjita guṇa upapannaḥ pramāṇam iva vicārāt prāk siddhāntaḥ siddhaḥ yena samartha viṣayaḥ syāt 
PVV_4.55,0–4.55,2	 kiñca yadi sādhanaḥ ekatra sarvam śāstram nidarśane darśayet sādhanam syāt iti eṣā lokottarā sthitiḥ yadi sādhanaḥ ekatra sarvvam śāstram śāstra artham nidarśane dṛṣṭānte vādī darśayet tadā tat sādhanam syāt na tu ekasya śāstra darśita dharmasya anvaye etat ca na kvacid sādhane karttum śakyam iti loka atikrāntā sthitiḥ eṣā 
PVV_4.56,0–4.56,2	 api ca asambaddhasya dharmasya kim asiddhau na siddhati hetuḥ tad sādhanāya uktaḥ kim duṣṭaḥ tatra sidhyati asambaddhasya sādhayitum apravṛttasya dharmasya ākāśa guṇa tva ādeḥ kṛtaka tvāt hetoḥ vviparyāsa nāt asiddhau satyām sisā dhayiṣitam hetu vyāpakam anitya tvam kim na sidhyati na hi vyāpakam antareṇa vyāpyam bhavati hetuḥ tasya vyāpakasya sādhanāya uktaḥ kinduṣṭaḥtatra sva sādhye sidhyati sādhya pratipādanam sādhya vyāpāraḥ tat ced asti katham duṣṭaḥ 
PVV_4.57,0–4.57,2	 śāstra artha bādhane abhimatasya api na siddhiḥ iti ced āha dharmān anupanīya eva dṛṣṭānte dharmiṇaḥ akhilān vāgdhūma ādeḥ janonvā iti caitanya dahana ādikam dharmiṇaḥ dharmān śāstra darśitān akhilān hetu vyāpaka tvena anupanīya apradarśyam vāgdhūma ādeḥ hetoḥ caitanya dahana ādikam yathākramam sva santāna vat mahān asa vat ca janaḥ anveti pratipadyate 
PVV_4.58,0–4.58,2	 kiñca svabhāvam kāraṇam ca arthaḥ avyabhicāreṇa sādhayan kasyacid vāda bādhāyām svabhāvāt na nivartate svabhāvam vyāpakam vṛkṣa tva ādi kāraṇam vahni ādi ca arthaḥ vyāpyaḥ śiṃśapā ādiḥ kāryam dhūma ādiḥ avyabhicāreṇa avinābhāvi tvāt sādhayan kasyacid śāstra para adhīnasya vādinaḥ vādasya bādhāyām svabhāvāt vyāpaka kāraṇa gamakān na nivarttate tatas śāstreṣu dharma antara vyāhatau= api hetuḥ sādhyīkṛtam sva sambaddham artham pratipādayati 
PVV_4.59,0–4.59,2	 tatas ca prapadyamānaḥ ca anyaḥ tam na antarīyakam īpsitaiḥ sādhya artha ehetunā tena katham apratipāditaḥ sādhyaiḥ arthaiḥ īpsitaiḥ āptam pratyetum aṣṭaiḥ nnāntirīyakam avinā bhāvinam tam hetum prapadyamānaḥ pratipadyamānonyaḥ prativādī kathantena hetunā apratipāditaḥ sādhyana antarīyaka tayā kvacid dharmiṇi sādhana pratītiḥ eva hi sādhya pratītiḥ sā ca asti prativādinaḥ 
PVV_4.60,0–4.60,4	 kiñca hetunā yaḥ śāstra arthaḥ bādhyate kintasmin sādhye vādīnāḥ hetuḥ asādhūktaḥ āha uśvit tatra sādhye hetuḥ ucyatām mā vā vastutas tad vādhakosau hetuḥ iti duṣṭa tā tatra ādya pakṣe bhavati eva doṣaḥ yadi evam iṣyate atha uktaḥ anuktā upi vā hetuḥ viroddhā vādinotra kim na hi tasya ukti doṣeṇa sa jātaḥ śāstra bādhanaḥ uktaḥ anuktā upi vā hetuḥ vastutas eva tasya viroddhā pratighātakaḥ tadā tatra śāstra artha bādhane vādinaḥ kindūṣaṇam na kiñcid hi yasmāt tasya vādinaḥ ukti doṣeṇa sa kṛtaka tva ādi hetuḥ śāstrasya śāstra arthasya ākāśa guṇa tva ādeḥ bādhanaḥ 
PVV_4.61,0–4.61,1	 bādhakasya abhidhānāt ced doṣaḥ yadi vadet na saḥ kin na bādheta saḥ akurvan= ayuktam kena duṣyati śāstra artha bādhakasya hetoḥ abhidhānāt vādinā upi doṣaḥ ced yadi tam hetum na vadet vādī tadā kim asau hetuḥ śāstra artha na bādheta vastutas tad virodhi tvāt avaśyam bādhate tatas ca sa vādya kurvan= ayuktam kena kāraṇena duṣyati parājitaḥ syāt 
PVV_4.62,0–4.62,2	 nanu yadi duṣṭa hetu vacanepi na vādinaḥ duṣṭa tā tadā asiddha ādi vacanepi na doṣaḥ syāt iti āha anyeṣu hetvābhāseṣu sveṣṭasi eva aprasādhanāt duṣyet vyartha abhidhānena na atra tasya prasādhanāt anyeṣu asiddha ādiṣu hetvābhāseṣu vādyukteṣu sva iṣṭasya vādī iṣṭasya eva aprasādhanāt vādī duṣyati vyarthasya sādhya sādhana anupayuktasya sādhanasya abhidhānāt atra kṛtaka tve tu vādi ukte vāñchitasya anitya tvasya prasādhanāt na vādī duṣyati śāstra arthe tu vādya niṣṭe bādhyamāne śāstram eva duṣṭam bhaviṣyati

PVV_4.65,0–4.65,2	 yadi tarhi ākāśa guṇa tva abhāvepya nitya tvam sidhyat a bādhyam śabde tadā śrāvaṇa tva ādi hetunā nitya tvam api sādhya mānam abādhyam syāt iti āha viruddhayoḥ eka dharmiṇī ayogāt aḥ tu bādhanam viruddha aikāntike na atra tadvat asti virodhitā viruddhayoḥ nnitya tva anitya tvayoḥ ekatra śabde dharmiṇī ayogāt viruddha aikāntike viruddha avyabhicāriṇi śrāvaṇa tva ādau nitya tva sādhake bādhanam astu na hi ekatra dharmiṇi viruddhau dharmaḥ bhavitum arhataḥ tadvat nitya tvayoḥ iva atra anayoḥ prakṛta aprakṛtayoḥ anitya tva ākāśa guṇa tva abhāvayoḥ vvirodhitā na asti tatas kṛtaka tvāt śabde anitya tva siddhau= ākāśa guṇa tva abhāvaḥ na bādhyate

PVV_4.67,0–4.67,1	 sambandhaḥ tena tasya eva bādhanāt asti ced asat hetoḥ saru u asya cintya tvāt sva sādhye guṇa doṣayoḥ atha tatra śabdaḥ eva dharmiṇi ākāśa guṇa tvasya sattvāt sambandha usti tena kṛtaka tvāt tasya eva bādhanāt virodhaḥ pṛthivī guṇa tvantu śabde dharmiṇī a sambaddham tatas tad bādhanepi śabde kṛtaka tvam aviruddham iti ced asat etat sarvu asya hetoḥ prakṛte guṇa doṣayoḥ cintya tvāt yat punar aprakṛtam dharmi sambaddham api na tat sādhyam tad vādhanepi na kācid kṣatiḥ

PVV_4.69,0–4.69,2	 yat api āhuḥ ācāryīyāḥ śāstram abhyupagamya yadā vādaḥ kriyate tadā śāstra dṛṣṭasya sakalasya dharmasya sādhyatā iti atra āha śāstra abhyupagamāt sādhyaḥ śāstra dṛṣṭaḥ akhilaḥ yadi pratijñā asiddha dṛṣṭānta hetuvādaḥ prasajyate śāstra abhyupagamāt śāstra dṛṣṭaḥ akhilaḥ dharmaḥ yadi sādhyaḥ iṣyate tadā a siddhayoḥ śāstra uddiṣṭayoḥ hetu dṛṣṭāntayoḥ vvādaḥ pratijñā sādhyam prasajyate śāstre dṛṣṭasya asiddhasya sādhya tvāt 
PVV_4.70,0–4.71,1	 syāt etat kintu uktayoḥ sādhana tvena no ced īpsita vādataḥ nyāya prāptam na sādhya tvam vacanāt vinivarttate vādinā īpsitasya sādhya tvena vādataḥ svayam sādhya tvena īpsitaḥ pakṣaḥ viruddha tvāt nirākṛtaḥ iti ādikāt sādhana tvena uktayoḥ asiddha hetu dṛṣṭāntayoḥ sādhya tā naḥ nanu asiddhasya śāstra abhyupagatasya sādhya tvam nyāya prāptam vacana mātrāt īpsita sādhya tvam pratipādaka tvāt na vinivarttate anīpsitam asādhyañcet vādinā anya upyanīpsitaḥ dharmaḥ asādhyaḥ tadā asādhyam bādhamānam virodhi kim śāstra abhyupagamepi vādinā anīpsi evantarhi ākāśa guṇa tva ādiḥ api dharmaḥ vādinā sādhya tvena anīpsitaḥ asādhyaḥ syāt tadā tad asādhyam ākāśa guṇa tvam bādhamānam kṛtaka tvam kim kasmāt virodhi 
PVV_4.72,0–4.72,2	 kiñca pakṣa lakṣaṇa bāhya arthaḥ svayaṃśabda upyanarthakaḥ śāstreṣu icchā pravṛtti arthaḥ yadi śaṅkā kutonu iyam yadi śāstra abhyupagata tvam pakṣa lakṣaṇam tadā svayaṃśabdopi pakṣa lakṣaṇa bāhya arthaḥ bhinna abhidheyaḥ anarthakaḥ syāt śāstra abhyupagame śāstra iṣṭasya sādhya tā prāptau vādīṣṭa mātram sādhyam na anyat iti hi svayaṃśabdasya prayojanam śāstra iṣṭa mātrasya tu sādhya tve niṣphalam eva tat śāstreṣu icchayā pravṛtti arthaḥ svayaṃśabdaḥ yadi kathyate svayaṃśabdam antareṇa śāstram icchayā na grahītavyam iti śaṅkā iyam kutas nu hetoḥ jātā yena tad nivṛtti arthā svayaṃśrutiḥ vvarṇyate 
PVV_4.73,0–4.73,1	 soniṣiddhaḥ pramāṇena gṛhṇan kena nivāryate niṣiddhaḥ ced pramāṇena vācā kena pravṛrttyate sa vādī pramāṇena śāstra artha bādhakena aniṣiddhaḥ śāstram gṛhṇan kena nivāryate na kenacid yatas svayaṃgrahaṇam śāstram grāhayat saphalam syāt pramāṇena ced śāstra artha bādhakena niṣiddhaḥ vādī vācā svayaṃśabdena śāstra abhyupagame kena lakṣaṇa kartrā pravarttyate na kenacid 
PVV_4.74,0–4.74,2	 kiñca pūrvam api eṣa siddhāntam sva icchayā eva gṛhītavān kiñcid anyam sa tu punar grahītum labhate na kiṃm eṣa vādī pūrvvam api sveccheyā eva siddhāntam kaḥ ṇā dā dipraṇītam gṛhītavān na tu anyapurāṇa ādi balāt sa katham icchayā śāstra uddiṣṭa kiñcid dharma vyabhicāra darśana ādinā śāstreṣu saphala dharma kalāpa sādhya tvāt anyam siddhāntam ākāśa guṇa tva rahita anitya tā ādikam grahītum kin na labhate icchā adhīna tve niyama ayogāt tasmāt svayaṃgrahaṇam śāstra icchā pravṛtti artham iti ayuktam 
PVV_4.75,0–4.75,2	 nanu iṣṭasya api sva icchayā eva sādhya tā parigrahaḥ siddhaḥ iti vyartham svayaṃgrahaṇam iti āha dṛṣṭeḥ vipratipattīnām atra akārṣīt svayaṃśrutim iṣṭa akṣatim asādhya tvam anavasthāñca darśayan śāstra kārasya iṣṭam sādhyam iti vipratipattīnām dṛṣṭeḥ tad nirākaṇa artham atra pakṣa lakṣaṇe svayaṃśrutim ācāryaḥ akārṣīt śāstreṣu ākāśa guṇa tva asiddhau= api vādī iṣṭasya akṣatim śāstra iṣṭasya asādhya tvam śāstra iṣṭa dharma antara asiddhau hetu bala prasiddha sādhya bādhane gandhe bhūta guṇa tā ābādhāyām śabde kṛtaka tvam anitya tva sādhanam viruddham syāt ityādi kāma navasthāñca parasya darśayat = ācā ryaḥ svayaṃśrutim akārṣīt iti pūrvveṇa sambandhaḥ 
PVV_4.76,0–4.76,1	 samayā ahita bhedasya parihāreṇa dharmiṇaḥ prasiddhasya gṛhi iti arthāḥ jagāda anyaḥ svayaṃśrutim samayena siddhāntena āhitaḥ āropitaḥ bhedaḥ viśeṣaḥ ākāśa guṇa tva ādiḥ yasya tasya dharmiṇaḥ parihāreṇa āgama nirapekṣa pramāṇa balāt prasiddhasya dharmiṇaḥ śabda mātra ādeḥ gṛhītiḥ iti arthaḥ prayojanam yaḥ tāḥ tām svayaṃśrutim anyaḥ svam prasiddhaḥ dharmī kāryaḥ na āgam a siddhaḥ iti arthaḥ 
PVV_4.77,0–4.77,2	 atra āha vicāra prastuteḥ eva prasiddhaḥ siddhaḥ āśrayaḥ sva icchā kalpita bhedeṣu padārtheṣu avivādataḥ dharmiṇi sādhya dharmasya bhāva abhāva vicāra prastuteḥ eva āgamam anapekṣya prasiddhaḥ āśrayaḥ dharmī siddhaḥ sva icchayā kalpitaḥ bhedaḥ viśeṣaḥ yeṣām teṣu padārtheṣu avivādataḥ vivāda abhāvāt na hi kalpita bhede dharmiṇi kaścid prekṣāvān kasyacid dharmasya sādhanam bādhanam vehate kintu pramāṇa pratīte vastuni atas tad artham api svayaṃgrahaṇam anupayuktam 
PVV_4.78,0–4.78,1	 asādhyatām atha prāha siddhādeśena dharmiṇaḥ sva rūpeṇa eva nirdeśyaḥ iti anena eva tad gatam atha siddhādeśena prasiddha artha vācakena svayaṃśabdena dharmiṇaḥ asādhya tām prāha yathā asti pradhānam bhedānām anupadarśanāt iti idam api ayuktam yasmāt sva rūpeṇa sādhya tvena eva nirdeśyaḥ iti anena pakṣa lakṣaṇa avayavena eva ca tad dharmiṇaḥ siddhasya asādhya tvam gatam pratītam 
PVV_4.79,0–4.79,2	 tathā hi ayam iṣṭaḥ anirākṛtaḥ pakṣaḥ iti anena siddha sādhana rūpeṇa nirdeśasya hi sambhave sādhya tva ena iva nirdeśyaḥ iti idam phalavat bhavet siddhasya siddha rūpeṇa nirdeśasya dharma vacanasya asiddhasya api sādhana rūpeṇa nirdeśasya asiddha vacanasya pakṣatva sambhave hi tat pratiṣedham vidadhat sādhya tvena eva nirdeśyaḥ iti idam phalavat bhavet sādhyasya eva nirdeśaḥ pakṣaḥ iti siddhasya dharmiṇaḥ asiddhasya ca sādhana tvena uktasya nirāsaḥ 
PVV_4.80,0–4.80,2	 kiñca anumānasya sāmānya viṣaya tvañca varṇṇitam iha evam na hi anuktopi kiñcid pakṣe virudhyate anumānasya sāmānya viṣaya tvam svayam ācāryeṇa varṇṇitam yadi ca dharmī pakṣaḥ tadā tasya sva lakṣaṇa tvāt sāmanya viṣaya tā vyāhanyeta kiñca iha pakṣa lakṣaṇaḥ eva krameṇa anuktepi svayaṃśabde siddha dharmya siddha sādhana vyavaccheda arthe kiñcid pakṣe pratipādye na virudhyate 
PVV_4.81,0–4.81,2	 nanu anukte svayaṃśabde pakṣa lakṣaṇam kuryāt ced dharmiṇam sādhyam tatas kintan na śakyate kasmāt hetu anvaya abhāvāt na ca doṣaḥ tayoḥ api dharmiṇam sādhyam kuryāt iti doṣaḥ tatas dharmiṇaḥ pakṣatva prasaṅgāt kindūṣaṇam tad dharmmi pakṣa tvam karttum na śakyate iti aśakyatā dūṣaṇam kasmāt kāraṇāt dharmī pakṣaḥ bhavitu na arhati dharmiṇaḥ sādhya tvena asiddha tāyām hetoḥ abhāvāt viśeṣasya dharmiṇaḥ dṛṣṭānte asambhavāt anvaya abhāvāt ca dharmī pakṣaḥ karttum na śakyate 
PVV_4.82,0–4.82,2	 nanu ayam doṣaḥ tayoḥ hetu dṛṣṭāntayoḥ na tu pakṣasya tathā hi uttara avayava apekṣaḥ na doṣaḥ pakṣaḥ iṣyate tathā hetu ādi doṣa upi pakṣa doṣaḥ prasajyate sādhana vākyasya pakṣāt uttare avayave hetu dṛṣṭānta ādike apekṣā yasya asau doṣaḥ pakṣe na iṣyate hetu dṛṣṭānta sambandhi tvāt tasya yadi tu uttara avayava apekṣā upi pakṣasya bādhanāt pakṣa doṣaḥ ucyate tathā sati hetu ādi doṣa upi pakṣa doṣaḥ prasajyate 
PVV_4.83,0–4.84,2	 sarvaiḥ pakṣasya bādhātaḥ tasmāt tanmātra saṅginaḥ pakṣa doṣāḥ matāḥ na anye pratyakṣa ādi virodha vat sarvvaiḥ hetu ādi doṣaiḥ pakṣasya bādhāt tasmāt tanmātraṅginaḥ pakṣa mātra sambaddhāḥ doṣāḥ pakṣa doṣāḥ matāḥ na anye avayava antara apekṣāḥ pratyakṣa ādi virodha vat yathā pratyakṣa ādi bādhita tvam avayava antara anapekṣam pakṣa doṣaḥ tasmāt hetu ādi lakṣaṇaiḥ bbādhyam muktvā pakṣasya lakṣaṇam ucyate parihāra artham avyāpti vyatirekayoḥ hetu ādīnām lakṣaṇaiḥ bbādhyam pariharttavyam doṣam anvaya virodha ādikam muktvā pakṣa mātra anuṣaṅgiṇa uḥ avya āpti vyatirekayoḥ parihāra artham pakṣa lakṣaṇam ucyatevyatireke ādhikyam abhivyāptiḥ iti arthaḥ 
PVV_4.85,0–4.85,2	 tatra yena padena yat dūṣaṇam parihriyate tat āha svayat nipāta rūpa ākhyāḥ vyatirekasya bādhikāḥ saha anirākṛtena iṣṭa śruti ḥ avyāpti bādhanī svayañca nipātañcaḥ evam rūpam sva rūpañcā ākhyā śrutayaḥ saha anirākṛtena padena vyatirekasya ati vyāpteḥ bbādhikāḥ svayaṃśabdena śāstra iṣṭasya nipātena asiddhasya api sādhana tvena uktasya sva rūpa śabdena siddhasya nirākṛta śabdena pratyakṣa ādi nirākṛtasya pakṣa tvam saktam niṣidhyate iṣṭa śrutiḥ avyāpteḥ bbādhanī iyamāṇe nirddiṣṭam eva sādhyam sādhyam syāt na prakaraṇa āpannam iṣṭam 
PVV_4.86,0–4.86,1	 yadi svayaṃnipāta rūpa ākhyāḥ vyatirekasya vā adhikāḥ pra mā ṇa sa mu cca yala kṣa ṇe nirddiṣṭāḥ tadā nyāya mukhe sādhya tvena īpsitaḥ pakṣaḥ viruddha artha anirākṛtā eti pakṣa lakṣaṇe tāḥ na santi iti kathantena avyāpti vyatirekayoḥ parihāraḥ iti āha sādhya tvena īpsitaḥ pakṣaḥ iti sādhya abhyupagamaḥ pakṣa lakṣaṇam teṣu apakṣatā nirākṛte bādhanataḥ śeṣe alakṣaṇa vṛttitaḥ 
PVV_4.86,2	 sādhya abhyupagamaḥ pakṣaḥ iti pakṣa lakṣaṇam avatiṣṭhate tathā ca teṣu śāstra iṣṭa ādiṣu pañcasu vyāvarttyeṣu madhye nirākṛte pratyakṣa ādi bādhite bādhanataḥ apakṣatā viruddha arthāḥ nirākṛtasya pakṣa vidhānāt śeṣe śāstra iṣṭe vādinā aniṣṭe sādhane ca siddhe sādhayitum iṣṭaḥ eṣyamāṇe siddhe ca sādhya viparīte aprastute ca ukta mātre lakṣaṇasya sādhya tvena īpsita tvasya āvṛttitaḥ apakṣatā siddhā iti paripūrṇṇam idam api lakṣaṇam 
PVV_4.87,0–4.87,2	 nanu yathā satyarthebhyaḥ varttamāne ku vidhānāt īpsita śabdaḥ varttamānam icchām āha tathā iṣṭa śabdopi tatra eṣiṣyamāṇe pakṣa tvam aprasaktam eva tat kim pra mā ṇasa mu cca yaḥ lakṣaṇe avadhāraṇam kṛtam iti āha svayam iṣṭa abhidhānena gata artha īpi avadhāraṇe kṛtya antena abhisambandhāt uktam kāla antara= chide svayam iṣṭaḥ iti anayoḥ padayoḥ abhidhānena avadhāraṇe nipāta arthe gate pratītepi kṛtya antena nirdeśya śabdena sarvu akāla sambandha yogya abhidhāyinā abhisambandha ādiṣṭa śabdasya āvarttamāna kāla icchā viṣayasya api pakṣa tvam syāt yathā āgataḥ devadattaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ iti yadā gamiṣyati tadā drakṣyate iti arthaḥ atas vartamāna kālāt kāla antarasya bhaviṣyat ādeḥ sādhye sādhya icchā viṣayasya cchide pratiṣedha artham uktam avadhāraṇam sva rūpeṇa eva iti 
PVV_4.88,0–4.88,2	 yasmāt kṛtyā antena abhisambandhāt kāla sāmānya vṛttiḥ iha anaṅga miṣeḥ nniṣṭhā tena īpsita pade punar aṅgam eva tayā asiddha hetu ādi pratiṣidhyate iha pramāṇa samuccaya lakṣaṇe niṣṭhā varttamāna sādhya tva iṣṭi pratipādanam ati anaṅga hetuḥ nyā yaḥ mu khe tena kṛtyā antena sambandha abhāvena īpsita pade punar aṅgam eva niṣṭhā varttamāna sādhya icchā bodhane tayā āvartta māna sādhya icchā bodhikayā asiddhapīṣyamāṇam sādhya tvena pratiṣidhyate tasmāt na dharmiṇaḥ sādhya tā pratikṣepa artham svayaṃgrahaṇam siddha tvena eva tad parihārasya labdha tvāt 
PVV_4.89,0–4.89,2	 na api śāstreṣu icchā pravṛtti artham icchā mātreṇa eva tad grahaṇasya siddha tvāt iti uktam avācaka tvat ca ayuktam tena iṣṭam svayam ātmanā anapekṣya akhilam śāstram tat vādīṣṭasya sādhya tā avācaka tvāt ca ayuktam tad artham svaya grahaṇam na hi svayaṃśabdaḥ sva icchayā śāstram grāhyām iti etad artha vācakam kintu vādinaḥ eva vācakaḥ tena tad vācaka tvena svayam vādinā atmanā śāstram akhilam anapekṣya yat iṣṭam tasya vādīṣṭasya sādhyateṣyate na śāstra iṣṭasya iti upasaṃhāraḥ 
PVV_4.90,0–4.90,1	 tena anabhīṣṭa saṃsṛṣṭasya iṣṭasya api hi bādhane yathā sādhyam abādhataḥ pakṣa hetūna duṣyataḥ tena kāraṇena vādinā ūna bhīṣṭena ākāśa guṇa tvena saṃsṛṣṭasya iṣṭasya anitya tvasya api abhidhīyamāne pakṣa hetū na duṣyataḥ kiṅgākāraṇam iti āha yathā sādhyamaḥ na hi vādinā akāśa guṇa tva eka artha samavāyi anitya tvam sādhayitum iṣṭam yena asya bādhaḥ syāt kintu a nitya tva mātram na ca asya pratyakṣa ādi bādhā asti hetoḥ vvā tad apekṣayā viruddhatā ādikam tat evam svayaṃnipāta rūpa ākhyāḥ vyatirekasya bādhikāḥ saha anirākṛtena iti vyākhyātam 
PVV_4.91,0–4.91,2	 anirākṛta padam vyākhyātum āha aniṣiddhaḥ pramāṇābhyām sa ca upagamaḥ iṣyate sandigdhe hetu vacanāt vyastaḥ hetoḥ anāśrayaḥ sa ca ukta lakṣaṇaḥ sādhyasya upagamaḥ pakṣaḥ pramā pratyakṣa anumānābhyām aniṣiddhaḥ iṣyate kasmāt iti āha saṃdigdhe arthe sādhaka bādhaka pramāṇa viṣaye hetoḥ vvacanāt pramāṇa pratikṣiptaḥ hetoḥ anāśrayaḥ aviṣayaḥ 
PVV_4.92,0–4.92,2	 yadi dvividhau pakṣa bādhau tadā pratyakṣa anumāna āptaiḥ prasiddhena iti katha mā cā rye ṇa caturvvidhā sā darśitā iti āha anumānasya bhedena sā bādhā uktā caturvidhāḥ tatra abhyupāyaḥ kārya aṅgam svabhāva aṅgam jagastthitiḥ anumānasya bhedena traividhyena pratyakṣeṇa ca ekena saha sā bādhā caturvvidha uktāḥ teṣu bādhakeṣu abhyupāyaḥ āpta sva vacane kāryam aṅgam jagataḥ sthitiḥ vyavahṛtiḥ prasiddhiḥ svabhāvaḥ aṅgam hetuḥ 
PVV_4.93,0–4.93,2	 kasmāt punar āpta vacanam sva vacanañca abhyupāyaḥ ucyate iti āha ātma aparodha abhimataḥ bhūta niścaya yukta vāc āptaḥ sva vacanam śāstram ca ekam uktam samatvataḥ ātma aparodha abhimataḥ bhūtasya arthasya niścayena yuktā prayuktā vāc yasya saḥ āptaḥ ucyate evam paraṃparayā artha kārya tvena sva vacanam śāstrañca samatvataḥ abhyupāyaḥ iti samasya kārya liṅgam ekam uktam 
PVV_4.94,0–4.94,2	 kiñca yathā ātmanaḥ apramāṇa tve vacanam na pravarttate śāstra siddhe tathā na arthe vicāraḥ tat anāśraye vaktuḥ ātmanaḥ apramāṇa tve prāmāṇya nimitta abhāvāt vacanaṃprāmāṇyam na pravarttate na hi asatyā arthena vacanena paraḥ pratipādayitum śakyate visamvādana āśrayasya vacanāt arthāpatteḥ tatas yathā pratipādayituḥ prāmāṇyaḥ eva sati vacanam pravarttate tathā śāstrasya śāstra prāmāṇyasya anāśrayeṇa na vicāraḥ pravarttate pramāṇa viṣayaḥ labdhaḥ sākṣāt asya eva pramāṇasya śāstrasya atyanta parokṣa arthe vicāraḥ prastūyate prekṣaiḥ nānasya tatas śāstra sva vacanayoḥ prāmāṇye abhyupagatepi sāmyam uktam 
PVV_4.95,0–4.95,2	 sāmyam eva punar kim artham upadarśitām iti āha tad prastāva āśraya tve hi śāstram bādhakam iti amum vaktum artham su avācā asya saha uktiḥ sāmya dṛṣṭaye hi yasmāt tad prastāvasya vicāra prakramasya āśraya tve adhikaraṇa tve sati śāstram dharmiṇi śāstram pratijñā artha viruddhaṃbādhakam na vastu bala pravṛtta anumānam iti amum artham masya śāstrasya sva darśana artham saha uktiḥ anayoḥ abhyupāyatā nirdeśe sva vacanam api hi uccāraṇa sāmarthyāt upagata prāmāṇyam siddhe dharmiṇi vicāra prakrame pratijñā artha viṣaya bādhakam bādhakam dṛṣṭam na vastu bala pravṛtta anumānena idam anayoḥ sāmya darśana prayojanam 
PVV_4.96–4.97,0–4.96–4.97,1	 udāhāraṇam api atra sadṛśam tena varṇitam pramāṇānām abhāve hi śāstra vācoḥ ayogātaḥ atra śāstra vacanayoḥ vyāghātenā cā rye ṇa udāharaṇam api sadṛśam abhinnam varṇṇitam yathā na santi pramāṇāni prameya arthāni iti katham punar atra śāstra artha sva vacanābhyām vyāghātaḥ iti āha pramāṇānām abhāve hi śāstra vācoḥ ayogātaḥ anupapatteḥ pramāṇa sambhave hi śāstra vacanayoḥ para pratipādana artha muktiḥ yuktā tasmāt uccāraṇa sāmarthyāt abhyupagata prāmāṇyāt prayoga vacanāt eva pramāṇa abhāva pratijñā bādhyate 
PVV_4.96–4.97,2–4.96–4.97,4	 etat ca udāharaṇam sva vāc virodhe vispaṣṭam udāharaṇam āgame diś mātra darśanam tatra pratyedharmaḥ sukha pradaḥ sva vāc virodhe sva vacana vyāhatau vispaṣṭam tathā hi pramāṇa abhāva pratijñā vacana uccāraṇa sāmarthya abhyupagata prāmāṇyena vacanena eva bādhyate āgame śāstre punar udāharaṇasya diś mātra darśanam upalakṣaṇa mātram etat na tu mukhyam udāharaṇam pramāṇasya dharmiṇaḥ āgama siddha tva abhāvāt idam punar mukhyam udāharaṇam āgame pretya para loke dharmaḥ asukha pradaḥ āgama siddhe dharmiṇi dharme sāmānye asukha pradatvasya viśeṣasya sukha pradatvena viruddhena āgama siddhena bādhanāt 
PVV_4.98,0–4.98,2	 kintu śāstriṇā upyatadālambe viruddha uktau tu vastuni na bādhā pratibandhaḥ syāt tulya kakṣatayā tayoḥ śāstriṇaḥ abhyupagata śāstrasya atad ālambe śāstra asiddhe pramāṇa siddhe vastuni dharmiṇi śāstra pratijñā viruddhasya dharmasya uktau na sā bādhā yathā mī mām sa kaḥ sya gṛhīta śāstrasya pratyakṣa siddhe śabde dharmiṇi kṛtaka tvāt anitya tva uktau= api śāstra pratijñātena nitya tvena na bādhā yadi bādhā kintarhi bhavati iti āha pratibandhaḥ kasmāt iti āha tulya kakṣa tvāt sama bala tvāt yathā mātā me bandhyā ca iti sva vāci tulya kakṣa tvāt padayoḥ parasparam pratibandhaḥ 
PVV_4.99,0–4.99,2	 nanu sva vacanayoḥ tulya kakṣa tvāt yuktaḥ pratibandhaḥ āgama sva vacanayoḥ tulya bala tā eva katham iti āha yathā sva vāci tat ca asya tadā sva vacana ātmakam tayoḥ pramāṇam yasya asti tat syāt anyasya bādhakam tat ca śāstram nitya tva pratijñātasya vādinaḥ tadā prasiddhe dharmiṇi śāstra viruddha pratijñā samaye sva upagama svīkṛta pramāṇa tvāt sva vacana ātmakam jātam vacanam śāstrañca svayam abhyupagata prāmāṇya yuktam tulya kakṣam yathā sva vāci mātā me bandhyā iti vacana mātrayoḥ pratibandha unyonyam tayoḥ śāstra vacanayoḥ vvirūddha artha abhidhāyinoḥ madhye yasya manuvarttakam asti tat pramāṇa vat anyasya apramāṇakasya bādhakam bhavati yathā anitya tvam nityasya śabde 
PVV_4.100,0–4.100,1	 pratijñām anumānam vā pratijñā apeta yuktikā tulya kakṣāḥ yathārtham vā bādheta katham anyathā anyathā yadi pramāṇa siddhe dharmiṇi pramāṇān anugṛhītayoḥ parasparam bādhā pramāṇa abhāve kena itarasya na ābādheti iṣyate tadā pratijñā viparītā śāstra vacana ākhyā a peta pratijñā pramāṇya abhyupagamāt tulya kakṣā satī katham bādheta yathā śabde nitya tva pratijñā śāstra uktāḥ anitya tva pratijñām vidyamānam anumānam vā yathārtham vastu bhūta kṛtaka tva liṅga samuttham nitya tva pratijñayā katham bādhitam syāt anitya tvāt 
PVV_4.101–4.102,0–4.101–4.102,2	 prāmāṇyam āgamānāñca prāk eva vinivāritam abhyupāya vicāreṣu tasmāt doṣoyam iṣyate tasmāt viṣaya bhedasya darśana artham pṛthakkṛtaḥ anumāna ābarhiḥ bhūta upi abhyupāyaḥ prabādhanāt tasmāt kārya liṅga tvāt anumānāt abahis bhūta upi abhyupāyaḥ viṣayasya bhedaḥ nānātvam tad darśana artham anumānāt pṛthakkṛtaḥ anumānam sarvu atra bādhakam śāstrantu śāstra āśraye dharmiṇī iti bādhaka tva viṣaya bheda upadarśanam pṛthak karaṇa phalam katham jñāyate anumānā śāstram iti āha sva siddhe dharmiṇi sva upagama viruddhasya dharmasya prabādhanāt na hi apramāṇamba adhakam pramāṇañcā pratyakṣa tvāt anumānam eva 
PVV_4.103,0–4.103,2	 anyathā atiprasaṅgaḥ syāt vyartha tā vā pṛthakkṛteḥ anyathā yadi viṣaya bheda upadarśana phalam pṛthak karaṇam na iṣyate tadā prabheda darśana artham vaktavyam tathā ca kārya svabhāva anupalambhānām prabhedaḥ yāvat sambhavam vācyaḥ iti atiprasaṅgaḥ syāt atha sat api bheda antaram na ucyate tadā anumānāt śāstrasya pṛthak kṛteḥ vyarthatā vā syāt prabheda vacanasya avivakṣita tvāt sāmānya vacanasya anumānena eva siddha tvāt yadi viṣaya bheda upadarśana artham anumānāt pṛthak vacanam śāstrasya tadā abhyupagamāt sva vacanam ācāryeṇa kim artham pṛthak kṛtam nyāya mukhe yathā sarvu amuktam mṛṣā iti tathā aulūkyasya nityaḥ śabdaḥ iti 
PVV_4.103,3–4.103,6	 atra āha bhedaḥ vāc mātra vacane pratibandhaḥ sva vāci api sva vāci api bhedaḥ sva vacanasya api śāstrāt pṛthak karaṇam apramāṇakam vacanam vāc mātram tasmin pratibandhaḥ uccāraṇa sāmarthyāt abhyupagata prāmāṇyam sva vacanam anyathā uccāraṇam eva na syāt satya artha tā ca prāmāṇyam tat mṛṣā artha tayā vācyayā niṣedhyate iti tulya kakṣa tayā pratibandhaḥ eva anayoḥ na bādhā tat enam vākyam sva artham pratibadhnāti vākya antara nirdiṣṭam vastu śāstram iti anayoḥ bhedaḥ iti uktam 
PVV_4.104,0–4.104,2	 syāt etat tena abhyupāgamāt śāstram pramāṇam sarva vastuṣu bādhakam yadi na icchet sa bādhakam kimpunar bhavet śāstrasya tena vādinā abhyupagamāt sarvu atra vastuṣu dharmiṣu śāstra siddhe vastu bala pravṛtte pramāṇa niściteṣu ca śāstram pramāṇam sat bādhakam eva syāt viparīta pratijñāyāḥ na pratibandhakam tat katham pramāṇīkṛta śāstrasya mīmān sakasya śabde pratyakṣa siddhe kṛtaka tvāt anitya tva pratijñāyāḥ sādhyamānāyāḥ śāstreṇa pratibandhaḥ na bādhā iti uktam atha sa vādī yadi śāstram pramāṇam na icchet tadā kim punar ddharmasya asukha pradatvasya bādhāyām pramāṇam bhavet na hi apramāṇam kvacid pramāṇīkṛta śāstrasya śabde pratyakṣa siddhe bhavitum arhati 
PVV_4.105,0–4.105,2	 dharmasya sukha pradatvena nirdeśāt asukha pradatve sādhye sva vacana virodhaḥ eva iti ced evam tarhi svavāc virodhe abhedaḥ syāt sva vāc śāstra virodhayoḥ puruṣa icchā akṛtā ca asya paripūrṇṇā pramāṇa tā svavāc virodhe abhyupagamyamāne sva vāc śāstra virodhayoḥ abhedaḥ eva syāt dvayoḥ abhyupagama siddha pramāṇa tvāt puruṣa icchā kṛtā ca asya śāstrasya paripūrṇṇā tyupahasati sati api āgamasu a vacanayoḥ abhyupagamāhita prāmāṇyāt abhede bheda darśana nimittañca uktam 
PVV_4.106,0–4.106,2	 yasmāt śāstram tat siddhaḥ eva dharmiṇi liṅge ca bādhakam na tu pramāṇa siddhepi tasmāt prasiddhaṣu artheṣu śāstra tyāgepi na kṣatiḥ parokṣeṣu āgamā aniṣṭau na cintā eva pravarttate tasmāt pratyakṣa anumānābhyām prasiddheṣu dharmi liṅga sādhya sambandha ādiṣu satsu śāstra tyāgepi na kṣatiḥ yathā śabda kṛta tva anitya tva sambandha ādiṣu pramāṇa siddheṣu śāstrasya ākāśa guṇa tva pratipādakasya tyāgepi na aniṣṭam parokṣeṣu dharma adharma ādiṣu punar āgamasya pramāṇa tvena aniṣṭau cintā eva na pravarttate na hi asiddhe dharmiṇi vicāraḥ 
PVV_4.107,0–4.107,2	 nanu śāstrañced na pramāṇam kathantad siddhe dharmiṇi liṅga ādau vā vicāraḥ iti āha virodha udbhāvana prāyā parīkṣā api atra tat yathā adharma mūlam rāga ādi snānañca adharma nāśanam atra śāstre parīkṣā api yā kriyate sā pūrvva aparābhyām virodha udbhāvana prāyā na vāstavī tat yathā adharmasya mūlam rāga ādi iti kvacid uktam snānañca adharma miti atra ucyamānam viruṇaddhi rāga ādayaḥ hi pāpanidānam na ca nidāna avirodhe nidāninaḥ bādhā tat katham rāga ādi avirodhi snānam pāpa virodhi syāt apramāṇe śāstre virodha udbhāvana prāya api cintā kasmāt pravarttyate iti ced dāna ādi cetanānām pravṛtteḥ mahā anusaṃśā śravaṇāt hiṃsā ādi cetanānām mahā pāpa śravaṇāt ca apekṣita phaleṣu dāna ādiṣu ayam puruṣaḥ pravṛtti kāmaḥ na āgama prāmāṇyam anāśritya asitum samarthaḥ 
PVV_4.108,0–4.108,2	 tatas śāstram yat siddhayā yuktyā sva vācā ca na bādhyate dṛṣṭe adṛṣṭepi tat grāhyam iti cintā pravarttyate yat śāstram dṛṣṭe pramāṇeviṣaye yuktyā pratyakṣa ādi ākhyayā na bādhyate adṛṣṭe pramāṇa viṣaye ca sva vācā agama āśrayeṇa anumānena na bādhyate tad pramāṇa tvena adṛṣṭe viṣaye pravṛtti kāmasya grāhyam na tu yat kiñcid iti anena prayojanena śāstre virodha udbhāvana prāyā cintā pravarttyate 
PVV_4.109,0–4.109,3	 śāstra sva vacana virodhau vyākhyātau pratīti bādhām vyākhyātum āha artheṣu apratiṣiddha tvāt puruṣa icchā anurodhinaḥ iṣṭa śabda abhidheyasya āptaḥ vā akṣata vāc janaḥ iṣṭa śabda abhidheya tvasya abhimata vācya tvasya puruṣa icchā anurodhinaḥ puruṣa icchā adhīnasya artheṣu apratiṣiddha tvāt na hi puruṣa icchāyām api śaśī candra śabdam vācaka tayā na svīkaroti tatas ca atra iṣṭa śabda abhidheya tve viṣaye āptaḥ vyavaharttā janaḥ akṣata vāga pratiṣiddha iṣṭa vacanaḥ anena śabdena ayam arthaḥ mayā abhidhātavyaḥ iti kalpanā viṣaya tvam iṣṭa śabda abhidheya tvam tatra ca puruṣasya āropeṇa sva icchā adhīnā vacana pravṛttiḥ tasmāt iṣṭa śabda abhidheya tva bādhaḥ pakṣī kriyam āḥ tena eva sva samvedana siddhena bādhyate 
PVV_4.110,0–4.110,1	 uktaḥ prasiddha śabdena dharmaḥ tad vyavahāra jaḥ pratyakṣa ādi mitāḥ māna śruti āropeṇa sūcitāḥ candraḥ candraḥ iti ādi śabda vyavahārāt jātaḥ dharmaḥ kalpanā viṣayaḥ yogyatā ākhya ācāryeṇa prasiddha śabdena tat yathā śābda prasiddhena ityādinā uktaḥ śābdī prasiddhiḥ vyavahāraḥ śābda prasiddhiḥ tad bhavaḥ viṣayaḥ śābda prasiddhaḥ tena bādhā iti arthaḥ na kevalam iha eva pratyakṣa ādi bādhāsu api māna śratau meyasya āropeṇa pratyakṣa ādibhyām anumāna āgamābhyām mita arthāḥ eva virodhinaḥ vācaka tve pakṣasya sūcitāḥ

PVV_4.112,0–4.112,2	 yatas ca iṣṭa śabda abhidheya tva yogya tā sarvu atra sambhavati atas viśeṣa anapekṣaṇāt artha mātra anurodhinyāḥ bhāvinyā bhūtayā api vā bādhyate pratirundhānaḥ śabda yogya tayā tayā artha mātra anurodhinyā tayā śabda yogya tayā bhāvi saṃketa apekṣayā bhāvinyā atīta saṃketa apekṣayā bhūtayā api vā vyavasthitayā tām eva yogyatām pratirundhānaḥ yathā acandraḥ śaśī satvāt iti bādhyate

PVV_4.114,0–4.114,1	 asādhāraṇa tā na syāt bādhā hetoḥ iha anyathā tad niṣedhaḥ anumānāt syāt śabda arthe anakṣa vṛttitaḥ anyathā yadi śabdaḥ asaṃmukhībhavan= api yogyatāyām na sambaddhaḥ tadā iha śabda yogya tā pratiṣedhe karttavye bādhā hetoḥ a candraḥ śaśī satva ādeḥ iti ādeḥ asādhāraṇa tā uktāḥ na sarvu asya candra śabda yogya tve sa pakṣa abhāva ātma tva sādhāraṇam syāt na anyathā śabda arthe yogya tā lakṣaṇe kalpite anakṣa vṛttitaḥ akṣa vṛtti abhāvāt pratyakṣa bādhaka mititasyāḥ yogyatāyāḥ niṣedha unumānāt syāt

PVV_4.118,0–4.119,1	 athavā bruvataḥ lokasya anumā abhāvaḥ ucyate kintena bhinna viṣayā pratītiḥ anumānataḥ athavā acandraḥśaśī satvāt iti vipratipadyamānam pratipad pratipādana artham lokasya śābda prasiddhena asādhāraṇa tvāt anumāna abhāvaḥ ācāryeṇa ucyate pāramārthikasya bādhya tvasya abhāvāt kalpitam niṣedhyam tat ca puruṣa icchā mātra adhīna tvāt sarvu atra sambhavati iti saru u asya candra śabda yogya tā yogāt na kaścid acandraḥ pakṣosti yatra varttamān aṃsattvam asādhāraṇa tām jahyāḥ  evandarśite kimbhavati iti ced tena anumāna abhāva abhidhāyinā śabda prasiddha abhidhānena śabda siddhā pratītiḥ vvastu bala pravṛtta anumānataḥ bhinna viṣaya uktā bhavati vastu viṣayam hi anumānam kalpita gocara antarā śābdī pratītiḥ iti arthaḥ tena anumānāt vastūnām sat asat ta anurodhinaḥ bhinnasya ātad vaśā vṛttiḥ tat icchā jā iti sūcitam tena viṣaya bhedena vastūnām sat asat ta anurodhinaḥ anumānāt bhinnasya kalpitasya arthasya śabda yogya tvasya vṛttiḥ atad vaśā vastu anāyattā tasya puruṣasya icchā jā iti sūcitam bhavati 
PVV_4.120,0–4.120,2	 kiñca candra tām śaśinaḥ anicchān kām prati iti sa vāñchati iti tam pratyadṛṣṭāntam tat asādhāraṇam matam śaśinaḥ sarvu ajana siddhām vyāvahārikī candra tā candra śabda vācya tām anicchan paraḥkām anyām pratītim sa vāñchati yayā vācya tā siddhiḥ kvacid syāt matā ca pāramārthikī vācya tā pratītiḥ na kvacid asti vastutas saru u asyauvācya tā pradarśanāt kalpiva ācyatā pratītiḥ tu puruṣa icchā mātra prabhava tvāt sarvu atra avyāhatā eva atas saru u asya candra śabda vācya tā yogāt sa pakṣaḥ na asti iti tam candra tā palāpinam vādinam prati satvam liṅgam uktam ācāryeṇa na tu candrasya ekasya anyatra asambhavāt sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ abhāvāt asādhāraṇa tvam abhipretamā cā ryaḥ sya acandra tve sādhye ghaṭa ādeḥ sa pakṣasya satvāt candraḥ tu vipakṣaḥ mā bhūt tathā api hetu nivṛttiḥ asmāt avyāhata eva asatā upi hetu nivṛtteḥ sādhanāt 
PVV_4.121,0–4.121,2	 api ca na udāharaṇam eva idam adhikṛtya idam ucyate lakṣaṇa tvāt tathā vṛkṣaḥ adhātri iti uktau ca bādhanāt acandraḥ śaśī sattvāt iti etat eva udāharaṇam adhikṛtya idam śabda vācya tva pratikṣepa heta urasādhāraṇa tvam na ucyate lakṣaṇa tvāt lakṣaṇena hi lakṣyam vyāptam darśanīyam na ca dvitīya candra abhāvena usādharaṇa toktiḥ udāharaṇa antaram vyāpnoti yathā vā candra tāyāḥ pratītyai bādhā iṣyate tathā adhātrī vṛkṣaḥ sattvāt ghaṭa ādi vat iti udāharaṇa uktau sarvu aloka siddhayā puruṣa icchā adhīnayā ghaṭa ādau= api vṛkṣa śabda yogya tā pratītyā sa pakṣa abhāvena asādhāraṇa tvāt vṛkṣa śabda vācya tva abhāvasya sādhanāt yathā uktam eva asādhāraṇa tvam ācāryasya iṣṭam 
PVV_4.122,0–4.122,2	 yat api ucyate dvitīyasya candrasya abhāvāt asādhāraṇa tā iti tatra āha atra api loke dṛṣṭa tvāt karpūra rajata ādiṣu samayāt vartamānasya kā asādhāraṇa tā api vā loke karppūra rajata ādiṣu gāndhika vācika ādīnām samayāt varttamānasya dṛṣṭa tvāt atra acandraḥ śaśī sattva āt iti udāharaṇe hetoḥ asādhāraṇa tā api kā vā yadi dvitīya candraḥ na bhavet evam asādhāraṇa tā syāt vastu tvasya 
PVV_4.123,0–4.123,5	 syāt etat tad samayāt api varttamānasya candra tva ādeḥ na śabdavācya tā tatas yathā na vahni śabda vācya tā karppūrasya tathā candra śabda vācya tā ca na syāt iti asādhāraṇa tā eva iti āha yadi tasya kvacid sidhyet siddham vastu balena tat tasya evaṃvādinaḥ sati api sāmayike candre kvacid artha viśeṣe candra śabda vācya tvam yadi sidhyet na tu sarvu atra karpūra rajata ādau tadā tat candra śabda vācya tva vastu balena siddham syāt na tu evam dṛśyate saru u asya karpūra ādeḥ ca śabda abhidheya tva darśanāt atha yatra eva kalpyate candra tvam tat eva tad śabda vācyam pratīyate iti tathā abhyupagamyate tadā pratīti siddha pagame aśaśini api anivāraṇam sāmayike candra tve kvāpi pratītyā siddhasya candra śabda vācya tvasya upagame śaśini api tad śabda vācyasya anivāraṇam 
PVV_4.124,0–4.125,1	 tasya vastuni siddhasya śaśini api anivāraṇam tat vasttu a bhāve śaśini vāraṇepi na duṣyati śukla tā ādike nimitta bhūte vastuni tasya candra śabda abhidheya tvasya siddhasyaśaśini api nimitta sadbhāvāt anivāraṇam tasya nimitta bhūtasya vastunaḥ śaśini abhāve tu candra śabda vācya tvasya vastu tvāt hetoḥ vvāraṇepi na kiñcid duṣyati nimitta abhāve naimittika abhāva asya iṣṭa tvāt sāmayikantu sarvu atra aśakya vāraṇam iti tad śabda yogya tasmāt avastu niyata saṃketa bala bhāvinām yogyāḥ padārthāḥ dharmāṇām icchāyāḥ anirodhānāt tasmāt avastu niyataḥ vastuni aniyate icchā adhīna tvāt saṃketaḥ tasya balāt bhāvinām vācya tva ādīnām padārthāḥ sarvve dharmi tvena yogyāḥ icchātaḥ puṃsaḥ kenacid pikāyāḥ icchāyāḥ anirodhāt 
PVV_4.126,0–4.126,1	 tām yogyatām virundhānam saṃketa apratiṣedha jāḥ pratihanti prati iti ākhyā yogya tā viṣaye anumā tām iṣṭa śabda abhidheya tva yogya tām padārthānām sattva ādikāt hetoḥ vvirundhānam prati vādinam prati iti ākhyā pratīti saṃjñitā anumā pratihanti saṃketa apratiṣe svabhāva liṅga ja tvam āha icchā adhīna tvāt yogya tā viṣaye viparīta dharma upasthānam āha prayogaḥ punar yaḥ puruṣa icchā anubhidhāyī sa sarvu atra sambhavī tat yathā vikalpaḥ puruṣa icchā anuvidhāyi ca artheṣu iṣṭa śabda abhidheya tvam iti

PVV_4.128,0–4.128,2	 yadi evantadā kvacid arthe niṣedham kurvvatā śabdaḥ bādhyaḥ syāt tatas ca guṇa ādikam nimitta bhūtam guṇa ādi śabdānām guṇa guṇi sambandha ādi pāramārthikam artham guṇi śabda ādīnām niṣedhan bādhyaḥ syāt iti āha yena kalpitam artham śabdānām bādhamānaḥ pratikṣipyate na tu guṇa ādikam tena naimittikyāḥ śruteḥ artham artham vā pāramārthikam śabdānām pratirundhānaḥ abādhana arhaḥ hi varṇṇitaḥ naimittikyāḥ vastu bhūta guṇa ādi nimittavatyāḥ śruteḥ artham guṇa ādikam pāramārthi guṇi guṇa ādi sambandham śabdānām guṇyādi vācinām pratirundhānaḥ abādhana arhaḥ bādhām na arhati iti uktaḥ bhavati 
PVV_4.129,0–4.129,2	 yasmāt ca sāṃketika artha nirākaraṇe pratīti bādhāḥ tasmāt viṣaya bhedasya darśanāya pṛthakkṛtā anumāna abahis bhūtā pratītiḥ api pūrvva vat tasmāt svabhāva liṅga ja tvena anumānāt abahis bhūtā pratītiḥ api tasmāt pṛthak kimartham iti āha viṣayasya bhedaḥ kalpita akalpita tvam tasya darśanāya kalpita artha viṣayā pratītiḥ vastu viṣayantu anumānam iti arthaḥ pūrvva vat iti yathā āgama sva vacane abhyupagata prāmāṇye apratyakṣa tvāt anumāna antargatepi viṣaya bheda darśanāya pṛthak darśite vastu bala pravṛttenu mānam sarvu aviṣaya vicāre tu āgama sva vacane adhikṛte tathā prati iti anumāne api bhinna viṣaye iti arthaḥ 
PVV_4.130,0–4.130,2	 anumāna bādhāyām antarbhāvāt anayoḥ abhyupagama pratīti bādhayoḥ siddhayoḥ pṛthak ākhyāne darśayan= ca prayojanam ete sa hetuke prāha na anumā adhyakṣa bādhane siddhayoḥ api pṛthak ākhyāne viṣaya bheda lakṣaṇam prayojanandarśayannā cā ryaḥ ete abhyupagama pratīti bādhe sa hetuke prāha na santi pramāṇāni prameya arthāni iti pratijñā mātreṇa iti atra pratijñā mātram śāstra sva vacanayoḥ siddhayoḥ aprāmāṇya pratijña ābādhakam uktam atopya sādhāraṇa tvāt anumāna abhāve śābda prasiddhena apodyate na sa pakṣaḥ iti atra śābda prasiddhena śaśinaḥ candra tvena acandra tva pratijñāyāḥ bādhanam uktam anumādhyakṣa bādhane tu na sa hetuke prāha aśrāvaṇaḥ śabdaḥ nityaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti tasmāt viṣaya bheda upalakṣaṇa artha sa hetu tva ahetu tva darśanam pratyakṣa anumāna bādhe sarvu ā viṣaye abhyupagama pratīti bādhe tu niyata viṣaye iti arthaḥ 
PVV_4.131–4.132,0–4.131–4.132,5	 uktā pratīti bādhāḥ pratyakṣa bādhā vaktavyā na kevalam śābda prasiddhe vyavahāra dharma prasiddhau tad pratiroddhā bādhyate kintu atra api adhyakṣa bādhāyām nānā rūpa tayā dhvanau prasiddhasya śrutau atra api adhyakṣa bādhāyām vyāvahārika kalpanā vaśāt nānā rūpa tayā loke prasiddhasya khyātasya dhvanau śrutau śravaṇa jñāne rūpam yat eva pratibhāsate advayam śabala ābhāsasya adṛṣṭeḥ buddhi janmanaḥ tad artha artha uktiḥ asya eva kṣepe adhyakṣeṇa bādhanam 
PVV_4.131–4.132,6	 yat eva rūpam advayam dharma ādi dvaya śūnyam pratibhāsate śabala ābhāsasya nānā ākārasya buddhi janmanaḥ adṛṣṭeḥ yadi nānā kara tā śabdasya vāstavī syāt tathā eva śruti jñāne pratibhāseta tad arthā tad pratipādana phalā acāryasya pratyakṣa anumāna artha prasiddhena nirākṛta eti atra artha uktiḥ artha grahaṇam asya adhyakṣa siddhasya eva rūpasya kṣepe adhyakṣeṇa bādhanam iṣṭam 
PVV_4.133,0–4.133,1	 tat eva rūpam tatra arthaḥ śeṣam vyāvṛtti lakṣaṇam avastu bhūtam sāmānyam atas tat na akṣa gocaraḥ tatra śruti jñāne bhāsamānam tad rūpam arthaḥ sva lakṣaṇam tat atiriktam śeṣam dharmi dharma ādi vyāvṛtti lakṣaṇam anya vyavaccheda svabhāvam avastu bhūtam sarvu atra sambhavāt sāmānyañca atas avastu tva ādeḥ tad guṇa jāti ādi na akṣa gocaraḥ

PVV_4.135,0–4.135,2	 evam tarhi śabda sva lakṣaṇam na asti iti eva kasmāt na ucyate kim śrāvaṇa tva mukhyam niṣedhya yuktiḥ iti āha sarvu athā avācya rūpa tvāt siddhyā tasya samāśrayāt bādhanāt tad balena uktaḥ śrāvaṇena akṣa gocaraḥ sva lakṣaṇasya sarvathā kenacid śabdena avācya tvāt mukhyam abhidhānam na asti eva atha sāmānya vṛttiḥ api sva lakṣaṇa śabdaḥ adhyavasāya anurodhāt sva lakṣaṇam upalakṣayati evam śrāvaṇa śabda upīndriya grāhya tā upalakṣaṇam śabdasva lakṣaṇam upalakṣayiṣyati iti na kaścid viśeṣaḥ athavā asti eva śrāvaṇa śabdena abhidhāne prayojanam iti āha śrotra indriya viṣasya yā siddhiḥ tathā bhāvaḥ tayā siddhyā tasya indriya jñānasya samāśrayāt śabdasya svarūpa vyavasthityā hetunā tena vyapadeśaḥ indriya jñāna balena śabda svarūpa pāvasthitaḥ tathā abhidhānam iti arthaḥ kiñca tasya indriya jñānasya balena śabda sva lakṣaṇa viparyaya bhāvasya bādhānāt kāraṇāt śrāvaṇena akṣa gocaraḥ sva lakṣaṇa muktaḥ nityaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti anumāne nitya tva viṣayeṇa kṛtaka tva liṅga bhuvā bādhitaḥ pakṣaḥ sa ca asakṛt darśitaḥ eva iti na iha vipañcitaḥ 
PVV_4.136,0–4.136,2	 idānīm pratyakṣa anumāna āpta prasiddhena svadharmiṇī iti svadharmi grahaṇasya sāphalyam ākhyātum āha sarvu atra vādinaḥ dharmaḥ yaḥ sva sādhyatayā upsitaḥ tat dharmavati bādhā syāt na anya dharmeṇa dharmiṇi sarvu atra vāda kāle sādhya kāle vā vādinaḥ sva sādhya tayā yaḥ dharmaḥ īpsitaḥ dharmiṇi bādhā syāt yathā śrāvaṇa tvavati śabde bādhite bādhā pakṣasya na tu vādīṣṭāt dharmāt anyena dharmeṇa dharmavati dharmiṇi bādhite bādhā pakṣasya syāt iti dharmi graha prayojanam yathā ākāśa guṇa tvavati śabde bādhitenam pakṣa bādhāḥ

PVV_4.144–4.145,0–4.144–4.145,3	 tathā eva dharmiṇā upyatra sādhya tvāt kevalasya na yadi evam atra bādhā syāt tatra yathā dharmi viśiṣṭasya sādhya tvam dharmasya tathā eva sādhya tva viśiṣṭa tvena dharmi dharmasya na kvacid sādhya tā tatas na kevalasya dharmiṇaḥ bādhane pakṣa bādhāḥ yadi sādhya dharma uparodhini dharmiṇi bādhite pakṣa bādha iṣyate evam satyatra hetau sām khyam prati bauddhena ukte dharmi bādhā dvāreṇa dharma bādhā syāt na anya anutpādya śaktikaḥ sakṛt śabda ādi ahetu tvāt sukha ādiḥ iti pūrvva vat virodhitā bhavet atra hetuḥ aikāntikaḥ yadi 
PVV_4.144–4.145,4	 tat yathā sukha ādiḥ sukha duḥkha moha ātmakam pradhānam na anyena sahākāriṇā a nutpādya nādheya sāmarthyaḥ sakṛt śabda ādīnām kāryāṇām ahehetu tvāt iti atra pūrvva vat paraiḥ anutpādya ityādi prayoga tvāt ca sukha ādi ātmakasya nitya tvasya bādhanāt sukha ādau dharmmiṇi bādhite tat dharmmasya nitya tvasya virodhane viparyaya sādhane bādhā syāt anitya svabhāvaḥ hi sukha ādiḥ sādhayitum iṣṭaḥ sukha ādi svabhāva bhūta nitya tva bādhane ca sukha ādiḥ eva bādhitaḥ iti dharma uparodhini dharmiṇi bādhite pakṣa bādhā syāt atra āha bhavet atra hetau pakṣa bādhāḥ yadi na sakṛt śabda ādi anutpādāt iti hetuḥ sādhyasya vastu bhūta sukha ādi anitya tvasya viparyaye sukha ādi dharmya bhāvāt anitya tva abhāvena aikāntikaḥ avyabhicārī bhavet 
PVV_4.146,0–4.146,2	 yāvatā yā ca krama kriyā anitya tayoḥ avirodhāt vipakṣattaḥ vyāvṛtteḥ saṃśayān na ayam śeṣavat bhedaḥ iṣyate krama kriyāḥ hetuḥ yā ca sādhya anitya tā tayoḥ avirodhāt avastu bhūta dharmi sukha ādi dharma anitya tve viparīte sādhye vastu bhūta sukha ādi dharma anitya tvam vipakṣaḥ tatas hetoḥ krama karaṇa vyāvṛtteḥ saṃśayān na ayam viruddhaḥ hetuḥ śeṣavat bhedaḥ anaikāntika viśeṣaḥ tu iṣyate sati ca viruddha tve dharmi bādhā dvāreṇa dharma bādhā syāt 
PVV_4.147,0–4.148,2	 svayam iṣṭaḥ yatas dharmaḥ sādhyaḥ tasmāt tad āśrayaḥ bādhyaḥ na kevalaḥ na anya saṃśrayaḥ vā iti sūcitam yatas kāraṇāt svayam vādinā iṣṭaḥ sādhya dharmasa āśrayaḥ yaḥ saḥ eva bādhyaḥ kevalaḥ na bādhyaḥ yathā vastu bhūta ākāśa bādhāyām api nitya eka rūpatva abhāvasya sādhya dharmasya na kṣatiḥ sādhya dharmāt anyasya ca dharmasya āśrayaḥ na bādhya svayaṃśabdena sūcitam yathā anitya tve sādhye śabde ākāśa guṇa tva āśraya tvena bādhāyām api na doṣaḥ tasmāt svayaṃśrutya ani adharmāṇām bādhā abādhā iti kathyate tathā svadharmiṇā anyasya dharmiṇā upī iti kathyate svayaṃśrutyā sādhyāt dharmāt anyeṣām dharmāṇām yathā bādhā yā sā abādhā iti kathyate sva dharmi vacanena sādhyāt anyasya dharmasya dharmiṇaḥ bādhā abādhā iti kathyate 
PVV_4.149,0–4.149,1	 tathā aparepi pakṣa ābhāsāḥ santi te kasmāt na ucyante tathā hi aprasiddha viśeṣyaḥ kaścid pakṣaḥ yathā vibhuḥ ātmā ātmanaḥ eva bauddha syāsiddha tvāt kaścid prasiddha viśeṣaṇaḥ yathā vināśī śabdaḥ sām khyam pramāṇam prati tasya vināśa asiddheḥ kaścid aprasiddha ubhayaḥ yathā samavāyi kāraṇam ātmā bauddhasya ubhayā siddheḥ iti nanu asiddha upya ātmā pakṣī bhaviṣyati tad lakṣaṇa yogāt na hi asiddhasya pakṣatā nirastāḥ āśraya asiddha tvāt hetoḥ na pakṣaḥ iti ced na 
PVV_4.149,2–4.149,4	 sādhana doṣoyam na pakṣa doṣaḥ tathā śabde anitya tvam viṣeśaṇam asiddham iti guṇaḥ eva ayam na pakṣa doṣaḥ asiddhasya eva sādhya tvāt atha viparyaya siddhyā asiddham ucyate tathā api mūḍhasya viparyaya siddhau= api na ayam pakṣa doṣaḥ virodhaḥ nāma hetu doṣaḥ eva ayam pramāṇena ca viparyaya siddhau pramāṇa bādhita tvam eva pakṣa doṣoḥ tu alama prasiddha viśeṣaṇa tva abhidhānena aprasiddha ubhayasya tu ubhaya doṣāt ca sarvve amī hetu doṣāḥ eva iti kim pakṣa doṣāḥ vaktavyāḥ atha sarva sādhana doṣeṇa pakṣaḥ eva uparudhyate tathā api pakṣa doṣa tvam pratijñā mātra bhāvinaḥ sarvveṇa sādhanasya doṣeṇa asiddha tva ādinā pakṣaḥ eva uparudhyate tena pakṣa doṣāḥ asiddha viśeṣya ādayaḥ abhidhīyante yadi api pakṣa uparodha phalāḥ sarvve doṣāḥ tathā api treṇa bhavana śīlasya doṣasya pakṣa voṣa tvam uktam iṣṭam 
PVV_4.150,0–4.150,2	 yasmāt sākṣāt uttara avayava apekṣaḥ yaḥ doṣaḥ sonubadhyate tena īyuktam atas apakṣa doṣaḥ asiddha āśraya ādikaḥ uttaraḥ avayavaḥ hetu dṛṣṭānta ādiḥ tad apekṣaḥ yaḥ doṣaḥ sa tena hetu ādinā anubadhyate ātmani sambadhyate iti uktam prāk uttara avayava apekṣaḥ na doṣaḥ pakṣaḥ iṣyate ityādinā atas asiddha āśraya ādikaḥ āśraya asiddha tva ādiḥ uttara avayava apekṣaḥ na pakṣa doṣaḥ 
PVV_4.151,0	 nanu aśrāvaṇaḥ śabdaḥ nityaḥ ghaṭaḥ na anumānam pramāṇam acandraḥ śaśī iti udāharaṇaiḥ ebhiḥ ddharma svarūpa nirākaraṇena bādhā darśitā yathāpratijñāta dharma mātrasya viparīta dharma upasthāpanena nirākaraṇāt dharmi viśeṣasya dharma viśeṣasya dharmi svarūpasya ca bādhanena pakṣa bādhā asti sā katham avagantavyā iti āha

PVV_4.152,0–4.152,1	 tatra udāhṛti diś mātram ucyate arthasya dṛṣṭaye dravya lakṣaṇa yuktonyaḥ saṃyogerthosti dṛṣṭi bhāj tatra āśrāvaṇaḥ śabdaḥ iti ādiṣu udāharaṇa diṅa mātram ucyate sādhyāṅaga bhūtasya saru u asya eva bādhā bhavati iti arthasya dṛṣṭaye darśana artha tatra parasya avayavebhyaḥ avayavinaḥ guru tva ādi guṇa yoginaḥ anya tve abhimate yadā ucyate na anyaḥ avayavi avayavebhyaḥ tulān ati viśeṣa agrahaṇāt iti etad dharma viśeṣa nirākaraṇena udāharaṇam boddhavyam tathā hi na atra anya tva mātram niṣeddhum iṣṭam tathā tve dharma svarūpa nirākaraṇa udāharaṇam etat syāt tasmāt anya tvasya sādhya dharmasya na antarīyakāḥ gaurava ādayaḥ viśeṣāḥ nirākarttum iṣṭāḥ tathā ca dharma viśeṣa udāharaṇam eva tat tathā hi paraiḥ ekasya avayavasya anyān i āvayava saṃyoge sati tad anyaḥ arthaḥ avayavi saṃjñitaḥ dravyasya lakṣaṇena kriyāvat guṇavat samavāyi kāraṇañce tyanena yuktaḥ dṛṣṭi bhāj dṛśyoḥ ti iti iṣṭam eva

PVV_4.154,0–4.155,1	 aviśiṣṭasya ca anyasya sādhane siddha sādhanam guru tva adhas gatī syātām yadi asya syāt tulā ānatiḥ yadi punar anindriya grāhya tvam dravya lakṣaṇena aviśiṣṭanta davayavi dravyam sādhyate tadā aviśiṣṭasya anyasya ca sādhane bauddhasya na kācid kṣatiḥ iti siddha sādhanam syāt tasmāt dṛśyaḥ dravya guṇavān bhāvaḥ avayavī iti sādhyam tatas ca asya avayavinaḥ guru tvam tadā mṛd ā ādi khaṇḍayoḥ saha tolitayoḥ yāvatī tulā gaurava vaśāt dṛṣṭā tatodhikā tulā ānatiḥ syāt yadā tayoḥ mṛd ā ādi khaṇḍayoḥ saṃyoge sati dravya antaram utpadya te tadā tayoḥ pūrvva avasthitayoḥ pūrvva avasthitam gauravam tadā utpannasya ca dravyasya adhika gaurava viśeṣāt tulā an ati viśaṣaḥ dṛśyeta na ca evam tasmāt na tatra kārya dravya sambhavaḥ iti avayavī nirguṇaḥ niṣkriyaḥ ca syāt tad nirguṇa kriyaḥ tasmāt samavāyi na kāraṇam tatas eva na dṛśyosa avadṛṣṭeḥ kārya rūpayoḥ tasmāt nirguṇa kriya tvāt guṇa karmaṇoḥ na samavāyi kāraṇam avayavī tatas eva dravya lakṣaṇa yogāt na tasya āvaraṇa ādi kāryam svarūpam vā kiñcid dṛśyate adarśanāt ca na dṛśyaḥ avayavī 
PVV_4.156–4.158,0–4.156–4.158,6	 tad bādhāni aviśeṣasya na antarīyaka bhāvinaḥ tat tasmāt asau= avayavinaḥ bādhā anyasya viśeṣasya gaurava adhas gati ādeḥ nā sādhya anya tva avinā bhāvinaḥ bādhā iti dharma viśeṣa nirākaraṇe nirdeśaḥ yuktaḥ āsūkṣmāt dravya mālāyāḥ tolya tvāt aṃśu pāta vat dravya antara guru tvasya gatiḥ na iti aparaḥ abravīt āsūkṣmāt dvi aṇukāt ārabhya dravya mālāyāḥ sthūla avayavi paryantāyāḥ tolya tvāt tat dadravya mālā varttinaḥ sthūlasya dravya antarasya na gatiḥ bhavati tulāyām aṃśu pāta vat karpāsa bhāra patitasya aṃśoḥ ekasya yathā guru tvam sat api na pratīyate tathā dravya mālā varttinaḥ sthūla dravyasya iti aparaḥ abravīt tasya krameṇa saṃyukte pāṃśu rāśau sakṛt yute bhedaḥ syāt gaurave tasmāt pṛthak saha ca tolite suvarṇa māṣaka ādīnām saṃkhyā sāmyam na yujyate
