PVV_4.164,4	 kṛtyānām pratyayānām kāla sāmānya vihita tvena tri kāla viṣaya tvāt sādhya śabdena kṛtyā antena na sādhya mātrasya grahaṇam sādhayiṣyamāṇasya api grahaṇāt tathā ca nityaḥ śabdaḥ mūrta tvāt buddhi vat ityādi prayoge tadā vāda kāle tad hetu dṛṣṭānta ādikam atathā ātmakam vastutas atad svabhāva ātmakam param prati tathā atad rūpa tvena nyastam upanyastam vādinā yatnatas sādhyam yadi api śabde mūrtta tvam na asti aniṣṭañca sādhya tvena tathā api hetu dṛṣṭāntayoḥ upanyāsāt avaśyam sādhyam sādhya nirdeśaḥ ca pratijñā iti pratijñā tvañca durvvāram 
PVV_4.165,0–4.166,2	 pratyāyana adhikāre tu sarva asiddha avarodhinī yasmāt sādhya śrutiḥ na iṣṭam viśeṣam avalambate pratyāyanasya jñāpakasya hetoḥ adhikāre tu sādhanasya saru u asya abhyupagama hetu dṛṣṭānta ādeḥ a siddha avarodhaḥ saṃgrahaḥ tadvatī yasmāt sādhyaśrutiḥ iṣṭam viśeṣam na sādhya tvena avalambate parigṛhṇāti yena pratyāyana adhikāre sādhanasya asiddhasya pakṣatva prasaṅgaḥ tena aprasiddha dṛṣṭānta hetu udāharaṇam kṛtam anyathā śaśaśṛṅga ādau sarva asiddhe api sādhya tā tena aprasiddhābhyām dṛṣṭānta hetubhyām pratijñā prasaṅgāt udāharaṇam kṛtam prāk tathā ca asiddha dṛṣṭānta hetuvādaḥ prasajyate iti anena anyathā yadi sādhanam asiddham vivakṣitam na syāt tadā śaśaśṛṅga ādau= api sarvasya asiddhasya pakṣatva prasaṅgaḥ 
PVV_4.167,0	 nanu sādhyam karma karmaṇi kṛtya vidhānāt karma ca īpsitatamam tat ca kriyā apya mātram payasā udanam bhuktam iti atra kriyā apyatvepya nīpsitatama tvāt payaḥ karaṇam tatas sādhanīya tvepi vādinaḥ anīpsitatama tvāt hetu dṛṣṭānta ādikam na pratijñā bhaviṣyati tathā caturvvidhaḥ siddhāntaḥ sarvvatantra siddhāntaḥ prati tantra siddhāntaḥ adhikaraṇa siddhāntaḥ abhyupagama siddhāntaḥ ca tatra abhyupagama siddhānta tvaṃśa astra dṛṣṭasya iti tad āśrayeṇa sādhyasya nirdeśaḥ pratijñā na hetu dṛṣṭānta ādeḥ pakṣatva prasaṅgaḥ iti āha 
PVV_4.167,1–4.167,2	 sarvasya ca aprasiddha tvāt kathañcid tena na kṣamāḥ karma ādi bheda upakṣepa parihārā vivecane sarvu asya pratijñā hetu dṛṣṭānta ādeḥ ca aprasiddha tvāt sādhayitum īpsitatama tvena abhyupagamāt karma tvam karma ca sādhyam pratijñā iti pratijñātva prasaṅgaḥ durvvāraḥ abhyupagamaḥ ca yathā nitya tve tathā mūrttattva ādau= api śāstra abhyupagamayoḥ ca bhedaḥ prāk uktaḥ tena karma tva aviśeṣeṇa sādhyam karma sādhanam karaṇam iti karma ādi bhedasya upakṣe sādhya viśeṣa avagamāpane kathañcid na kṣamāḥ 
PVV_4.168,0–4.168,3	 yadi api ucyate yaḥ sādhyaḥ avayavaḥ tasya nirdeśaḥ pratijñā tatas hetu ādeḥ siddhasya avayavasya na pratijñātvam iti tat api asat kiñca prāc asiddha svabhāva tvāt sādhyaḥ vayavaḥ iti asat tulyā siddhānta tā te hi yena upagama lakṣaṇāḥ lakṣaṇa vacanāt prāk sādhya asādhyayoḥ asiddha svabhāva tvāt lakṣaṇena hi sādhya tā pratipattavyā tri kāla viṣaya tvāt kṛtya pratyayasya sādhayiṣyamāṇepi sādhyaḥ iti sādhanam ca sādhyam syāt siddhānta tā hetu dṛṣṭānta ādeḥ api tulyā pratitantra ādi siddhāntāḥ yena kāraṇena upagama lakṣaṇāḥ abhyupagama svabhāvāḥ yathā hi nitya tvam abhyupagamyatetathā mūrtta tva ādikam api iti na viśeṣaḥ 
PVV_4.169,0	 kiñca sādhyaḥ dharmaḥ dharmī dvayam vā syāt yadi dharmaḥ tadā sādhya sādharmyāt tad dharma bhavī dṛṣṭānte udāharaṇam iti dṛṣṭānta lakṣaṇam virudhyate na hi sādhya dharmasya anitya tvāt eḥ ddharmaḥ utpattimatu ādiḥ kintu śabdasya tatas sādhya dharmeṇa sādharmyāt dṛṣṭāntasya tad dharma bhāvi tvam sādhya dharma utpattimatu ā ādi bhāvava tvam na asti 
PVV_4.169,1–4.169,3	 atha dharmī sādhyaḥ tadā udāharaṇa sādharmyāt sādhya sādhanam hetuḥ iti hetu lakṣaṇam na yujyeta na hi śabdaḥ dharmma siddhaḥ yena tad sādhanāt sādhya sādhanaḥ hetuḥ syāt atha ubhayam sādhyam tadā ubhaya pakṣa bhāvi doṣa prasaṅgaḥ samudāyasya asiddha tvāt saḥ eva sādhyaḥ iti āha samudāyasya sādhya tva ipi anyonyasya viśeṣaṇam sādhyam dvayam tadā asiddham hetu dṛṣṭānta lakṣaṇam 
PVV_4.169,4	 samudāyasya sādhya tvepīṣyamāṇe anyonyasya parasparam viśeṣaṇam vaktavyam dharma viśiṣṭaḥ dharmi viśiṣṭaḥ vā asādhyaḥ yathā śabda viśiṣṭam anityam iti tathā ca dvayam sādhyam syāt tadā dvaya sādhya tva abhyupagame tu hetu dṛṣṭāntayoḥ lakṣaṇam asiddham syāt na hi dharmi dharma viśiṣṭena dharmeṇa anitya śabda sambandhinā utpattimatu ādinā ghaṭa ādeḥ sādharmyam asti yena dṛṣṭānta tā bhavet tathā dharma viśiṣṭe dharmiṇi prāk anumānāt hetuḥ api na kasyacid siddhaḥ iti hetu lakṣaṇam ca na syāt 
PVV_4.170,0–4.170,1	 asaṃbhavāt sādhya śabdaḥ dharmi vṛttiḥ yat i iṣyate śāstreṇa alam yathāyogam lokaḥ eva pravarttatām yathā utpattimatu a ādeḥ samudāya dharma tva asaṃbhavāt dharmi dharma tva saṃbhavāt ca sādhya śabdaḥ yadi dharmi vṛttiḥ upacāra āt iṣyate tadā śāstreṇa durvihitena alam loke eva yathākramam yathāyogam yasya yādṛśam lakṣaṇam yuktam tat avadhārya pratijñā hetu ādiṣu pravarttatām yat tu pakṣaḥ dharmī avayava samudāya upacārāt iti asmābhiḥ ucyate tat sarvam dharmi dharma pratiṣedha artham upacāra yogya parigraha artham tasmāt ayuktam parasya pratijñā lakṣaṇam 
PVV_4.171,0–4.171,2	 kiñca sarva vākyānām avadhāraṇa phala tvāt sādhya nirdeśaḥ eva pratijñā iti pūrva pada avadhāraṇam vā syāt sādhya nirdeśaḥ pratijñā eva iti uttara pada avadhāraṇam vā syāt tatra prathama pakṣe siddha nivṛtyā asiddha parigrahaḥ prayojanam tat ca anyathā api labhyate tathā hi sādhana ākhyāna sāmarthyāt tad arthe sādhya tā gatāḥ hetu ādi vacanaiḥ vyāpteḥ anāśaṅkyam ca sādhanam 
PVV_4.171,3–4.171,4	 siddhe api sādhana upanyāsaḥ anupayuktaḥ iti sādhana ākhyāna sāmarthyāt tasyāḥ pratijñāyāḥ arthe asiddhe sādhya tā pratītā pratijñā lakṣaṇam vinā api naca asiddhe hetu dṛṣṭānta ādike pratijñā artha prasaṃgaḥ tathā hi hetu ādi vacanaiḥ pṛthak lakṣaṇa pratipādakaiḥ vyāpteḥ viṣayi kṛta tvāt sādhanam hetu dṛṣṭāntam asiddham ca pratijñā arthe vā anāśaṅkyam 
PVV_4.172,0–4.172,1	 pūrva avadhāraṇe tena pratijñā lakṣaṇa abhidhā vyarthā vyāptiphalā soktiḥ sāmarthyāt gamyate tatas tena ati prasaṃga abhāvena pūrvasya padasya avadhāraṇe pratijñā lakṣaṇa abhidhā vyarthāḥ tatas pāriśeṣyāt sāmarthyāt sādhya nirdeśaḥ pratijñā eva ityayoga vyavaccheda phalam uttara pada avadhāraṇam syāt tathā ca asiddha hetu dṛṣṭānta ādau= api pratijñātvam durvāram asiddhasya sādhana aṅgasya katham api pratijñātvā ayaḥ gatā virahāt nirastam pratijñā lakṣaṇam 
PVV_4.173–4.175,0–4.173–4.175,1	 parasya pratijña ābhāsa lakṣaṇam saṃprati nirākaraṇīyam hetu pratijñayoḥ vyāghātaḥ pratijñā doṣaḥ mataḥ yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ sarvasya nitya tvāt yadi sarvam anityam tadā śabdasya api sarvatra antarbhāvāt kutas nityatā atha śabdaḥ nityaḥ katham sarvasya anitya tā iti pratijñā hetvoḥ virodhāt pratijñā viruddha tā doṣaḥ viruddha teṣṭa asambandhaḥ anupakāra saha āsthitī evam sarva aṅga doṣāṇām pratijñādoṣa tā bhavet 
PVV_4.173–4.175,2–4.173–4.175,3	 viruddha tā ceṣṭasyā sādhya dharmasya dharmiṇī asambandhaḥ nāma sa ca vicāryamāṇaḥ hetunā sādhya dharmasya anupakāraḥ aniścāyanam vā syāt dharmiṇi sādhyena saha āsthitiḥ vā syāt tatra yadi hetoḥ sādhye pratipādaka tva abhāvāt pratijñā doṣaḥ ucyate evam sati sarveṣām aṅgasya hetoḥ doṣāṇām pratijñādoṣa tā bhavet sarvaiḥ heṃtu doṣaiḥ pratijñāyāḥ eva vyāhananāt pakṣa doṣaḥ parāpakṣaḥ na iti ca pratipāditam iṣṭa asambhavya siddhaḥ ca saḥ evam syāt nirākṛtaḥ 
PVV_4.173–4.175,4–4.173–4.175,5	 pratijñā mātra bhāgī ca pakṣa doṣaḥ para apekṣaḥ sādhana ādi sāpekṣaḥ na doṣaḥ iti ca pratipāditam prāc uttara avayava apekṣaḥ na doṣaḥ pakṣaḥ iṣyate ityādinā atha saha asthiti svabhāvaḥ virodhaḥ tadā iṣṭe pakṣe asambhavī hetu doṣaḥ eva ayam na pakṣa doṣaḥ atha tena hetunā pratijñā artha nirākaraṇāt pratijñā virodhaḥ pakṣa doṣaḥ eva tat ca ayuktam tathā hi sādhya dharmaḥ dharmiṇī evam nirākṛtaḥ syāt anitya tva sahetu tve śabdaḥ evam prakīrttayet dṛṣṭānta ākhyān ataḥ anyat kim asti atra artha anudarśam 
PVV_4.173–4.175,6	 yadi śabde dharmiṇī anitya tvena dharmeṇa sa hetu tve pratipādye evam sarvasya anitya tva ādi prakīrttayet na ca īdṛśam vādinaḥ vivakṣitam sarvu asya parasya anitya tvāt śabdaḥ nityaḥ iti vivakṣita tvāt tathā ca sāmānya viśeṣa bhāvāt virodha bhāvaḥ bhavatu vā śabde anitya tva nirākaraṇam vivakṣitam tathā api pramāṇa bādhā eva apakṣatā iti na pratijñāvirodhaḥ nāma pakṣa doṣaḥ tasmāt hetu artha tā anupapatteḥ saru u asya anitya tvāt iti atra vaidharmyeṇa dṛṣṭānta ākhyān ataḥ anyat artha anudarśanam kim asti vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntaḥ eva su śikṣitaiḥ ittham ākhyātaḥ sarvu asya nitya tve vyāpti darśana artham yadi punar vvaidharmya dṛṣṭānta upadarśanam etat na bhavati tadā 
PVV_4.176–4.188,0–4.176–4.188,1^1	 viśeṣebhinnam ākhyāya sāmānyasya anuvarttane na tad vyāptiḥ phalam vā kim sāmānyena anuvarttane viśeṣeṇa śabde bhinnam nitya tvam ākhyāya saru u asya anitya tvāt iti vyāpi tvā at sāmānyasya anitya tvasya anuvarttane kriyamāṇe tasya anitya tvasya vyāptiḥ aśeṣa padārtha grahaḥ na bhavati yathā kauṇḍinyasya takra dānam vihitam brāhmaṇebhyaḥ sāmānyena vihita dadhi dānena na bādhyate prakalpya apavāda viṣayam utsargasya pravṛtteḥ tathā śabde nitya tvasya viśeṣa vihitasya sarvvā anitya tvena sāmānya vihitena bādhā āśaṅkā na asti iti katham pratijñā hetvoḥ vvirodhaḥ 
PVV_4.176–4.188,0–4.176–4.188,1^2	 yadi śabda vyatiriktasya saru u asya anitya tvam iṣṭam na syāt tadā saru u asya anitya tvāt iti sāmānyena anuvarttane kim phalam syāt nityaḥ śabdaḥ śabdasya anitya tvāt iti eva vācyam evam virodhasya vaktavya tvāt śabdaḥ eva udāharaṇam bhaviṣyati iti ced na anunmattaḥ evam brūyāt yadi ātmanaḥ anitya tvam hetuḥ siddhaḥ katham tat viruddham sādhyam tatra eva pratijānīyāt atha asiddhaḥ tadā hetu doṣaḥ eva asau na pratijñā doṣaḥ tasmāt na asti śabde nitya tvam atas sva virodhinam api nirākarttum aśaktam 
PVV_4.176–4.188,2–4.176–4.188,4	 syāt nirākaraṇam śabde sthitena eva iti atas bravīt atas eva ācārya śabdesthitena eva anitya tvena nirākaraṇam nitya tvasya syāt iti abravīt tadā ca syāt atra pratijñā arthasya nirākaraṇam yadi nityaḥ śabdaḥ saru u asya anitya tvāt iti vaidharmya dṛṣṭānta upadarśanam etat yathā nitya tva viśiṣṭa śabdaḥ iti tadā hetu nirdeśaḥ na syāt iti āha asarvaḥ ca śabdaḥ iti upanayāt hetuḥ vaktavyaḥ 
PVV_4.176–4.188,5–4.176–4.188,8	 viruddha viṣayeni asmin vadan= āha anyatām śruteḥ tathā hi nitya tvasya viruddham śabdāt anyasmin vadan sarvu asmāt anyatām śruteḥ ba śabdasya āha sa ca bheda upratikṣepāt sāmānyānāt na vidyate sa ca sarvu asmāt bhedaḥ asarvva lakṣaṇaḥ śabdasya na vidyate sāmānyānām vyāpinām bhedasya apratikṣepāt svīkārāt niḥ śeṣa artha saṃgṛhīta tvāt sarvvaśabdaḥ na kiñcid pariharati 
PVV_4.176–4.188,9–4.176–4.188,11	 nanu sāmānyānām viśeṣa pratikṣepaḥ dṛśyate eva yathā kim śiṃśapā eva vṛkṣaḥ na vā iti praśne kathyate na śiṃśapā eva vṛkṣaḥ tadā śiṃśapā vṛkṣa tva pratikṣepaḥ bhavati eva asat etat na hi tatra śiṃśapā vṛkṣa tvam niṣidhyate kintu śiṃśapā eva vṛkṣaḥ iti niyamaḥ pratikṣipyate tad itarasya api vṛkṣa tvāt vṛkṣaḥ na śiṃśapā eva iti yathā prakaraṇe kvacid 
PVV_4.176–4.188,12–4.176–4.188,13	 sarva śruteḥ eka vṛtti niṣedhaḥ syāt na ceyatā sosarvaḥ sarva bhedān ām a tattve tad asambhavāt yathā ca kvacid prakaraṇe śiṃśapā mātra vṛkṣa tva praśna hetau yathā vṛkṣaḥ na śiṃśapā eva iti śiṃśapā mātra vṛkṣa tva niṣedhaḥ iṣṭaḥ tathā niḥśeṣa vastu saṃgrāhikāyāḥ sarvu aśruteḥ ekatra śabda mātra vṛtti niṣedhaḥ syāt na ceyatā sa śabdaḥ asarvvaḥ sarvva antargamāt tasya pratyekam sarvu eṣām bhedānām viśeṣāṇām atatve asarvva tve tasya saru u asyā sambhavāt 
PVV_4.176–4.188,14–4.176–4.188,16	 atha pāribhāṣikam sarvva tvam śabda āditara tvam tathā asarvva tvam śabde siddham eva iti ced tat ayuktam evam hi sarvva tvam eva sarvvaśabdena uktam syāt tathā aprasiddha tā eva tathā hi jñāpya jñāpakayoḥ bhedāt dharmiṇaḥ hetu bhāvinaḥ asiddheḥ jñāpika tvasya dharmya siddhaḥ sva sādhane jñāpya jñāpakayoḥ bhedāt kāraṇā t sādhya abhinnam sādhanam vaktavyam tatas dharmiṇaḥ hetu tvena bhāvinaḥ hetuḥ bhaviṣyataḥ nitya tvena sādhya tvāt jñāpakasya asiddheḥ kāraṇāt dharmī sādhya tvāt svasya sādhane asiddhaḥ asiddham hi sādhyam siddhañca sādhanam anayoḥ katham aikātmyam 
PVV_4.176–4.188,17	 nanu śabda tvam siddham eva nityavat tayā tu tat asiddham sādhyate na ca tathā eva tad sādhanam śabda tva mātreṇa sādhana tvāt tad kathandharmī sva sādhane asiddhaḥ ucyate ayam abhiprāyaḥ na śabda tvam iti eva gamaka tvam kintu sa adhyapi āptam tasya ca asādhāraṇa tvena na anyatra vyāpti upalambhaḥ tatas ca anyatra anitya tva niyamāt śabde śabda tvam nitya tā vyāptam sat hetuḥ vvaktavyaḥ tathā ca yaḥ eva sādhyaḥ saḥ eva hetuḥ iti sādhya siddheḥ hetu asiddhiḥ ca iti yuktam uktam dharmya siddhaḥ prasādhanaḥ iti 
PVV_4.176–4.188,18–4.176–4.188,20	 dharma dharmi vivekasya sarva bhāveṣu asiddhitaḥ sarvatra doṣaḥ tulyaḥ ced na saṃvṛtyāḥ viśeṣataḥ nanu evam sati sarvu atra bhāveṣu dharmayāḥ sādhya sādhanayoḥ ddharmiṇaḥ ca vivekasya bhedasya asiddhitaḥ sarvu atra tulyaḥ doṣaḥ na hi śabdāt anyat nitya tvam kṛtaka tvam vā anitya tva asiddhau ca yathā nityaḥ sādhyaḥ tathā tad ātmavān kṛta kopi śabdaḥ asiddhaḥ aivati ced na eṣa doṣaḥ saṃvṛttyā bhinna vyāvṛtti viṣayayā sādhya sādhana dharmiṇaḥ viśeṣataḥ bhedāt yathā svam vikalpaiḥ saṃketa vāsana anugama niyamita ekaika vṛtti mātra viṣaya arthaiḥ śabda tva kṛtaka tva nitya tva ādi asaṃkīrṇṇāni eva dharmi sādhana sādhya tayā vyavasthāpyante iti na doṣaḥ 
PVV_4.176–4.188,21–4.176–4.188,23	 yadi dharma dharmi vivekaḥ asti eva tadā tattva anyatva pratiṣedhaḥ katham kṛtaḥ iti āha parama artha vicāreṣu tathābhūta aprasiddhitaḥ tattva anya tvam padārtheṣu sāṃbṛteṣu niṣidhyate sāṃvṛteṣu kalpanā viṣayeṣu dharmi dharma ādiṣu tattva anya tvam parama arthasya tattvasya vicāreṣu niṣidhyate tathābhūtasya yathākalpanam para sparataḥ bhinnasya dharmi dharma ādeḥ pramāṇena aprasiddhitaḥ na tu sāṃvṛtopi teṣām bheda abhāvaḥ na ceyatā kalpite dharmiṇi kalpitāt sādhanāt kalpitasya sādhyasya siddhiḥ iti anumānāt avastu pratīti abhāva prasaṅga aśabda vyāvṛttyā niścitasya vastunaḥ eva dharmi tvāt evam kṛtaka tva anitya tvābhyām niścitasya tasya eva sādhana tvāt sādhya tvāt ca iti ukteḥ anyonyasya teṣām bhedaḥ punar kalpitaḥ eva 
PVV_4.176–4.188,24–4.176–4.188,26	 anumāna anumeya artha vyavahāra sthitiḥ tu iyam bhedam pratyaya saṃsiddham avalambya ca kalpyate atonumāna hetu tvāt anumānasya liṅgasya anumeya arthasya anayoḥ upalakṣaṇa tvāt dharmiṇaḥ ca vyavahāra sthitiḥ tu iyam anityaḥ kṛtaka tvāt ityādau kriyamāṇā teṣām para sparataḥ bheda vikalpakena eka vyāvṛtti mātra viṣayeṇa saṃsiddham niścitam avalam vyāśritya ca kalpyate 
PVV_4.176–4.188,27–4.176–4.188,28	 yathā svam bheda niṣṭheṣu pratyayeṣu vivekinaḥ dharmī dharmāḥ ca bhāsante vyavahāraḥ tad āśrayaḥ tathā hi yathā svam yasya yaḥ ātmīyaḥ grāhyaḥ bhedaḥ vyāvṛttiḥ tad niṣṭheṣu vikalpeṣu vivekinaḥ dharmī dharmāḥ ca sādhya sādhana ādayaḥ bhāsante tad āśrayaḥ vikalpa gocara āśrayaḥ dharmi dharma ādi bhedasya vyavahāraḥ pravarttate 
PVV_4.176–4.188,29–4.176–4.188,33	 evantarhi nityaḥ śabdaḥ asarvva tvāt iti atra api vyāvṛtti bhedāt eva sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ bhaviṣyati iti āha vyavahāra upanītotra saḥ eva āśliṣṭa bheda dhīḥ sādhyaḥ sādhana tām nītaḥ tena asiddhaḥ prakāśitaḥ atra prayoge sa śabdaḥ eva sādhyaḥ aśliṣṭa bheda dhīra saṃspṛṣṭa anyādṛśa buddhiḥ dvābhyām api śabdābhyām ekasyāḥ vyāvṛtteḥ pratipādanāt vyavahāreṇa vyāvṛtti samāśrayeṇa upanītaḥ pratyupasthāpitaḥ yena kāraṇena sādhana tām nītaḥ tena asiddhaḥ prakāśitaḥ nanu saṃskṛta śabdaḥ anityaḥ saṃskṛta tvāt iti pratijñā artha eka deśasya yathā hetu tvam tathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ śabda tvāt iti asya api syāt iti āha bheda sāmānyayorddharma bhedāt aṃgāṃgitā tatas yathā anityaḥ prayatna utthaḥ prayatna uttha tayā dhvaniḥ 
PVV_4.176–4.188,34	 sādhya dharmi mātra niṣṭha tvāt sarvu adharma gocara tvāt ca bheda sāmānyayorddharma bhedāt vyāvṛtti bhedāt sādhya dharmaḥ hi sādhya dharmi niṣṭha tvena sajātīyāt vijātīyāt ca vyāvṛtta tvāt viśeṣaḥ sādhana dharmaḥ tu vijātīya mātra vyāvṛtta tvena sāmānyam tatas bheda sāmānya bhāvena bhedāt aṅga aṅgitā hetu sādhya tā yuktāḥ viśeṣaḥ sādhyaḥ sāmānyam hetuḥ iti kutas pratijñā artha eka deśa tā yathā anityaḥ prayatna utthaḥ dhvaniḥ iti pratijñā prayatna utthatayā iti hetuḥ śabdaḥ punar abhinna viṣayaḥ hetuḥ sādhyaḥ ca iti pratijñā artha eka deśa tvam 
PVV_4.176–4.188,35–4.176–4.188,38	 prayatna anantarīyaka tvasya dharmi viśeṣaṇa tvāt pratijñā artha eka deśa tvam asti eva iti āha pakṣa aṅga tvepi a bādha tva at na asiddhiḥ bhinna dharmiṇi yathā aśvaḥ na viṣāṇi tvāt eṣa piṃḍaḥ viṣāṇavān pakṣa aṅga tve viśeṣaṇa tvepi na asti eva tāvat sādhanasya pakṣa aṅga tvam viśeṣa sādhya tvāt bhavatu vā tathā api na asiddhasya tena viśeṣaṇena bhinne viśeṣite dharmiṇi dharmmi antara vyāvṛtte prayatna anantarīyaka tvasya avirodhāt abādha tvāt dharmiṇam viśeṣayat api prayatna uttha tvam śabde prasiddham eva yathā bahuṣu piṇḍeṣu dṛśyamāneṣu kim ayam aśvaḥ navā iti saṃśayaḥ abhidhīyate viśāṇavān eṣa piṇḍaḥ dharmī na aśvaḥ viṣāṇi tvāt iti viṣāṇi tvam dharmiṇam viśeṣa yat ipa pramāṇa pratīta tva at na asiddhaḥ hetuḥ sādhya kāla aṅga tā vā na nivṛtteḥ upalakṣya tat viśeṣa upi pratijñā arthaḥ dharma bhedāt na yujyate 
PVV_4.176–4.188,39–4.176–4.188,40	 athavā viśeṣaṇasya prayatna uttha tva ādeḥ tad śabda rūpam viśeṣya tvena upalakṣya anumānāt prāk eva nivṛtteḥ sādhya kāle anumeya pratīte kāle aṅga tā viśeṣaṇa tā na asti eva apratītam hi anumānāt pratyetavyam prayatna uttha tvāt iti ca pratītam na ca tatra vivādaḥ tatas dharmi mātra upalakṣaṇantat yathā kākaḥ devadatta gṛha upalakṣaṇa tvāt na kārya upayogī yadi api viśiṣṭe dharmiṇi pratijñā artha eka deśa tvam hetoḥ tathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ śrāvaṇa tvāt iti śabda svabhāva bhūtasya śrāvaṇa tvasya śabda tva vat pratijñā artha eka deśa tā syāt nāsā ādhāraṇa tā iti āha na kevalam viṣāṇi tva ādiḥ vviśeṣaḥ śrāvaṇa tva ādiḥ api pratijñā artha eka deśaḥ na yujyate dharmasya vyāvṛtteḥ bhedāt śrāvaṇa tvam śravaṇa grāhya tā aśrāvaṇa vyāvṛttiḥ tat ca śabdepi kvacid kañcid puruṣam apekṣya bhavati aśabda vyāvṛttiḥ tu śabda tvam tat ca sarvu atra asti tatas vyāvṛtti bhedāt śabde siddhasya śrāvaṇa tvasya anyatra ananuvṛtteḥ asādhāraṇa tā eva yuktā iti uktam sa parikaram pakṣa lakṣaṇam iti pakṣa lakṣaṇam 
PVV_4.189–4.194,0–4.189–4.194,2	 hetu lakṣaṇam idānīm vaktavyam tatra hetu lakṣaṇam eva tatra yaḥ san sajātīyeiti ādikam yuktam vaktum sa pakṣe sannasan dvedhā pakṣa dharmaḥ punar tridhā ityādinā navadhā pakṣa dharma prabhedaḥ tu kasmāt uktaḥ iti āha pakṣa dharma prabhedena sukha grahaṇa siddhaye hetu prakaraṇa arthasya sūtra saṃkṣepaḥ ucyate pakṣa dharmasya navadhā prabhedena hetu prakaraṇa arthasya hetu hetu ābhāsa lakṣaṇa ātmakasya sukhena grahaṇasya siddhaye tad artha vācakānām sūtrāṇām saṃkṣepataḥ saṃgrahaḥ ucyate sa pakṣe san= ityādinā 
PVV_4.189–4.194,3–4.189–4.194,4	 yadi pakṣasya dharmaḥ hetuḥ tadā tad viśeṣaṇa apekṣasya dharmasya anyatra dharmiṇī ananu vṛtteḥ asādhāraṇa tā syāt atha pakṣeṇa na viśiṣyate tadā na pakṣa dharmaḥ hetuḥ syāt asat etat na hi anya yoga vyavacchedena eva viśeṣaṇam anyathā api sambhavāt iti darśayitum āha ayogam yogam aparaiḥ atyanta ayogam eva ca vyavacchinatti dharmasya nipātaḥ vyatirecakaḥ 
PVV_4.189–4.194,5–4.189–4.194,7	 nipātaḥ eva kāraḥ vyatirecakaḥ niyāmakaḥ kvacid dharmasya viśeṣaṇasya ayogam vyavacchinatti kvacid aparaiḥ vviśeṣyāt anyaiḥ yogam vyavacchinatti kvacid atyanta ayogam vyavacchinatti nanu nipātaḥ na svayam vācakaḥ kintu dyotakaḥ tat asya katham ayam artha prabhedaḥ iti āha viśeṣaṇa viśeṣābhyām kriyayā ca saha uditaḥ 
PVV_4.189–4.194,8–4.189–4.194,11	 dyotaka tvāt eva nipātaḥ viśeṣaṇena saha uditaḥ ayogasya vyavacchedakaḥ viśe saha uktonya yogasya kriyayā ca saha uktaḥ atyanta ayogasya iti viśeṣaṇa ādi pada vācyaḥ eva ayoga vyavaccheda ādiḥ tad saha ukta nipāta dyotyaḥ iti arthaḥ bhavatu tāvat nipāta prayoge vyavaccheda viśeṣasya pratītiḥ pakṣaḥ iti ādau tu katham iti āha vivakṣātaḥ aprayogepi sarvaḥ arthoyam pratīyate vyavaccheda phalam vākyam yatas caitraḥ dhanurdharaḥ pārthaḥ dhanurddharaḥ nīlam sarojam iti vā yathā 
PVV_4.189–4.194,12	 aprayogepi nipātasya vaktuḥ vvivakṣātaḥ sarvu oṃyama yoga vyavaccheda ādiḥ arthaḥ miti uktam prāk vākyañca upalakṣaṇam padam api vyavaccheda phalam na hi ghaṭena udakam ānaya iti pratipādam anavadhāraṇe aghaṭena ānayana pratiṣedhaḥ pakṣaḥ iti ādau tu katham iti āha aprayogepi nipātasya vaktuḥ vvivakṣātaḥ saru vaḥ yama yoga vyavacchedaḥ anudaka ānayana pratiṣedhaḥ anānayana nivṛttiḥ vvā śakya upadarśanā ayoga vyavaccheda ādīnām udāharaṇam āha yathā caitraḥ dhanurddharaḥ pārthaḥ dhanurddharaḥ nīlam caitre dhanurddharatu asan dehāt viśeṣaṇena ayoga mātram vyavacchidyate pārthe dhanurddhara tvam prasiddham eva kintu tādṛśam anyasya api kim asti iti sandehe anya yoga vyavaccheda phalam viśeṣaṇam na khalu sarvvam eva nīlam sarojam yena ayoga vyavacchedaḥ syāt na api sarojam eva nīlam yena anya yoga vyavacchedaḥ bhavet kintu nīlam sarojam saṃbhavati na vā iti anta ayoga saṃdehe viśeṣaṇena saḥ eva vyavacchidyate 
PVV_4.189–4.194,13	 nanu bhavatu tāvat caitraḥ dhanurddharaḥ eva pārthaḥ eva dhanurddharaḥ sarojam nīlam saṃbhavati eva iti nipāta prayoge vivakṣā vaśāt viśeṣaṇa ādi padānām eva vā vyavaccheda pratipādaka tvāt aprayoge a pi nipātasya caitraḥ dhanurddharaḥ iti ādi prayogeṣu yoga vyavaccheda ādīnām pratītiḥ pakṣa dharmaḥ iti atra punar pakṣaḥ viśeṣaṇam dharmaḥ viśeṣyaḥ tat yadi pakṣasya eva dharmaḥ iti viśeṣaṇena saha nipātaḥ ucyate aprayogepi vā viśeṣaṇasya tad artha vṛtti teṣyate upa bhayathā api anya yoga vyavaccheda pratipādaka tvam eva syāt 
PVV_4.189–4.194,14	 atha dharmaḥ eva viśeṣyaḥ nipāta sahacaraḥ tad artha vṛttiḥ vveṣṭaḥ tadā ayoga vyavacchedaḥ labhyate eva param viśeṣaṇa sahitaḥ anya yogam vyavacchinatti iti ukteḥ vvirudhyate atra ucyate bāhyaḥ nipātaḥ śrūyamāṇā upi viśeṣya ādibhiḥ saha vaktṛ vivakṣa avaśāt gamyamānaḥ vā ayoga vyavacchedakaḥ bhavati iti dṛṣṭānta pradarśana artham uktam tathā eva caitraḥ dhanurddharaḥ iti ādi udāharaṇa pradarśanāt vyavaccheda phalam vākyam iti ukteḥ ca samāse tu viśeṣaṇam eva ayoga ādi vyavacchedakam vivakṣā vaśā ādiṣṭam ayoga vyavacchedena viśeṣaṇāt iti ukteḥ pakṣa dharmaḥ iti pakṣa śabdaḥ ayoga vyavacchedakaḥ pakṣa asambaddhaḥ na bhavati iti arthaḥ cākṣuṣam rūpam iti cākṣuṣa tvasya rūpe vivāda abhāvāt śabda ādīnām viśeṣaṇena vyavacchedaḥ kriyate nīlotpalam iti utpale nīlatva niyama abhāvāt pareṣu abhāvāt ayoga ani ayogayoḥ vyavaccheda abhāvāt nīla śabdena atyanta asambhava mātram vyavacchidyate iti na kaścid virodhaḥ 
PVV_4.189–4.194,15–4.189–4.194,19	 nanu yathā pārthaḥ eva dhanurddharaḥ iti viśeṣaṇasya sannidhānāt nipātasya viśeṣya antara vyavacchedaḥ tathā viśeṣaṇa sannidhānāt avadhāraṇasya caitraḥ dhanurddharaḥ eva iti guṇa antara vyavacchedaḥ syāt iti āha pratiyogi vyavacchedaḥ tatra api artheṣu gamyate tathā prasiddheḥ sāmarthyāt vivakṣā anugamāt dhvaneḥ tatra viśeṣaṇa ādiṣu artheṣu vyavaccheda īpi kriyamāṇe prakaraṇāt buddhi viṣayīkṛtasya pratiyogina vyavacchedaḥ viśeṣaṇena gamyate na anyasya tathā prasiddheḥ pratiyoginaḥ eva buddhi sthīkṛtya viśeṣaṇena vyavacchedaḥ na itarasya iti loka prasiddheḥ vivakṣāyāḥ rvi avaccheda ādau sāmarthya anna avivakṣita vyavacchedaḥ yatas eva ayoga vyavaccheda upi asti tad ayoga vyavacchedāt dharmī dharma viśeṣaṇam tad viśiṣṭa tayā dharmaḥ na niranvaya doṣa bhāj tat tasmāt dharmī pakṣaḥ dharmasya ayoga vyavacchedāt viśeṣaṇam dharmiṇaḥ na adharmaḥ hetuḥ iti arthaḥ ayoga vyavacchedāt tena dharmiṇā viśiṣṭa tayā dharmaḥ niranvaya t oṣa bhāj bhavati 
PVV_4.189–4.194,20	 sa pakṣe ghaṭa ādau san śabda anitya tve sādhye kṛtaka tvam hetuḥ asan sa pakṣe vyoma ādau śabda anitya tve sādhye kṛtaka tvam hetuḥ sa pakṣe dvedhā sannasan= ca śabda anitya tve sādhye yatna ja tvam hetuḥ ghaṭa ādau sa pakṣe san vidyut ādau ca āsan punar tridhā sa pakṣe san asan sadasan= ca śabdasya yatna ja tve sādhye sa pakṣe ghaṭa ādau= anitya tvam hetuḥ san śabda anitya tve sādhye yatna ja tvam hetuḥ asan vidyut ādau sa pakṣe śabde ayatna ja tve sādhye anitya tvam hetuḥ sa pakṣe vidyut ādau san vyoma ādau ca āsan evam pratyekam asapakṣepi san asan dvedhā ca iti yojyam śabda nitya tve sādhye prameya tvam hetuḥ asapakṣe ghaṭa ādau san śabda nitya tve sādhye śrāvaṇa tvam hetu rasa pakṣe asan śabda nitya tve sādhye asparśava tvam hetu rasa pakṣe ghaṭāt āvasan buddhi ādau san= iti dvidhā pakṣa dharma nirdeśaḥ kimartha hetu prakaraṇe navadhā pakṣa dharma nirdeśaḥ 
PVV_4.195–4.198,0–4.195–4.198,2^1	 samyak hetuḥ asiddha viruddha anaikāntika hetvābhāsāḥ eva yukta nirdeśāḥ iti āha svabhāva kārya sidhi artham dvau dvau hetu viparyayau vivādāt bheda sāmānye śeṣaḥ vyāvṛtti sādhanaḥ svabhāva kāryayoḥ eva hetu tvena siddhi artham tatra dvau śabde a nitya tva siddhi artham kṛtaka tva prayatna ānantarīyaka tva ākhyau hetū nirdiṣṭau tathā śabdaḥ eva nitya tva sādhane dvau hetu viruddhau hetu bhāve ca uktau yathā hi samyak hetoḥ sva sādhye vyāpya kārya tayā pratibaddhasya gamaka tvam tathā sādhya viparyaye vyāpya kārya tayā pratibaddhasya eva tad gamaka tvena viruddha tā na anyasya iti arthaḥ 
PVV_4.195–4.198,0–4.195–4.198,2^2	 vyatirekīanvayī ca hetuḥ iti pareṣām vivā tad pratiṣedha artham bheda sāmānye asādhāraṇa sādhāraṇe śrāvaṇa tva prameya tve nirddiṣṭe yadi vipakṣe na asti iti sa ātmaka tve sādhye prāṇa ādima tvam hetuḥ tadā śrāvaṇa tvam api syāt na ca evam tasmāt na vyatirekī hetuḥ yadi ca kevala anvayinaḥ darśana mātra adhyavasita avyabhicārasya hetu tvam tadā prameya tvasya ākāśa ādau darśanāt avyabhicāra niścaye sati śabde nitya tva gamaka tvam syāt na ca evam tatas na kevala anvayī hetuḥ śeṣaḥ aprayatna utthaḥ śabdaḥ anitya tvāt nityaḥ śabdaḥ asparśava tvāt prayatna ānantarīyaḥ śabdaḥ anitya tvāt iti hetu trayam vipakṣāt hetoḥ vyāvṛtti sādhanaḥ 
PVV_4.195–4.198,3–4.195–4.198,4	 yadi hi sa pakṣe darśana mātreṇa gamaka tvam tadā ete hetavaḥ prāptāḥ sarvu eṣām sa pakṣe satvāt tasmāt na anvaya sambandha mātreṇa gamaka tvam kintu vipakṣāt vyatireka niścaye na ca asti vyatireka niścayaḥ pradhānam hetu tva nibandhanam iti arthaḥ katham punar jñāyate svabhāva hetuḥ kṛtaka tvam kārya hetuḥ prayatna ānantarīyakam iti āha na hi svabhāvāt anyena vyāptiḥ gamyasya kāraṇe sambhavāt vyabhicārasya dvidhā vṛtti phalam tatas 
PVV_4.195–4.198,5	 na hi svabhāvāt hetoḥ anyena hetunā gamyasya sādhyasya vyāptiḥ yatra yatra anitya tvam tatra kṛtaka tvam iti dṛśyate ca vyāptiḥ tasmāt svabhāva hetuḥ eva na avaśyam kāraṇāni kāryavanti bhavanti iti kāraṇe kāryasya vyabhicāra sambhavāt kāryam kāraṇa vyāpakam na bhavati tatra sa pakṣe dvidhā vṛtti bhāva abhāvāt pratyatna ānantarīya tvam phalam kārya hetuḥ prayatna kāryasya tathā abhidhānāt 
PVV_4.195–4.198,6–4.195–4.198,8	 nanu prayatna jena jñānena anityaḥ śabdaḥ anumeyaḥ iṣṭaḥ śabdāḥ ca nityāḥ eva tad viṣaya jñāna utpāda ādinā yatnena te vyajyante tat katham kārya hetu udāharaṇam idam iti āha prayatna anantaram jñānam prāc sataḥ niyamena na tasya āvṛtyakṣa śabdeṣu sarvathā anupayogataḥ prayatnāt prāk sataḥ śabdasya niyamena prayatna anantaram jñānam yajyate prayatnam vinā api kadācid upalabhyeta na ca prayatna vyajyatā śabdānām yuktāḥ tasya prayatnasya āvṛtau= upalambha āvaraṇe śabda viṣaya jñāna janake śrotre śabdeṣu ca viṣayeṣu sarvu athā akiñcid kara tvena anupayogataḥ iti uktam prāk 
PVV_4.195–4.198,9–4.195–4.198,11	 kiñca kadācid nirapekṣasya kāryā akṛti virodhataḥ kādācid ka phalam siddham tat liṅgam jñānam īdṛśam sahakāribhiḥ anādheya atiśaya tvet nityasya kadācid prayatna kāle kāryasya jñānasya kṛti virodhataḥ kāraṇāt tat śruti viṣayam jñānam kādācid kasya anityasya śabdasya phalam liṅgam kāryam īdṛśam niyamena prayatna anantara bhāvi siddham 
PVV_4.199,0–4.199,1	 etāvatā eva siddhepi svabhāvasya pṛthak kṛtiḥ kāryeṇa saha nirddeśe mā jñāsīt sarvam īdṛśam etāvatā prayatna anantarīyaka tvena eva svabhāva hetu nirdeśa ipi siddhe prayatna anantaram utpādasya abhivyakteḥ ca tathā abhidhānāt tathā api svabhāvasya kṛtaka tvasya hetoḥ yā pṛthakkṛtiḥ sā kāryeṇa saha śleṣeṇa nirdeśe mā jñāsīt pratipattā sarvvam svabhāva hetum īdṛśam sa pakṣe dvidhā vṛttim kṛtaka tva ādeḥ viparyaya vyāpti sambhavāt 
PVV_4.200,0–4.200,2	 kiñca vyutpatti arthā ca hetu ukti rukta artha anumitau kṛtā atra prabhedaḥ ākhyātaḥ lakṣaṇantu na bhidyate anumitau sva artha anumāne hetu ukti rukta arthā abhihita lakṣaṇā api pratipattṝṇām vyutpatti arthā ca para artha anumāne kṛtā atra ca prabhedaḥ ākhyātaḥ lakṣaṇam punar hetoḥ na bhidyate tathāvidha lakṣaṇa hetu vacanasya para artha anumāna tvāt 
PVV_4.201,0–4.201,1	 tena atra kārya liṅgena svabhāva upi eka deśa bhāj sadṛśa udāhṛtiḥ ca atas prayatnāt vyakti janmanaḥ tena prayatna antarīyaka tvena kārya liṅgena śleṣa nirdeśāt svabhāva hetu dharma bhājā svabhāvopi sa pakṣa eka deśa bhāj bhavati iti aktaḥ bhavati atas eva kārya svabhāva tayā sadṛśasya prayatna anantarīyaka tvasya udāhṛtirā cā rye ṇa kṛtā prayatnādnaḥ ca bhāvāt yadā prayatnāt vyaktiḥ tadā kārya hetuḥ yadā janma tadā svabhāva hetuḥ 
PVV_4.202,0–4.202,2	 kārya svabhāvayoḥ prabheda nirdeśasya kim phalam iti āha yat na antarīyakā sattā yaḥ vā ātmani avibhāgavān sa tena avyabhicārī syāt iti artham tad prabhedanam yat na antarīyakā sattā bhede sati yam antareṇa hetuḥ na bhavati yaḥ vā sve ātmīyaḥ sādhyāt avibhāgavān ātmā svabhāvaḥ sa kāraṇena vyāpakena vā avyabhicārī vyabhicāra rahitaḥ syāt na anyaḥ iti artham etat prayojanam tayoḥ kārya svabhāvayoḥ prabhedanam 
PVV_4.203,0–4.203,2	 evañca sati saṃyogi ādiṣu yeṣu asti pratibandhaḥ na tādṛśaḥ na te hetavaḥ iti uktam vyabhicārasya sambhavāt saṃyogi samavāyi eka artha samavāyi ākāśa ādiṣu para abhimateṣu hetuṣu yeṣu pratistādātmya tad utpatti lakṣaṇaḥ na asti na te hetavaḥ iti uktam bhavati atada ātmanaḥ atad utpatteḥ ca sādhya vyabhicārasya sambhavāt 
PVV_4.204,0–4.204,2	 atha saṃyogi ādiṣu tad utpatti pratibandha usti tadā sati vā pratibandheḥ tu saḥ eva gati sādhanaḥ niyamaḥ hi avinābhāvaḥ aniyataḥ ca na sādhanam sati pratibandhe sādhya pratipatti hetuḥ astu niṣphalā saṃyogi ādi kalpanā niyamaḥ niyata tvam hi sādhanasya sākṣāt avinābhāvaḥ ucyate sa ca tādātmya tad utpattibhyām na anyathā sa ca tad vikala tvāt sādhye aniyataḥ na sa sādhanam yathā saṃyogi tvepi sa vahniḥ ddhūmasya iti svabhāva kārya siddhi artham dvau dvau ti vyākhyātam 
PVV_4.205,0–4.205,3	 vivādāt bheda sāmānyaḥ iti vyākhyātavyam syāt prāṇa ādima tvam hetuḥ yadi vipakṣāt hetu vyatirekaḥ syāt saḥ eva tu na sidhyati iti āha aikāntika tvam vyāvṛtteḥ avinā abhāvaḥ ucyate tat ca na apratibaddheṣu tatas eva anvaya sthitiḥ vipakṣāt bhedaḥ vyāvṛtteḥ bbādhaka pramāṇa niścita tvāt aikāntika tvam avinā abhāva vyāvṛtteḥ aikāntika tvam sva sādhya apratibaddheṣu prāṇa ādiṣu na asti yadi hi ātmani pratibaddhāḥ prāṇa ādayaḥ tad ātma nivṛttau nivṛttāḥ vipakṣāt gamyeran anyathā tu pakṣaḥ eva sandehaḥ kim amī ātmā abhāvepi varttante uta na iti yathā ca pratibandhāt vyatireka niścayaḥ tathā tatas pratibandhāt eva anvayasya sthitiḥ na tu saha darśana mātreṇa 
PVV_4.206,0–4.206,2	 tasmāt sādhyasya sva ātma tve hetu bhāve vā siddhe hi vyatirekitā sidhyet atas viśeṣe na vyatirekaḥ na ca anvayaḥ sva ātma tve hetu svabhāva ātmaka tve hetu bhāve vā siddhe sati tad abhāve niyamena vyatirekāt vipakṣāt vyāpaka kāraṇa vyatireke svabhāva kārya hetvoḥ vyatirekitā sidhyet na anyathā iti nyāyaḥ eṣaḥ yatas pratibandhena eva anvaya vyatireka siddhiḥ atas viśeṣe asādhāraṇe hetau na anvayaḥ na vā vyatirekaḥ sidhyati 
PVV_4.207,0–4.207,2	 evam tarhi sa pakṣa vipakṣa vyatirekābhyām vyāvṛtteḥ viśeṣaḥ katha mā cā rye ṇa uktaḥ iti āha adṛṣṭi mātram ādāya kevalam vyatirekitā uktā anaikāntikaḥ tasmāt anyathā gamakaḥ bhavet adṛṣṭi mātram bādaka pramāṇa rahitam ādāya para abhiprāyeṇa sa pakṣāt vyatireki tasya adarśana mātreṇa vyatireka aniścayāt anaikāntikaḥ ācāryeṇa uktaḥ anyathā vipakṣāt vyatireka niścaye gamakaḥ hetuḥ bhavet tatas ca anaikāntika varge na prakṣipyeta 
PVV_4.208,0–4.208,2	 nanu sādhya nivṛttau niyamena sādhanam nivarttate iti sādhya abhāvaḥ sādhana abhāvena vyāptaḥ tatas ca prāṇa ādi abhāvaḥ nairātmya vyāpī iti vinivarttane ātmanaḥ vinivartteta prāṇa ādiḥ yadi tat ca na prāṇa ādeḥ sādhanasya abhāvaḥ nairātmyasya sa ātmaka tva sādhya abhāvasya vyāpi iti hetoḥ ātmanaḥ ghaṭa ādeḥ vvipakṣāt vinivarttane sati prāṇa ādiḥ vvinivarttate na hi anyathā sādhana abhāvaḥ sādhya abhāvasya ca vyāpakaḥ bhavati tatas yatra prāṇa ādi bhāva nivṛttiḥ tatra sa ātmaka tva bhāva nivṛttiḥ api iti yadi ucyate tat ca na yuktam 
PVV_4.209–4.210,0–4.209–4.210,1	 anyasya vinivṛtya anya vinivṛttyeḥ ayogataḥ tad ātmā tad prasūtiḥ ced na etat anyasya kāraṇasya ātmanaḥ vinivṛttyā prāṇa ādeḥ vvinivṛtteḥ ayogataḥ tādātmya tad utpattau= eva hi sādhya nivṛttau sādhana nivṛttiḥ yuktā tad svabhāva tvāt tad āyatta tvāt ca sati ca sādhya sādhanayoḥ niyamena nivartti a nivarttaka bhāve sādhya abhāvaḥ sādhana abhāvena vyāpyate prāṇa ādiḥ tasya ātmanaḥ ātmā svabhāvaḥ tasmāt prasūtiḥ vvāsya iti ced na etat asti yuktam tathā hi 
PVV_4.209–4.210,2–4.209–4.210,4	 ātma upalambhane tasya upalabdha avagata avagatau ca prasidhyati te ca atyanta parokṣasya dṛṣṭi adṛṣṭī na sidhyataḥ ātmanaḥ upalambhane sati tasya prāṇa ādeḥ upalabdhau satyām ātmanaḥ agatau prāṇa ādeḥ agatau ca satyām kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ prasidhyati te ca dṛṣṭi adṛṣṭī kārya kāraṇa bhāva sādhane atyanta parokṣasya ātmanaḥ na sidhyataḥ atyanta parokṣasya katham adṛṣṭiḥ api na sidhyati iti ced abhāva sādhikā dṛśya anupalabdhiḥ na sidhyati eva adṛṣṭi mātrantu na abhau= a sādhakam tatas prāṇa ādeḥ ātmanā saha pratibandhā siddheḥ na ātma nivṛttyā prāṇa ādi nivṛtti siddhiḥ 
PVV_4.211,0–4.211,2	 kiñca anyatra adṛṣṭa rūpasya ghaṭa ādau na iti vā kutas ajñāta vyatirekasya vyāvṛtteḥ vyāpitā kutas ātmanā uni atra jīvat śarīre adṛṣṭa rūpasya ghaṭa ādau na sattvam iti yat ucyate tat kutas siddham dṛśya anupalabdhyā hi abhāva siddhiḥ na ca adṛṣṭa care tad sambhavaḥ ajñātaḥ abhāvaḥ yasya tasya ātmanaḥ yā vyāvṛttiḥ ghaṭa ādau tasyāḥ prāṇa ādi nivṛttyā vyāpitāḥ vyāpanam kutas sambhavi yena jīvat śarīre prāṇa ādi nivṛtti abhāvāt sa ātmaka tva nivṛtti abhāve satya ātma siddhiḥ syāt 
PVV_4.212,0–4.212,2	 nanu yathā ghaṭa ādau prāṇa ādi abhāva niścayaḥ tathā ātma abhāva niścayopi kim na bhavati iti āha prāṇa ādeḥ ca kvacid dṛṣṭyā sattva asattvam pratīyate tathā ātmā yadi dṛśyeta sattva asattvam pratīyate prāṇa ādeḥ kvacid jīvat śarīre dṛṣṭyā sattvam pratīyate mṛta dehe ca upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya asya adṛṣṭyā asattvam pratīyate tathā yadi kvacid dehe ātmā dṛśyeta tadā tatra sattvam asya pratīyeta anyatra upalabhya svarūpasya asya anupalabdheḥ asattvam pratīyeta na ca ātma upalabdhiḥ asti kvacid iti na tad abhāva niścayaḥ 
PVV_4.213,0–4.213,2	 yat api ucyate yadi na sa ātmakam jīvat śarīram tadā asya prāṇa ādi viraha prasaṅgaḥ narātmyāt ghaṭa vat iti prasaṅga sādhanam tat ca ayuktam darśayitum āha yasya hetoḥ abhāvena ghaṭe prāṇaḥ na dṛśyate dehepi yadi asau na syāt yuktaḥ dehe na sambhavaḥ yasya buddhi deha atiśaya prayatna ādeḥ hetoḥ a bhāvena ghaṭe prāṇaḥ na dṛśyate dehepi buddhi deha atiśaya prayatna ādiḥ na syāt tadā dehepi hetu virahāt prāṇa ādeḥ na saṃbhavaḥ yuktaḥ yathā mṛta śarīre jīvat dehe tu buddhi ādi sadbhāvāt eva prāṇa ādi rucita saṃbhavaḥ iti na ātma abhāve tad abhāva prasaṅgaḥ saṅgataḥ 
PVV_4.214,0–4.214,2	 atha ghaṭa jīvat śarīra ādīnām nairātmyena yathā sādharmyam tathā prāṇa ādi rahita tayā api syāt na ca bhavati tasmāt nirātmake ghaṭa ādau prāṇa ādiḥ adṛṣṭaḥ yatra varttate tatra sa ātmaka tvam sādhayati iti āha bhinnepi kiñcid sādharmyāt yadi tattvam pratīyate prameya tvāt ghaṭa ādīnām sa ātma tvam kinna mīyate ghaṭabhinnepi jīvat dehe kiñcit mātreṇa nirātmaka tvena sādharmyāt yadi tattvam prāṇa ādi virahita tayā ghaṭa sadṛśa tvam pratīyate tadā aprameya tvāt hetoḥ ghaṭa ādīnām jīvat śarīrasa ātmaka tvam kinna mīyate 
PVV_4.215,0–4.215,1	 aniṣṭeḥ ced pramāṇam hi sarva iṣṭīnām nibandhanam bhāva abhāva vyavakthām kaḥ karttum tena vinā prabhuḥ aniṣṭeḥ ced nanu pramāṇam hi sarvu a iṣṭīnām nibandhanam tad vaśena arthān na sthiteḥ tena pramāṇena bhāva abhāvayoḥ vyavasthām karttum kaḥ prabhuḥ yadi ca kiñcid sādharmya mātrāt sādhanam sādhya sādhakam tadā prameya tvāt ghaṭasya api sa ātmaka tva sādhanāt aniṣṭiḥ anupayuktāḥ 
PVV_4.216–4.217,0–4.216–4.217,2	 yadi tarhi na ātmā prāṇa ādeḥ hetuḥ kaḥ tarhi bhaviṣyati iti āha yathā yogam smṛti icchā āyatna jaḥ prāṇa nimeṣa ādiḥ tad udbhavaḥ viṣaya indriya cittebhyaḥ smṛti icchā prayatnebhyaḥ jātaḥ prāṇa nimeṣa ādiḥ samāhitasya niruddhavāyoḥ samādhi vyutthitasya smaraṇāt prāṇa vṛttiḥ gāḍha prahāra ādibhiḥ vyāhata prāṇasya icchā prayatnābhyām prāṇa pravṛttiḥ svasthasya sādguṇyāt nimeṣa ādeḥ icchā prayatna ja tvam vyaktam teṣām ca smṛti icchā āyatnānām udbhavaḥ viṣaya indriya cittebhyaḥ yathāyogam kvacid viṣayāt vadarāde rasanā srava ādi hetaḥ rasa ādi smṛtiḥ bhavati indriyāt vā vilādera paṭu jāna hetoḥ pradīpa maṇḍala ādi smaraṇam bhavati buddheḥ eva atad viṣayasya atīta anukūla tā ādi smṛtiḥ udbhavati 
PVV_4.216–4.217,3–4.216–4.217,6	 nanu ṣaḍ pravṛtti buddhayaḥ eva ātmajāḥ pravṛtti buddhi jāḥ ca smṛti ādayaḥ tad bhavāḥ ca prāṇa ādayaḥ iti paraṃparā atma hetukāḥ eva iti āha tāḥ ṣaṣ buddhayaḥ tāḥ sva jāti samudbhavāḥ anyonya pratyaya apekṣā anvaya vyatireka bhāj etāvatī ātma bhāvoyam anavasthāni akalpane anyonya pratyaya apekṣā yasyāḥ yaḥ ātmīyaḥ pratyayaḥ sahakāri kāraṇam indriya ādi tasmin= apekṣā ayat tiḥ yāsām tāḥ tathā satyaḥ sva jāti samudbhavāḥ samanantara prabhavāḥ na tu paraṃparayā api ātma apekṣiṇyaḥ iti arthaḥ etāvati kāraṇa kalāpe ayam ātma bhāvaḥ ṣaṣ āyatanam gṛhītaḥ anvaya vyatireka bhāj pratibaddhaḥ kāraṇa tvena tatonyasya kalpane anavasthā kāraṇānām tasmāt na adṛṣṭa sāmarthyasya ātmanaḥ nivṛttau prāṇa ādi nivṛttiḥ yuktā 
PVV_4.218,0–4.218,2	 kiñca śrāvaṇa tvena tat tulyam prāṇa ādi vyabhicārataḥ na tasya vyabhicāri tvāt vyatirekepi ced katham tat prāṇa ādi sādhanam śrāvaṇa tvena hetunā vyabhicārataḥ anaikāntika tvāt tulyam na etat asti tasya śrāvaṇa tvasya vipakṣāt bahulam vyatirekepi vyatirekasya vyabhi na hi śrāvaṇa tvam anityebhyaḥ prāyas vyāvṛttam iti anitya tva vyatireka avyabhicāri śakyam avasātum pakṣaḥ eva anityena saha akārya virodhāt prāṇa ādi tu niyamena vipakṣāt vyatireka avyabhicāri iti na yuktam śrāvaṇa tvena tulyam iti ced pṛcchatyā cā ryaḥ prāṇa ādi śrāvaṇa tvena atulyam katham iti 
PVV_4.219,0–4.219,2	 itaraḥ āha na asādhyāt eva viśleṣaḥ tasya nanu evam ucyate sādhyenu vṛtya bhāva ūrthāt tasya anyatra api asau samaḥ tasya śrāvaṇa tvasya asādhyāt vipakṣāt eva na viśleṣaḥ vyāvṛttiḥ kintu sa pakṣāt api prāṇa ādeḥ tu saru u asya jīvat śarīrasya sa ātma tvena sādhya tvāt sa pakṣaḥ eva na asti iti kathantataḥ vyāvṛttiḥ iti atra āha nanu evam asādhyāt eva śrāvaṇa tvasya na viśleṣa eti ākhyānesādhya sādhyavati sa pakṣe anuvṛtteḥ anvayasya abhāvaḥ arthāt uktaḥ syāt yaḥ hi vipakṣa mātrāt avyāvṛttaḥ sa sa pakṣāt api vyāvṛtteḥ anvaya rahitaḥ uktaḥ bhavati tathā ca prāṇa ādeḥ asau sa pakṣa anuvṛtti abhāvaḥ samaḥ na hi prāṇa ādi sapakṣe kvacid siddham sarvvaṃsya jīvat śarīrasya pakṣa tvāt 
PVV_4.220,0–4.220,1	 asādhyāt eva vicchedaḥ iti sādhyeḥ titā ucyate artha apatyā atas eva uktam ekena ubhaya darśanam asādhyāt vipakṣāt eva sādhanasya vicchedaḥ vyāvṛttiḥ iti abhidhānena artha apatti asāmarthyena sādhye sa pakṣe astitā ucyate yadi tu sa pakṣāt api vyāvṛttiḥ tadā vipakṣāt eva vyāvṛttiḥ iti asaṅgatam yatas vipakṣāt eva vyāvṛttiḥ iti vyatirekaḥ ākṣipta anvayaḥ eva bhavati atas evā cā rye ṇaḥ ekena vyatirekeṇa anvayena vā niyamavatā dṛṣṭena ubhayam uktam arthāpattyā anyatareṇa ubhaya darśanāt iti 
PVV_4.221,0–4.221,2	 yasmāt aikāntikaḥ vyatirekaḥ ākṣipta anvayaḥ eva bhavati atas īdṛś avyabhicārotaḥ ananvayiṣu na sidhyati pratiṣedha niṣedhaḥ ca vidhānāt kīdṛśaḥ aparaḥ īdṛś vipakṣe vyatirekaḥ vyabhicāraḥ ananvayiṣu hetuṣu na sidhyati yaḥ eva sādhyena anvitaḥ hetuḥ tasya eva vipakṣāt eva vyatirekaḥ yadi tu sati api sādhye hetu abhāvaḥ tadā sa pakṣāt api vyatirekāt katham vipakṣāt eva nivṛttiḥ kiñca prāṇa ādeḥ sa pakṣe pratiṣedhasya nivṛtteniṣedhaḥ vidhānāt aparaḥ kīdṛśaḥ pratiṣedha niṣedhaḥ hi vidhiḥ eva paraspara parihāreṇa avasthiteḥ tatas prāṇa ādeḥ sa pakṣāt nivṛttiḥ na asti iti arthāt vṛttiḥ eva uktā syāt iti na vyatireki tvam 
PVV_4.222,0–4.222,2	 syāt evam yadi sa pakṣaḥ bhavati kintu nivṛttiḥ na asataḥ sādhyāt asādhyeṣu eva no tatas na iti sā eva nivṛttiḥ kim nivṛtteḥ asataḥ matā sa ātmaka tve sādhye sa pakṣaḥ na asti iti asataḥ sādhyāt sa pakṣāt prāṇa ādeḥ nivṛttiḥ na asti vipakṣeṣu eva naḥ vṛttiḥ iti vyatireki tvam iṣṭam evantarhi sa pakṣāt asataḥ hetoḥ nivṛtteḥ nivṛttiḥ asmākam astitvena yeṣṭā sā eva kinna iti bhavataḥ matā yadi hi asat nivṛtteḥ na adhikaraṇam tadā nivṛtta nivṛtteḥ katham bhaviṣyati 
PVV_4.223,0–4.223,2	 kiñca nivṛtti abhāvaḥ tu vidhiḥ vvastu bhāvaḥ asatā upi san vastu abhāvaḥ tu na asti iti paśya bāndhya vijṛmbhitam asatā upi sa pakṣāt hetu nivṛtteḥ nīrūpāyāḥ abhāvaḥ tu vidhiḥ vastu bhāvaḥ hetu sambhavaḥ sa na iṣyate yadi asati sa pakṣe hetu nivṛttiḥ na asti tadā hetuḥ eva asti iti uktam syāt vastunaḥ hetoḥ abhāvaḥ tu nivṛtti śabda vācyaḥ na asti iti paśya bāndhya vijṛmbhitam pareṣām asatya sattavam aviruddham viruddhantu sattvam iti arthaḥ

PVV_4.269,0–4.269,1	 kāraṇāt kārya saṃsiddhiḥ svabhāva antargamāt iyam hetu prabheda ākhyāne na darśita udāhṛtiḥ pṛthak kāraṇāt dṛśya adarśanāt asat jñāna śabda vyavahāra kārya yogya tā saṃsiddhiḥ ba svabhāva hetau= antarga mā atra hetu antaram tena iyam svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ hetunā prabhedasya ākhyāne kriyamāṇe svabhāva hetunā eva darśita udāhṛtiḥ na pṛthak nirddiṣṭā 
PVV_4.270,0–4.270,2	 bhavatu tāvat dṛśya anupalabdheḥ asat vyavahāra yogya tā siddhiḥ sā eva tu katham sidhyati iti āha eka upalambha anubhavāt idam na upalabhe iti buddheḥ upalabhe vā iti kalpikāyāḥ samudbhavaḥ eka jñāna saṃsargiṇaḥ ekasya pradeśa saya upalambha anubhavāt sva samvedanāt anantaram ghaṭa ādi na upalabhyate idam pradeśa ubhyupala bhyatas iti kalpikāyāḥ buddheḥ sva vedana viṣayī kṛta vidhi pratiṣedha anukāriṇyāḥ samudbhavaḥ bhavati iti sva samvedanā t eva anupalambha siddhiḥ 
PVV_4.271,0–4.271,2	 bhavatu jñānam sva samvedana viṣayayoḥ jñānayoḥ anyonya bhedaḥ tu kena jñāyate iti āha viśeṣaḥ gamyate arthānām viśiṣṭāt eva vedanāt tathābhūta ātma saṃpattiḥ bheda dhī hetuḥ asya ca arthānām viṣeśaḥ anyonyam bhedaḥ gamyate viśiṣṭa pratiniyata ākārāt eva vedanāt asya samvedanasya tayoḥ bheda aniyata ākāra tvam tasya dhiyaḥ samvedanasya tu sādhanaṃtathā bhūtā pratiniyata ākārā para nirapekṣa prakāśa ātma saṃpattiḥ aparokṣa tā 
PVV_4.272,0–4.272,1	 tasmāt svatas dhiyoḥ bheda siddhiḥ tābhyām tad arthayoḥ anyathā hi anavasthātaḥ bhedaḥ sidhyet na kasyacid tasmāt dhiyaḥ bhedasya svatas pratiniyatāt aparokṣa prakāśāt svarūpataā iva siddhiḥ tābhyām bhinna tayā siddhābhyām tayoḥ arthayoḥ sārūpya janakayoḥ bheda siddhiḥ anyathā yadi evam na iṣyate tadā aparābhyām bheda siddhiḥ vvaktavyā tayoḥ ca bheda siddhau bheda grāhaka tā yuktā iti tad bheda grāhakam aparam dvayameṣṭavyam evam apara apara apekṣāyām anavasthātaḥ na kasyacid bhedaḥ sidhyet 
PVV_4.273,0–4.274,1	 viśiṣṭa rūpa anubhavāt anyathā anya nirākriyā tad viśiṣṭa upalambhotaḥ tasya api anupalambhanam atas viśiṣṭasya niyatasya rūpasya anubhavāt an yathā anyasya nirākriyā na bhavati atas tasmāt pratiṣedhyāt viśiṣṭasya bhinnasya pradeśa ādeḥ upalambhaḥ tasya pratiṣedhyasya api anupalambhanam tasmāt anupalambhoyam svayam pratyakṣataḥ gataḥ sva mātra vṛtteḥ gamakaḥ tad abhāva vyavasthiteḥ tasmāt ayam jñāna ātmakā anupalambhaḥ svayam ātmanā pratyakṣatas sva samvedanāt gataḥ pratītaḥ san sva mātra vṛtteḥ ātma mātra pratītāyāḥ tasya anupalabhyamānasya abhāva vyavasthiteḥ gamakaḥ anupalambhaḥ hi nimittam viṣayaḥ vā abhāva vyavahārasya iti ubhayathā api sva sattā mātreṇa abhāva vyavahāra hetuḥ 
PVV_4.275,0–4.276,2	 anyathā arthasya nāstitvam gamyatenu palambhataḥ upalambhasya na astitvam anyena iti anavasthitiḥ anyathā yadi svatas na anupalambha siddhiḥ tadā arthasya na astitvam anupalambhaḥ tatas gamyate upalambhasya na astitvam anupalabdhiḥ anyena anupalambhena gamyate sa upyanapalambha antareṇa iti apekṣāyām anavasthitiḥ syāt bhavatu tāvat dṛśyeṣu anupalabdhau= abhāva pratītiḥ adṛśye punar katham iti āha adṛśye niścaya ayogāt sthitiḥ anyatra bādhyate yathā aliṅgaḥ anya sattveṣu vikalpa ādiḥ na sidhyati anyatra dṛśya anupalabdhau satyām adṛśye viṣaye abhāva niścaya ayogāt sat vyavahārasya sthitiḥ bbādhyate upalambha pūrvvaka tvāt tasyāḥ yathā anyeṣu sattveṣu prāṇiṣu rāga ādi viṣayaḥ vikalpaḥ para citta jñāna ādiḥ ādinā a liṅgaḥ liṅga rahitaḥ sat vyavahāra viṣaya tvena na sidhyati 
PVV_4.277,0–4.277,4	 kim punar adṛśya anupalabdhau satyām api na sidhyati iti āha aniścaya phalāḥ hi eṣā na alam vyāvṛtti sādhane eṣā hi sati api arthe sambhavantī abhāvasya aniścaya phalāḥ tasmāt vyāvṛtteḥ abhāvasya sādhane na alam śaktāḥ ādya adhikriyate hetoḥ nniścitena eva sādhane ādyā dṛśya anupalabdhiḥ punar vyāvṛtti sādhane adhikriyate kasmāt iti āha hetoḥ vvipakṣāt kāraṇa vyāpaka anupalabdhibhyām vyāvṛtteḥ niścitenai sādhya artha sādhane adhikārāt na hi vipakṣāt aniścita vyāvṛttikaḥ hetuḥ gamakaḥ na hi kāraṇa vyāpaka anupalabdhibhyām anyaḥ vyāvṛtti sādhanaḥ kāraṇa viruddha upalambha ādiṣu api kāraṇa abhāvāt abhāvaḥ pratipādyaḥ 
PVV_4.278,0–4.278,1	 tasyāḥ svayam prayogeṣu svarūpam vā prayujyate artha bādhana rūpam vā bhāve bhāvāt abhāvataḥ tasyāḥ anupalabdheḥ prayogeṣu svayam śabda pratipāditam vā svarūpam prayujyate yathā svabhāva kāraṇa vyāpaka anupalabdhi ādiṣu niṣedhyasya arthasya bādhanam viruddham vā prayujyate yathā svabhāva kāraṇa vyāpaka viruddha upalabdhi ādiṣu prayujyate iti āha avikala kāraṇa tayā śītasya bhāve sattāyām satyām dahanasya bhāvāt abhāvataḥ nivṛtteḥ yathā śīta abhāva sādhane saha anavasthāna viruddhaḥ vahneḥ prayujyate na atra śīta sparśaḥ vahreḥ iti 
PVV_4.279,0–4.279,1	 anyonya bheda siddheḥ vā dhruva bhāva vināśa vat pramāṇa antara bādhāt vā sa apekṣa dhruva bhāva vat niṣedhya vidhīyamānayoḥ anyonyasya abhāva ātma tayā bheda siddheḥ vvā artha bādhana rūpam prayujyate dhruva bhāva vināśa vat nitya tva anitya tvayoḥ anyonya abhāva ātmaka tvena bheda siddhau paraspara parihāra sthiti lakṣaṇa tayā viruddham vināśi tvam nitya tva bādhane prayujyate yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ vināśi tvāt sa ca ayam paraspara parihāra sthiti viruddhaḥ kvacid sākṣāt vā prayujyate yathā nitya tvasya vināśi tvam kvacid dharma antara virodha grāhiṇā pramāṇa antareṇa paramparayā bādhanāt abādhita viruddha bhāvaḥ vā prayujyate sa apekṣa dhruva bhāvi tva vat yathā sa apekṣa dhruva bhāvayoḥ sākṣāt virodha abhāvepi dhruva bhāvi tvasya yat vyāpakam tena viruddham sa apekṣa tvam vyāpya vyāpakayoḥ ca vastutas tāt ātmyādayaḥ yat vyāpake virudhyate sa tat vyāpyena api iti pramāṇa antara bādhanāt eva avadhṛta viruddha bhāvam sa apekṣa tvam dhruva bhāvi tva bādhane prayujyate yathā na dhruva bhāvī kṛtakasya vināśaḥ hetu antara sāpekṣa tvāt iti 
PVV_iv.vii–2,0–4.280,4	 kasmāt punar hetu antarasā apekṣaḥ na dhruva bhāvi iti āha hetu antara samutthasya sannidhau niyataḥ kutas utpādakāt hetoḥ hetu antara dharmasya sannidhau sannidhāne niyataḥ kutas yathā kāraṇa antara sāpekṣasya vāsasi na avaśyaṃbhāva niyamaḥ rāgasya syāt etat bhāva hetuḥ eva anitya tva ākhyam dharmam bhāva nāśakam janayati tena naśvara svabhāva niyataḥ bhāvaḥ iti āha bhāva hetu bhava tve kim pāramparya pariśramaiḥ bhāva hetu bhava tve anitya tva ākhyasya dharmasya bhāva nāśakasya iṣyamāṇe pāramparye pariśramaiḥ ebhiḥ svīkṛtaiḥ kim prayojanam 
PVV_4.281,0–4.281,2	 tathā hi nāśanam janayitvā anyam sa hetuḥ tasya nāśakaḥtam eva naśvaram bhāvam janayet yadi kimbhavet sa bhāva hetuḥ anyam anitya tva ākhyam dharmam bhāva nāśanam janayitvā tasya abhāvasya na aśakaḥ iṣyate paraṃparayā yadi tu tam eva naśvaram bhāvam sākṣāt bhāva hetuḥ janayet tadā kiṃndūṣaṇam bhavet na kiñcid 
PVV_4.282,0–4.282,2	 api ca ātma upakārakaḥ kaḥ syāt tasya siddha ātmanaḥ sataḥ na ātma upakārakaḥ kaḥ syāt tena yaḥ samapekṣyate yaḥ yāvān anitya tva ākhyaḥ dharmaḥ ātmā bhāvasya sa kim upakārakaḥ san vināśakaḥ bhāvasya uta anupakārakaḥ eva tatra ādye pakṣe siddha ātmanaḥ bhāvasya sataḥ sarvu atas nirāśaṃsi asya kaḥ ātmā anitya ākhyaḥ dharmaḥ anyaḥ vā upakārakaḥ syāt atha dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ tadā anātmā upakārakaḥ syāt tena bhāvena yaḥ na aśaka tvena samapekṣyeta upakārakaḥ eva hi apekṣyate anupakāraka tve kā tasya apekṣā na aśaka tā vā 
PVV_4.283,0–4.283,2	 atha nāśa hetu ayogāt anapekṣyaḥ eva bhāvaḥ naśvara tāyām tadā anapekṣaḥ ca kimbhāvaḥ atathābhūtaḥ kadācana yathā na kṣepa bhāj iṣṭaḥ saḥ eva udbhūta nāśakaḥ anapekṣaḥ ca nāśe bhāvaḥ kim kasmāt kadācanā tathābhūtaḥ anaśvara svabhāvaḥ sarvadā eva naśvara svabhāva tā asya yuktāḥ yathā tvad mate saḥ eva kṛtakaḥ bhāvaḥ udbhūta nāśakaḥ unmukha nāśaka anitya tva svabhāvaḥ nāśa kāle akṣepa bhāga cira vināśī iṣṭaḥ tathā utpāda anantaram naśvara svabhāva tayā vinaśyet iti 
PVV_4.284,0–4.284,1	 kṣaṇam api anapekṣa tve bhāvaḥ bhāvasya na iti ced bhāvaḥ hi sa tathā bhūtaḥ abhāve bhāvaḥ tathā katham kṣaṇa kṣayi svabhāvāḥ bhāvāḥ sva hetoḥ eva jāyante vināśam pratyanapekṣa tve bhāvasya yathā dvitīye kṣaṇe bhāvaḥ na asti tathā prathamepi kṣaṇe na syāt iti kṣaṇam api bhāvasya bhāvaḥ na syāt iti ced ayuktam etat hi yasmāt sa bhāvaḥ tathā naśvara svabhāvaḥ iṣyate yadā tu bhāvaḥ eva na asti tadā abhāve bhāvasya bhāvaḥ tathā naśvaraḥ katham ucyate tatas labdha janmataḥ bhāvasya kṣaṇa antarān anuvṛtteḥ naśvaratā 
PVV_4.284,2–4.284,4	 tasmāt ye apara apekṣa tadbhāvāḥ tad bhāva niyatāḥ hi te asambhavat vibandhā ca sāmagrī kārya karmaṇi ye bhāvāḥ anapekṣa tadbhāvāḥ para apekṣām vinā sambhavat dharma viśeṣa saṃbhavāḥ te tasya bhāve dharmasya niyatāḥ kāraṇa sāmagrī va asambhavat vibandhāḥ vibandha kāraṇa rahitā kāryasya karmaṇi kriyāyām niyatā para nirapekṣāḥ ca bhāvāḥ sva nāśaḥ iti kṣaṇikāḥ sarvu asaṃskārāḥ iti akampyaḥ sau ga taḥ siṃhanādaḥ 
PVV_4.284,5–4.284,8	 na yat iha tat na nyāyyam tena uditena ca kim phalam yadim bahuśas tasyāḥ vṛttau guṇaḥ katham kasya kaḥ yadi paramasau vyākhyeya artha grahasya virodhinī vivṛtti racanā mātre tasmāt kṛtotra bhaya ādaraḥ ācārya śrīmanoratha nandi kṛtāyām vārttika vṛttau caturthaḥ paricchedaḥ samāptaḥ likhitā iyam paṃḍitavi bhū ti ca ndre ṇa yat atra puṇyam tad bhavatu a ācārya upādhyāya pūrvvaṅgam asakala satva rāśeḥ anuttara jñāna phala avāptayaḥ iti
